yasmin na staḥ karma vipākau yatas āstām kleśāḥ yasmai na alam a laṅghyāḥ nikhilānām
na avacchinnaḥ kāla dṛśā yaḥ kalayantyā loka īśaḥ tam kaiṭabha śatrum praṇamāmi
yaḥ sarva vid sarva vibhūti śaktiḥ vihīna doṣa upahita kriyā phalaḥ viśva udbhava anta sthiti hetuḥ īśaḥ namaḥ astu tasmai gurave guroḥ api
atha ityādi pātañjala yoga śāstra sūtra bhāṣya vivaraṇam ārabhyate
tatra anākhyāta sambandha prayojanam na puruṣa pravṛtti nivṛttibhyām paryāpnoti iti sūtrakāra abhiprete puruṣa pravṛtti nimitta bhūte sambandha prayojane pūrvam prakaṭīkriyete
tatra prayojanam tāvat cikitsā śāstre
tat yathā cikitsā śāstram catur vyūham rogaḥ roga hetuḥ ārogyam bhaiṣajyam iti
vidhi pratiṣedha niyama dvāreṇa ca tat catur vyūha viṣaya vyākhyāna param
evam iha api pariṇāma tāpa saṃskāra duḥkhaiḥ guṇa vṛtti virodhāt ca duḥkham eva sarvam vivekinaḥ iti
ārabhya catur vyūha tvam śāstrasya pradarśitam
tat yathā duḥkha pracuraḥ saṃsāraḥ heyaḥ
tasya avidyā nimittaḥ draṣṭṛ dṛśya saṃyogaḥ hetuḥ
viveka khyātiḥ aviplavā hāna upāyaḥ
viveka khyātau ca satyām avidyā nivṛttiḥ tad nivṛttau ātyantikaḥ draśṭṛ dṛśya saṃyoga uparamaḥ hānam tat eva kaivalyam iti
ārogya sthānīya kaivalya prayukta tvāt asya tat eva kaivalyam prayojanam
nanu ca heya tad hetū na prastotavye niṣprayojana tvāt
hāna prayuktam hi śāstram tad upāya bhūtā viveka khyātiḥ eva vaktavyā
na hi kaṇṭaka viddha caraṇa talasya tad apanayanam muktvā duḥkha tad hetū codyete
na etat evam heya tad kāraṇa apekṣa tvāt hāna upāyasya
yāvat idam anena upāyena hātavyam saṃsāra cakram asya ca avidyā nimittaḥ draṣṭṛ dṛśya saṃyogaḥ hetuḥ iti naḥ ākhyāyate tāvat na avidyā pratipakṣa bhūtā viveka khyātiḥ ākhyātum śakyate
heya tad hetumataḥ hāna upayā arthinaḥ rogiṇaḥ bhaiṣajya arthi tva darśanāt
na hi rogam roga hetum ca an apekṣya cikitsā śāstram upadiśyate
sambandhaḥ api viveka khyāteḥ hānam eva phalam sādhyam hānasya api viveka khyātiḥ eva sādhanam iti sādhya sādhanayoḥ itaretara niyamaḥ eva na anya sambandhaḥ
tat yathā bhaiṣajyasya ārogyam eva phalam ārogyasya api bhaiṣajyam eva sādhanam iti itaretara niyamaḥ sa ca śāstrāt iti
tasmāt sa saṃbandha prayojanam yoga anuśāsanam
nanu ca yadi hānam prayojanam tad upāyaḥ ca viveka khyātiḥ iti tatra vaktavyam atha viveka khyāti anuśāsanam iti
kim artham atha yoga anuśāsanam iti sūtritam
tad upāya tvāt yogasya
upāyaḥ eva vaktavyaḥ syāt
upeya upapradarśane hi upeyam upāyam prati sākāṅkṣam eva iti upāyaḥ sa aṅga kalāpaḥ punar api vaktavyaḥ syāt
tasmin ca abhihite sarvam eva abhihitam iti
katham tat upāya tvam
yatas āha sūtrakāraḥ yogāṅga anuṣṭhānāt aśuddhi kṣaye jñāna dīptiḥ ā viveka khyāteḥ iti
nirvicāra vaiśāradye adhyātma prasādaḥ ṛtaṃbharā tatra prajñā iti ca
tathā bhāṣyakāraḥ api āha yaḥ tu ekāgre cetasi sa bhūtam artham pradyotayati iti
bhūta artha avagatiḥ ca viveka khyātiḥ
tasmāt yuktam tat upāya yoga anuśāsanam eva ādau sūtritam iti
nanu ca yogāṅga anuṣṭhānāt viveka khyātiḥ tatra vaktavyam atha yogāṅga anuśāsanam iti na phalena upakramāt
iti
yadi evam ha anena upakramyeta na tasya upeya tvāt upeyam eva hi tat
yogaḥ punar sva aṅgānām upeyaḥ ca upāyaḥ ca viveka khyāteḥ aṇima ādi prāpteḥ ca iti abhi arhitataraḥ
phala tad upāya rūpa tvāt phala paya nimitta tvāt
uttara sūtra artha tvāt ca
na hi atha yoga aṅga anuśāsanam iti ukte yogaḥ citta vṛtti nirodhaḥ iti yuktam vaktum
tadā hi yama niyama ādi sūtram eva paṭhitavyam syāt
atha tat eva paṭhitavyam iti ced na yogopeyāyāḥ upeyāyāḥ hāna upāya bhūtāyāḥ viveka khyāteḥ phalasya ca hānasya sambandha yogaḥ citta vṛtti nirodhaḥ iti asya
sa katham punar etat sambandha pradarśana artham yāvatā nirbīja samādhi lakṣana abhidhānam etat
satyam evam tathā api hāna tad upāya sambandam avadyotayat eva sūtram nirbīja samādhi lakṣaṇa tām āpadyate
na hi nirodha lakṣaṇāt samādheḥ artha antaram hānam
kim tu etāvatā viśeṣaḥ nirodha lakṣaṇa samādhau samādheḥ na punar pravṛttiḥ hāne tu ātyantikī nivṛttiḥ iti
samādhi avasthāyām tu hāna aviśeṣaḥ eva
tathā ca āha tadā draṣṭuḥ svarūpe avasthānam iti
śvarūpa pratiṣṭhā ca citi śaktiḥ kaivalyam iti svarūpa pratiṣṭha tvam pratiṣṭham hi kaivalyam āha
tatas ca nirbīja samādhinā kaivalyam eva śāstra artha pratyaya draḍhimne sākṣātkriyate
tasmāt yat ucyate kaiḥ cit sa bīja samādhiḥ kaivalya sādhanam iti tat na
kim tarhi khyātiḥ eva sādhanam avidyā nivṛtti dvāreṇa
avidyā nimittaḥ hi bandhaḥ
tasmāt yadi api yoga anuśāsanam sūtritam tathā api khyāti artha tvāt yogasya tat dvāreṇa khyāti hāna saṃbandham api darśayati iti suṣṭhū ucyate uttara sūtra saṃbandha artham ca yoga anuśāsanam iti sūtrayitavyam iti
yadi api phala arthinām tat phala sādhanam pratyutpanna ākāṅkṣāṇām sādhana upadeśaḥ api asti
tathā api na tat prayojanam sarvasya phala uddeśena pravṛtteḥ tat eva prayojanam iti
yoga anuśāsanam iti
yathā śiṣyaḥ anuśiṣyate viśiṣṭa pravṛtti nivṛtti niyama dvāreṇa tathā viśiṣṭa sādhya sādhana tad aṅga niyama mātra sādṛśyāt antevāsi anuśāsana vat yogāḥ anuśāsanam iti ucyate
anuśiṣtṭiḥ anuśāsanam yogaḥ anuśiṣyate anena asmin iti vā yoga anuśāsanam śāstram
atha iti ayam adhikāra arthaḥ
adhikāraḥ ārambhaḥ prastāvaḥ arthaḥ abhidheyaḥ asya śiṣṭa smṛti pramāṇyāt
nanu ca ānantarya arthasya atha śabdasya smaranti śiṣṭāḥ
tathā ca āha vṛttāt anantarasya prakriyāḥ arthaḥ dṛṣṭāḥ iti
na sarvatra ārambha artha tvāt
ānantaryasya ca gamyamāna tvāt
yathā putraḥ iti ukte pitā gamyate na ca putra śabdasya arthaḥ pitā tathā iha api ārambhaḥ evā abhidhīyate ānantaryam tu pratīyate
atas eva ca vṛttāt anantarasya prakriyā dṛṣṭaḥ iti ucyate
yadi ca ānantarya arthaḥ abhaviṣyat tadā vṛttāt anantaye arthe prakriyāyāḥ iti avadiṣyat
anantarasya iti ca anantara bhāvinaḥ eva abhidhānam
api ca evam hi smṛtiḥ kiñcid avyayam vibhakti artha pradhānam kiñcid kriyā pradhānam
uccais nīcais ityādi vibhakti artha pradhānam hi ruj pṛthak ityādi kriyā pradhānam iti
na ca etat vyatirekeṇa avyayānām arthaḥ vidyate
tatra atha śabdasya ānantarya artha tve sati vibhakti aśravaṇam vibhakti śravaṇam ayuktam sattva pradhāna tvāt
ārambha kriyā artha tve tu na vibhakti artha aśravaṇam ayuktam a sattva pradhāna tvāt iti
tasmāt atha śabdaḥ prastāva arthe eva iti yuktam atha iti adhikāra arthaḥ iti
svarūpa avadyotana arthaḥ iti śabdaḥ
yathā gauḥ iti āha iti
prasiddhaḥ pi atha śabda arthaḥ adhikriyamāṇa viṣaye śiṣya buddhi samādhāna artham kīrtyate
siddhaḥ hi ayam nyāyaḥ śrutau vyākhyāsyāmi te vyācakṣāṇasya tu nididhyāsasva iti
kaḥ punar yogaḥ yasya anuśāsanam prastutam iti āha yogaḥ samādhiḥ iti
samādhi grahaṇāt yuji yoge iti nivartya yujaḥ samādhau iti ayam gṛhītaḥ
yogaḥ samādhānam
nanu ca yogaḥ samādhiḥ iti evam antena vyākhyāyate sūtre sa ca sārvabhaumaḥ ityādi bhāṣyam asaṃbandham dṛśyate
na eṣa doṣaḥ
iha samādhiḥ iti ukte samādhīyamāna apekṣa tvāt samādhīyamānānām ca bahu tvāt kimātmā samāḍhīyate
kim vā śarīram āhosvit indriyāṇi iti bahu vidām bahudhā vipratipatteḥ sva viśeṣaṇa ākāṅkṣa tvāt ca samādheḥ kasya ayam
kiṃviśeṣaṇakaḥ
iti anuṣakte praśne idam āha sa ca sārvabhaumaḥ cittasya dharmaḥ iti
cittasya dharmaḥ na ātma ādīnām
tat ca cittam svayam eva samādhīyate samādhāḥ atra ntar apekṣa tvāt
kāḥ punar bhūmayaḥ iti atas āha kṣiptam mūḍham ityādayaḥ bhūmayaḥ iti
kṣiptam iti karma kartari niṣṭhā
yathā bhinnaḥ kusūlaḥ svayam eva iti
kṣiptam aniṣṭa viṣaya asañjanena stimitam
mūḍham nirvivekam
vikṣiptam nānā kṣiptam
karma kartari eva
viveka kṣamam ca vikṣipta tvāt eva
ekāgram tulya pratyaya pravāham
niruddham iti pratyaya śūnyam cittam
nanu ca bhūmiṣu dharmeṣu vivakṣiteṣu kimartham kṣiptam ityādinā dharmī ucyate
na eṣa doṣaḥ dharmiṇā dharmaḥ eva upadiśyate
dharmāṇām dharmi viṣaya tvāt
yathā go tve kim liṅgam iti pṛṣṭe viṣāṇī kakudmān prānta vāladhiḥ iti dharmiṇā dharmaḥ eva upadiśyate
tasmāt kṣepa ādayaḥ cittasya bhūmayaḥ dharmāḥ iti arthaḥ
nanu ca bhūmīnām citta dharma tve samādheḥ ca katham bhūmibhiḥ samādhiḥ ādhāra tvena viśeṣyate sārvabhaumaḥ iti
sāmānya bhūta tvāt samādheḥ
bhūmīnām ca viśeṣa tvāt
yathā kṣiptam tiṣṭhati mūḍham tiṣṭhati vikṣiptam ekāgram ca iti kṣipta ādi bhūmiṣu sthitiḥ anuvartate sāmānyam
sthitiḥ ca samādhiḥ
tasmāt sāmānya rūpam sarvāsu bhūmiṣu prādhānyena vartate iti
sarva bhūmi pṛthivī iti aiśvarya arthīyaḥ n pratyayaḥ
anuśatika ādi tvāt ubhaya pada vṛddhi h
anye punar bāhya ādhyātmakān saṃyama viṣayān bhūmayaḥ iti ācakṣate
teṣām vikṣipte cetasi iti sāmānādhikaraṇya anupapattiḥ
sva vacana virodheḥ ca katham kṣipyate asmin iti kṣiptam muhyate smin iti mūḍham yadā ca evam na tadā saṃyama viṣaya tā
tatra kṣepa ādi asaṃbhavāt ekāgra avasthāyām hi saṃyamaḥ bhavati
kim ca anyat kṣipeḥ ca dhrauvya ādi artha abhāvāt adhikaraṇe niṣṭhā pratayayā abhāvaḥ
kim ca niruddhe cetasi saṃyamasya api tatra abhāvāt vṛtti śūnya tvāt saṃyama viṣaya abhāvaḥ
na hi nirodhe viṣaya viśeṣe cittam nirudhyate
tadā hi viṣayi tvāt nivartate
pri gaṇanā anupapattiḥ ca
na hi kṣipta ādayaḥ pancā eva saṃyamasya viṣayāḥ
teṣām ānantyāt
nanu ca anyathā yogam kecid icchanti
tathā ca āhuḥ indriya manaḥ artha sannikarṣāt sukha duḥkhe tad anārambhaḥ ātma sthe manasi sa śarīrasya sukha duḥkha abhāvaḥ prāṇa manaḥ vinigraha apekṣaḥ saṃyogaḥ yogaḥ iti
tat iti prakṛta apekṣam
yaḥ asau sukha duḥkhayoḥ ātma indriya monaḥ artha sannilarṣaḥ hetuḥ tasya anārambhaḥ tad anutpattiḥ
sa katham bhavati
ātma sthe manasi na indriya sthe
sa śarīrasya a viśīrṇa śarīrasya
tadā kāraṇa abhāvāt kārya abhāvaḥ iti sannikarṣa abhāve sukha duḥkhayoḥ api abhāvaḥ tasyām avasthāyām yaḥ asau vibhoḥ ātmanaḥ manasā saṃyogaḥ sa prāṇa manaḥ vinigraha apekṣaḥ saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ yogaḥ iti
atra ucyate ātma sthe manasi iti ayuktam sarvadā ātma stha tvāt manasaḥ
indriya ādi sannikarṣa anārambha apekṣayā ātma sthe iti ced tad anārmbhe iti eva siddha tvāt ātma sthe manasi iti anarthakam syāt
kim ca anyat muktasya api manasaḥ ātma stha tvāt indriya sannikarṣa abhāvāt ca yogaḥ prāpnoti
tasya api hi sarva gata tvāt manasaḥ ca nitya tvāt sarvadā ātma stha tvam eva
kim ca ātmanaḥ pradeśa abhāvāt ātma sthaḥ iti ayuktam
na ca api upacarita ātma pradeśa saṃyogaḥ paramārthasya yogasya hetuḥ syāt
upacaritasya mithyātvāt
kim ca anyat manaḥ artha sannikarṣa abhāvaḥ iti eva sddheḥ siddham indriya grahaṇam anarthakam syāt
atha indriyaiḥ vinā manaḥ artha sannikarṣa abhāvāt tad anārambhaḥ iti prāpti abhāve pratiṣedhaḥ na yuktaḥ iti ced
na etat evam vinā indriyaiḥ manaḥ artha sannikarṣaḥ na asti iti arthāt sannikarṣa pratiṣedham kurvatā viṣaya prāptiḥ indriya dvārā pratipāditā syāt
kim ca anyat sarva prāṇabhājām indriya manaḥ artha sannikarṣāt sukha duḥkha pratilambhasya prasiddha tvāt ātmanaḥ saṃbandhasya ca nitya tvāt sukha duḥkha abhāvaḥ yogaḥ iti eva siddheḥ tatra sūtra śeṣaḥ narthakaḥ syāt
atha api syāt indriya manaḥ artha sannikarṣa grahaṇāt ṛte sukha duḥkha abhāvaḥ iti etāvati sati muktasya api sukha duḥkha abhāvāt yogi tva prasaṅgaḥ iti tad nivṛtti artham sūtra śeṣa grahaṇam iti
tat ca na muktasya sukha duḥkha prāpti abhāvāt prāpti pūrva pratiṣedhasya nyāyya tvāt yasya sukha duḥkha prāptiḥ tad viṣayaḥ sukha duḥkha abhāvaḥ eva yogaḥ iti sūtra śeṣa pratyākhyānam yujyate
kim ca anyat upātte api sa śarīra grahaṇe muktāt vinivṛttiḥ na śakyate kartum niṣprayojana tvāt
sukha duḥkha abhāvaḥ ced yogaḥ vidyamānam api śarīram kārya akaraṇāt anarthakam syāt
kārya anapekṣāyām hi mukta amuktayoḥ aviśeṣaḥ eva
kim ca anyat prāṇa manaḥ vinigraha apekṣaḥ iti api na ghaṭate
vidhārakasya prayatnasya ātma samaveta tvāt a vidyamāne api manasaḥ kriyāvat tve indriyeṇa a saṃyujya manaḥ prāṇa manaḥ nigrahau na kartum paryāpyate
indriya saṃyoge ca manasaḥ tad anārambhaḥ iti ayuktam
manasaḥ ca prāṇa nigrahe vyāpṛta vyāvṛta tvāt anārambha anupapattiḥ
na ca asati indriya vāyu sannikarṣe prāṇa nigrahaḥ
na ca anigṛhīte prāṇe yogaḥ ātma stha vidhāraka prayatna dvārā manaḥ gata kriyā saṃbandha hetu tvāt prāṇa nigrahasya
atha api syāt yogaḥ samādhiḥ iti
tat ca na niṣkriya tvāt ātmanaḥ nitya samādhānam eva sthitiḥ ca samādhiḥ iti ucyate
tasmāt yuktam abhidhīyate sa ca sārvabhaumaḥ cittasya dharmaḥ iti
yadi evam samādhiḥ ced yogaḥ sa ca sārvabhaumaḥ citta dharmaḥ sa ca sarva janānām ayatna siddhiḥ kṣipta ādi anugata tvāt
tathā ca sati yathā eva śvāsa praśvāsa ādīnām prayatnāt ṛte siddhi tvāt tad karaṇam anarthakam evam yoga anuśāsanam api anarthakam prāptam iti atas āha tatra vikṣipte anavikṣipte cetasi vikṣepa upasarjanī bhūtaḥ samādhiḥ na yoga pakṣe vartate iti
kṣipta ādi anugatasya yogapakṣa anabhipreta tvāt
na hi kṣepa ādi anugataḥ samādhiḥ bhūta artha avadyotana ādi kṣamaḥ kṣepa ādi pradhāna tvāt
vikṣepa niṣedhena eva hi pradhāna malla nibarhaṇa nyāyena kṣipta mūḍhayoḥ api niṣedhaḥ kṛtaḥ
pradhāna tā ca vikṣepa samādheḥ adhikāra yogya tvāt
vikṣepa stham hi cittam apakṣapātāt iṣtam viṣayam upanetum śakyate
na hi viṣaya āsañjana ādinā kṣiptam iṣta viṣaya viyoga ādinā vā mūḍham anyathā upanetum pāryate
yoga pakṣaḥ iti
samādhi tve sati api kārya akaraṇāt pakṣaḥ iti ucyate
yathā gacchataḥ pratipadam vidyamānā api sthitiḥ sthiti kārya ākārāt na sthitiḥ iti ucyate

sārvabhaumaḥ iti tu prādhānyam sāmānyena sarva bhūmiṣu vṛtteḥ
yadi upasarjanī bhāvaḥ samādhi pakṣa āvṛttau kāraṇam iha api ekāgre ekāgra tā upasarjana tvam syāt
tatas ca yoga pakṣa āvṛttiḥ iti ced atas āha yaḥ tu ekāgraḥ iti
na ekāgra tāyām bhūmi upasarjana tvam
kutas
kleśa karma a prabala tvāt
kleśa karma a prabala tve na hi vikṣepa ādīnām udayaḥ
ekāgra tā bhūmau samādhiḥ yaḥ sa bhūtam artham yathā ātmānam pradyotayati avagamayati
ayogi artha jñānam ayathā bhūta tva gandhitam eva iti bhūta grahanam
kṣiṇoti kṣapayati pañca parvaṇaḥ vidyā ādīn kleśān
karma bandhanāni karmāṇi eva bandhanāni dharma adharma vimiśra karma jātāni janma ādi nibandhanāni ślathayati śithilīkaroti nirodham āmukhīkaroti abhimukhīkaroti
sa samprajñātaḥ iti ākhyāyate ācāryaiḥ
sa ca vitarka anugataḥ vicāra anugataḥ ityādi bhāṣyam
samprajñātasya lakṣaṇa abhidhāne prāpte abhyarhita tvāt asamprajñātasya eva lakṣaṇam yuktam iha vaktum iti samprajñātam upariṣṭāt pravedayiṣyāmaḥ iti ucyate
itas ca asaṃprajñātasya lakṣaṇam iha eva vaktavyam samprajñāta nirapekṣaḥ u pi asamprajñātaḥ vairāgya virāma pratyaya abhyāsābhyām sidhyati iti etat pradarśana artham
iha samprajñāta lakṣaṇa abhidhāne tad uttara kāle ca asamprajñāta lakṣaṇa abhdhāne samprajñāta apekṣayā eva asamprajñāta samādhau adhikāraḥ iti āśaṅkā syāt tasmāt upariṣṭāt pravedayiṣyāmaḥ iti āha
sarva vṛtti nirodhe tu asaṃprajñāte iti
tuśabdaḥ arthaḥ
tasya evaṃvidhasya samādheḥ asaṃprajñātasya eva kevalasya lakṣaṇa abhidhitsayā idam sūtram pravavṛte pravṛttam yogaḥ citta vṛtti nirodhaḥ vaktavyam
nanu ca tasya lakṣaṇam abhidhātum etat sūtram pravṛttam tathā ca sati yogasya citta vṛtti nirodhaḥ iti vaktavyam sāmānādhikaraṇyam na yuktam
na hi lakṣyam eva lakṣaṇam syāt
citta vṛtti nirodha lakṣaṇaḥ iti vā vaktavyam
na eṣa doṣaḥ
lakṣye lakṣaṇa adhyāsāt
yathā yam piṇḍaḥ devadattaḥ iti lakṣye lakṣaṇam adhyasyate pratyasyate
nanu ca sarva vṛtti nirodhe tu asamprajñātaḥ tasya ca idam lakṣaṇam tatas ca yogaḥ sarva citta vṛtti nirodhaḥ iti vaktavyam
na ca uktam
lakṣaṇam
sarva śabda agrahaṇe tāvat kāraṇam ucyate yadi sarva grahaṇam kriyate tadā eka deśa nirodha nimittasya saṃprajñātasya yoga tvam nivartitam syāt
tat mā abhūt iti sarva śabda agrahaṇam
astu tarhi saṃprajñāta asaṃprajñātayoḥ sāmānya lakṣaṇam viśeṣa anupādānāt
na eṣa doṣaḥ
yoge prakṛte punar yoga grahaṇāt
viśeṣa avivakṣāyām hi yoga grahaṇam na arthavat syāt
nanu ca anuśāsane bhūta tvāt yogasya iha yoga grahaṇe asati citta vṛtti nirodhaḥ iti anuśāsana artha tā bhavet sūtrasya nā evam yoga anuśāsanasya prastuta tvāt
yoga anuśāsanam hi prārabdham na ayoga anuśāsanam tad lakṣaṇa abhidhāne hi atiprasaṅgaḥ padārtha asaṅgatiḥ ca
na hi citta vṛtti nirodhaḥ yoga anuśāsanam iti padārthaḥ saṅgacchate
evam api yoga grahaṇāt kutas
asaṃprajñātasya eva lakṣaṇam na punar saṃprajñātasya lakṣaṇam syāt yoga grahaṇasya aviśiṣṭa tvāt iti
ucyate avyabhicārāt
vyabhicarati na tat tasya lakṣaṇam nirodhaḥ tu asaṃprajñāte api vartate iti saṃprajñātam vyabhicarati
na hi viṣāṇi tvam goḥ liṅgam mahiṣī ādibhiḥ vyabhicārāt
nanu ca asaṃprajñātam api vyabhicarati saṃprajñātasya api heya vṛtti nirodha tvāt
satyam evam kim tu na nirodhāt anyena lakṣayitum asaṃprajñātaḥ śakyate
nirodhaḥ eva tu tasya lakṣaṇam anyasya abhāvāt
saṃprajñātasya tu asādhāraṇa vitarka ādi lakṣaṇa lakṣya tvāt
yathā sparśa lakṣaṇam iti ukte vāyuḥ eva asādhāraṇyāt lakṣyate sparśavat tvena atha ca vidyate eva sparśavat tvam tejaḥ prabhṛtiṣu api
evam ca sati yoga grahaṇam anuvāda mātram
atas eva ca sarva grahaṇam na kṛtam sūtre
nirodha grahaṇena eva asaṃprajñāta lakṣaṇa tve siddhe yadi sarva grahaṇam kriyate tat saṃprajñātasya yoga tām nivārayet
tasmāt asaṃprajñātasya eva idam lakṣaṇam
tathā ca upasaṃharati bhāṣyakāraḥ na tatra kiṃcid saṃprajñāyate iti asaṃprajñātaḥ sa yogaḥ citta vṛtti nirodhaḥ iti
citta vṛtti tad nirodha vyācikhyāsayā cittam hi ityādi bhāṣyam kimātmakam punar tat cittam yasya vṛtti nirodhe yogaḥ iti atas āha cittam hi prakhyā pravṛtti sthiti śīla tvāt triguṇam iti
tatra cittam triguṇam iti vyākhyāyate prakhyā pravṛtti sthiti śīla tvāt iti hetuḥ
prakhyā prakhyānam prakāśanam sa hi sattva guṇasya dharmaḥ
pravṛttiḥ pravartanam vyāpāraḥ sa hi rajaḥ dharmaḥ
sthitiḥ sthānam varaṇam pratibandhaḥ iti sa ca tamaḥ dharmaḥ
evam śīlāḥ hi sattva ādayaḥ guṇāḥ cittam ca prakhyā ādi śīlam tasmāt trayāṇām guṇānām pariṇāmaḥ cittam bhavitum arhati
tasya ca prakhyā ādi hetoḥ asiddham āśaṅkya āha prakhyā svarūpam hi citta sattvam iti
hi śabdaḥ prasiddha avadyotana arthaḥ
prasiddham hi loke śāstre ca sarva avabhāsaka tvam cittasya
cittam eva sattvam citta sattvam sattva pradhāna guṇa pariṇāma tvāt
atha vā anya saṃsarga viyogābhyām aneka vṛtti khyāti mātram ca cittam spaṣṭam darśayitum śakyate iti bravīti prakhyā svarūpam hi citta sattvam iti
idānīm vṛttayaḥ vyākhyāyante
tāsām ca aneka tvam rajaḥ tamasoḥ udbhāvi bhava nimittam viruddha tvam ca iti āha rajaḥ tamobhyām saṃsṛṣṭam sampradhānābhyām yadā saṃsṛṣṭam tadānīm aiśvarya viṣaya priyam bhavati
prītiḥ rāgaḥ aiśvarya viṣaya rāga yuktāḥ vṛttayaḥ bhavanti iti arthaḥ
tat tamasā anuviddham
tat eva prakhyā svarūpam cittam yadā guṇa bhūta rajaskena udbhūtena tamasā anuviddham tadānīm adharma ādi catuṣṭaya viṣayāḥ vṛttayaḥ kliṣṭāḥ jāyante
tat eva prakṣīṇa moha āvaraṇām iti
bhūta tamaskam tamaḥ kṣayāt eva jaladhra apagamāt iva pari ravi bambam sarvatas pradyotamānam rajaḥ mātrayā rajaḥ leśena anuviddham yadā tadā dharma ādi upagatam
dharma ādi catuṣṭaya viṣayāḥ vṛttayaḥ akliṣṭāḥ bhavanti
yadā tat eva rajaḥ mala apetam sva rūpa pratiṣṭham kevalena svena prakhyā rūpeṇa avasthitam tadā sattva puruṣa anyathā khyāti mātram bhavati
sattvam cittam puruṣaḥ bhaktā tayoḥ anya tā vivikta tā tad khyātiḥ tad avagamaḥ tanmātra grahaṇam kleśa ādi abhāva pradarśana artham
dharma megha dhyāna upagam bhavati dharma meghaḥ nāma samādhiḥ
tat eva prasaṃkhyāna balāt rajaḥ tamasī tiraskṛtya kevalena khyāti ātmanā puruṣa sva rūpa mātra darśanena avasthānam dhyānam prasaṃkhyānam iti ācakṣate dhyāyinaḥ yoginaḥ
evam vṛtti svarūpe vyākhyāte tad nirodha pradarśana artham āha citi śaktiḥ iti ādi
citiḥ eva śaktiḥ citi śaktiḥ
yathā paci ādayaḥ śaktayaḥ śaktimat apekṣā prāpaṇīya janmānaḥ na svayam śaktayaḥ
citiḥ punar svayam eva śaktiḥ na artha antaram apekṣate
tena nitya avasthita tvam
citi śabdasya cit mātra abhidhyāyinaḥ śakti śabdena sāmānādhikaraṇyam avikṛta rūpāyāḥ eva citeḥ viṣayi tva pradarśana artham
yasmāt evam atas apariṇāminī
vyavasthite dharmiṇi dharma antara tiras bhāvena dharma antara prādur bhāvaḥ pariṇāmaḥ
na pariṇāmitum śīlam asyāḥ iti apariṇāminī
atas eva apratisaṅkramā pariṇāminaḥ eva citta ādeḥ viṣaya ādau pratisaṅkrama darśanāt
atas eva darśita viṣayā darśitaḥ antaḥkaraṇena viṣayaḥ asyāḥ iti
tena eva śuddhā
atas eva anantā deśataḥ kālataḥ ca
pūrva pūrvam uttarasya uttarasya hetu tvena draṣṭavyam
vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ cittam indriyāṇi ca
sattva guṇa atimikā sattvam eva guṇaḥ sattva guṇaḥ tasya iva ātmā svarūpam avabhāsaḥ yasyāḥ sā iyam sattva guṇa āatmakā avabhāsa svarūpā iti arthaḥ
vṛtti aviśiṣṭa vṛtti tvāt vā sattva guṇa ātmikāḥ iti ucyate
yadi vā khyātyā saṃbandhyate khyātiḥ sattva guṇa ātmikā iti
atas citi śakteḥ ukta lakṣaṇāyāḥ viparītā vilakṣaṇā viveka khyātiḥ pariṇāma ādimatī
yasmāt puruṣāt utkṛṣṭāt pariṇāma ādi guṇa rahitāt nikṛṣṭā priṇāma ādi guṇa yuktā atas sva rūpa doṣa darśanāt tasyām viraktam aparaktam tām api khyātim ātmanaḥ niruṇāt hi
tat avastham nirodha avastham saṃskāra upagam saṃskāra mātra avaśeṣam
niruddhāsu vṛttiṣu vṛtti janitāḥ saṃskārāḥ eva avaśiṣyante
etasyām nirodha bhūmau yaḥ samādhiḥ sa nirbījaḥ
nirgatam bījam atra kleśa ādi bījam sarvam utsannam asmin iti
tasmāt asaṃprajñāta samādhi lakṣaṇa artham eva sūtram iti upasaṃharati sa yogaḥ citta vṛtti nirodhaḥ iti
yogaḥ citta vṛtti nirodhaḥ iti uktam tatra boddhṛ tvena eva puruṣa sadbhāva adhigamaḥ viṣaya bhūta vṛtti nirodhe ca viṣayiṇaḥ api boddhuḥ puruṣasya nirodham kaścid api tathā ca sati tad kaivalya prāpti upāyasya api viveka khyāteḥ anarthaka tvam manvīta yoga anuśāsanasya api tad arthasya niṣphala tvam pratipadyeta tasmāt puruṣasya vṛtti nirodhāt anirodham darśayitu kāmaḥ khyāteḥ ca api phalam sākṣāt darśayan āha tad avasthe cetasi ityādi
tad avasthe nirodha avasthe
sva viṣaya abhāvāt sva viṣayaḥ citta vṛttiḥ tad abhāve abhāvāt
buddhi bodha ātmā buddhim vṛtti rūpena pariṇatām budhyate iti buddheḥ boddhā puruṣaḥ
tad bodhanam eva hi puruṣasya svam rūpam na anyaḥ boddhā na anyat boddhanam
boddhuḥ ca bodhanāt anya tve sati vikriyā ātmaka tā syāt
tatas ca darśita viṣaya tvam ca na syāt tathā ca karaṇa antara apekṣi tvam puruṣasya prasajyate
tasmāt bodhanam boddhṛ tvam ca upacaritam tad vṛtti sārūpyeṇa
tathā ca vakṣyati draṣṭā dṛśi mātraḥ iti
tasmāt āha buddhi bodhanam eva ātmā svarūpam yasya sa buddhi bodha ātmā puruṣaḥ kiṃsvabhāvaḥ kim naśvara svabhāvaḥ sadbhāve vā kiṃsvabhāvaḥ katham vā sadbhāvaḥ iti
tadā draṣṭuḥ svarūpe
avasthānam
yadā niruddhāḥ vṛttayaḥ svarūpa pratiṣṭhā tadānīm citi śaktiḥ
svarūpa pratiṣṭhā iti arthaḥ
yathā kaivalye
tadā sadbhāvam tu na tat su ābhāsam dṛṣya tvāt iti evamādinā vakṣyati
tatra siddhe sadbhāve tatas ākṛṣya prāpta āśaṅkā nivṛtti artham ucyate svarūpa pratiṣṭhā iti
siddha vat vyākhyātam sūtram tatra idam prasaktam itaratra na sva rūpa pratiṣṭhā iti
anyathā hi tadā iti viśeṣaṇa ānarthakyam syāt
na ced anyatra svarūpa pratiṣṭhā tatra avasthā antara yogāt pariṇāmi tvāt adoṣaḥ prāpnoti iti tat parijihīrṣaye āha vyutthāna citte tu sati tathāḥ api bhavanti iti
anena anyatra api sva rūpa pratiṣtha tvam darśayati
na tathā iti anena tadā iti viśeṣaṇasya arthavat tvam khyāpayati
itaraḥ tu tathā api bhavanti anena ced sva rūpa pratiṣṭha tvam ucyate na tathā iti ca sva rūpa pratiṣṭha tva niṣedhaḥ ced ekasya vastunaḥ tathābhāvaḥ ca atathā bhāvaḥ ca virudhyate iti vīkṣā āpannaḥ pṛcchati katham tarhi iti
itaraḥ āha vṛtti sārūpyam itaratra iti
kasmāt punar vṛtti sārūpyam
darśita viṣaya tvāt
ubhayatra svarūpa pratiṣṭha tva aviśeṣe api vṛtti sārūpya asārūpya kṛtaḥ viśeṣaḥ iti na tathābhāva atathābhāva virodhaḥ
nanu ca vṛtti sārūpya yoge sati avasthā antara yogāt pariṇāmi tva ādi doṣaḥ prāpnoti eva
na
darśita viṣaya tvena parihṛta tvāt
citta vṛtti adhyāropitam hi tat na svatas sphaṭika ādi upadhāna uparoga vat
vyutthāne iti
nirodhāt anyatra yaḥ cittasya kliṣṭa ādayaḥ vṛttayaḥ tābhiḥ aviśiṣṭā sadṛśī vṛttiḥ svarūpam asya citta vṛtti vyatirekeṇa sva rūpa vti atirekeṇa ca puruṣasya vṛtti abhāvāt sadā jñāta viṣaya tve pariṇāma anupapatteḥ ca
tathā ca pūrva ācārya sūtram ekam eva darśanam buddhi puruṣayoḥ
kim tat iti āha khyātiḥ eva darśanam
buddhi vṛttiḥ eva darśanam
khyāyate puruṣeṇa iti ca khyātiḥ khyāte nayā ca buddhi puruṣayoḥ svarūpam iti khyātiḥ
sā eva arthākāra tayā arthākāraḥ nayā gṛhyate iti karaṇam svena ca khyāti rūpeṇa gṛhyate iti karma ca bhavati
tathā dṛśyate iti darśanam dṛśyate nena iti ca jñāyate iti jñānam jñāyate nena iti ca sarvam evamādi drṣṭavyam
yat tu khyāti kartṛ tve cittasya tat eva jñāyate jānāti ca iti jñānāt iti ca iti jñāna antara kalpnā vaiyarthya prasaṅgaḥ iti tasya na tat su ābhāsam dṛśya tvāt iti atra eva parihāram vakṣyāmaḥ
nanu ca yadi citta parvi jṛmbhitam evā idam sarvam paruṣaḥ ced udāste katham asau bhoktā iti
na kāraka vaicitryāt
kānicid vyāpriyamāṇāni kārakāṇi kānicid vyāpārāt ṛte sannidhi mātreṇa kartṛ tvam pratipadyante
yathā pacati iti adhiśrayaṇa ādiṣu vyāpriyamāṇaḥ puruṣaḥ kartā iti ucyate
sthālī sambhava dhāraṇābhyām a vyāpriyamṇā eva pacati iti ucyate
tathā sthālī madhya gatam ākācam avakācam dadāti na tasya vyāpāram pratīmaḥ
yathā ca rājā darśana mātreṇa eva kartā
sarvāṇi ca kārakāṇi sveṣu vyāpāreṣu kartyṇi
na ca ādityaḥ prakāśayan karaṇa antaram apekṣate vyāpriyate vā
na hi prakāśanam a vidyamānam utpādayati gamana ādi vat
prakāśa ātma tā eva hi tasya sadbhāvaḥ tathā api dṛśi mātreṇa ghaṭa ādīnām prakāśa rūpeṇa abhivyakteḥ prakāśayati iti ucyate evam iha api dṛśi mātreṇa puruṣeṇa dṛśyamānām citta vṛttīnām cit ātmanā vyāpyamāna tvāt draṣṭā puruṣaḥ iti imam artham darśayati cittam ayaskānta maṇi kalpam iti
yasya api ātma manaḥ saṃyogāt jñānam utpadyate tasya api jñānena jñeyam vyāpnuvan na ātmā jñātā iti ucyate na vyāpriyamānaḥ
jñānasya api jñānam api guṇa tve sati niṣkriya tvāt ātmanaḥ eva artham darśayati
nā api kriyān abhyupagamāt jānāti ityādi na upapadyate
jñānena hi jñeyam vyāpnivan jānāti iti ucyate
kim ca anyat ātma manaḥ saṃyogāt apūrva jñāna utpattau satī ātma manaḥ tat jñānam na manasaḥ
ātmā eva jñnāti na manaḥ iti kaḥ hetuḥ bhavet
atha api syāt ātmanaḥ samavāyi kāraṇa tvāt iti
na etat evam asiddha tvāt
yathā eva jñānam ātmanaḥ iti sādhyam evam ātmanaḥ eva samavāyi kāraṇa ttvam na manasaḥ iti sādhyam anātma svarūpa tve sati ubahaya saṃyoga ja tva abhyupagamāt
atha api syāt jñāna āhita saṃskārasya ātma naḥ smṛti eka kartṛ tvena pratisandhāna darśanāt iti na tasya api sādhya tvāt
tatra api jñāna saṃskāra smṛti pratisandhāna ādīni ātmanaḥ eva na manasaḥ iti sādhanīyāni
phalena samāna āśraya tvāt icchā ādīnām iti ced na tatra api tulya tvāt
saṃyoga ja tve sati ātmanaḥ phala icchā ādīni na manasaḥ iti duḥsādham eva
kim ca asya jñānasya api jñeya tva abhyupagamāt anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ
na hi jñānam anyena karaṇa bhūtena jñānena vijñātum śakyam tat api anyena tat api anyena iti aniṣṭha prasaṅgāt
atha anavasthā prasaṅga parihārāya dūram api gatvā kiṃcid jñānam ādyam vā jñāna antareṇa na gṛhyate svayam ātmanā eva gṛhyate iti tathā jñāna vat arthasya api svayam grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ
atha dīpa vat svayam avabhāsate ca avabhāsayati ca avabhāsa ātmaka tvāt arthasya an avabhāsa ātmaka tvāt adoṣaḥ iti ced tathā api prakāśa svarūpeṣu artheṣu vijñānena agrahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ
atha ātma samaveta tva avabhāsana rūpābhyām svayam grahaṇam bahis prakāśa ātmakānām tu jñāna viparīta dharna tvāt adoṣaḥ iti ced tat ca na yadi ca ātma samaveta tvam prakāśa ātmaka tvam ca jñānasya svayam grahaṇe hetuḥ syāt sarve sarvajjāḥ prāpnuvanti
atha grāhya ākāra tvam api kāraṇam ced tat ca na anyasya jñānasya anya ākāra tayā karaṇa tvam yathā tathā jñānasya api grāhyasya anya ākāreṇa anyat eva jñānam karaṇam syāt tathā ca anavasthā duṣpariharā eva
kiṃca anyat na hi kaścid svayam grāhya grāhaka tva prasādhanāya dṛṣṭāntaḥ vidyate pradīpasya api cakṣuḥ ādi grāhya tvāt
na ca api aṃśa dvayam asti jñānasya niravayava tvāt
sati api ca aṃśa dvaye tayoḥ prakāśa ātmaka tvāt na anyonya grāhya grāhaka bhāvaḥ pradīpayoḥ iva dvayoḥ
kim ca anyat jñānasya grāhya grāhaka tva abhyupagame sati ātma sadbhāvaḥ api dussampādaḥ eva
tasmāt artha ākāra jñāna smṛti pratisandhāna prayotna icchā ādīnām anātma dharma tvam grāhya tvāt rūpa ādīnām iva
parārtha tvāt ca saṅghāt āśraya tvam rūpa ādi nidarśanena eva
tathā āśrayavat tvāt anitya tvāt ca prayatra pūrvaka tvāt ca iti evamādibhyaḥ anātma dharma tva siddhiḥ
ayaskā ānata maṇi kalpam
aya kānta maṇiḥ eva
yathā aya kānta maṇiḥ ayasaḥ sva ātma vyāptim pratyupakaroti sannidhi mātraṇa tathā cittam api cit svarūpasya ātmanaḥ sva ātma vyāptim pratyupakaroti dṛśya tvena
nartakī iva darśita viṣaya tvāt antaḥkaraṇena iti uktam tatra darśayitṛ tvam cittasya draṣṭṛ tvam ca puruṣasya kiṃkṛtam
sva svāmi tva kṛtam
katham punar sva svāmi tvam
vastu svabhāva tvāt
katham id ced uktam cittam ayaskānta maṇi kalpam iti
atha citta vṛttīnām bodhe kaḥ hetuḥ puruṣasya iti
ucyate yasmāt evam sannidhi mātra upakāri cittam dṛśya tvena tasmāt citta vṛttīnām bodhe puruṣasya ayam hetuḥ bhavati anādi sambandaḥ
tāḥ punar niroddhavyāḥ bahu tve api sati cittasya yābhiḥ vṛttibhiḥ vyutthāne sārūpyam uktam puruṣasya
kasmāt punar niroddhavyāḥ iti āha yatas vṛttayaḥ kliṣṭa akliṣṭāḥ
nanu ca bahu tve sati na śakyāḥ niroddhum iti atas āha pañcatayyaḥ iti
yadi api kliṣṭa akliṣṭāḥ vṛttayaḥ nantāḥ tathā api pañcatayyaḥ pañcavidhāḥ pañca kulāḥ eva
tatas ca pañca prakāra vṛtti pratipakṣa bhūta abhyāsa vairāgya prayogāt eva nirodha upapatteḥ prati avayava nirodha sādhana aprayojaka tvāt vṛttīnām tat bahutve na nirodha acakyatva prasaṅgaḥ
kleśa hetukāḥ kleśa nimittāḥ
avidyā ādi pañca kleśa prayuktam hi cittam vṛttibhiḥ ātmānam punar punar āvedayati
karma ācaya pracaye karmāṇi kuśala akuśala vimiśrāṇi tāni eva a phala pradānāt śerate iti karma āśāya śabda vācyāni teṣām pracayaḥ itaretara guṇa pradhāna bhāvena saṃhananam tasmin karma āśaya pracaye nimitte avidyā ādi kṣetrībhūtāḥ kliṣṭa āśrayāḥ iti arthaḥ
satīṣu hi tāsu karma āśayaḥ vipāka abhimukhī bhavati
khyāti viṣāyāḥ khyāti āspadāḥ

khyāti viṣaya tvāt eva tāḥ ākliṣṭāḥ apavarga hetu tvāt
atha kliṣṭa paṅkti madhye kliṣṭāḥ vṛttayaḥ kim kliṣṭāḥ eva kṣīrakubha prakṣipta ambu bindu vat
evam akliṣṭa pravāha patitāḥ api kliṣṭāḥ kim akliṣṭāḥ eva
kim ca atas yadi kliṣṭa pravāha gatāḥ akliṣṭāḥ kliṣṭāḥ syuḥ tadā vṛtti saṃskāra anuvidhāyinī smṛtiḥ tad anurūpaḥ eva vyavahāraḥ
sa ca api na sidhyati svarūpa vyabhicāre
tasmāt āha kliṣṭa chidreṣu api akliṣṭāḥ akliṣṭāḥ eva bhavanti
akliṣṭa chdreṣu api kliṣṭāḥ kliṣṭāḥ eva
yasmāt evam tasmāt tathā jātīyakāḥ saṃskārāḥ vṛttibhiḥ eva kriyante
yadi api kleśa ādayaḥ api saṃskāram ārabhante tathā api vṛtti dvārā eva teṣām api saṃskāraḥ iti vṛttibhiḥ eva iti eva kārā arthaḥ
tathā saṃskāraiḥ api vṛttayaḥ sva anurūpam kriyante iti evam vṛtti saṃskāra cakram aniśam anavaratam āvartate
tat evam bhūtam cittam evam hetu hetumat vṛtti saṃskāra dharmakam
pravṛttikam hetu mātra avasthā tvāt
ātma kalpena puruṣa kalpena khyāti mātreṇa eva kañcid kiñcid kālam avatiṣṭhate pārabdha saṃskāra śeṣa anuvṛttyā
pralayam vā gacchati saṃskāṛa avasānāt iti
kāḥ punar tāḥ kliṣṭa akliṣṭāḥ pañca kārāḥ vṛttayaḥ iti āha pramāṇa viparyaya vikalpa nidrā smṛtayaḥ iti
etāvatyaḥ eva vṛttayaḥ
tatra pratyakṣa anumāna āgamāḥ pramāṇāni
pramāṇa ākhyā vṛttiḥ tridhā eva bhidyate
tatra pramāṇa ākhyāyāḥ citta vṛtteḥ prathamaḥ bhedaḥ pratyakṣam
atas tat lakṣaṇam eva abhidhīyate tad pūrvaka tvāt bheda dvayasya
indriya pranāḍikayā
indriyam iti śrotra ādi pañcakam na karmendriyam tasya citta vṛtti ahetu tvāt
kriyā artham hi tat
tasmāt indriya śabdasya sāmānya artha tve api citta vṛtteḥ upavyācikhyāsita tvāt śrotra ādi viṣāyatā eva
vṛtti artha tvāt ca śrotra ādīnām
indriyam eva pranāḍikāḥ dvāram śabda ādi ākāra vṛtti rūpeṇa parigamānasya cittasya
atas tat tena indriya dvāreṇa sāmānya viśeṣa ātmaka bāhya vastu ākāra tayā pariṇamamānam uparajyate
tasya tad uparāgāt hetoḥ cittasya yā mudrā pratimudrā vat vṛttiḥ sāmānya viśeṣa ātmaka vastu uparoge api viśeṣa avadhāraṇa pradhānā sā eva pratykṣam
atha sva viṣaya sāmānya viśeṣa avabhāsana sāmarthaye śrotra ādīnām cittasya ca kiṃkṛtam viśeṣa avadhāraṇa pradhānyam iti
ucyate viśeṣa pratibandha tvāt hāna upādāna ādīnām viśeṣa avadhāraṇa pradhāna natā iti āha pradhāna natā iti
na sāmānyam na avadhāryate guṇa bhūtam tu gṛhyate eva
yathā nīlam rūpam iti nīla avadhāraṇa pradhanye sati api rūpam eva nīlam iti guṇa bhūtam avadhārayati
yathā duḥkha śabdaḥ sukha śabdaḥ mūḍhaḥ śabdaḥ iti
tathā ca viśeṣa avadhāraṇa pradhānā vṛttiḥ iti hi upapadyate
kim ca saṃśaya viparyaya nimitta tvāt ca sāmānya uplabdheḥ
sāmānye hi upalbdhe bubuhutsita viśeṣasya saṃśayaḥ jāyate samupalbdha sāmānya smṛteḥ vā viparyayaḥ samadhigata viśeṣasya tu saṃśaya viparyayau na sthitim upāśnuvāte iti viśeṣa avadhāraṇa pradhāna tā ucyate
yatra api sāmānyam gauḥ iti vā aśvaḥ iti vā tatra api anyatara parityāgena anyatara avadhāraṇā iti viśeṣa avadhāraṇa pradhāna tā eva
sarvam eva hi vastu vastu antara apekṣayā sāmānyam viśeṣaḥ ca
yasya punar sāmānyam avastu adhyāropitam eva ūṣara ambu vat na indriya viṣayam iti tasya pratiniyata sāmānya āshyāropaṇa anupapattiḥ
na hi sukhye saṃbhavati adhyāropaṇā smṛti asaṃbhavāt
na kadācid adṛṣṭa mukhya udakasya salila adhyāropaṇam ūṣareṣu vidyate
atha a smaran api adhyāropayet rūpa sva lakṣaṇe śabda tva ādi api adhyasyet
atha indriya antara viṣaya tvāt rūpa sva lakṣaṇe śabda tva ādi adhyāsaḥ viruddhaḥ iti ced na avastu tve sati aviśeṣāt
viśeṣa abhyupagame ca vastu tva prasaṅgaḥ
śabda sva lakṣaṇāt iva rūpa sva lakṣaṇasya
kim ca anyat deśa kāla anya viśiṣṭa pratyakṣāḥ na abhyupagame samasta loka vyavahāra vilopaḥ syāt
na hi idam aham amuṣmin avakāśe kāle ca asmin adrākṣam etasmāt nimittāt evam viśeṣaṇam iti ca smṛti upapattiḥ
na ca pratyakṣa adṛṣṭeṣu viśeṣya vat viśeṣaṇeṣu smṛtiḥ saṃbhavati na ca kalpanā apoḍhena vyavahāra gocara atīten vyavaharamāṇaḥ dṛśyate
tasmāt loka prasiddha pratyakṣa anusaraṇam eva nyāyyam
nanu ca yoginām nirvikalpa samādhi jam darśanam tasya anevam lakṣaṇa tvāt tathā sukha rāga ādi vijñānasya ca an indriya pranāḍī pūrva tvāt pramāṇa antara tvam abhyupetavyam pratyakṣa tvam vā vaktavyam
ucyate
pratyakṣasya na pramāṇasya puruṣa pratyaya apekṣa tvena parihṛta tvāt
na hi apratyayā vṛttiḥ pratyakṣam
caitanya udaya hetoḥ eva sa pratyayāyāḥ pratyakṣa tvam
tathā ca āha phalam tad aviśiṣṭaḥ pauruṣeyaḥ citta vṛtti bodhaḥ iti
evam ca sati sukha rāga ādi jñānasya kliṣṭa akliṣṭa rūpasya tad aviśiṣṭa puruṣa pratyaya phala avasāna tvāt pratyakṣa tā siddhā eva
indriya pranāḍikā grahaṇam laukika pratyakṣa udbhava anuvādaḥ eva
anyathā hi indriya nirapekṣasya yogi īśvarayoḥ jñānasya apratyakṣa tā syāt
asti hi kleśa ādi pratibandha abhāve sarva arthena citta sattvena sarva viṣayeṇa yugapad sūkṣma vyavahita ādi grahaṇam
tathā tārakam sarva viṣayam sarvathāviṣayam akramam ca iti viveka jam jñānam iti
tasmāt na avadhāryate indriya pranāḍikayā eva iti

viśeṣa avadhāraṇa pradhāna tvena saṃśaya nivṛttiḥ iti
tatra keṣām cit phalam tat eva pramāṇam
apareṣām tu pramāṇāt anyatra anyat pramāṇa vyakti antare antaram
yathā ghaṭa vijñānasya hāna upādāna apekṣāḥ buddhayaḥ phalam iti guṇa doṣa tat śūnyatva viṣaya tvāt upādāna ādi buddhīnām pramāṇa bhūta ghaṭa vijñānāt atyanta bhedaḥ tatas ca anya viṣayasya pramāṇasya prameyasya viṣaya pramāṇa vyakti antaram re phalam iti
na hi khadiḥ chedanasya khadira upādānam tat parityāgaḥ vā phalam bhavitum yuktam
api vi yoga sabandha phala tvāt tyāga upādānayoḥ
na ca phalasya phalam sambhavati
dvaidhī bhāva phala vyavahita tvāt ca
kim ca phalasya ced phalam kriyā anapekṣā prasaṅgaḥ
phala artham hi kriyā apekṣyate
tat ced phalam vinā api kriyayā phalāt api sidhyati atas hi tatas na hi anekāyasa apekṣita niṣpatti kriyām anutiṣṭhet
sādhana anveṣaṇa anupapattiḥ ca
kriyāyāḥ abhāvāt
nā api kriyāḥ eva phalam kriyāḥ anuprarama prasaṅgāt
phala avasanā api hi kriyā
kriyāyāḥ ca phala tve phala anabhilāṣi tva prasaṅgaḥ
tasyāḥ duḥkha tvāt
tasmāt nityāḥ na pramāṇa svarūpam eva phalam na api tad vyatirikta pramāṇa antaram iti āha phalam tad aviśiṣṭe ityādi
tad aviśiṣṭaḥ tayā pramāṇa ākhyayā vṛttyā aviśiṣṭaḥ tulyaḥ tad ākāra tvena pauruṣeyaḥ puruṣasya ayam bodhaḥ iti
puruṣasya hi vṛtti ākāra tā
tasmāt nityāḥ na akriyā jam dravya svarūpa mātram phalam
kim tarhi dravyasya eva avasthā antara viśeṣaḥ kriyā jāḥ jaḥ kriyā paryavasāna kālaḥ kriyā uparama upapatteḥ phalam
phala niṣpattau eva hi kriyā uparame upapadyate
evaṃbhūtasya mukhya phala tve pradhāna kriyā viprakṛṣṭāyāḥ kriyāyāḥ dravyam dravyasya vā kriyā phalam iti anyonya pratyupasthāpaka tvena pradhāna phala abhimukhīkaraṇāt phala tva upacāraḥ na virotsyate
nanu ca bhavataḥ api upacritam eva phalam vṛtti aviśiṣṭāyāḥ phala tvena abhupagamāt puruṣasya ca śuddha tvāt tad ākāra tayā anṛta tvam
na hi sphaṭika maṇeḥ alaktaka upadhāna ākāra tā satyā
bāḍham tathā api tu etat eva phalam mukhyam dṛṣṭa tvāt
mukhya phala antara adarśanāt
sarvasya eva kriyā kāraka jātasya etad phala artha tvāt
etad avasānam hi tat sarvam
tathā ca pradarśitam
nanu ca mithyā bhūtasya eva mukhya phala tvam vṛtti ākārasya tathā ca tad abhilāṣa anupapattiḥ
bāḍham mithyā bhūtaḥ eva vṛtti anugataḥ bhogaḥ
tathā ca āha sattva puruṣayoḥ atyanta asaṃkīrṇayoḥ pratyaya aviśeṣaḥ bhogaḥ iti
bhāṣyam api tayoḥ svarūpa upalmbhe sati kutas bhogaḥ iti
atas eva ca samyak darśanāt ātyantokī nivṛttiḥ upapadyate
yeṣām a mithyā phalam teṣām vairāgya kāraṇa abhāvāt samyak darśana anveṣaṇa anupapatteḥ mokṣa abhāvaḥ
na ca kriyā pariniṣpādyaḥ mokṣaḥ anitya tva prasaṅgāt
atha buddhi boddhṛ tvam puruṣasya sattvam ca asiddham iti ced āha pratisaṃvedī boddheḥ puruṣaḥ iti upariṣṭāt pravediyiṣyāmaḥ iti
ye ca api indriy artha sannikarṣasya pratyakṣa tvam abhyupayanti na teṣām api samyak abhyupetam sannikarṣasya kriyā phala tvāt
sannikarṣaḥ ca saṃyogaḥ sa ca kriyā jaḥ taiḥ iṣyate
yatas yat upajāyate tat tasya pramāṇam
tat ca tasya phalam yat upajāyate
phalam api sannikarṣī jñānam prati pramāṇam iti ced tat ca na jñāpaka pramāṇa prastāve kāraka pramāṇe upanyāsasya ayukta tvāt
sannikarṣī hi jñānasya utpādakaḥ na tasya jñāpakaḥ
prameya adhigamāya hi pratyakṣa ādīni yaḥ tāni na jñāne utpatti kāraṇam
tat prakriyāyāma prakṛtam prakriyeta
atha api syāt jñānasya api prameya tvāt tat ca api utpadyamānam pramīyate iti tad ytpatti kāraṇasya sannikarṣasya jñāpaka tvam eva iti tat ca na jñānam jñanena eva jñāyeta teṣām tathā abhyupagamāt
na ca sannikarṣaḥ jñānam
jñāna utpādaka tvena abhyupagamāt
atha jñānasya jñāne sannikarṣaḥ nimitta tvāt pramāṇam iti ced adṛṣṭaḥ īśvaraḥ icchā viṣaya nimeṣa ādīnām api nimitta tvāt pramāṇa tve kaḥ pradveṣaḥ
na ca jñānasya jñeya tve ātmanaḥ ca svabhāva cit rūpa tu anabhyupagame śakyā anavasthā parihartum
atha ātma samaveta mātra tayā eva jñānasya jñeya tā na jñāna antaram apekṣyate yena atiprasajyeta iti ced asya api anyat pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam vācyam anindriya sannikarṣa ādi lakṣaṇa tvāt ātmani jñāna samavāya tvasya
sannikarṣasya ca jñāne utpatti phala tvāt tad utpatti vyavadhāne sati tasya jñānasya na ānantaryam
tasmāt tat ānantaryeṇa api na sannikrṣa phala tvam jñānasya
tathā hāna ādi buddhīnām api rūpa ādi jñāna phala tve anupapattiḥ uktā
vyabhicārāt ca
yathā ekasmin aṅganā ādi piṇḍha viṣaye jñāne samāne bahūnām utpanne kasyacid upādāna buddhiḥ anyasya heya buddhiḥ kasyacid abhāvaḥ tatra hāne upādāna buddhiḥ vyabhicarati
anyataratra ekam eva jñānam tat eva uhayam vyabhicarati upekṣakasya
yat ca yat vyabhicarati na tat tasya phalam
kim ca hānaḥ upādāna bhāva mātra tvāt abhāvaḥ eva upekṣā
na ca abhāvaḥ pramāṇasya phalam bhavitum arhati
rāda dveṣābhyām ca upādāna parityāga buddhī
tad abhāvāt kāraṇa abhāve kārya abhāva iti pramāṇa vijñāne sati api hāne upādāna buddhi abhāve eva upekṣe iti vyabhicārāt na hāne ādi buddhi phala tvam
kim ca rāga dveṣa tad abhāvānām api upādāna ādi buddhi phalatve pramāṇa tva prasaṅgaḥ
pauruṣeya cittavṛtti bodha tve tu na kiñcid viruddhyate iti
nanu ca citta vṛtteḥ saṃvedya tvam asiddham
na hi karaṇam eva karma bhavati
na hi dātram eva lūyate
na eṣa doṣaḥ
kriyā kārakayoḥ bhinna dharma tvāt
kriyā nivṛttim prati sambhūya kārakāṇi vyāpriyante parasparam viṣaya viṣayi bhāvena
kriyā tu sattā mātreṇa eva phala hetuḥ iti karaṇa tvam asyām upacaryate na kāraka vat
kurvat hi kārayet iti kriyā adhikārakam syāt na bhūtam bhavyāya upadiśyate
kim ca anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ ca
kriyā ced karaṇam syāt tad nivṛttyayā ca anyayā kriyayā bhavitavyam
na hi anyām kriyām antareṇa tasyāḥ kāraṇa karaṇa tvam ghaṭate
yā api ca anyā sā api kāraṇam syāt anyasyāḥ kriyāyāḥ
sā api anyasyāḥ iti anavasthā
tatas ca kriyā santāna anuparamāt phala anabhinivṛttiḥ
tatra antyā ced kriyā antareṇa vinā phala hetuḥ bhavet prathamasya tathātve kaḥ pradveṣaḥ
citta vṛtteḥ tu abhivyañjaka tvāt samvedyate ti adoṣaḥ
dṛśyate ca abhivyañjakānām sva rūpa saṃvedya tā eva karaṇa tvam pradīpa ādīnām
tathā citta vṛtteḥ api
cakṣuḥ ādiṣu abhivyañjaka tve api vyabhicāraḥ iti ced samāna cetana samāna jātīya saṃkarāt katham
yeṣām tāvat bhautikāni indriyāṇi teṣām cakṣuṣaḥ taijasa tvāt bāhyena ālokena tulya jātīyena vyatibhedāt gṛhyamāṇasya eva avivekaḥ
yathā pradīpānām bahūnām prabhā vyatibhedāt kasya kā prabhā iti na vivicyate
tathā śrotra ādiṣu api
yeṣām api abhautikāni teṣām api abhivyañjaka tvena samāna jātīya tā vṛtteḥ abhivyañjaka tvāt agrahaṇam iti
tat na prāpta caitanyaḥ upagrahatayā vibhāvya tvāt avyavahita tvāt ca
sarvagata tve api ātmanaḥ sūkṣma tvena svacchara tvena ca cittena avyavadhānāt ca saṃvedyamānaḥ eva phalam iti siddham
yeṣām punar pratyakṣeṇa a saṃvedyā citta vṛttiḥ teṣām phala grahaṇa pramāṇa abhāvaḥ
phale ca gṛgīte jñāna asiddha tvasya arthāpattiḥ
na ca phalam gṛhyate pramāṇa vyāpāraḥ anabhyupagamāt
tad abhyupagame ca anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ
yat phala avagrahaṇāya pramāṇam abhyupagamyate tasya api anyat phalam tat pramāṇasya api anyat iti na kvacid avatiṣṭheta
atha na pramāṇa vyāpāraḥ tasya tadā pramāṇa abhāvāt phalasya asattvam prasaktam
yatra hi sat upalambhakāni pramāṇāni na vyāpāram gacchanti tat na asti iti abhyupagacchāmaḥ teṣām
atha agṛhyamāṇam api tat eva jñānam phalasya api iti ced na abhivyañjaka dharma vyatikramāt
na hi abhivyañjakam gṛhyamāṇam abhivyañjayat dṛṣṭam
na hi ulkā giri śikhare api nijam dharmam atikramati
athā abhivyañjayat eva phalam prati api pramāṇam iti ced siddham tarhi īpsitam asmākam
rāga ādīnām vṛtti viśeṣaṇa tvena grahaṇe upapatteḥ
raktaḥ ham dviṣṭaḥ ham iti yadi aham pratyaya viśeṣaṇam tat api vṛtti bhāvaḥ abhāvi tvena eva grahaṇāt vṛtti viśeṣaṇānām rāga ādīnām grahaṇam upapadyate
tena nyathā rūpa ādi vat māna antara apekṣa tva prasaṅgāt
tatas ca anavasthā iti
tasmāt pramāṇa phala anabhijñānam abhimāna mātram eva kevalam paṇḍitam manyānām iti upekṣaṇīyam iti
anumānam atha ucyate anumeyasya tulya jātīyeṣu anuvṛttaḥ iti
anumeyasya jijñāsita dharma viśiṣṭasya
tat dharmavat tayā tulya jātīyeṣu anuvṛttaḥ sadbhāva mātreṇa bhinna jātīyebhyaḥ tad viruddha dharmakebhyaḥ vyāvṛttaḥ teṣu asān iti arthaḥ
sambandhaḥ iti
kaḥ sambandhaḥ
kayoḥ vā
na hi sambandhinau an āpekṣya sambandhaḥ sambandha tām iyāt yat asau prasiddha vat ca ucyate yaḥ iti
nanu ca anumānasya prakṛta tvāt liṅga liṅginoḥ sambandhaḥ prasiddhaḥ eva na āgamaka tvāt
na kevalaḥ sambandhaḥ gamakaḥ
ucyate liṅgasya eva vyāvṛtti anuvṛttyoḥ
kaḥ punar asau
liṅgam eva
na hi liṅgāt anyat anuvṛttam vyāvṛttam ca
tat ca gamakam
nanu liṅgam api na eva gamakam liṅgi sambandha anapekṣam yadi ca anapekṣita liṅgi sambandham gamakam yad vṛtti bhūmi jaya krameṇa kiñcid gamakam syāt tasmāt liṅga liṅgi sambandhaḥ vaktavyaḥ
na ukta tvāt
anumeyasya tulya jātīyeṣu anuvṛttaḥ iti ādinā eva ukta tvāt
na hi anumeyena asaṃbaddham liṅginā tat sadṛśa jātīyeṣu anuvartate bhinna jātīyebhyaḥ vā nivartate
tasmāt yaḥ iti ca prasiddham eva saṃbandham anuvadati
tad viṣayā evam vṛttiḥ
sāmānya avadhāraṇa pradhānā liṅga sāmānya avadhāraṇa pradhānā anumānam
yathā deśa antara prāpteḥ gatimat candra tārakam caitra vat iti
yadi api tat abhivyaktiḥ tad jāḥ api udāharaṇa pratyudāharaṇa pradarśanāt atitarām iti udāharaṇa pratipādanam
tatra gatimat candra tārakam iti candra tārakasya gatimat tvam anumeyam
tad sumana jātīyeṣu anuvṛttā deśa antara prāptiḥ gatimatsu caitra ādiṣu bhinna jātīyebhyaḥ ca agatibhyaḥ vindhya ādibhyaḥ vyāvṛttā iti avyabhicarantī
nityam gatimatā sambandhāt
bhavatu tāvat aviruddhānām nitya sambandhāt deśa antara prāpti ādīnām gamya gamaka tā vadhya ghātaka ādīnām tu sambandh abhāve katham iti ucyate gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ
tatra api nitya sambandhāt adoṣaḥ
na hi atra api prāpti lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ abhipreyate
sāmānyatodṛṣṭāḥ nu bhāva prasaṅgāt
na hi candra tārakā ādiṣu deśa antara prāpteḥ prāpti lakṣāṇa sambandhaḥ pratyakṣeṇa gṛhyate
a gṛhyamāṇaḥ ced gamakaḥ sarvam sarvasya gamakam syāt
na hi kiṃcid kenacid asaṃbaddham ākāśa ādīnām sarvatra bhāvāt
tasmāt ganya gamaka buddhi utpatti hetuḥ eva sambandhaḥ anumāna visaye
tathā ca badhya ghātakayoḥ api bhāva darśane nyatara bhāvaḥ gamyate iti anumānam eva
yasya api ucite deśe abhāva darśanāt anyatra bhāvaḥ gamyate
yathā ghātaka darśanena badhya abhāvaḥ numīyate
caitrasya jīvataḥ gṛhe abhāva gṛhya bhāva darśane bahis bhavaḥ ca iti
nanu ca abhāva arthāpattī ete na anumāne na lakṣaṇa asaṅga tā īṅ gavādi vat
na yathā ukta lakṣa anopapatteḥ badhya ghātakayoḥ virodha lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ
yatra yatra ghātaka bhāvaḥ tatra badhyāḥ bhāvaḥ eva iti a vinā bhāvaḥ
na hi badhyasya abhāvam bhāvaḥ vyabhicarati
badhyasya vā bhāvaḥ bhāvam agni bhāvam iva dhūma bhāvaḥ
katham punar avagamyate ghātaka bhāva darśanat eva tat gocare badhyasya abhāva buddhiḥ iti
na punar sat upalambhaka pramāṇānām ghātake iva badhye vyāpāra abhāvāt iti
ucyate ghātaka bhāve eva badhyā bhāva buddhi upapattiḥ dhūma bhāve badhya viśeṣa abhāva buddhi utpattiḥ dhūma viśeṣa vyāpṛ vṛ ta pramāṇasya iva agni viśeṣa buddhiḥ iti
abhāva pramāṇa vādinaḥ tu sarvatra pramāṇa abhāvasya aviśiṣṭa tvāt virodhi viśeṣa darśana anuvidhānam virodhi antara abhāva darśanasya anupapannam liṅga viśeṣa iva liṅgi viśeṣa darśanasya
na hi sat upalambhaka pramāṇa vyāpāra abhāvasya kaścid viśeṣaḥ yena viśeṣa buddhiḥ tat viśeṣam anuvidhīyate
atha viśeṣe sat upalambhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt iti ced tat na asataḥ icchā ādi sahabhāva
na hi asat sahāya apekṣaya kāryam nirvartayat dṛṣṭam śaśa viṣāṇa ādi
dṛṣṭam iha iti ced na vipratipatti sthāna tve dṛṣṭānta abhāvāt
tulyam iti ced na ghaṭa ādeḥ sataḥ upekṣā darśanāt
na ca api nirvyāpārasya avastu tvāt abhāvasya pramaṇa bhāvaḥ yoktaḥ
na hi nirasta vyāpārakam kiṃcid kārya ārambhakam dṛśyate loke
tasmāt vyāpāra rūpa pramāṇa janitā prameya abhāva buddhiḥ prameya viṣaya tvat ghaṭa ādi buddhi vat
tathā ca vastu tvāt pravṛtti nivṛtti hetu tvāt
vipakṣaḥ śaśaviṣāṇa ādiḥ
tathā abhāva pramā na bhāva janitā na bhavati yathā bhihita hetu dṛṣṭānta darśanāt nena
ghātaka darśanam badhya abhāva buddheḥ liṅgam tat bhāvi tvāt agni ādi buddhi nimitta dhūma ādi buddhi vat saṃśaya nivartaka tvāt ca
badhyā bhāva buddhiḥ vā liṅga janitā niścaya rūpa tvāt agni buddhi vat iti
iha gaṭaḥ na asti iti kila na anumānam liṅga liṅgi sambandha agrahaṇāt
na hi yathā anveṣaṇam tathā iha na asti ghaṭaḥ iti atra liṅga anveṣaṇam asti
prāk eva liṅga anveṣaṇāt buddhi utpatteḥ
na eṣa doṣaḥ ihapratyaya ākārasya eva liṅga tvāt
na hi prathamam eva liṅga buddhu upajanane sati liṅga anveṣaṇam bhavati
iha iti ākāraḥ uparañjitā buddhiḥ liṅgam um uparañjaka vyatirikta ghaṭa ādi abhāva buddeḥ ghātaka buddhi vat eva
virodha lakṣaṇaḥ eva ca atra api sambandhaḥ
yatra punar aviruddhāni uparañjakāni tatra astitva buddheḥ etena eva arthāpatteḥ anumāna tvam avinābhāvena sambandhena
tatra api jīvataḥ hi devadattasya gṛha abhāve bahis bhāvaḥ yadā gṛhe bhāvaḥ na tadā bahis bhāvaḥ iti anyatareṇa anumānam

vṛtti uparañjaka an uparañjaka tvena hi abhāva grahaṇasya abhihitaḥ hetuḥ
agni ādau api dhana ādi śakti grahaṇam anumānam eva
kārya nirvartakayoḥ a vinā bhāva sambandhasya ātmani dṛṣṭa tvāt bhujya ādau
dṛśyate hi pratyagātmani śaktaḥ ham idam kāryam kartum aśaktaḥ ham iti ātma vat ātma viśeṣaṇasya śakteḥ grahaṇam
śakti nirvartyam eva dahana ādi kāryam api iti anumāna siddhiḥ
nanu ca abhāvasya pratyakṣa tām upagāyanti kecid
yathā kila ādarśakena pradīpa ādinā sati gṛhyamāṇe vastuni na tat avayavini yat tat na asti iti evam sataḥ prakarśakam pramāṇam asat api prakāśayati
tathā ca udāharanti an aṅkitam vāsaḥ ānaya iti praviśya bhāṇḍāgāram aṅkita an aṅkita vāsaḥ sannidhau aṅkita vāsaḥ grahaṇena eva pratyakṣeṇa aṅkita abhāva viśiṣṭam vāsaḥ upalabhya nayati
tasmāt pratyakṣaḥ eva abhāvaḥ lakṣaṇa antaraḥ anupapatteḥ iti
tat na buddhi ākāreṇa artha avadhāraṇa anṛta tva prasaṅgāt
yad ākārā hi buddhiḥ tasya pratyakṣaḥ avadhriyamāṇa ātma tā abhyupagamyate
yathā nīlam vastu pītam iti atra api viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya sambandha pratyayaḥ mithyā prāpnoti
tat yathā iha ghaṭaḥ na asti iti iha pradeśasya ghaṭa abhāvena asati sambandhe sambandha pratyayaḥ na hi ghaṭa abhāvasya iha pradeśasya sambandhaḥ taiḥ iha devadattaḥ iti
tasmāt nīlam vastu iti viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya sambandha pratyayaḥ api sambandha pratyaya tvāt mithyā prasajyeta
yathā ca asti api iha deśa ghaṭa abhāva sambandhe sabandha pratītiḥ tathā eva anīle api vastuni asati eva nīla tva sambandge nīla tva sambandha pratyayaḥ prāpnoti tathā sambandhiṣu api
atha asti eva sambandhaḥ dviṣṭhatā viruddhyeta sambandhasya
abhāvasya avastu tva abhyupagamāt
atha api ekaśatam ṣaṣṭhī arthāḥ iti yāvat ṣaṣthī arthāḥ sambandhaḥ iṣyeta tadā dvividhaḥ eva sambandhaḥ samavāya ākhyaḥ samyoga ākhyaḥ ca iti na yujyate
api ṣaṣṭhī arthānām ubhaya antaḥpāti tvam ucyeta na abhāve anyatarasya api asambhavāt
kiñca ntva nyat
iha nabhasi kusumam na asti iti sambandhinaḥ nabhasaḥ api apratyakṣa tvāt gagana kusuma abhāvasya apratyakṣa tvam prāpnoti
atha apratyakṣa tvam eva iti ced āpatitam gagana kusuma abhāva vat apratyakṣa tvam iha bhū pradeśe ghaṭa abhāvasya api
viśeṣaḥ vaktavyaḥ
atha vyomnaḥ pratyakṣa tvāt iti tat na puṣpasya patataḥ nabhasi astitva darśanāt vyoma apratyakṣa tvam ahetuḥ
yathā eva nipatat kusuma sadbhāve vyoma apratyakṣa tvam ahetuḥ tathā sadbhāva viruddha grahaṇe api ahetuḥ syāt
atha ākāśa apratyakṣa tvāt eva iti ced asambandham api yat kiṃcid vyavahita apratyakṣa tva ādi saḥ api hetuḥ syāt
atha nabhaḥ kusuma abhāvaḥ pratyakṣa iti ced indriya artha sannikarṣa anarthakyam sarvatra prasajyate
tathā ca sati asannikarṣṭe upalabdheḥ sarveṣām sarvajña tvam prasaktam
atha anumeyam tatra iti ced nabhaḥ kusuma abhāva vat iha ghaṭa abhāvasya aviśeṣāt eva siddham
evam ca sati abhāva pramāṇa vādinaḥ api vyavahita viprakṛṣṭa udaka ādau anala ādi abhāvasya anumeya tvāt iha ghaṭa abhāvaḥ api tad sāmānyāt anumāna grāhyaḥ eva iti niścetum yuktam
vindhyāḥ ca aprāpteḥ agatiḥ iti ca prayoga antaram
agatiḥ vindhyaḥ iti pratijñānam
aprāpteḥ iti hetuḥ caitra vat iti kāka locana vat ubhayatra sambadhyate
gatimat candra tārakam iti anena sādharmyeṇa vindhyāḥ ca a aprāpteḥ iti anena vaidharmyeṇa sambandhaḥ evam ca sati darśana kṛtaḥ na doṣaḥ
atha vā etasmin prayoge vyatireka viparyaya darśanena doṣa abhāvaḥ iti upanyastam
lakṣaṇasya ca lakṣya viśeṣeṇa ūhya tvāt adoṣaḥ
āptaḥ para anujighṛkṣā prayuktaḥ doṣa rahitaḥ dṛṣṭa anumitaḥ arthaḥ
tena dṛṣṭaḥ vā anumitaḥ vā arthaḥ paratra śrotṛ viśeṣe sva bodha saṅkrāntaye sva adhigama saṃkramaṇāya śabdena śabdaḥ iti vākyam tatas viśiṣṭa artha pratipatteḥ
tasmāt tad upadiṣṭāt vākyāt
tad artha viṣayā vākya artha viṣayā yā citta vṛttiḥ sā anumāna vat eva sāmānya avadhāraṇa pradhānā
ittham āpti ādi dharma grahaṇa pūrvakā śrotuḥ āgamaḥ na vaktuḥ
dṛṣṭa anumita arthaḥ hi vaktā tasya laiṅgakam aindriyakam vā tat jñānam
śrotuḥ eva tu śravaṇa pūrvakam niścitam vijñānam laiṅgika aindriyaka vyatiriktam
sa āgamaḥ na pratyakṣam indriyā viṣaya viṣaya tvāt yathā abhihita liṅga liṅgi sambandha nirapekṣa tvāt ca na anumānam
na hi artha anvitam jñānam āsādita liṅga liṅgi sambandha purassaram upajāyate
phalam tu sarvatra pauruṣeyaḥ vṛtti bodhaḥ eva
yasya āgamasya vaktā āgamaḥ ākhya vṛtti utpatti nimitte śabda uccāraṇāt āgamasya prayoga upanyāsena pratipāditam phalam tu pūrvavat eva
api ekaḥ eva prayogaḥ api abhāva mātrasya vivakṣita tvāt na viparīta vyatireka darśanāt iti ucyate
aśraddheya āgamaḥ eva viśiṣyate
katham asau aśraddheyaḥ arthaḥ vaktā iti atas āha na dṛṣṭaḥ numitaḥ vā arthaḥ tena vaktā
śiṣṭaleka prasiddha anyathā pratipādanāt buddhārhata ādiḥ
na hi rāga ādi doṣa anupahata antaḥkaraṇaḥ prasiddham anyathā nirvarṇayati
sa āgamaḥ plavate ābhāsī bhavati
yadi api pratyakṣaḥ anumāna viṣayaḥ ābhāsa darśanam sva śabdena na kṛtam tathā api āgamaḥ ābhāsaḥ upadarśanena eva pūrvatra api yathā abhihita lakṣaṇa viparīta tvena pratyakṣa anumāna ābhāsa ādi draṣṭavyam arthāt uktam
mūla vaktari tu ādya vaktari īśvare tad nimittaḥ yaḥ āgamaḥ sa viplava nimitta abhāvāt nirviplavaḥ syāt
yathā artha ya vaktṛvat
upamānam mānam śabda pūrvakam tad āgamaḥ antaḥpāti tvāt na pramṇa antaram
yathā gauḥ iva gavayaḥ iti vanecara abhihatāt eva vākyāt punar vane gavaya darśane api pūrva śruta vākye upasthāpita sādṛśya smaraṇa mātram eva na adhikam
sādṛśyam tu vākyāt eva pūrva pratipannam
na api saṃjñā saṃjñi sambandha pratipattitaḥ eva mānam tasyāḥ api tad vākyāt eva avagata tvāt
na hi gauḥ iti etāvatā anavagata gavaya nāmakasya vana gata gavaya darśinaḥ api gavayaḥ yam iti saṃjñā saṃjñi sambandha avabodhaḥ bhavati
tasmāt gauḥ iva gavayaḥ iti gavaya śabdaḥ api tad vākye pekṣitavyaḥ
tathā ca sati pūrva śrutāt eva sarvam pratītam
atha api syāt ayam dasya gavayaḥ iti na pūrva buddhi viṣayam iti tat api tatrabhavatām api paricodana parihāram ava śyatām api pīḍita kaivale kaule iva lakṣyate
tathā hi deśa kāla sannikarṣa viprakarṣa ādi bhedena aneka upamāna bhedaḥ prasajyeta
tathā astu iti ced tat pūrva dhiyā antar nihita samasta viśeṣam eva hi vā neyau pūrvam upapāditam
na hi gauḥ iti ukte deśa kāle ādi viśeṣa abhāve na go śabdāt artha pratipattiḥ
kim ca anyat na hi saṃjñā saṃjñi sambandha pratipattiḥ upamānam yena hi apamīyate tat upamānam sādṛśya jñānam hi tat
na hi nāmi nāma sambandha pratipattyā kiṃcid upamīyate uttara kāla tvāt
avadhṛta sādṛśyasya hi paścāt ā sya yam gavayaḥ iti evam saḥ api nipatati
evam tarhi syāt aśabda pūrvakam pramāṇa antaram yathā gavaya darśanāt etat sadṛśaḥ gauḥ iti grāmīṇasya buddhiḥ tat api na prameya abhāvāt
sati hi prameye sat upalmbhaka tva abhimatasya pramāṇasya vyāpāraḥ na hi go gavayayoḥ vyāvṛttam anuvṛttam ca vastutas sādṛśyam nāma ekam asti
nanu ca sādṛśya buddhiḥ asti eva na asau nirālambanā bhavitum arhati
satyam evam tatra eva vicāraṇā kim asau vana yūtha ādi pratyaya vat
atha ghaṭa ādi buddhi vat iti
kim ca atas yadi vana pratyayavat bhavet tadā yathā eva viśiṣṭa sanniveśa anugatāḥ mahīruhāḥ eva ātma vyatirekeṇa avidyamāna vana pratyaya hetavaḥ tathā eva go gavaya avayavāḥ eva dvaya darśana smṛti apekṣayā sva ātma vyatirekeṇa asataḥ sādṛśyasya pratītau kāraṇam iti prāptam avastu tvam
atha punar ghaṭa ādi pratyaya vat vastu tvam pramāṇa tvam ca tadā syāt iti
tatra kīdṛśam vastu iti vicāryate kim goḥ gavayayoḥ anuvṛttam ekam sādṛśyam go tva gavaya tvābhyām anyat
te eva vā anyonya viśiṣṭe yadi vā tābhyām bhinne goḥ gavaya ādhāre dve sādṛśye paraspara anupekḍe sāpekṣe vā
kim vyaktiḥ eva sā anyatara jāti viśiṣṭā vā kim jātiḥ sācā anyatara vyakti viśiṣṭā vyakti dvaya viśiṣṭā vā sambandhaḥ vai teṣām yathā vikalpa yogam iti ekaika anyonya viśiṣṭa viśeṣaṇa tva ādinā bhūyāṃsaḥ nye api vikalpāḥ udbhāvayitavyāḥ
tatra yadi ekam sādṛśyam ubhaya gatam tadā na upameya tvam ekatvāt yathā gauḥ iva gauḥ iti
atha tena anyatara vyaktiḥ upamīyate na etat api sva ātma gata tvāt gauḥ iva go tvena
atha tadvatyā vyaktyā vyakti antaram upamīyate na etat api na hi go tvvam khaṇḍa muṇḍe upameya tva kāraṇam
atha dharma antara apekṣayā sādṛśyam tad buddheḥ kāraṇam iti naṣṭam tarhi sādṛśyam saḥ eva astu dharmaḥ tad buddheḥ kim te sādṛśya hatakena kalpitena
kim ca sa ca api apekṣyamāṇaḥ dharmaḥ kim ekaḥ sādṛśya vat ubhayatra atha bhinnaḥ iti evam ādi vikalpāḥ syuḥ iti asambhavaḥ pūrvavat eva
atha bhinnam sādṛśyam ucyate tat ca na bhedāt eva na hi bhavati gauḥ iva aśvaḥ iti
yathā eva eka eka tvāt aghaṭamāna tā tathā bahubhiḥ apekṣyamāṇaiḥ
etena jāti vyakti sambandha ādayaḥ pūrva vikalpitāḥ pratyuktāḥ
atha buddhi utpatti anyathā anupapattyā sādṛśya kalpanā satī evam vana vivara pūrva dakṣiṇa uttara ādi buddhi yoga anyathā anubhavāt nyathā anupapattyā vastu tvam kim na kalpyate
syāt eṣā tava buddhiḥ vṛkṣa ādayaḥ eva tatra tad buddhi janma hetavaḥ iti
yadi evam mithyā pratyayaḥ gavayena sadṛśī gauḥ iti vana buddhi vat
atha ye vyāvṛttāḥ kaḥ iha upamā arthaḥ gauḥ iva aśvaḥ iti
atha ubhaye api te vayavāḥ vyāvṛtta nuvṛtta ātmānaḥ tad budhdi hetavaḥ tathā api vana pratyaya vat eva prāptam
tasmāt parikṣyamāṇam na ati vimardana kṣamam iti te eva avayavāḥ ubhayatra bhūyāṃsaḥ sādṛśya buddheḥ kāraṇam vana buddheḥ iva pādapāḥ iti na upamānam nāma prmāṇa antaram iti siddham
nā api premeya dvi tvāt pramāṇa dvi tva kalpanam
kutas pramāṇa vaśāt artha pratīteḥ
na hi artha vaśāt pramāṇa kalpanā
yadi ca artha vaśāt pramāṇa kalpanā syāt adhunā tat na śakyam jānānām asarvajña tvāt caitya vandanāt svargaḥ bhavati iti atra caitya vandanasya svarga hetu tva buddheḥ pratyakṣa numāna aviṣaya tvāt mithyātvam syāt
tad artham vā pramāṇa antara kalpanam
atha sā buddhiḥ iti ced pramāṇāt anyatra phala prasaṅgaḥ evam ca nirmokṣaḥ ka raṇa traya ādi vākya artha viṣya buddhiḥ api iti
na api ca atra pramāṇa lakṣaṇa nirūpaṇa tātparyam prasiddha pramāṇa ādi vṛtti nirodha abhyupāyaḥ abhipradarśana paratvāt
atas eva na sūtrakāraḥ sūtrayāñcakāra
bhāsyakāreṇa tu kiñcid prasiddha anuvāda mātram avalambitam iti tat anusareṇena kim api jalpitam iti
pramāṇa ākhyām vṛttim vyākhyāya viparyaya abhidhānam vṛttim idānīm upavyācikhyāsamānaḥ āha viparyayaḥ mithyā jñānam iti
nanu nirodhasya prakṛta tvāt tasya ca hāna tvāt dhānasya ca heya apekṣa tvāt dheyasya ca avidya mūla tvāt avidyā ca viparyaḥ iti saḥ eva prādhānyena
tat prabhava tvāt dheyasya
kāraṇa nirodhe hi kāryam arthāt eva niruddham syāt
tasmāt viparyayaḥ prādhānyāt pramāṇāt pūrvam
satyam evam asya iva prāthamyam viparyayasya nirodhanīya tayā tathā api guṇa doṣa jñāna apekṣa tvāt nirodham prati puruṣa pravṛtteḥ
pramāṇam eva hi guṇa doṣa jñānam
na hi apremāṇena viparyayasya duṣṭa tvam gamyate nirodha tat phala sādhanāni vā jñāyante
tasmāt pramāṇa vṛtteḥ eva prāthamyam yuktam
jñāyete ca guṇa doṣau iti tat anantaram viparyaya abhidhānam
vṛtti antara apekṣayā tu viparyayasya prāthamyam
tat mūla tvāt ca vṛtti antarāṇām tad nirodha pūrvam eva anya nirodha upapatteḥ
viparyayaḥ mithyā jñanam iti paryāya kathanam
a tat rūpa pratiṣṭham iti lakṣaṇa uktiḥ
tasya rūpam tat rūpam yat ābhāsam vijñānam tasya vijñānasya ca sā pratiṣṭhā ālambanam
agṛhīta viśeṣasya sāmānya mātra buddhiḥ upalabdha pūrva anya vastu smṛti upasaṃhitā niścaya ākāreṇa upasaṃhitā niścaya ākāreṇa upājāyamānā viparyayaḥ
saṃśayaḥ hi ubhayoḥ idam sāmānyam iti evam gṛhīta sāmānyasya viśeṣam eva bubhutsamānasya jāyate iti smṛtau eva antarbhavati
yathā sthāṇuḥ kim vā purusaḥ iti gṛhīta pūrvasya eva viśeṣasya smarataḥ saṃśayaḥ jāyante na tathā viparyayaḥ
anyatara smaraṇa mātreṇa eva avasita tvāt
tat yathā sthāṇau purastāt avasthite pariṇāha ārohaṇa ādi sāmānya mātra upalambhena samupajāta puruṣaḥ araṃasya puruṣaḥ eva ayam iti niśtirā buddhiḥ utpadyate
sā yadi api indriya mārgeṇa upalabhyamāna vastu sāmānya pradhānā tathā api smaryamāṇa a tad vastu pratiṣṭha tvāt na pramāṇam
smṛti avasānā hi sā yatas pramāṇena prabādhyate ā ā bhūtārtha artha ādi viṣaya tvāt
iti atas pratiṣṭha tvāt iti etat abhūtaḥ hi smaryamāṇaḥ rthaḥ tadā
yadi evam smṛtiḥ eva prāpnoti na viśiṣṭa tvāt
upalabhyamānam vastu nimittīkṛtya anyatra smṛtiḥ jāyate yathā anubhūta vastu viṣayā
na viparyayaḥ tathā
sannihita sāmānya mātre deśa kāla ādi viśeṣa anugate vastuni smaraṇa paryavasāna tve sati api ayam iti viśeṣa rūpeṇa viparyaya pratyayaḥ jāyate
tasmāt evam na pramāṇa dharmaḥ nā api smṛtiḥ dharmaḥ iti vṛtti antara tvam
tatra āmramāṇasya pramāṇena bādha saṃdarśana artham udāharaṇam darśayati tat yathā dvi candra darśanam iti
yathā kāca kāmalā ādi upahata darśanasya abhūta artha viṣaya tvāt dhi dvi candra darśanasya sat viṣayeṇa bhūta artha viṣayeṇa eka candra darśanena dvitīya candra abhāva upapatti jñāna smṛti anugṛhītena bādhanam
nanu ca dvi candram iti dvi pūlī paṇca pūlī iti vat dvigu samāsa tvāt dviguḥ ekavacanam iti pratibandhe tad bhāvāt akāra anta uttara padaḥ dviguḥ striyām iṣṭaḥ iti dvigoḥ akāra antāt iti dvi candra śabdāt īkāraḥ prāpnoti na eṣa doṣaḥ pātra ādi pratiṣedhāt
tatra ca ādi śabdāḥ asya prakāra vacana tvāt
prakārasya ca śiṣṭa prayoga anusāri tvāt dvi candre api pātra ādiṣu draṣṭavyaḥ
dvau candrau yasmin darśane iti bahuvrīhiḥ
eka candra śabdasya a dvigu tvāt eva ca odya abhāvaḥ
sā ca pañca parvā avidyāḥ sā viparyaya vṛttiḥ avidyā paṇca parvaṇi asyāḥ iti kāni punar tāni iti āha avidyā asmitā ityādi
atas eva avidyā ādayaḥ kleśāḥ sva saṇjñabhiḥ svābhiḥ śāstra antara prasiddhābhiḥ tamaḥ ādi saṃjñabhiḥ viśiṣṭāḥ dvitīya pāde
idānīm vikalpam darśayati śabda jñāna anupātī vastu śūnyaḥ vikalpaḥ
śabdasya jñānam śabda jñānam vācya vācaka niyamena sādhu asādhu śabda jñānam tat anupatitum śīlam asya iti śabda jñāna anupātī
vastu śūnye iti
yathā vācya artha śūnyāḥ yasya śabdasya jñānam anupatati tasya śabdasya yathā bhūta abhidheyena śūnyaḥ iti yāvat
yathā bhūta artha vyatirekeṇa hi vikalpanam vikalpaḥ
tasya hi śabda jñāna anupāti tvāt āgama antaḥpāti tvam prāptam atas āha sa na pramāṇa upārohī iti
na pramāṇa antaḥpātī vastu śūnya tvāt
na hi āgamasya śabda jñāna anupāti tve api vastu śūnyatā
yatas śābda arth viṣayāḥ vṛttiḥ āgamaḥ vikalpaḥ tu vastu śūnya tvāt na pramāṇam
kiñ ca vaktṛ śrotroḥ ca tulyaḥ vikalpaḥ
dvayoḥ api śabdāt uccaritāt hi buddhiḥ jāyate
na tathā āgame
śrotuḥ eva hi āgamaḥ
vaktā tu dṛṣṭa anumita arthaḥ
kiñ ca niḥ vitarka samāpannasya vikalpaḥ nirvartate na āgamaḥ
tasmāt nityā na pramāṇa upārohī
yadi evam vastu śūnya tvāt viparyaya antaḥpāti tvam prāptam atas āha na viparyaya upārohi iti
kutas śabda jñāna anupāti tvāt
na hi vastu śūnya tve api viparyayaḥ śabda jñānam apekṣate
yatas viparyayaḥ mithyājñānam a tat rūpa pratiṣṭham iti uktam
pramāna pariddha idya pratyayam prati ari guṇa bhūta tvāt ca vikalpasya
na hi yathā sarveṣām viparyayaḥ virodhāt bādhyate tathā vikalpaḥ
pramāṇa pratyaya guṇa bhāvāt eva
tasmāt vastu śūnya tva grahaṇena śabda jñāna anupāti tva grahaṇena ca paraspara saṃbandhena pramāṇa viparyayābhyām pramāṇa viparyaya gandha mātra anuliptam api bhinnam vikalpa ākhyam vṛtti antaram darśitam
tadvat gandha anulepanāt eva tat ānantaryeṇa vikalpasya ārambhaḥ
na api smṛti tvam
smṛteḥ kevala anubhūta āspada tvāt
atha na tu īdṛśī citta vṛttiḥ prasiddhā
na hi svabhāvam kiṃcid vṛtti nimittam iti ced āha vastu śūnyatve api śabda jñāna māhātmya mātra nibandhanaḥ vyavahāraḥ dṛśyate iti
mātra grahaṇam śabda jñāna vyatirikta kāraṇa abhāva khyāpana artham
kva dṛśyate iti ced āha tat yathā caitanyam puruṣasya svarūpam iti
citi śaktiḥ apariṇāminī iti ukta tvāt caitanyam eva puruṣaḥ tat eva ca svarūpam iti vyatireka abhāvāt vyatireka upanibandhanaḥ vyapadeśaḥ na syāt puruṣasya caitanyam iti
tathā ca imam eva artham upaśritya śabdavidā vārttikakāreṇa uktam siddham tu vyapadeśi vat bhāvāt iti
tathā eva iha api yathā sati vyatireke caitrasya gauḥ iti tadvat eva caitanyam puruṣasya iti
na hi yathā goḥ anyaḥ caitraḥ vyapadeśa hetuḥ tathā citeḥ artha antaram puruṣaḥ sti yena vyapadiśyeta
na api citiḥ puruṣa artha antaram vyapadiśyeta
tathā api vyatireka saṃbandha viṣaye bhavati caitanyam puruṣasya svarūpam iti vyapadeśe vṛttiḥ
pratiṣiddha vastu dharmā iti
vastunaḥ dharmaḥ vastu dharmaḥ
pratiṣiddhaḥ vastu dharmaḥ syaḥ iti pratiṣiddha vastu dharmā
dharmāt an it kevalāt iti vacanāt samāsa antaḥ cintya samādhiḥ
vastu śabdena sattva ādi guṇāḥ ucyante teṣām dharmāḥ pratiṣiddhāḥ asya iti
na hi pratiṣiddhāḥ sattva ādi dharmāḥ pratiṣiddha tvāt eva asya puruṣasya sambandhinaḥ bhavanti
yena te puruṣeṇa asya iti vyapadeśyeran
tat abhāva mātram eva tu tatra arthaḥ
tathā api yathā citrāḥ gāvaḥ syaḥ iti vyapadeśe buddhiḥ tathā pratiṣiddhāḥ vastu dharmāḥ asya iti vyapadeśe buddhiḥ
nirgatā kriyā asmāt iti atra apinirgatiḥ apāyaḥ
apāyaḥ ca sambandha pūrvaḥ
yathā caitrāt nirgatā kriyā
na ca evam puruṣe kriyāyāḥ asambhavāt nirgatiḥ puruṣāt sambhavati
tathā api niṣkriyaḥ puruṣa iti vyapadeśe bhavati vṛttiḥ
tathā n utpatti dharmā puruṣaḥ iti
na vidyate utpatti dharmaḥ syaḥ iti pūrvavat eva
atra svayam eva artham ācaṣṭe bhāṣyakāraḥ utpatti dharmasya abhāva jñāna mātram gamyate
yathā nirguṇaḥ nirañjanaḥ niṣkalaḥ iti evam ādīni api udāharaṇāni
ātma viṣaya aneka udāharaṇa pradarśanam ātma tattva nirdhāraṇa artha tvāt
tiṣṭhati bāṇaḥ iti loka prasiddha udāharaṇa pratipādanam aprasiddhi āśaṅkā nivṛtti artham
tiṣṭhati iti gati nivṛttiḥ gati abhāvaḥ
na ca abhāvasya kāla traya yogaḥ bhavati
na api bāṇasya kriyā nirapekṣasya dravyasya
nā api ca abhāvena gati nivṛttyā bāṇasya vastunaḥ sambandhaḥ
tiṣṭhati bāṇaḥ sthāsyati sthitaḥ iti evam trīṇi udāharaṇāni
gati nivṛttau dhātvarthaḥ iti
nanu gati nivṛttiḥ eva dhātvarthaḥ tatra katham gati nivṛttau iti ādhāraḥ atas eva udāharaṇa antaram etat
asati vyatireke ādhāra ādheya bhāvasya abhāvāt
asti ca gati nivṛttau dhātvarthaḥ iti vyapadeśe śabda sāmarthya samutthāpitā buddhiḥ ādhāra ādheya bhāva sambandhau
tasmāt ittham jātīyam vikalpa viṣayam anekam udāharaṇam draṣṭavyam
nidrā ākhyām vṛttim idānīm ācaṣṭe abhāva pratyaya ālambanā vṛttiḥ nidrā
jāgrat viṣaya tvāt prāk uktasya trayasya tad upamardena ca nidrā samudbhavaḥ iti tat anantaram nidrā ākhyā vṛttiḥ vyākhyāyate
abhāvaḥ iti jāgrat viṣaya abhāvaḥ na tu atyanta abhāvaḥ eva
tatra pratyaya anupapatteḥ
abhāve pratyayaḥ abhāva pratyayaḥ
saḥ eva ālambanam yasyāḥ sā vṛttiḥ abhāva pratyaya ālambanā
sā nidrā suṣūpta avasthā
nanu ca svapna avasthā nidrā eva na eṣa doṣaḥ svapna nidrā jñāna ālambanam vā iti sūtrakāreṇa bhedena upadiṣṭa tvāt iha suṣupta avasthā eva nidrā abhipretā
kim ca abhāva pratyaya ālambana tvāt ca suṣuptam eva
na hi svapnasya abhāva pratyaya ālambana tā smṛti tvāt
smṛteḥ ca anubhūta viṣaya tvāt
tathā bhāṣyakāraḥ svapne bhāvita smartavyāḥ iti smṛti tvam darśayati
kiñ ca svapnasya citta vṛtti tā sva saṃvedyā iti na āśaṅkā eva upapadyate
tathā ca citta vṛtti tām āśaṅkya āha sā tu ca sam prabodhe pratyavamarśāt iti ādi
tasmāt pratyaya viśeṣaḥ nidrā
na hi asati pratyaya viśeṣe parāmarśaḥ yaktaḥ
asti ca ayam prabuddhasya pratyavamarśaḥ sukham aham asvāpsam ityādiḥ
pratyavamarśaḥ nāma kim api anvabhūvam iti pratyaya ālocanā na anubhava abhāve sā bhavet
nā api tad viṣayāḥ smṛtayaḥ yuktāḥ
nidrāyāḥ apratyaya tve prajñām viśāradīkaroti manaḥ manasaḥ kartṛ tvam satyānam stimitam akarmaṇyam guru gurūṇi iti prakāre guṇavacanasya iti dvis vacanam guru prakārāṇi alasam muṣitam iva mallena apahṛtam iva etāni pratyaya anubhava kāryāṇi na syuḥ
kāḥ cana smṛtayaḥ kānicid kāryāṇi kecana pratyavamarśāḥ
tat etat trayam api bhāṣyakāra upanyastam pratyaya viśeṣa tve eva upapadyate
kiñca garbhagṛha ādiṣu ca adṛṣṭa bāhya nimittānām asati viśeṣe ciram aham suptavān kṣiptam iti ca parāmarśaḥ nyathā na yujyate
nanu ca na atra smṛtayaḥ smṛtīnām anvabhavam iti evam viśiṣṭa tvāt
na hi suṣuptāt utthitaḥ viśeṣam smarati atra ucyate bālasya iha janmani ananubhūta stanya sambandhasya janma anantaram eva tasya abhilāṣaḥ dṛśyate
na ca sa svābhāvikaḥ
abālānām smṛti pūrva pravṛtti darśanāt
tathā iha api
tasmāt pratyaya pūrvakaḥ suṣupta utthitasya gātra gaurava ādi kāryam duḥkha ādi anubhava pūrvam gātra ādi viṣaya gaurava ādi kārya tvāt prasiddha duḥkha anubhava gārta gātra gaurava vat iti pratyaya viśeṣaḥ nidrā iti siddham
smṛtim idānīm vyācaṣṭe anubhūta viṣaya asaṃpramoṣaḥ smṛtiḥ
smṛteḥ pramāṇa ādi sarva vṛtti kārya tvāt ante niveśaḥ
anubhūtaḥ ca asau viṣayaḥ ca anubhūta viṣayaḥ
yaḥ asau ānanda mahā udanvat taraṅgāyamāṇaḥ anubhūtaḥ saḥ eva viṣayaḥ na punar yaḥ viṣayaḥ saḥ eva anubhūtaḥ iti tathā ca smṛteḥ aśabda ādi tvāt smṛti viṣayāyāḥ smṛteḥ asmṛti tvam prāpnoti iti
iṣyate ca smṛti visayāḥ api smṛtiḥ sva saṃvedya tvāt anubhūta visayasya asaṃpramoṣaḥ na apaharaṇam a tiras bhāvaḥ
pārokṣye api sādṛśya ādi nimitta apekṣayā anubhūtasya viṣayasya dṛśyamāna vat avabhāsaḥ smṛtiḥ
tatra pratyaya smaraṇayoḥ kiṅkṛtaḥ tayoḥ bhedaḥ iti tat vivekam āha kim pratyayasya cittam smarati ityādi
yadi api anubhūta anubhūyamāna viṣaya tvena vivekaḥ tathā api sādṛśya nimittām bhrāntim tayoḥ kārya kāraṇatva pradarśanāya
etat eva ca vaināśikānām bahis artha anupapatteḥ buddhi kāraṇam
kim pratyayasya smarati iti karmaṇi ubhayatra ṣaṣṭhī
cittam smarati iti puruṣa kartṛ tvam nivārayati smṛti pratyayayoḥ eka kartṛ tva pradarśana artham
na hi puruṣasya pratyaya kartṛ tvam smṛti kartṛ tvam vā
dṛśya tvāt pratyayānām
dṛśyānām ca sva ātma atirikta dṛśya tvam ghaṭa ādi vat iti vakṣyāmaḥ
kiñca atas yadi viṣayasya smarati pratyayasya api viṣaya viṣaya tvāt anartha antaram smṛtiḥ pratyayāt
atha pratyayasya smarati tadā tu idam ayuktam anubhūta viṣaya asaṃpramoṣaḥ iti
tadā hi anubhava asaṃpramoṣaḥ iti syāt tatra āha grāhya uparatktaḥ grāhyaḥ viṣayaḥ ālambanam tena uparaktaḥ lākṣā ādi uparaktaḥ phaṭika vat
grāhya grahaṇa ubhaya ākāra nirbhāsaḥ grāhyasya ca ghata ādeḥ pṛthu budghna ādi ākāreṇa svena ca avabhāsa rūpeṇa upajāyamāna tvāt ubhaya nirbhāsaḥ
sa ca pratyayaḥ utpadya vinivartamānaḥ sva āśraye pratyayini saṃskāram ādadhāti
sa ca saṃskāraḥ kāraṇa anuvidhāyi tvāt kāraḥ eva
sva vyañjaka añjanaḥ iti saṃskāra adhyinaḥ pratyayasya hetu bhūtam yat karma datta phalam tat tulya jātīyam yat karma antaram phala pradānāya abhimukhībhavati tat sva vyañjakam
tathā ca vakṣyati tatas tad vipāka anuguṇānām eva abhivyaktiḥ vāsanānam iti tat karma pratyupanītam vā sādṛśya praṇidhāna ādi
svena vyañjakena abhivyajyate iti sva vyañjaka añjanaḥ
grāhya grahaṇa ātmikām smṛtim janayati
anyathā tad vyañjakasya karmaṇaḥ vipāka anupapattiḥ
tatra grahaṇa ākāra pūrvā buddhiḥ grahaṇam svī karaṇam svīkaraṇam eva pūrvam prathamam utpdyamānasya pratyayasya
na hi viṣaya viśeṣam apekṣate pūrvam iṣṭa aniṣṭa grahaṇāt nirbhagna ghaṭa pradīpa vinirgata prabhā jāla vat
grāhya ākāra pūrvā smṛtiḥ anubhūta apekṣa tvāt
yadi ca smṛtiḥ pratyaya vat abhaviṣyat anubhūtam na apaikṣiṣyata
apekṣate tu
tasmāt grāhyaḥ viṣayaḥ pūrvaḥ syāḥ na grahaṇam
tathā api tu ubhaya ātmikāḥ eva
smṛti saṃskārayoḥ eka rūpa tvāt na api anyatara pratyākhyānena sambhavati
tathā ca anubhūta viṣaya asaṃpramoṣaḥ iti upapadyate
smṛti pratyayayoḥ api amāna viṣaya tvāt grahaṇa tvasya ca sarvatra sambhavāt
tasmāt pakṣa dvaye api abhihita doṣaḥ na dṛśyate iti
sā ca dvayī
katham hāvita smartavyāḥ bhāvitam para niṣpannam asakṛt bhāvita tvāt
yathā dravya antareṇa asakṛt bhāvitam taila ādi
asakṛt bhāvita tvāt eva praṇidhāna ādi prayatna antaram na apekṣate
bhāvitam smartavyam praṇidhāna ādi yatna antarā na pekṣayā yasyāḥ sā svapne bhāvita smartavyā
samaye tu apekṣate praṇidhāna ādi yatna antaram iti tad viparītā
sarvāḥ ca pramāṇa ādi vṛtti pañcatayā anubhavāt udbhavanti
sarvāḥ ca etāḥ sukha ādyāḥ rasa ttva ādyā ātmikāḥ
tad ātmakaḥ ca saṃsāraḥ
sukha duḥkha mohāḥ ca kleśeṣu vyākhyātāḥ sūtrakāreṇa
sarvam duḥkham vivekinaḥ iti hi vakṣyati
tad hānam ca iha vivakṣitam
tasmāt sukha duḥkha moha ātmaka tvāt niroddhavyāḥ vṛttayaḥ
kiñca āsām nirodhe samprajñātaḥ vā samādhiḥ bhavati a samprajñātaḥ vā
atha āsām nirodhe kaḥ upāyaḥ iti
upāyam pravedayati abhyāsa vairāgyābhyām tad nirodhaḥ iti
abhyāsa vairāgye vakṣyamāṇa lakṣaṇe
tābhyām yathā ukta lakṣaṇānām vṛttīnām nirodhaḥ viroghāt
nirodhaḥ upaśamaḥ
abhyāsa vairāgyayoḥ viṣaya viveka pradarśana artham etat bhāṣyam citta nadī ityādi
cittena nadī eva saṃsāriṇaḥ satatam viṣaye pariṇīyante saṃsāra prāk bhārā saṃsāra avasānā samudra avasānā iva
khilīkriyate pratibadhyate iti
uddhāṭyate pravartyate
uddhāṭaḥ kriyate iti uddhāṭyate
anyathā mi tvāt ghaṭa ādayaḥ mitaḥ iti ha tu mitām iti syāt
evam ubhayatantraḥ iti arthaḥ
tatra abhyāsa svarūpam pratipādayiṣyan āha tatra sthitau yatnaḥ bhyāsaḥ
tatra tasmin nirodhe sā ca nimitta saptamī
nirodha nimittā cittasya yā sthitiḥ yatnasya phala bhūtā tasyāḥ yaḥ yatnaḥ saḥ bhyāsaḥ
tathā ca āha avṛttikasya pariṇāmaḥ niruddha vṛttikasya cittasya
yatnaḥ vīryam abhyutsāhaḥ iti paryāyāḥ
sthiti saṃpipādayiṣayā yama niyama ādi yoga sādhana anuṣṭhānam abhyāsaḥ iti
sa tu katham sthirībhavati iti atas āha dīrgha kāla nairantarya sevitaḥ tu avarjitaḥ vā nairantarya varjitaḥ vā na dṛḍha bhūmiḥ bhavati abhyāsaḥ
tasmāt ubhayoḥ api viśeṣya viśeṣaṇa tvam eva
saṃskāra āsevitaḥ iti tu abhyāsaḥ eva viśeṣyate
dṛḍha bhūmiḥ iti asya vyākhyānam vyutthāna saṃskāreṇa iti
vyutthāna jena saṃskāreṇa drāk iti sahasā na abhibhūyate
vairāgya pratipādana artham āha dṛṣṭa ānuśravika viṣaya avitṛṣṇasya vaśīkāra saṃjñā vairāgyam viṣaya śabdaḥ pratyekam abhisaṃbandhyate vitṛṣṇaye iti ca drṣṭa viṣaya vitṛṣṇasya ānuśravika viṣaya vitṛṣṇasya ca iti
dṛṣṭaḥ ca asau viṣayaḥ ca tasmin
kaḥ punar asau striyaḥ nnam pānam aiśvaryam iti vyakti apekṣayā
śabdaḥ ādīnām ānantye api rāga prabala tvam eteṣu atitarām iti strī ādi grahaṇam prādhānyāt
atra hi prabalataraḥ rāgaḥ sa prayatna tareṇa niṣeddhavyaḥ
evam ānuśravika viṣayaḥ
ānuśravikaḥ nāma āgamikaḥ iha sa ca svarga ādi prāptyā anubhavanīyaḥ prakṛti laya gata bhogyaḥ vaidehyā aprāptau upabhogyaḥ ca
nanu ca vaitṛṣṇyam eva vairāgyam tathā rāgaḥ tṛṣṇā garddhaḥ iti hi vakṣyati
na avasthā viśeṣasya vivakṣita tvāt
tathā ca yatamāna saṃjñā vyatikrānta saṃjñā eka indriya samjñā vaśīkāra saṃjñā iti catasṛṣṇām āsām sāmānya saṃjñā vairāgyam iti
evam sati dṛṣṭa ānuśravika viṣaya vitṛṣṇasya iti etat uktam bhavati a vigata pūrva avasthā trayasya caturthīm yā avasthā sā tu iha vairāgyam iti vivakṣitam
tasmāt iha vaitṛṣṇyāt anya vairāgyam abhipretam
tathā ca darśayati viṣya doṣa darśinaḥ doṣa darśanasya viṣaya nicṛtti hetu tvāt
tat guṇa darśanam hi rāga kāraṇam prasaṃkhyāna balāt tat doṣa darśana abhyāsa balāt

divya adivyayoḥ samprayogaḥ api heya upādeya śūnyā rañjana avamuktasya iva sphuṭikasya viṣaya rāga vimuktasya cittasya avasthānam
vaśīkāra saṃjñāḥ vaśīkartum śakyante syām avasthāyām sarve gauṇāḥ padārthāḥ vaśīkartavya tvena saṃjñāyante vaśīkṛtāni ca tasyām avasthāyām indriyāṇi saṃjñāyante vaśīkaraṇam vā saṃjñāyate syām iti
tat ca dvividham param ca aparam ca viṣaya nimitta bhedena
aparam vyākhyātam
adhunā param ucyate tat param puruṣa khyāteḥ guṇa vaitṛṣṇyam
tat iti vairāgyam parāmṛśyate
param iti pūrva ukta vairāgyāt uttara kāla bhāvi iti
yadi vā tasya utkṛṣṭa nimitta viṣaya tvāt kaivalyasya vā pratyāsannatara tvāt param utkṛṣṭam
kim nimittam asya iti āha puruṣa khyāteḥ nimittāt
kim viṣayam iti āha guṇa vaitṛṣṇyam iti kuṇeṣu sattva ādiṣu vaitṛṣṇyam
dṛṣṭa ānuśravika viṣaya doṣa darśi iti
pūrva vairāgya nimitta viṣaya parāmarśanam asya viṣaya nimitta bheda viveka artham
puruṣa darśana abhyāsāt nimittāt
tad śuddhi praviveka āpyāyita buddhiḥ
tat iti puruṣa darśanam parāmṛśyate

atha vā tasya puruṣasya śuddhiḥ tad śuddhiḥ
tad śuddheḥ tad ālambana darśanam pravivicyate
tat pravivekena api āyitā buddhiḥ asya yoginaḥ
guṇebhyaḥ iti viṣaya pratipādanam
pūrvaḥ tu dṛṣṭa ānuśravika viṣayebhyaḥ api viraktaḥ eṣa tad kāraṇebhyaḥ guṇebhyaḥ eva
vyakta avyakta dharmakebhyaḥ mahat ādi saṃsthitāḥ vyakta dharmakāḥ
pradhāna avasthitāḥ avyakta dharmakāḥ tebhyaḥ viraktaḥ iti tat dvayam vairāgyam pūrvam idam ca tatra yat uttaram puruṣa darśana nimittam guṇa viṣayam tad jñāna prasāda mātram
puruṣa darśanasya eva paraḥ pravivekaḥ iti yāvat
puruṣa darśī hi heya upādeya śūnya cittaḥ bhavati
tat āha prasṃkhyāne api a kusīd asya sarvathā viveka khyāteḥ dharmameghaḥ samādhiḥ iti
yasya udaye yasya vairāgyasya udaye
pratyudita khyātiḥ pratyutpanna darśanaḥ
evam manyate prāptam prāpaṇīyam iti ādi etasya hi nāntarīyakam kaivalyam tatas param sādhana anapekṣa tvāt
vairāgyasya jñāna prasāda mātra tve jñāna vairāgyayoḥ ananya tvāt tad viparītayoḥ ca rāga ajñānayoḥ anartha antara tvam eva siddham
evam sati rāgaḥ api avidyāyāḥ eva avasthā antaram iti pañca parvā avidyā iti upapannam bhavati
nanu ca evam buddheḥ aṣṭaguṇa tvam bādhyeta
ṣaṣ guṇa tvam hi dhyāna avasthā bheda abhyupagamāt
jñāna tve api vairāgyasya prasannatara tva abhyupagamaḥ
rāgaḥ api ajñānasya avasthā antara viśeṣaḥ
nanu ca evam sati jñāna ajñānayoḥ aneka avasthā bhedāt aṣṭaguṇa tvam punar api na prāpnoti
na eṣa doṣaḥ phalavat tva pratyanīka tva niyamāt

tathā ajñāna avasthā catuṣṭaya pratyanīka tvena adharma ādi catuṣṭaya niyamaḥ iti aṣṭaguṇa tva siddhiḥ dharma ādi pratidvandvinaḥ eva hi guṇa tvena niyamyante na ajñāna bhedāḥ sarve eva
uktam purastāt samprajñātaḥ samādhiḥ vitarka ādi anugataḥ iti upariṣṭāt pravedayiṣyāmaḥ iti
saḥ vasara prāptaḥ idānīm lakṣyate
upāya dvayena niruddha vṛtteḥ vairāgya dvatam para apara tvena
abhyāsasya api dvi tvam sāmarthyāt avasīyate
katham viśiṣṭam asamprajñāta samādheḥ abhyāsam sūtreṇa eva vakṣyati virāma pratyaya abhyāsa pūrvaḥ iti
tena sa ālambana viṣayaḥ pūrva abhyāsaḥ iti niścīyate
vakṣyati ca tad pratiṣedha artham eka tattva abhyāsaḥ iti
bhāṣyakāraḥ api avadīt vairāgyeṇa viṣaya srotaḥ khilīkriyate
viveka darśana abhyāsena kalyāṇa srotaḥ uddhaṭyate iti na avocata vṛtti svarūpa tiraskāram eva samprajñāta samādheḥ
vṛtti nirodha prabhava tvam aniṣṭa viṣaya pravṛtti uparama uttara kāla bhāvi tva apekṣayā vṛtti viṣaya viśeṣa anugataḥ eva hi saḥ
tathā ca dvitīya sūtre samprajñātasya nirodhaḥ na lakṣaṇam iti vyākhyātam
atas bhyāsa vairāgya upāya dvayena niruddha vṛtteḥ cittasya katham ucyate katham lakṣaṇam ucyate iti yāvat
vitarka vicāra ānanda asmitā rūpa anugamāt samprajñātaḥ
anugama śabdaḥ pratyekam saṃbandhanīyaḥ
vitarka anugamāt vicāra anugamāt ānanda anugamāt asmitā rūpa anugamāt iti
rūpa śabdaḥ mātrā arthaḥ vitarka ādi pūrva dharma traya varjita tva khyāpana arthaḥ
vitarkaḥ cittasya ālambante sthūlaḥ āmogaḥ
sthūla api miśrī bhāvaḥ prathamam ālambana ākāreṇa pariṇamamānasya cittasya yaḥ ālambana vyatikaraḥ sa vitarkaḥ
sūkṣmaḥ vicāraḥ āmogaḥ sūkṣmaḥ iti saṃbandhaḥ
ānandaḥ hlādaḥ vicāraḥ sūkṣmataraḥ ābhogaḥ tṛtīyaḥ
sa ānanda tā viśeṣaḥ
eka rūpa ātmikā saṃvid asmitā svasyām prakṛtau asmitāyām samāpannasya asmitā pratyaya mātra tā eka rūpa ātmaka tvam
tathā ca udāhariṣyati tam aṇum ātmānam anvavaitya asmi iti etāvat saṃjānīte iti
nanu ca asmitā kleśeṣu paṭhiṣyati dṛś darśana śaktyoḥ eka ātma tā iva asmitā iti tat katham iva asmitā rūpeṇa kleśena samādhiḥ anugamyate iti
satyam evam prakṛṣṭa sva kāraṇa ākāra avabhāsaka tvāt anya viṣaya vinivṛtta ātmaka tvāt ca asmitāyāḥ mama adhirūpa tve api adoṣaḥ
yadi vā asmitā rūpasya ālambanasya avisyātve api na yogi pratyayasya avidyā tvam
na hi khalu para citta vividiṣāyām
na hi khalu para citta pratyayam gṛhṇan parakīya avidyā pratyaya rūpa ālambana doṣeṇa svayam avidyāvān bhavati
yaḥ punar kleśaḥ sa viparyaya viśiṣṭaḥ eva
yathā aham gacchāmi kṛśaḥ ham iti
yogi cittasya tat nyak bhūtam rajaḥ tamasī iti na tathā
tatra pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ svakīya uttara uttara dharma anugataḥ paraḥ paraḥ tu pūrva pūrva dharma vikalaḥ
yasmāt ca etat dharma catuṣṭaya anugataḥ eva ayam samprajñātaḥ tasmāt etat lakṣaṇaḥ iti lakṣaṇa artham sūtram
loke api yaḥ yat asādhāraṇa dharma anuyātaḥ sa tad lakṣaṇaḥ yathā sāsnā ādi lakṣaṇaḥ gauḥ iti
asmitā mātra grahaṇāt nirālambana tām eṣām samādhīnām mā kaścid āśaṅkiṣṭa iti āha sarve ete sa ālambanāḥ iti
yaḥ punar manyate nirvikalpa tvam asmitā iti tat asataḥ
asmitā śabdasya ahaṅkāre prasiddha tvāt
tathā ca āha smitā
atha asamprajñātaḥ yogaḥ citta vṛtti nirodhaḥ iti upapādita lakṣaṇaḥ kim upāyaḥ kim sādhanaḥ kena upāyena upetyaḥ iti arthaḥ
kim svabhāvaḥ kim svarūpaḥ kim avasthaḥ iti svabhāva viśiṣṭa sādhana saṃbandha pradarśana artham āha virāma pratyaya abhyāsa pūrvaḥ saṃskāra śeṣaḥ
virāma pratyaya abhyāsa pūrvaḥ iti etāvatā sādhana sambandham ācaṣṭe
saṃskāra śeṣaḥ iti tu svabhāva vyākhyānam
anyaḥ iti anantara ukta lakṣaṇāt samprajñātāt anyaḥ ayam nirbījaḥ asamprajñātaḥ
anyaḥ iti ubhābhyām saṃbandhyate virāma pratyaya abhyāsa pūrvaḥ ca saṃskāra śeṣaḥ ca
kaḥ sau ubhya viśiṣṭaḥ iti āha anyaḥ iti
viramaṇam viramaḥ
virāmaḥ ca asau pratyayaḥ ca virāma pratyayaḥ
virāma rūpa tvāt saḥ eva pratyayaḥ virāmaḥ iti ucyate
sarva viṣayebhyaḥ vinivartamānasya vinivartana kāle prāk apratyaya āpatteḥ pratyaya rūpa tvam
etat yathā pāvakasya jvalataḥ prakṣīyamāṇa idhanasya śanais śanais upaśāmyataḥ prāk aṅgāra tā āpatteḥ jvālā ātmaka tā
tasmāt virāma rūpaḥ pratyayaḥ virāma pratyayaḥ tasya abhyāsaḥ pūrvaḥ mukhyam yasya saḥ virāma pratyaya abhyāsa pūrvaḥ
saṃskāraḥ eva śeṣaḥ yasya sa saṃskāra śeṣaḥ
pratyaya uparame tu pratyaya saṃskāraḥ eva avaśiṣyate
viṣaya pratyayebhyaḥ uparatam cittam saṃskāra śeṣam eva iti arthaḥ
tasya param vairāgyam upāyaḥ tasya samādheḥ param uttaram
nanu ca param vairāgyam ca iti vaktavyam abhyāsa vairāgyābhyām vṛtti nirodhasya abhipreta tvāt
na eṣa doṣaḥ
virāma pratyaya abhyāsasya sūtra upātta tvāt anāśaṅkyaḥ tad abhyāsaḥ
vairāgyam punar an upātta tvāt āśaṅkyeta
tasmāt tat eva prapayatā na ca nirmokṣaḥ caḥ paṭhitaḥ
yadi evam kasmāt na sūtre eva vairāgya grahaṇam kṛtam pūrvatra paṭhita tvāt
tatra kim artham paṭhitam iti ced vairāgya prasaṅgāt
pūrva vairāgya viśeṣaḥ eva uttaram vairāgyam iti prasaṅgāt uttaram duktam
pūrvasya ca vairāgyasya samprajñāta viṣaye viniyogāt a viśiṣṭya parasya sādhana tvāt anya viṣaya tvāt ca nirbījena eva sambandhaḥ iti na sūtre vairāgya grahaṇam kṛtam
sāmarthya prāptam tu bhāṣyakāraḥ darśayati
abhyāsa vairāgyābhyām tad nirodhaḥ iti hi pratipāditam
sa ālambanaḥ hi abhyāsaḥ viruddha tvāt nirālambanasya samādheḥ
sādhana tvāya na kalpate iti nirvastukaḥ api virāma pratyayaḥ nirālambana samādhi anurūpa tvāt ālambanīkriyate
tasmāt tad abhyāsa vairāgya upāya pūrvakam cittam nirālambanam abhāva prāptam iva bhavati
saḥ eṣa nirbījaḥ saṃskāra śeṣa svabhāvaḥ samādhiḥ asamprajñātaḥ iti
sa khalu ayam dvividhaḥ
