saḥ nirbījaḥ samādhiḥ upāya pratyayaḥ bhava pratyayaḥ ca
upāyena pratīyate prāpyate iti upāya pratyayaḥ yoginām bhavati
yadi api videhāḥ api yoginaḥ eva
tathā api yama ādi yoga sādhana anuṣṭhāyinaḥ bhipretāḥ
teṣām śraddhā vīrya ādi upāya labhyaḥ samādhiḥ
videha prakṛti layānām tu janmanā eva labhyaḥ
te hi tanutara pratibandha avaśeṣāḥ sa tu pratibandha avaśeṣaḥ teṣām sakṛt āsādita punarjanmanām samādhi vyāghātāya na paryāpnoti
sa tu janma pratilambha mātra nimittam
tvāt jñāna vairāgya ādi anuṣṭhāna kārya tvāt videha prakṛti laya tvasya tat iti artha sūtram
īdṛśām hi tad anusṭhāna māhātmyam
yat uta sāmarthya ādi vaikalyāt amhi īṣsita phala anavāptau api mahanīyataram videha prakṛti laya tvam prāpyate
videhāḥ nāma devāḥ puryaṣṭaka śarīra upabandhāḥ
te sva samskāra mātra upbhogena vairāgya abhyāsa āhitaḥ samskāra śeṣaḥ tad mātra upabhogena cittena kaivalyam iha anubhavantaḥ iti sattva guṇa vinirbhogāt sva saṃskāra paripākam kṣpayanti
prakṛti layāḥ sa adhikāre aparyavasitāḥ hi kāre
yāvat hi na kṛtā guṇa puruṣa antara khyātiḥ tāvat a parisamāpta adhikāram eva cittam tasmin prakṛt laya āpanne kaivalyam iva anubhavanti iti
pūrvavat
yāvat na punar āvartate dhikāra vaśāt vidyā kartavya tā vaśāt tāvat anubhavanti kaivalyam iva
yeṣām upāya pratyayaḥ yoginām teṣām śraddhā vīrya smṛti smādhi prajñā pūrvakaḥ samādhiḥ śraddhā nāma apavarga prāptau tat sādhana śravaṇe ca kataka phala saṃparkaḥ iva salilasya cetasaḥ samprasādaḥ saṃprasattiḥ
sa hi jananī iva kalyāṇī yoginam pāti rakṣati aśubhebhyaḥ
tasya hi viveka arthinaḥ samyak darśana arthinaḥ vīryam utsāhaḥ upajāyate yoga sādhana anuṣṭhānam prati
sañjāta vīryasya āgama jñāna ādi viṣayā dṛḍhatarā smiṛtiḥ upatiṣṭhate
viveka arthinaḥ iti sarvatra anuṣajyate
dṛḍha smṛti upasthāne ca cittam an ākulam samāḍhīyate
samāhita cittasya prajñāyāḥ buddheḥ vivikta tā sarva artha prakāśana sāmarthyam
ta thā t viśinaṣṭi yena yathābhūtam ātmā adhi vastu jānāti iti
tad abhyāsāt etat uktam bhavati ātma darśana virāma pratyaya abhyāsāt iti
tat viṣayāt ca vairāgyā khyāt viṣayā parasmāt vairāgyāt iti
asamprajñātaḥ samādhiḥ iti
te api śraddhā ādi sādhanāḥ nava yoginaḥ bhavanti
tat darśayati tat yathā mṛdu upāyaḥ madhya upāyaḥ dhimātra upāyaḥ iti
teṣām ekekaḥ tridhā bhidyate tatra mṛdu upāyaḥ iti sādhana anuṣṭhānam prati manda upakramaḥ madhya upakramaḥ iti
evam itaratra api iti
na atra tirobhūtam
tatra adhimātra upāyānām tīvra saṃvegānām āsannaḥ samādhi lābhaḥ samādhi phalam ca
teṣām api mṛdu madhya tīvra upāya krama tayā viśiṣyamāṇa tvāt tatas api viśeṣaḥ sādhana anuṣṭhāna saṃskārasya
tad viśeṣāt api uttarasya samādhi lābhaḥ pratyāsīt aitarām
etat asya sūtrasya prayojanam yoga sādhana anuṣṭhānam prati yoginaḥ katham upabṛṃhita utsāhāḥ bhaveyuḥ iti
yathā loke drutataram sīmāntam pari prati dhāvatām etat phalam bhavati iti tadvat
atha vā manda manda itara upakramāṇām api yoginām abhimata phala avāpti prakāśanāt anavasanna cetasaḥ pravarteran iti
itarathā tīvratara āyāsa janita bhītayaḥ vasīdeyuḥ iti
kim etasmāt eva āsannataraḥ bhavati atha tasya asya lābhe bhavati anyaḥ api kaścid upāyaḥ na vā iti
upāya antaram asti iti āha īśvara praṇidhānāt vā
īśvara śabda artham uttaratra vyākhyāsyati
praṇidhānam iha vyācaṣṭe bhakti viśeṣāt āvarjitaḥ iti
anugraham prati abhimukhībhāvam āpāditaḥ tam bhakti atiśaya yoginam yoginam abhidhyāna mātreṇa paramaḥ īśvara tvāt eva nirāyāsa tayā satya saṃkalpa tvāt anugṛhṇāti
tad anugrahāt api pratyāsannataraḥ samādhi lābhaḥ phalam ca iti
atha pradhāna puruṣa vyatiriktaḥ kaḥ yam īśvaraḥ iti sāṃkhya śāstre prasiddhi abhāvāt īśvara sadbhāve ca upapattim avaśyam anavagataḥ īśvara viśeṣaḥ vā pṛcchati
tatra tāvat pratijānīte kleśa karma vipakā āśayaiḥ aparāmṛṣṭaḥ puruṣa viśeṣaḥ īśvaraḥ
kleśāḥ iti
avidyā ādayaḥ kleśayanti iti kleśāḥ
tat pūrva anuṣṭhitāni kuśala akuśalāni karmāṇi
kuśalāni ca akuśalāni ca kuśala kuśalāni ca iti ekaśeṣaḥ
kuśala akuśalāni iti yāvat
tad phalam vipākaḥ jāti āyuḥ bhoga lakṣaṇaḥ
te eva kleśa ādayaḥ nirvāṇāt śerate iti kleśa karma vipakāḥ āśayāḥ
yadi vā kleśa ādīnām rāśayaḥ
te manasi vartamānāḥ manaḥ vṛtti prabhava tvāt puruṣe vyapadiśyante
kasmāt sa hi tat phalasya bhoktā iti
yathā rājani jaya parājayau yuddheṣu vartamānau apadiśyete tat phalam rāja saṃbandhaḥ iti
yaḥ hi anena bhogena aparāmṛṣṭaḥ iti ucyate
na kāla vivakṣā upalakṣaṇa ṛtha tvam na parāmṛśyate na api parāmṛkṣyate na api parāmṛṣṭaḥ iti
ti arthaḥ
sūtra artha viśuddhim kurvan āha kaivalyam prāptaḥ tarhi iti
kleśa ādi aparāmarśasya kādācitkatayā api saṃbhavāt
santi bahavaḥ kevalinaḥ kim te śvarāḥ iti
parāmarśasya api saṃbhavāt na te ekāntena kleśa ādibhiḥ aparāmṛṣṭāḥ
parāmarśa aparāmarśau hi staḥ teṣām
īśvaratva parāmṛṣṭaḥ eva
na hi anavadhṛtaḥ śabda arthaḥ lakṣaṇa tvena upādeyaḥ aparāmṛṣṭaḥ iti
tasmāt yaḥ ekāntena aparāmṛṣṭaḥ iti ucyate
te hi trīṇi bandhanāni prākṛta vaikṛta dākṣiṇāni samyak darśanena hitvā kaivalyam prāptāḥ
īśvarasya tu tad saṃbandhaḥ kleśa ādi sambandhaḥ na bhūtaḥ yathā muktasya pūrvā bandha koṭeḥ muktvā upapatteḥ eva jñāyate
bandha pūrvikā hi kuktiḥ
na api bhāvī
yathā prakṛti līnasya
tasya hi anārabdha saṃsārasya uttarā bandha koṭiḥ sambhāvyate
pravṛtta saṃsārasya ca aprakṛti līna cittasya sā samā adhikāra tvāt pūrva uttara bandha koṭī sambhavataḥ
tat idam sarvam atra aparāmṛṣṭe iti kāla avivakṣā pradarśana artham
sa tu sadā eva muktaḥ sadā eva īśvaraḥ
tatra puruṣa viśeṣaḥ īśvaraḥ iti ukta tvāt īśvarasya puruṣasya anaiśvarya dharma tvāt cittasya ca aiśvarya dharma tvāt niratiśaya aiśvaryasya ca prakṛṣṭa citta sambandha apekṣa tvāt prāptam eva uttara artham anuvadati prakṛṣṭa sattva upādānāt īśvarasya śāśvatikaḥ utkarṣaḥ iti

tatra pratijñā viśuddhi artham praśna pūrvam upakramate sa kim sa nimittaḥ āhosvit nirnimittaḥ iti
nimitta śabdaḥ kāraṇa paryāyaḥ
sa kim sakāraṇaḥ āhosmin niṣkāraṇaḥ iti
kiñca atas yadi tāvat sa kāraṇaḥ tadā sadā eva īśvaraḥ iti ayuktam anitya tvāt
atha niṣkāraṇaḥ tathā ca utkarṣasya kārya tvāt asattva prasaṅgaḥ
na hi niṣkāraṇam kāryam dṛśyate loke
atra ucyate na niṣkāraṇaḥ śāstra nimitta tvāt
śāstram jñānam
śāstrasya hetu tvāt
yatas satva viṣayam jñānam nityam dravya svabhāva sādhya sādhana vyavahita viprakṛṣṭa āspadam
yadi evam jñānasya anyatas dhigama pūrva tvāt prāk anutkarṣaḥ prāptaḥ iti atas āha śāstram punar kim nimittam iti
yadi svābhāvikam jñānam matta unmatta jñāna vat anutkarṣa hetu tvam
atha punar sa nimittakam nimittāt prāk anutkarṣaḥ iti manyate
na tāvat nirnimittam
yatas prakṛṣṭa sattva nimittam prakṛṣṭa sattva āśrayam iti yāvat
atas eva svabhāva jñāna doṣa abhāvaḥ
kiñ ca svābhāvika jñāna tve api na matta ādi jñāna vat apakarṣa hetu tvam
nitya mukta kleśa ādi sattva āśraya tvāt
tatra yathā eva jñāna saṃskāra smṛti prabandhānām anyonya nimitta naimittika bhāvena bīja aṅkur vat anādi saṃbandhaḥ tathā eva śāstra prakarṣayoḥ īśvara cetasi nitya pravṛtta prabandha rūpeṇa pravartamānayoḥ anādi antaḥ saṃbandhaḥ
tatra utkarṣaḥ jñanasya kāryam eva api tasya kāraṇam eva
anyeṣām vyākhyānam nimitta śabdaḥ pramāṇa vācī
tasya śāstram nimittam pramāṇam tena hi tad utkarṣaḥ pramīyate
śāstram punar kiṃpramāṇakam īśvara nirmala sattva pramāṇam
viśuddha sattva praṇīta tvāt hi śāstrasya prāmāṇyam yathā manu ādīnām
tathā ca śrutiḥ yat kiṃcid manuḥ abhyavadat tat bheṣajam iti yathā ca loke guruṇā bhihitam iti
etayoḥ śāstra utkarṣayoḥ pramāṇa prameya tayā nirādi antaḥ sambandhaḥ
nanu ca nā eva īśvara sattve ā vartamānena tad utkarṣaḥ pramīyate
na eṣa doṣaḥ
tat prabhava tvāt tatra vartamānam
te eva tat prabhavam api śāstram tasmin sarvajña tvāt eva
loke api yatas yat prabhavati vartate tat tasmin yathā tantu ādiṣu paṭa ādi
tat prabhava tvam anumāna āgamābhyām avagamyate
śāstra pramāṇakaḥ utkarṣaḥ īśvara pramāṇakam śāstram iti bhinna āśraya tvāt śāstra utkarṣayoḥ na itaretara āśraya tvam
nanu ca śāstrāt īśvara prāmāṇyam tat prāmāṇyāt ca śāstra prāmāṇyam iti syāt anyonya āśraya tvam usyate īśvara prāmāṇyasya anumānena siddha tvāt adoṣaḥ
etasmāt etat bhavati
kasmāt īśvara prakṛṣṭa sattva āśrayayoḥ niratiśaya jñāna utkarṣayoḥ kārya kāraṇa rūpe nitya tvāt etat bhavati sa tu sadā eva muktaḥ sadā eva īśvaraḥ iti
iti atra āha tat ca tasya aiśvaryam sāmya atiśaya vimuktam iti vakṣyamāṇa pramāṇa phalam
etad sūtra piṇḍa arthaḥ vā
atiśaya vimukta tām vyācaṣṭe na tāvat aiśvarya antareṇa ā tat atiśayyate
kutas yat eva aiśvarya antaram tat atiśayānam manyase tat eva te aiśvaryam mayā bhihitam
yatra eva aiśvarya antara atiśayi bhavati aiśvaryam saḥ eva īśvaraḥ iti yāvat
na ca tad samānam aiśvaryam asti
samān da dharma prakarṣa asaṃbhavāt
na hi ekasmin rājye dvayoḥ sabhavaḥ rājñoḥ
ekasya vā dve rājye
tathā pratipādayati tat dvayoḥ tulya tvam prasaktam
na hi ekasya anyataratra prākāmyam a bādhitvā anyatarasmin pravṛttiḥ upapadyate
dvayoḥ ca yugapad eka arthayoḥ ekasya prākāmyeṇa pravṛttiḥ eva na asti
prakāmite vastuni samāna prakarṣasya arthasya viruddha tvāt
yena ca samāna prakarṣa tā tasya tena eva sa bādhyate
te ca tat ca na vācā bādhanam itarasya rūpa atiśayāḥ āvṛtti atiśayāḥ ca viruddhyante
sāmānyāni tu atiśayaiḥ saha vartante iti vakṣyāmaḥ
tasmāt yasya sāmya atiśaya viproṣitam aiśvaryam saḥ īśvaraḥ iti pradhāna puruṣa vyatiriktaḥ pūruṣa viśeṣaḥ īśvaraḥ siddhaḥ
yathā pratijñātasya īśvarasya siddhau pramāṇam upanyasyate tatra niratiśayam sarvajña bījam
tatra tasmin yathā pratijñāta lakṣaṇe īśvare niratiśayam bhavitum arhati
kim tat iti yat idam avyabhicāri pratyakṣa anumāna jñānam atīta viṣayam anāgata viṣayam vartamāna kāla atīta ādi samuccaya viṣayam atīndriya viṣayam ca
atīndriyayoḥ atīta anāgatayoḥ saṃbhavāt iti ucyate
tat ca atīndriya grahaṇam trividham sūkṣma viṣayam vyavahita viṣayam viprakṛṣṭa viṣayam ca
alpam bahu iti
yathā prasiddham etat vivardhamānam sa atiśaya tvena sarvajña bījam yathā dhūma vijñānam agni vijñānasya
katham yatra prakarṣa kāṣṭhām pratipadyate
jñānasya jñātṛ āśraya tvāt yatra iti jñātā ucyate yasmin jñātari iti
sa sarvajñaḥ siddhaḥ
tathā śaktiḥ api sa atiśaya tvena vivardhamānā yatra kāṣṭhām prāpnoti sa sarvaśaktiḥ
tena jagat nirmāṇa sthāpana upasaṃhāra ādi kartṛ tva siddhiḥ
tathā aiśvaryasya api vardhamānasya yatra kāṣṭhā prāptiḥ sa paramaḥ īśvaraḥ
tatas ca aśakti ādi viparyaya doṣa abhāva siddhiḥ
atha api syāt ajñānasya api vivardhamānasya svabhāva siddhasya kāṣṭhā prāptasya tasmin īśvare siddhiḥ iti na jñāna virodhāt
na hi jñāna ajñānayoḥ viruddhayoḥ ekasmin abhisaṃyogaḥ sti
na hi jñāne prakarṣavati tatra ajñānam saṃbhavati
yatra hi jyotiḥ vivardhate tatra tamā u pakṛṣyate eva
viparyayaḥ pi iti ced tat ca na sati jyotiṣi tamasaḥ n upalambhāt
vidyamānam hi tamaḥ jyotiṣā tiraskriyate na kadācid vidyamānam jyotiḥ tamasā abhibhūyate
yat api jaladhara uparodhāt prāvṛṣi svera darśanam tat api dṛṣṭa vyavadhāna mātram
na punar prakāśaḥ eva torodhīyate tamaḥ vat
tasmāt nityā na yatra jñāna vivṛddhiḥ tatra ajñānasya bhāvaḥ samitari iva tamasaḥ

kim ca na ajñānasya avastu viṣaya tvāt vivṛddhiḥ saṃbhavati

ajñānasya hi vastu viṣaya tve jñāna tva prāptiḥ
yaḥ ca api ajñāna prakarṣaḥ iti na asau prakarṣaḥ
atyanta jñāna abhāva apekṣayā hi saḥ ucyate
ajñānasya prakarṣe hi sati ajñāna sahasrasya na jñānena ekena bādhaḥ syāt
tathā hi prati ajñānam bādhanam syāt
tasmāt nityāḥ na ajñānasya prakarṣaḥ sverūpeṇa
yasya hi sa atiśaya tvam tasya kāṣṭhā prāptiḥ dṛśyate
yathā phala ādi parimāṇānām ākāśa paryanta tā
tathā sarvajña bījam api parām kāṣṭhām prāptum arhati
samastam vyastam ca sarvam vastu jātam ekasya pratyakṣam jñeya tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat
jñāna viṣaya tvena puruṣa artha tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat eva
utpattimatī ca pṛthivī sāvayavatvāt ghaṭa ādi vat
niṣpāditam jagat tad upabhogya sthāna ādi racanā viśeṣavat tvāt prāsāda ādi vat
aneka prāṇi upabhoga vijñāna vat eka nirvartitā pṛthivī aneka prāṇa vat upabhogya tvāt brīhi yava ādi vat
aneka prayojana arthinā ekena nirmitā pṛthivī gṛha ādi vat eva
sarva prāṇi āśrayaḥ giri nadī samudāyaḥ tad nivāsa paribhoga yogya vijñāna vat eka kuśala utpāditaḥ prakṛta hetu nidarśanābhyām eva
aneka prāṇa bhāj prakāśa ādi sāmarthya jñānavatā ekena nirvartitaḥ savitā prakāśa ātmaka tvāt pradīpa ādi vat
niyata kālam āditya udaya astamaya ādi sañcaraṇam etat prayojana jñānavat eka prayuktam pratiniyata kāla tvāt kṛṣi ādi vat
budhimat ekaḥ īśvara prayuktā sūrya graha candra nakṣatra ādi pravṛttiḥ pravṛtteḥ duḥkha ātmaka tve sati niyata samaya tvāt dharma śiṣya bhṛtya ādi pravṛtti vat
candramasaḥ vṛddhi kṣayau tithi ādi kāla jñānavatā ekena prayuktau kāla paricchedaka tvāt ghaṭikāḥ harāḥ di vat
kala pariccheda jñānavatā ekena nirvartataḥ candramāḥ vṛddhi kṣaya yukta tvāt ghaṭikā ādi vat eva
buddhimat eka svāmikam jagat anyonya viruddha saṃhata aneka prāṇi nāyaka adhiṣṭhita bahu maṇḍala tvāt itthaṃjātīyaka eka rājyavat
sarvam etat sādhana sādhya vyāpāra avastham pratyakṣam kasyacid ekasya avāntara virodha anugrahavat tayā eka prayojana tvāt sāṃgrāma vastu vat
saṃhata tvāt kulāla ādi vastu vat
sā eva pratijñā
yugapad ca sarvam pratyakṣam anyonya saṃbandhāt prasiddha sambandha aneka artha vat
agnihotra ādi sādhana sādhanīye kasyacid pratyakṣe sādhya sādhana rūpa tvāt bhuji tṛpti vat
sarvāḥ śaktayaḥ kasyacid pratyakṣāḥ vastu tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat
a vā ntara prativbandha abhāve sarvam vastu jātam nairantaryeṇa kasyacid pratyakṣam śabda ādimat tvena sambandhāt drāghīyasīm iva śaṣkulīm bhakṣayataḥ śabda ādayaḥ
svatantra tayā kenacid ekena sarvam pratyakṣayaḥ upalabhyate jñeya tvena abhimata tvāt nāṭya vastu vat
apratibandhena kasyacid pratyakṣa upalabhyam sarvam sattve tve sati anyonya saṃbandhāt nāṭya saṃbandfi nartaka ādi vat
saṃsāra rahitaḥ sarvajñaḥ ajñāna abhāvāt mukta ātma vat


sarva artha grahaṇa samarthasya parame īśvara cittasya sarva vyāpinaḥ yugapt sarva viṣya yogi tvāt
evam sati samasta vastu grahaṇa abhāve kāraṇa abhā vā anu vā upapatiḥ
nā api mūrtimat pratibandhaḥ api ākāśa vat eva sarva viṣaya yoginaḥ api cittasya
viṣaya anāvasthānāt āvis bhāva tiras bhāva smṛti saṃkalpa anavasthita tva upapattiḥ
viṣaya ākāra tayā vṛttilābhāt arka prabhā vat
na hi citta sattvam tasya adharma ādi yogāt sarvagatasya sarva arthasya api sattvasya adharma ādi pratibandhaka niruddha svakīya pravṛtti mārga tvāt indriya ādi dvāra apekṣi tvam upapadyate
yathā apavaraka ādi āvaraṇa āvṛtaḥ pradīpaḥ tad āvaraṇa gata chidra dvāreṇa bahis prakāśayati
saḥ eva tu pradīpaḥ prabhinna apakaraka āvaraṇaḥ san an apekṣya tat tat chidra mārgam samantataḥ prakāśayati
tathā eva īśvara sattvam kleśa ādi āvaraṇa yoga abhāvāt asati viṣaya viśeṣa nirodhi kāraṇe yugapad aśeṣa artha grahaṇam
ca sva atilaṅghana anatilaṅghana ādi doṣa abhāvaḥ
sarvasya viṣaya tvāt sarvam ekaḥ īśvaram jagat paripālaka apekṣa sthāna ādi ādi aneka vastu viśeṣa tvāt prasiddha evaṃbhūta eka rājya vat
tathā niyata sthiti hetu aneka upakaraṇa tvāt anyonya abhibhavanīya prabhūtatara durga yukta aneka deśa tvāt abhaṅgura vyavastha śarīra bhedavat tvāt ca pratīta evaṃvidha eka rājya vat
aneka kartṛ bhoktṛ kriyā sādhana phala saṃbandha viśeṣa jñāna vat upadiṣṭāni varṇa āśrama ādi anuṣṭhānāni phala arthibhiḥ pratyavāya bhīubhiḥ taiḥ ca anuṣṭhīyamāna tvāt bhaiṣajya rasāyana ādi anuṣṭhāna vat
tathā tad upadeśāḥ parārtha tvāt upadeśa tvāt vidvat śradveya tvāt upadeśāt ṛte manuṣya an avagamya artha tvāt ca bhaiṣajya ādi upadeśa cat
śarīra indriyāṇi sarva tad prayojana vid eka nimitta kāraṇa abhinirvartitāni niyama kriyā sthiti hetu sādhana tvāt prāsāda gṛha dāruyantra ādi vat
niyata prayojana racanāvat tvāt ca tadvat eva
tathā indriyāṇi karaṇa tvāt vādī vṛkṣa ādāna ādi vat
tathā sarvam kārya niyata upādāna tvāt bhoktṛ artha tvāt bhoga sādhana tvāt ca ghaṭa ādi vat
utpattimat tve api ete hetavaḥ
evam madhyama parimāṇa tvāt aneka vināśa hetu saṃbandha yogya tvāt bhoka adhiṣṭhāna tvāt kriyā phala sādhana tat rūpa ādimat tvāt ca ādhīyamāna apacīyamāna āpūryamāṇa apanīyamāna dahyamāna abhidyamāna aneka deśa tvāt vinaśvarī pṛthivī
śarīra ādi vat aśvarāṇi pṛthivī ādi bhūtāni anyonya nāśaka śaktimat tvāt śastra puruṣa ādi vat
tathā eva virodhāt puruṣa viparīta tvāt ca utptti vināśa dharmakam ākāśam sākṣāt upakaraṇa tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat bāhya indriya grāhya guṇa āśraya tvāt ca
tasmāt nityāḥ niratiśaya śakti jñāna aiśvaryaḥ paramaḥ īśvaraḥ siddhaḥ
atra ucyate īśvara śabda arthaḥ sarvajñaḥ na bhavati prameya tva vastu tva śabda abhidheya tva ātma tva sādhana apekṣā upalabdhṛ tva ādibhyaḥ asmat ādi vat
īśvara śabdaḥ api niratiśaya jñāna yukta abhidhāyī na bhavati śabda tvāt ghaṭa ādi śabda vat

bhūta bhaviṣyat kālayoḥ api idānīm iva sarvajñasya an upalabdhāraḥ sarva prāṇinaḥ prāṇi tvāt asmat ādi vat
vādi antara paikalpitaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvaḥ īśvaraḥ ca na asti anupalabhyamāna tvāt śaśa viṣāṇa vat
tathā asarvajñaḥ nīśvaraḥ ca aśarīra tvāt muktātma vat
sa śarīraḥ ced dharma ādi apekṣa śarīra tvam tathā ca saṃsāri tvam asmat ādi vat eva
aśarīra tvam eva iti ced jagat kartṛ tva anugrāhaka tva ādi anupapattiḥ muktātma nidarśanena
viśiṣṭa paribhoga yogya jagat racanā viśeṣa upapattiḥ svabhāvāt eva kaṇṭaka tīkṣṇa tva kumuda kamala saṅkoca vikoca ādi vat
niśākara divākara tārakā ādi gamana āgamana ādi api svābhāvikam loha ayaskānta maṇi vat
atrā abhidhīyate svābhāvikī tāvat na bhavati pṛthivī adi racanā
dṛṣṭāntaḥ na eva tad sādhanasya vidyate
kaṇṭka ādīnām ca taikṣṇyam na svābhāvikam abhyupeyate
agni ādīnām iva ūṣṇi ādi svabhāvaḥ vastu dharma tvāt hetoḥ pṛthivī ādi racanā iti ced prāsāda ādi racanāyāḥ vastu dharma tvāt syāt anaikāntika tvam
atha svābhāvika tvāt iti ced asiddha tvam jagat racanāyāḥ dharma adharma phala upabhoga artha prayukta tva abhyupagamāt
kartṛ dharma adharma astitvam upariṣṭāt sādhayiṣyate
tasmāt pṛthivī ādi racanā svābhāvikī na bhavati prāṇi upabhoga artha tvāt prāsāda ādi racanā vat
candra ādi pravṛttiḥ na svābhāvikī pravṛtti tvāt asmat ādi pravṛtti vat
asmat ādi pravṛttiḥ na svābhāvikī iṭi ced na agni uṣṇa tva vat nitya tva prasaṅgāt
na hi agni uṣṇa tvam svābhāvikam sat niyatam nimittam ātma lābhāya kāṅkṣati dharmi sattā vyatirekeṇa
kriyā phala racanā ādīnām tu viśiṣṭa nimitta ākāṅkṣṇam ātma pratilambhāya iti na svābhāvika tvam
niyata nimitta kāṅkṣṇam api prāsāda ādi racanānām svabhāvaḥ iti ced astu tathāvisha svabhāva tvam
tathā api pṛthivī ādi racanāyāḥ niyata nimitta kāṅkṣṇa svabhāva tvam prāsāda ādi vat eva
tatas ca nāmni vipratipattiḥ na doṣāya iti pratijñā pratirūpa kāriṇī ca
anumānāni loka anumā āgama virodhāt apramāṇāni anumāna virodham tāvat sa atiśaya tva ādibhyaḥ brūmaḥ
āgama virodhan ca yaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva vid ekaḥ vaśī iti evamādibhyaḥ samācakṣmahe
samasta loka virodham ca api
sarve evāḥ na arogopālam saṃvyavaharamāṇāḥ satatam śiva nārāyaṇa ādi nāmnā praṇihita cetasaḥ pratiṣedhasu api saṃbhinna buddhiṣu akarṇīkṛta tad pratiṣedha viṣaya pallavāḥ parame īśvaram praṇatam ūrdhānaḥ kusuma anjali prabhṛtibhiḥ arcayanti
phalam ca api tatas eva prārthayante
atha ced brūyāt sarvajña abhāva pratipādibhiḥ asmad anumānaiḥ itara pratijñānām vridhaḥ iti atrā ucyate na etāni anumānāni
katham prathamam tāvat pratijñā iva duṣṭā
yadi tāvat īśvara śabda arthaḥ sarvajñaḥ na bhavati iti yuṣmad abhipretaḥ īśvaraḥ ucyeta tathā ca siddha sādhya tā syāt
atha asmad abhipretaḥ tathā api yuṣmākam asiddha viśeṣya tā bhavet
atha īśvara tvasya asarvajña tvam ucyate tathā api siddham sādhyate
tathā e abhyupagama virodhaḥ api
katham aiśvarya sarvajña bīja tvayoḥ vivardhamāna tvāt kāṣṭhā prāptiḥ parimāṇa vat evā abhyupagamanīyā
tathā kāṣṭhā prāpta aiśvarya sarvajña tva vācinau api īśvara sarvajña śavdau eṣitavyau
kāṣṭhā prāptiḥ ca niravadhika tvam
yathā parimāṇa ādīnām ātma ākāśa ādi ananta parimāṇa anta tvam
tathā ca anumāna abhyupagama sva vacana virodhāḥ syuḥ
kiñca anyat kāṣṭhā prāpte īśvara tvasya śabda arthasya parityāge śabda artha vādaḥ prāpnoti
na hi śabdaḥ parityakta abhidheya eka deśaḥ uccaritaḥ
atha parimāṇa ādeḥ api niravadhika niṣṭhatvam na iṣyate siddhānta virodhaḥ
ātma ākāśa ādīnām hi sarvagata tva abhāve madhyama parimāṇa tva anitya tva ādi doṣa prasaṅgāḥ ca
atha api ātmanaḥ sarvatra kārya darśanāt sarvagata tvam tatra api śakuni ādi ātmanām manuṣya gocara ākāśa ādi gata tvam kena vāryate
atha anumāna virodhāt na avadhāryate iti ced ātma ādīnām api prameya tva vastu tva dibhyaḥ pṛthivī ādi vat iti anumāna virodha udbhāvanā śakyate kartum vaktum
na ca tāvatā trā anumāna virodhi tvam anumāna abhāva prasaṅgāt
tathā anumāna abhāvaḥ eva iṣyate iti ced pratyakṣe api anāśvāsaḥ syāt
atha niścīyamāna buddhi utpatteḥ pratyakṣa pramāṇa tvam anumānasya api tarhi niścita buddhi samudhbhavāt astu prāmāṇyam
atha dṛṣṭa sambandha dhūma di viṣayam eva anumānam iti ced tatra api anumāna abhāvaḥ eva anagniḥ dhūmavān predeśaḥ pratyakṣa anupalbhyamāna agni sambandhe sati pradeśa tvāt agni śūnya upalabhyamāna pradeśa vat iti
atha pramāṇa antara saṃvāda dṛṣṭa sambandha viṣaye numānasya anumāna tvam ucyate pratyakṣam api pramāṇa antara saṃvādāt pramāṇam bhavet pramāṇa tvāt anumāna vat eva
apramāṇam syāt pramāṇa antara saṃvāda abhāvāt sāmānyatodṛṣṭa ādi vat iti
tasmāt nityāḥ na sāmānyatodṛṣṭasya pramāṇa tvam niścita buddhi tvāt bādhitum śakyam
kim ca sāmānyatodṛṣṭasya māna tvam anabhyupagacchataḥ sva śarīra maraṇa sambandha lakṣaṇasya anupalabdha pūrva tvāt sarpa ādibhyaḥ bhaya anupapattiḥ
vyādhi pratīkārāya cikitsā ādi prayogaḥ ghaṭeta
maraṇa śaṅkā kāraṇa abhāvāt
tathā upalambha abhāvāt ātma śarīrasya aja tvam
hāna upādāna niyoga abhāvaḥ ca syāt

kim ca anyat īśvara sarvajña tvasya pratiṣiddhyamāna tvāt sattva abhyupagamaḥ padārthasya pratiṣedha asambhabāt
na hi kevalaḥ na iti na prayujyate
īśvaraḥ sarvajñaḥ naḥ bhavati iti ucyate
tatra kvacid sarvajña tvam abhyupagatam bhavati
tat yathā śaśasya viṣāṇam na asti vandhyāyāḥ sutaḥ na asti kusumam ākāśasya na asti iti kvacid vidyamānānām eva viṣāṇa suta kusuma ādīnām śaśa ādi saṃbandhena pratiṣedhaḥ tadvat iha api syāt
kim ca īśvaraḥ sarvajñaḥ na bhavati iti īśvara śabda artha sarvajñatva sambandha pratiṣedha ādinā īśvarāt anyasya sarvajñatva abhyupagamaḥ
sambandhinau an abhyupagamya sambandha pratiṣedhaḥ hi na śakyaḥ kartum
saḥ eṣa yuktaḥ sambandhaḥ pratiṣidhyate ayuktaḥ ca abhyupagamyate
tat pariśrama mātram
īśvara sarvajñayoḥ prasiddha padārthayoḥ apratiṣedhāt
na hi ananta parimāṇam ākāśam na bhavati iti ākāśasya prasiddham ananta parimāṇa tvam pratiṣidhya aprasiddha ananta parimāṇa tveṣu ghaṭa ādiṣu tat vyavasthāpayitum yuktam
atha sambandhinau eva īśvara sarvajña rve pratiṣidhyate sva vacana virodhinī pratijñā syāt
īśvara sarvajja tvayoḥ īśvara sarvajña śabda artha tva abhyupagamāt
na hi bhavati agniḥ agni śabda arthaḥ na bhavati iti
atha aprasiddha padārthau īśvara sarvajña śabdau tathā api tad artha pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ
aprasiddhasya arthasya prāpti abhāvāt
na hi kiṃcid a prasiddham etat śikhare meṣakuṭumbinīm pratiseddhum arhati
kim ca śabda upādāna ānarthakyam ca
aprasiddha padārtha tvāt
atha prasiddha arthayoḥ īśvara sarvajña śabadayoḥ niravadhikaḥ īśvara sarvajña tvābhyām aprasiddhābhyām gaganasya iva kusumaiḥ saṃbandhaḥ kaiḥ cit kalpitaḥ sa pratiṣidhyeta tathā api a hi upeta artha pratiṣedhāt sva vacana virodhinī eva pratijñā syāt
sa atiśaya niratiśaya anekaḥ īśvara sarvajña vyaktimat sāmānyayoḥ īśvara sarvajña śabda artha tvena abhyupagamāt
prasiddham hi loke īśvara sarvajña śabdayoḥ utkarṣa apakarṣa yukta aneka vyakti viṣaya buddhi utpādaka tvam
na hi grāma adhipatiḥ īśvaraḥ iti dvi tri grāma viṣaya adhipatayaḥ uttarottare īśvarāḥ na bhavanti
yaḥ vā kuṭumba adhipatiḥ īśvaraḥ na bhavati sarvaiḥ ca asau ānanda mahā udanvat taraṅgāyamāṇaḥ arthavān īśvara śabdaḥ
tathā vaiyākaraṇaḥ sarvajñaḥ iti ukte na adhika vijñāna yuktaḥ na bhavati
niravadhikau sāvadhikau vā īśvara sarvajñau īśvara sarvajña cabdayoḥ arthau
atas tad pratiṣedhāt abhyupagama virodhinī pratijñā syāt ātma ākāśa ādīnām mahat tvasya mahat śabda artha tva pratiṣedha vat
atha īśvara sarvajñau niravadhikau na staḥ anupalabhyamāna tvāt anīśvara dvitīya śiraḥ vat iti ucyeta tathā api śabda artha abhyupagamāt abhyupagama virodhinī pratijñā
sātiśaya tva ādibhiḥ aiśvarya sarvajñatva bīja ādi liṅgaiḥ nirabadhikaḥ īśvara sarvajñatvayoḥ upalabhyamāna tvāt niravadhika parimāṇa tva vat iti asiddhiḥ anupalabdheḥ
atha a viśeṣyaḥ eva īśvara śabda arthaḥ sarvajñaḥ na bhavati iti ucyeta vastu tva ādi hetubhiḥ asmad ādi vat iti tadā sarva pramāṇa virodhinī pratijñā syāt
prasiddhe īśvara śabda arthasya prākṛta sarvajña tvasya sarva pramāṇa siddha tvāt
yathā īśvara śabda arthaḥ sarvajñena bhavati prameya tva ādibhiḥ hetubhiḥ ghaṭa ādi vat iti ukte yat brūyāt tat eva aham vakṣyāmi
iha sarvajña śūnyam jagat
kālaḥ vā diśaḥ ākāśam vā prāṇimat deśaḥ vā prāṇinaḥ vā sarve sarvajña śūnyāḥ
pramāṇāni vā sarvajña a viṣayāṇi
pramātāraḥ vā sarvajñasya apratipattaraḥ iti evaṃjātīyāsu pratijñāsu niravadhike īśvare sarvajñe vā pratiṣidhyamāne prasiddhe īśvara sarvajña śabda artha abhyupagama virodhāḥ pratijñā doṣāḥ vacanīyāḥ
nanu ca vandhyā sutaḥ na asti iti tat śūnyam jagat kālaḥ vā iti pratijñāyamāne yathā ukta pratijñā doṣa prāptiḥ bhavet na eṣa doṣaḥ vandhyā suta sattā lakṣaṇasya pratiṣeddha vayasya vākya arthasya īśvara sarvajña śabda artha vat aprasiddha tvāt kevala śabda prāpita sannidhāna buddhi mātra pratipanne padārtha padārthe pratiṣedha vyāpāraḥ sti iti vandhyā suta astitvasya vā nāstitvasya na abhyupagamaḥ sti
tatas na abhyupagata pratiṣedha doṣaḥ
nanu ca īśvaraḥ sarvajñaḥ na bhavati iti atra api buddhimātram prāpyamāṇam pratiṣidhyate na kvacid api prāpnuvat vastu na pratiṣeddham śakyate pratihastinā iva hastī
yadi ca nañā vastu nirākariṣyate nac mātreṇa aiśvara vādi pakṣa tvam api pakṣe api nirākariṣyate atas tasmāt iha api busshi mātra pratiṣedhaḥ iti na abhyupagata pratiṣedhaḥ pratiñā doṣaḥ
satyam evam
kim tu asti viśeṣaḥ
pramāṇa siddha vastu viṣayā buddhiḥ vastu antare kāla viśeṣe vā pratiṣidhyate vastu sāmānyāt prāpnuvatī yathā ghaṭaḥ na asti iti
kvacid vinā api arthena buddhiḥ eva śabda pratyupanīta sannidhānā kalpita vastu antarā pratiṣidhyate
yathā vandhyā sutaḥ na asti iti
yatra tu pramāṇa antara siddha vastu pratiṣedhaḥ tatra api sti abhyupagata artha pratiṣedha doṣaḥ
yathā īśvara śabda arthaḥ sarvajñaḥ na bhavati iti
īśvara sarvajña śabdayoḥ abhivardhamānaḥ īśvara sarvajña vyakti anugata sāmānya vacana tvena liṅgena niravadhikaḥ īśvara sarvajña sattva avadyoti tvam siddham eva
mahat bahu sarva ananta parimāṇa ādi śabdavat
yathā eva ete mahat ādi śabdāḥ prasiddha sātiśaya mahat ādi anugata sāmānya artha abhidhāyinaḥ santaḥ niravadhika mahat bahu sarva ananta parimāṇa vyaktīnām astitva avadyotana liṅgāḥ bhavanti
mahat ādi sāmānyānām sa atiśaya vyakti anugatānām śakti tvāt
na hi santam vyāpyam artham tad vyāpakaḥ san arthaḥ na vyāpnoti iti
niravadhikāt tu paraḥ vyāpyaḥ na asti iti vyāpakasya sāmānyasya kṣayaḥ vyāpya viṣaya tvena eva prasiddha tvāt tatra
tasmāt pramāṇa siddha tvāt īśvara sarvajña śabda arthyoḥ abhāvam sādhayataḥ bhyupagata artha pratiṣedhaḥ eva iti duṣṭā pratijñā
na ca īśvara sarvajña śabdayoḥ atadartha tvam anya artha tvam vā kartum vaktum śakyate
tathā śakti jñāna aiśvaryāṇām prati puruṣam samuccitānām sa atiśayānām niravadhikam tattvam atas na an unmattaḥ pratiṣeddhum utsametāḥ iti anumāna virodhi tvam pratijñāyāḥ
kim ca anyat pari kalpitasya īśvarasya pratiṣedham kuruvantaḥ pratyakṣa para citta aniṣṭāḥ prāpnuvanti
para vākyāt iti ced na sa atiśaya tva ādi sarvajña sādhaka liṅga pratipādaka vat aviśiṣṭa tvāt para vākyasya
tādṛśa vākya artha pratiṣedhe ca abhyupgata pratiṣedhaḥ pūrvavat eva anumāna virodhaḥ ca
kim ca prameya tva ādi hetūnām api asiddha tvam
kutas asmābhiḥ niratiśaya jñāna aiśvarya viśiṣṭa tvasya abhyupagata tvāt
atha svayam api tād ṛṛśam abhyupagacchet tadā sarvajña siddhiḥ abhyupgata tvāt
kim ca anyat abhyupagata tādṛś pratiṣedhe yathā ghaṭaḥ na bhavati vastu tvāt paṭa vat iti evam iha api syāt
kim ca niravadhikasya anabhyupagame prameya tva ādīnām a pakṣa dharma tvam āśraya asiddha tvam ca
tad abyupagame hi kim sādhyam
yaḥ hi tṛptavantam brūyāt mā
atrātsīḥ iti kim tena kṛatam syāt
atha api syāt niravadhikam īśvaram abhisandhāya tasya sarvajña tvam niṣedhāmi iti
na etat api yuktam sarvajñatvasya api niravadhika tvāt
api ca sātiśaya aiśvarya sarvajña tvayoḥ utkarṣa anutkarṣa viṣaya tvena vyabhicārāt na īśvara sarvajña śabda mukhya abhidheya tvam
yathā mahat ādayaḥ śabdāḥ vyabhicarita mahat tva ādiṣu ghaṭa ādiṣu amukhyāḥ na ākāśa ādiṣu tathā eva atra api niratiśayam aiśvaryam sarvajña tvam ca avyabhicāri iti saḥ eva mukhyaḥ śabda arthaḥ
na ca mukhya nirākaraṇam sādhimānam ṛcchati
kim ca yathā bhavatā anumāna āgama prasiddha īśvarasya prameya tva ādi dharma vikalpa tayā sarvajña tvam nirākriyate tathā eva prameya tva ādhibhiḥ acetana tvam api ghaṭa ādi vat eva prāpnuyāt
avirodhāt
yathā prameya tvam a sarvajña tvena vyāptam evam acetana tva ādibhiḥ api
pratyakṣa virodhaḥ iti ced iha api anumāna āgama virodham kim kaṭākṣeṇa api nā īkṣase
nā api ca prameya tvāt dharma sāmānyena sapakṣe vipakṣe vā kiñcid kvacid adhyāropayitum śakyam
vastu viṣaye sarvatra prameya tva ādīnām astitvāt
na mati mohana arthaḥ prameya tva ādi upanyāsaḥ
atha ātma tvāt iti ced muktātma vat ajña tva prasaṅgaḥ syāt bhavat īśvarāṇām
pratyakṣa ādi virodhaḥ iti ced atra api anumāna ādi virodhaḥ pūrvavat eva
bhūta bhaviṣyat kālayoḥ api īśvarasya anupalabdhāraḥ iti idānīntana īśvarāṇām upalabdhṛbhiḥ anaikāntikam prāṇi tvāt ityādi
kim ca atīta nāgata kālayoḥ api sātiśaya tva ādi liṅaiḥ upalabdhavantaḥ upalapsyamānāḥ ca prāṇinaḥ pramāṇa kuśalāḥ pramāṇa kuśala tvāt asmat ādi vat
atha aśarīra tvāt asarvajñaḥ mukta ākāśa ādi vat iti ced na sa śarīra tvāt
vyakta avyaktam hi sarva śarīram sa śarīra tvāt anitya īśvara tvam dharma ādi apekṣa tvāt iti ukta tvāt iti ced na aśarīra tvāt
sa śarīra aśarīra tva virodhaḥ iti ced na mukta mucyamāna eka ātmanaḥ
aśarīra tva sa śarīra tva darśanāt
tatra bhinna kāla tvāt avirodhaḥ iti ced na atra api bhinna kāla abhyupagamāt
kim ca yugapad īśvara tvāt eva dvaya sambhavaḥ
sa karaṇa tā a karaṇa tā
api īśvara tvāt eva yuktā

na hi karma śeṣa tve śruti liṅga ādīnām anyatamat api pramāṇam asti
svādhyāya vidhi parigrahāt darśa pūrṇamāsa ādi śeṣaḥ iti ced na jyotiṣṭoma ādi vat vidhi antarasya bhāvāt

atha evam api upāsanā vidhi śeṣa tvāt stutiḥ evā iti ced na atyantam asatā stutiḥ asti
na hi vāyuḥ vai kṣepiṣṭhāḥ devatāḥ iti vāyoḥ a kṣepiṣṭa tvam
kvacid asatā
api stuti ādi sambhavaḥ iti ced na anumāna siddhasya iha upādānāt
atha sarva kārya karaṇa yogāt īśvarasya sarva prāṇi sukha duḥkha ādi saṃbandhaḥ iti ced na nimitta bhedāt
dharma ādi nimittaḥ saṃsāriṇām śarīra ādi sambandhaḥ
dharma ādi nimi ttānām ttaḥ duḥkha ādi yogaḥ
na īśvarasya dharma ādayaḥ
niratiśaya aiśvarya ādi hetu tvāt śarīra ādi kārya karaṇa saṃbandhasya
yathā graha tad āviṣṭayoḥ
atha cakṣuḥ ādi karaṇa tvāt asmat ādi vat sarva anupalabdhiḥ iti ced na sarva viṣaya grahaṇa samarthānām pratibandha kāraṇa abhāvāt
sarvagatānām hi karaṇānām a dharma ādi saṃvaraṇena sva viṣaya saṅgocaḥ kriyate
yasya punar āvaraṇam dharma ādi na vidyate tasya tad abhāvāt aśeṣa sva viṣaya grahaṇāni karaṇāni iti na duṣyati
atha vā sarva prāṇi karaṇaiḥ īśvaraḥ pṛthak ātmanaḥ karaṇa abhāve
api āveśa grahaḥ iva sarvam anubhavati
na ca prāṇi śūnyaḥ viṣayaḥ kaścid vidyate yad pṛthivyām tiṣṭhan
yaḥ
apsu tiṣṭhan iti evamādi śruteḥ antaryāmi nāmnaḥ īśvarasya sarveṣu avasthita tva śravaṇāt
api vā prakṛṣṭam eva sa rvam ttvam niryān atiśāyita śakti jñāna īśvara tva dharmakam sarvagata tvāt ākāśa vat sarva yogi sarva artha tvāt sarva viṣaya prakāśakam dharma adharma ādi viprayogāt apratibandha śaktikam ca iti akāya anindriya tva pakṣe
api īśvara sarvajña tva siddhiḥ
cakṣuḥ ādi apekṣam eva cittasya rūpa ādi pratilambha sāmarthyam iti ced na aiśvarya dharma ādi abhāvābhyām parihṛta tvāt
api ca cakṣuḥ grāhyasya api cakṣuṣā agrahaṇam loke dṛśyate
cakṣuḥ grāhyam sat sarvam tamaḥ sat nimīlita locanaiḥ api svastha antaḥkaraṇaiḥ upalabhyate
tat eva ca andhatamasam viṣphārita nayanaiḥ api anya gata cittaiḥ nā eva gṛhyate
yathā gṛhyamāṇaḥ eva ākāśe prakāśaḥ
atha api prakāśa abhāva mātram eva tamaḥ na vastu iti brūyāt tat ca na abhāvasya vastu tirodhāna sāmarthya abhāvāt
atha grahaṇa nimittasya prakāśasya abhāvāt eva ghaṭa ādi agrahaṇam na vastu tirodhāyakam tamaḥ iti bruvīta na cakṣuṣaḥ prakāśaka tvāt prakāśa sāhāyaka apekṣā anupapattiḥ
asati bhinna jātīye vastuni vastūnām tirodhātṛṇi tatra yā ca yāvatī ca mātrā prakāśaka tvāt cakṣuṣā prakāśyeta
na hi pradīpaḥ pradīpa antara dvaitīyaka apekṣaḥ prakāśayati
kim ca anyat cakṣuṣaḥ prakāśa antara sahāya tva apekṣa tāyām ca niśāyām api tārādhipati prakāśa dvitīyena cakṣuṣā divase iva rūpa ādi grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ tirodhāna asya asati nimitte
kim ca anyat abhāvaḥ ced tamaḥ candra bhāsu niśāyām bhā bhava ntīṣu tamasā mandena na pravartitavyam
sarva ātmanā eva hi tena vinaśanīyam
bhāsām bhāvāt
bhāsām tu vastu tvāt manda tva pāṭava ādi viśeṣaḥ ghaṭate na bhāvasya abhāvasya nirviśeṣa tvāt
kim ca sahāya abhāvāt cakṣuṣaḥ upalabdhi sāmarthya abhāvāt agrahaṇam iti etat api vyabhicarati
yathā sati api viduyllatā prakāśe tīvratare vidyut latā vilāse ca kim tad dṛṣṭiḥ nā upalabhate
na hi shāyake dṛṣṭa cakita tvena agrahaṇam virodha abhāvāt yuktam
kiñca cikitsā śāstre chāyā madhura śītalā iti ucyate
na hi avastunaḥ madhura śītala tvam
tathā
na abhāvasya pathya apathya tvam brūyuḥ
pradīpāt chāyā upalabdheḥ ca
abhāvaḥ ced tamaḥ pradīpa prabhā maṇḍale pradīpāt chāyā katham bhavet
vastu tve
api virodhāt ayuktam iti ced na viṣa sarpayoḥ iva saṃbhavāt
yathā prāṇi viyoga karam api viṣam pannaga prāṇa viyogāya na paryāpnoti tathā pradīpa tad chāyayoḥ api
tasmāt vastu tamaḥ prakarṣa apakarṣavat tvāt prabhā vat
virodhi dravya apaneya tvāt ca ghaṭa vat upalabdhṛ vyavadhāna kara tvāt ca bhitti vat iti
itas c ā indriya nirapekṣam api antaḥkaraṇam indriya viṣaya grahaṇāya samartham
pihita karṇa vivarasya ghoṣa upalambhāt
na ca pihita karṇa saṃpuṭasya śrotra antaram anumātum śakyam
badhirasya api pihita śrotra puṭasya tad agrahaṇāt
kiñca pratijñā jñānena api rūpa ādi grahaṇam indriya nirapekṣam dṛśyate
kiñca anyat smṛteḥ ca anupapattiḥ syāt indriya nirapekṣasya cittasya sa atiśaya grahaṇa sāmarthye
api
spaṣṭāḥ ca smṛtayaḥ svāpnāḥ rūpa ādi viṣayāḥ
yadi cakṣuḥ ādi antar akaraṇābhyām samanvitābhyām rūpa grahaṇam pūrvam api nirvartiṣyate svapna ādau api samuccitābhyām eva paryagrahīṣyata
na ca civam asti
sukha ādi grahaṇe svātantryam cittasya sarva prasiddham

iti
atha ucyate indriyāṇām āloka apekṣā vat antar akaraṇam api indriya sāhāyaka apekṣam eva grāhakam iti tat na vyabhicārāt
tātriñcarāṇām vibhinna vyāloka dvaitīyakena divasaḥ iva rūpa grahaṇam
sati api prakāśe na rūpasya grahaṇam ulūka ādibhiḥ dine
kiñca sādhana apekṣasya vijñāna sādhanāt ṛte
api tulā ādau darśana mātreṇa eva suvarṇa ādi parimāṇa jñānam dṛśyate
atha ced brūyāt ānarthakyam cakṣuḥ ādīnām iti sa vaktavyaḥ tulā ādi vat eva anyatra arthavat tvam indriyāṇām iti
yathā eva tulā ādi viṣaya vaimalya prakarṣātu puruṣasya vinā api tulā ādi sādhanena darśana mātrāt eva kanaka ādi vastu pariccheda kauśalam tathā eva antaḥkaraṇasya an apekṣita cakṣuḥ ādi sāhāyakasya api vaimalya prakarṣāt rūpa ādi grahaṇa sāmarthyam na vihanyate
nā api hi aneka nirvartanīyam kriyā jātam ekena nā abhinirvartyate
dṛśyante ca bahubhiḥ uttolyamānam śilā ādikam advitīyāḥ hasti puruṣa ādayaḥ kecid uttolayantaḥ
tathā eva indriya sahāyena anyeṣām antaḥkaraṇena gṛhyamāṇāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ parameśvara citta sattvena an ākalita cakṣuḥ ādi parispandena kevalena eva gṛhyante
kāṣṭhā gata tvāt vaimalya śakya aiśvarya prakarṣasya
saṃsāriṇām tatas nikṛṣṭa tvāt avidyā ādi malena aiśvarya śakti jñāna ādīnām indriya sahakāri tva apekṣi tvam antar akaraṇasya
śilā ādi samuttolane iva hīna balānām
ye ṣām punar saṃsāriṇaḥ eva santaḥ īśvarībhavanti buddha ṛṣabha ādayaḥ teṣām niratiśaya śakti jñāna aiśvarya anupapattiḥ
kāla paricchedya tvāt
abhyupagacchnati ca kāla paricchedanīyakam teṣām
na asmat īśvarasya kāla paricchedya tā
tad kālaiḥ tad ādya kālaiḥ ca buddha ādibhiḥ aparijñāta aiśvarya ādi sātiśaya tvāt liṅgaiḥ anumeyaḥ eva asau
na amuṣmin kāle utpannaḥ utpadyate utpatsyamānaḥ iti tridhā kaiścid anumīyate
niratiśaya tva virodhaḥ hi tathā syāt
tasmāt buddha ādīnām siddhi apekṣa tvāt pūrva buddhānām kāla dhikya prāpteḥ uttara kāla buddhasi api na niratiśaya śakya aiśvarya jñāna tvam
viruddham
atha tulya śakti jñāna aiśvaryāṇām eva teṣām samāna rājya rājānām iva asamāna kāla tvam iti brūyāt tathā api buddha antara kālasya vyāpti abhilāṣa vighātāt niratiśaya aiśvarya ādi abhāvaḥ
abhilaṣati hi kaścid buddha antaram vaśīkartum tad viṣayam ca vyāptum
aniyata tvāt icchāyāḥ
buddha antara avaśikaraṇe ca sarva vaśitvam
atha ced ucyeta buddha antarasya an anugrāhya tvāt rāga ādi abhāvāt ca tad viṣaya vyāptau anabhilāṣaḥ iti atas ṛcyate yathā eva prāpta buddhatvasya kaṃcid kālam avasthānam abhilāṣa pūrvaka tathā buddha antara kāla avasthāna abhilāṣeṇa avaśyam bhavitavyam
anugrāhya prāṇi antara bhāvāt ca kāla antara avasthāna abhilāṣeṇa yuktam bhavitum
na ca bhaviṣyatā buddhena sarve prāṇabhṛtaḥ
anugrahīpyante
buddhatvasya ca duḥkha ādi ātmaka tve
api prāṇi anugraha artha tvāt buddha sthiteḥ kāla antara avasthāna icchayā
siddheḥ ca prāk avidyā ādi parāmarśāt buddha sva rūpasya ca duḥkha śūnya ādi ātmaka tvasya taiḥ abhyupeta tvāt buddha ṛṣabha ādi anya tīrtha karaṇāt karāt niratiśaya śakti jñāna aiśvarya anupapattiḥ
kāla anavacchedāt tu nā ete doṣāḥ asmat īśvare kramante
śakti jñāna aiśvaryāṇām tu niravadhika tva anumānāt sātiśaya tva anavasthita tva ādi doṣaḥ na ātma ākāśa ādīnām iva atiśaṅkanīyaḥ
tathā ca darśayati sāmānya mātra upasaṃhāre kṛta upakṣayam anumānam iti
niratiśaya śakti jñāna aiśvarya yukta puruṣa viśeṣa sattva sāmānya mātra upasaṃhāre kṛta upakṣayam kṛtaḥ upakṣayaḥ yasya anumānasya tat kṛta upakṣayam sa atiśaya tvāt iti
tat uktam anumāne yatra prāptiḥ tatra gati mātram iti
tasmāt aneśvara saṃjñā guṇa ādi viśeṣāṇām satām api pratipādane samartham
sāmānya mātra upasaṃhāra paratvāt
tat etat uktam bhavati
tadā evam satām api guṇānām sāmānya pratipādana kṛta kṣaya tvāt na pratipādakam anumāna kim aṅga punar atyanta asambhāvyamāna sannidhīnām anumeya dharma viruddhānām aśaya jñāna dharma adharma anaiśvarya ādānām sic na tat pratyāyakam iti
atas eva ca viruddha pratisādhana anupapattiḥ
sarvajña astitva anumāna vat prathamam tad abhāva pratipādaka anumāna apravṛtteḥ
na hi anumānasya parokti udīkṣā dharma tvam asti
na hi dhūma darśanena agni anumāne vaktṛ antara uktiḥ udīkṣyate
na ca svayam eva sarvajña astitvam nāstitvam vā buddhi prati pūrvam āśaṅkyate
ghaṭa ādi vat sarvajña sadbhāvasya svayam anabhyupagamāt
na hi anirdhārita śaśa svarūpaḥ śaśe viṣāṇam asti na asti iti kaścid āśaṅkate
para vākyāt pratipādya āśaṅkate iti ced pareṇa api katham aprasiddha īśvara sadbhāvena āśaṅkitam iti vaktavyam
atha parasya bhrāntiḥ iti ced na sāmānya anupalambhe bhrānti kāraṇam asti
na hi śukitkāyām pika bhramaḥ kasyacid upajāyate
tasmāt āha saṃjñā ādi viśeṣa pratipattiḥ āgamataḥ paryanveṣyāḥ iti
veda itihāsa purāṇa yoga dharma śāstra ādi āgamataḥ paryanveṣyā
tasya ātma anugraha abhāve
api tasya ātma artham avāptavya abhāvāt bhūtānām ca avidyā paṅka nimagnānām saṃsāra sāgara uttaraṇa upāya plava upadeśi antarasya abhāvāt tad anugrahaḥ prayojanam
jñāna dharma upadeśena ye
an anya śaraṇāḥ tasmin sarva ātmanā nivedita ātmānaḥ tān kalpa pralaya mahāpralayeṣu īśvara anugṛhīta āgama jñāna viśeṣeṣu ācāryeṣu pralīneṣu punar punar jāta kāruṇya amṛtaḥ san uddhariṣāmi iti pravartate iti vākyaśeṣaḥ
tathā ca uktam ādi vidvān iti ādau vidvān ādi vidvān rajaḥ tamobhyām anabhibhūta jñānaḥ iti arthaḥ
jñāna dharma ādi vā tatas ādīyate iti ādiḥ ādiḥ ca asau vidvān ca ādi vidvān nirmāṇa cittam saṃkalpa mātra nirmitam yogi cittam āveśa graha vat upadeśana artham adhiṣṭhāya bhagavān parama ṛṣiḥ parama darśanaḥ iti arthaḥ
parama tvam ca āgamataḥ
darśana arthasya vā gati arthasya vā dhātoḥ ṛṣeḥ grahaṇam
parama ṛṣiḥ īśvaraḥ eva kapila nārāyaṇa ādi saṃjñaḥ āsuraye provāca iti
tasmāt pradhāna puruṣa vyatiriktaḥ sarva prāṇi bhāva karma phala parisphuraṇa jñānāt tad anugraha kāraṇam īśvaraḥ siddhaḥ
saprakṛṣṭa sattva dhana upādāne īśvaraḥ katham kartā
katham ca anugṛhṇāti
iti evam adi na codayitavyam
āgamataḥ paryanveṣyāḥ iti ukta tvāt
anumānasya ca tad viṣayasya anupapattiḥ viśeṣa saṃbandha agrahaṇāt iti
saḥ yathā ukta rūpaḥ parameśvaraḥ pūrveṣām api gurūṇām abhyudaya niḥśreyasa sarva sādhana sādhya saṃbandha upadeśinām guruḥ teṣām api jñāna upadeśasya kartā iti arthaḥ
tad udbhava tvāt sarva jñānānām
yathā jvalana lavaṇa jaladhi samudbhavāḥ viṣphuliṅga lavalṇa kaṇāḥ
tasya ca ādi vidvas tām avocāma
atīta anāgata pratyupādīyamāna tva viśiṣṭena kālena anye guravaḥ
avacchidyante
sa tu īśvaraḥ sarvadā mukta īśvara tvena taiḥ api asmābhiḥ iva anumeyaḥ
kasmāt punar tasya vastu tve guru tva sāmānye ca sati na avacchedakaḥ kālaḥ iti ced āha yatra avaccheda arthaḥ kālaḥ na upāvartate iti
yasmin īśvare viṣaye avaccheda arthaḥ prastha ādi vat pariccheda karaḥ na upāvartate na paricchedaka tvena īśvaram viṣayīkaroti sarva pariṇāmi vastu avaccheda karaḥ
api san
nanu ca īśvara prakṛṣṭa sattvasya pradhāna kārya tvāt pradhāna kāryasya ca kāla avaccedya tvāt kasmāt tat sattvam na avacchidyate puruṣa svarūpam hi sarveṣām eva kāla anavacchedyam iti na āśaṅkanīyam mapariṇāmi tvāt puruṣasya
atha manyethāḥ tantra antara prasiddha īśvara vat sattva nirapekṣaḥ īśvaraḥ iti tat ayuktam
atha api manvīthāḥ īśvara sattvāt pravṛttam eva kāryam avacchinatti kālaḥ na īśvara sattvam iti tat api ayuktam vyaktasya paricchedya tvāt
vyaktam ca īśvara sattvam
atha api abhisandadhīthāḥ pradhāna avastham eva īśvara sattvam iti tat anupapannam jñāna anupapatteḥ
atha api pratipadyethāḥ satkārya abhyupagamāt bīja phala vat larī kusuma ādi vat jñāna ādīnām pradhāna avasthā yat sattvam eva iti tat ca na sādhu vyavahāra yogya tvāt
sarveṣām ca tathā sati anavacchedya tvam jñāna ādi sattā mātra sambandha aviśeṣāt
atha api bruvīthāḥ vyakta tve sati api kāryāṇām kasyacid paricchedya tvam kālīnām kasyacid na iti tat ca na nyāya virodhāt
atha api pratyavatiṣṭheyāḥ īśvara sattvasya kāla paricchedya tvam āgama siddham iti tat ca na avadyotaka tvāt āgamasya
atha api ācakṣithāḥ vidyamānasya eva kāla a paricchedya tvasya ajñātasya avadyotakaḥ āgamaḥ iti tat ca api na nirodha ādi samanuṣṭhāna nimitta tvāt kālāḥ na vat hedyaḥ vaimalyāt an avaddhdyaḥ ca iti viruddham syāt
atrā ucyate īśvara sattva vaimalya prakarṣa apekṣa tvāt kāla anavacchedya tvasya adoṣaḥ
yathā anyeṣām gurūṇām yoga dharma di samanuṣṭhāna nimitta tvāt kāla anavacchedyaḥ vaimalya prakarṣaḥ tathā na bhagavataḥ
katham sarvadā tyanta tirobhūta rajaḥ tamaḥ tvāt an apekṣita dharma ādi nimittam sakala artha avadyota karam kāla anavacchedyam sattva sva rūpa vat bhagavat sattve jñānam
tathā tat kāryam api utkarṣaḥ kālena na avacchedyate
yathā ca agniḥ uṣṇa prakāśau agnau kāla an avacchdyau tathā bhagavat sattvasya vaimalya jñāna prakarṣāḥ tad sattve kāla an avacchdya tām upayānti iti etat apekṣayā abhihitam yatra avaccheda arthaḥ kālaḥ na upāvartate iti
na tu akārya apekṣayā hi ucyate
guru tvam hi na avadhimat
tat eva āha yathā asya sargasya ādau jñāna vaimalya prakarṣa gatyā siddhaḥ sarga ādi janmanām anumeya tayā siddhiḥ āgamataḥ ca ajñāyi tathā tikrānta sarga ādiṣu api tad kāla janmanām tatas prāktanānām api siddhiḥ
tathā bhaviṣyat kāle api anumāna āgamābhyām avagamyate
asya ca sūtrasya idam prayojanam yathā dṛṣṭāḥ guravaḥ jñāna dharma ādi updeśi tvāt ananya śaraṇaiḥ upāsyante tathā bhagavān ayam api sarva gurūṇām api guru tvāt tatas api viśeṣeṇa nārāyaṇa ādi nāmā sva hṛdayena aniśam dhārayitavayaḥ iti

yat api tasya bhagavataḥ bhigamana ādi lakṣaṇam ārādhanam ajasram ananya citta tayā abhipreyate tat api na pratiṣidhyate śruti smṛtyoḥ īśvara praṇidhānasya prasiddha tvāt
yathā dṛṣṭa guravaḥ upāsanena abhimukhīkṛtāḥ tad upāsana parān anugṛhṇanti tathā yam parama guruḥ api abhidhyāna mātreṇa anugraham karoti
tathā ca śrutiḥ yasya deve parā bhaktiḥ yathā deve tathā gurau
tasya ete kathitāḥ hi arthāḥ prakāśante mahā ātmanaḥ
iti
smṛtiḥ api mad karma kṛt mad paramaḥ mad bhaktaḥ saṅga varjitaḥ
nivairaḥ sarva bhūteṣu yaḥ sa mām eti pāṇḍava
iti
īśvara praṇidhānāt iti uktam sa katham praṇidhātavyaḥ kim ca tat praṇidhāna sādhanam yena praṇidhātā praṇidhatte iti tat praṇidhāna sādhana pratipādana artham āha tasya vācakaḥ praṇavaḥ iti
tasya īśvarasya yathā ukta lakṣaṇasya vācakaḥ abhidhāyakaḥ praṇavaḥ sāsnādimataḥ iva kośabdaḥ
prakarṣeṇa nūyate stūyate anena iti praṇavaḥ
yadi vā praṇauti stauti īśvaram iti praṇavaḥ oṅkāraḥ
praṇdhīyate ca anena bhagavān praṇidhātṛbhiḥ iti praṇamanti vai anena iti praṇidhatte vā tena bhagavantam cetasi iti dhāñaḥ vakāra upajanam kṛtvā
śabdena hi parokṣāṇām arthānām manasi praṇidhānam meruḥ indraḥ iti yathā
tasya ca oṅkārasya vācyaḥ īśvaraḥ
navartham khalu api nirvacanam
avateḥ rakṣaṇa ādi arthāt man iṣṭi lopaḥ ca iti
saṃsārāt avati iti gamayati vā saṃsāriṇam nirvāṇam iti niratiśayam vā prīṇayati samādhi ādi anugraheṇa avagamayati vā paramārtham iti evam ādi artha anugatam sarvathā tu nediṣṭham priyam nāma bhagavataḥ
tena hi manasi satatam praṇidhīyamānaḥ prasīdati
yathā ca anekaśas śrutayaḥ om kham brahma om iti brahma ityādayaḥ
smṛtayaḥ ca om tat sat iti
om viśvam viṣṇuḥ ityādayaḥ
om śabdasya kṛt antam yad ma antam iti avayaya tvāt vibhakti nivṛttiḥ
kim asya saṅketa kṛtam vācya vācaka tvam atha pradīpa prakāśa vat asthitam iti
kim ca atas
yadi tena bhagavatā anyaiḥ vā saṃvyavahāra artham asya nāma idam astu iti saṃketitam tatas asya prāk oṃ śabda avācya tvāt oṃ śabdena vā praṇidhātāraḥ prāṇi adhiṣata anyena vā nāma antareṇa adhītavantaḥ tathā idānīm api astu kim oṃkāra viśeṣa vacanena atha api pradīpa prakāśa vat avasthitam tathā api prathama śravaṇaḥ u pi īśvaraḥ upalabhyeta yathā prakāśena savitā
kim ca saṅketaḥ api anarthakaḥ sthita sambandhana tvāt atha apūrvam saṅketyeta pūrva ukta dosa prasaṅgaḥ iti manyate
atrā ucyate sthitaḥ asya vācyasya vācakena sambandhaḥ yadi nityaḥ śabdaḥ yadi vā anityaḥ saṅketaḥ tu tam eva sthitam sambandham avajvalayati
nanu ca uktam sthitaḥ ced prathama śravaṇe api tam pratīyuḥ iti
ucyate na hi pratyāyya prattyāyaka sambandhaḥ śabda arthayoḥ sthitaḥ api san indriyeṇa gṛhyate
yathā indriya arthayoḥ
apratyakṣe hi vācya vācaka śaktī
tatas ca yena udyate śabdāt arthaḥ numeyaḥ iti tat asat
sambandha agrahaṇāt
para prayoga vyaṅgya tvāt ca sambandhasya
na hi anumānam para prayogam apekṣate
atha brūyāt anumitāt sambandhāt artha anumānam iti
sa vaktavyaḥ katham anumitaḥ śabda artha sambandhaḥ iti
sa ced brūyāt kārya darśanāt artham hi pratītya paścāt anuminoti tad saṃbandham
yathā cakṣuṣā rūpam upalabhya cakṣuḥ sambandham iti
sa prati vaktavyaḥ siddhā tarhi vinā numānena śabdāt eva pratipattiḥ iti
yaḥ hi grāṣṭra pākena eva kṛtārthaḥ kim tasya kila ūśipākena
atha asakṛt prayoga darśanāt gṛhyate sambandhaḥ yathā agni dhūmayoḥ iti ced na tu brūmaḥ na hi sahasreṣu api prayogeṣu pratyakṣeṇa śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ gṛhyate yathā agni dhūmayoḥ ādau api sambandhaḥ gṛhyate
vākye api ayam eva
tasmāt avasthitam eva vācyasya īśvarasya vācakena praṇavena sambandham avadyotayati saṅketaḥ yathā sthitam pitā putra sambandham
saṅketa upayā apekṣa tvāt prathama śrutāt na arthaḥ pratīyate
yathā cakṣusaḥ āloka abhāve
nanu ca śabda anitya tva pakṣe katham anitye sambandhani nityaḥ sambandhaḥ iti
na hi anityayoḥ ajju ghaṭayoḥ sambandhaḥ nityaḥ syāt
ucyate yathā pramāṇa prameyayoḥ indriya viṣayayoḥ ca kriyā kārakāṇām sambandhaḥ sthitaḥ eva anityeṣu api sambandhiṣu tadvat atra api sthitaḥ eva avyabhicāreṇa sambandhaḥ sarga ādiṣu api vācya vācaka śakti apekṣaḥ saṅketaḥ
yathā eva rūpa cakṣuṣoḥ grāhya grāhaka śakti apeksayā eva sarga ādau sargaḥ tathā iha api vācya vācaka śakti apekṣayā eva saṅketaḥ kriyate
sampratipatti nitya tayā vṛddha paramparayā eva gamya gamaka bhāvena śabda arthayoḥ sampratipatti nityā na anyathā iti āgaminaḥ veda vādinaḥ pratijānate
sampratipattiḥ ca śabda artha sambandhasya hetuḥ tat eṣām
tat etat yuktam bhavati yadi āgami pakṣaḥ syāt atha anya pakṣaḥ sarvathā sthitaḥ eva sambandhaḥ pitāputrayoḥ iva saṅketena abhivyasyate iti
vācya vācakayoḥ asthita sambandha tve tu praṇava rūpeṇa abhimukhībhavati īśvaraḥ iti nā avakalpate
na hi pācya pācaka sambandhe na ca sthite pācaka agni upādānam pāka artham kalpate
sthite tu vācya vācaka sambandhe bhava vat ārādhana sādhanasya praṇavasya upādāna bhava kalpate iti tad pratipādana artham sarvam bhāṣyam
evam avagata vācya vācaka sambandhasya yoginaḥ parame īśvara prasādanam katham kriyate iti tad artham āha tad japaḥ tad artha bhāvanam tasya īśvara vācakasya praṇavasya ardha catur mātrasya tri mātrasya vā japaḥ manasā upāṃcu vā āvartanam japaḥ tad arthasya ca īśvarasya praṇavena vācakena samarpitasya samāropitasya bhāvanam abhidhyānam tad artha bhāvanam
kartavyam iti vākya śeṣaḥ
tat evam ubhyam kurvataḥ yoginaḥ cittam ekāgram sampadyate
ekāgra sampattim ca tad ārādhana phalam darśayati tathā ca uktam svādhyāyāt tiṣṭhet sīta svādhyāyāt praṇava japāt īśvaram pratyavanata dittaḥ san yogam āsīta
tad artham īśvaram dhyāyet
rasyayat tad artha dhyānāt ca a pracalita manāḥ svādhyāyam praṇavam āmanet manasā bhijapet
manasaḥ bhijapaḥ praśasyate dhyānasya āsannatara tvāt
mā viṣaya pravaṇa cittaḥ bhūt iti
evam svādhyāya yoga sampattyā tad virodhinā pratyaya antareṇa anabhighātaḥ svādhyāya yoga sampattiḥ
tayā ca praṇava japa paramaḥ īśvara dhyāna sampattyā paraḥ ātmā parameṣṭhī prakāśate yoginaḥ iti
kiñca asya bhavati pūrva sūtre cittam ekāgram sampadyate iti uktam ekam phalam tad apekṣayā kiñca iti cakāraḥ
kiñca anyat api asti phalam āhosvit citta ekāgra tvam eva iti tatra āha tatas pratyak cetanā adhigamaḥ api antarāya abhāvaḥ ca
tatas tasmāt īśvara praṇidhanāt pratyak cetanā adhigamaḥ pratyak sva buddhim iti pratyak cetanaḥ ātmā tasya adhigamaḥ yathāvat sva rūpa saṃvedanam
nanu ca adhigataḥ eva pratyātmam puruṣaḥ ham sukhī duḥkhī ca aham iti
evam prasiddham tatas kim viśeṣaṇā ucyate iti
satyam evam kim tu a viśiṣṭaḥ sau pratyayaḥ sittasya vṛttyā
kiñ ca sukhī duḥkhī ca aham iti sukha duḥkhi sāmānādhikaraṇyāt iha aham pratyayasya citta vṛtti viṣaya tvāt avidyā pratyayaḥ eva prasiddhiḥ
katham āha īśvaraḥ puruṣaḥ śuddhiḥ kleśa ādi mala varjitaḥ tatas eva prasannaḥ tatas eva kevalaḥ nistriguṇaḥ tatas eva nirupasargaḥ tāpa traya varjitaḥ prakṛṣṭa sattva pratisaṃvedī ca tathā yam api madīyaḥ puruṣaḥ śuddhaḥ prasannaḥ kevalaḥ nirupasargaḥ buddheḥ pratisaṃvedī iti avagacchati
yathā tathā iti ca dṛṣṭānta dārṣṭāntika nirdeśāt īśvara kṣetrajñayoḥ bhedaḥ uktaḥ bhavati buddham ukta upapatteḥ ca
pradhānasya pārārthya upapatteḥ kṣetrajñānām ca atas eva paraspara bhedaḥ
kim ca asya bhavati ye tāvat antarāyāḥ vyādhi prabhṛtayaḥ vakṣyamāṇāḥ te api ca asya īśvara praṇidhānāt na bhavanti
tatra ke te ntarāyāḥ kiyantaḥ vai iti āha vyādhiḥ tyāna ityādi
saṃkhyayā tāvat nava antarāyāḥ
svarūpeṇa ca vyādhi ādayaḥ
vyādhiḥ dhātuḥ a sa karaṇa vaiṣamyam
dhātavaḥ vāta pitta śleṣmāṇaḥ teṣām viṣama bhāvaḥ vaiṣamyam tat ca vāta pita śleṣma bhūyiṣṭha dravya upayoga ādibhyaḥ jāyate
hi dhātūnām vṛddhim ācakṣate
rasaḥ upayukta āharasya pariṇāma viśeṣaḥ sa ca saptadhā rasa kārya tvāt rasaḥ iti ucyate rasa lohita medaḥ māṃsa asthi majjā śukla ākhyaḥ
tasya vaiṣamyam vṛddhi kṣayau karaṇa vaiṣamyam andha badhira tva ādi
styānam akarmaṇya tā cittasya stimitam
saṃśayaḥ sthāṇuḥ vā puruṣaḥ vā iti viruddha ubhaya koṭi smṛś pratyayaḥ
pramādaḥ samādhi sādhanānām abhāvanam aśīlam
ālasyam kāyasya cittasya ca guru tvāt apravartanam
aviratiḥ cittasya viṣaya samprayoga svabhāvaḥ viṣaya samprayoga nimittaḥ vā garddhaḥ abhikāṅkṣā tṛṣṇā
bhtānti darśanam viparyaya jñānam yoga sādhaneṣu tad mārge vā viparīta vṛttiḥ
alabdhi bhūmika tvam samādhi bhūmeḥ alābhaḥ
bhūmayaḥ vitarka ādayaḥ cittasya dharma viśeṣāḥ uktāḥ vakṣyamāṇāḥ ca
an avaritāyām api samādhi bhūmau tatas katham api pracalitasya cittasya punar atra avasthita tvam eva syāt tad alābhaḥ tu anavasthita tvam ucyate
tat ete nava antarāyāḥ
antaram vivaram vicchedam kurvantaḥ āyānti iti antarāyāḥ vikṣepāḥ pratipakṣāḥ yoga prāpteḥ upasargāḥ
ete ca saha citta vṛttibhiḥ bhavanti
cittam vikṣapanti viṣayeṣu iti citta vikṣepāḥ
kṣiptam te kṣipanti saha ete vṛttibhiḥ paścatayībhiḥ anyonya prayojaka bhāvena bhavanti
atha iṣām abhāve vyādhi prabhṛtīnām abhāve sahāya vala abhāvāt na bhavanti pūrva uktāḥ pramāṇa ādayaḥ citta vṛttayaḥ
tat bhāva bhāvi tvāt tulya pratyanīkāḥ vṛtti vikṣepāḥ iti uktam bhavati
duḥkham yena abhihatāḥ prāṇinaḥ tad apaghātāya prayatante ceṣṭante
tat ca trividham
ādhyātmikam adhi ātmani iti adhyātmam tatra bhavam ādhyātmikam
tat ca śarīram mānasam ca
śārīram dhātu vaiṣamya ādi nimittam
mānasam iṣṭa vighāta ādi hetukam
ādhibhautikam adhi bhūteṣu iti adhibhūtam tatra bhavam ādhibhautikam
tat ca paśu mṛga ādi upanipatitam
ādhidaivikam iti adhi deveṣu iti adhidevam tatra bhavam ādhidaivikam
adhyātma dibhyaḥ ṭhak iti upasaṃkhyānāt ṭhak
anuśatika ādi tvāt ubhaya pada vṛddhiḥ
tat ca api vāta varṣā ādi nimittam
tat ekam eva sat nimitta bhedena rajaḥ rūpam bhidyate
daurmanasyam icchā vighātāt cetasaḥ kṣobhaḥ ākulī bhāvaḥ
yat aṅgāni ejayati kampayati tat aṅgam ejayatvam
na tat ca prāṇāyāma ādi atha abhyāsa prabhavaḥ ca asau ānanda mahā udanvat taraṅgāyamāṇaḥ api tathā samudbhavaḥ yat bāhyam vāyum ācāmati bāhya vāyoḥ ākarṣaṇa bāhulakam lyam niṣkramaṇam anda tā ca śvāsaḥ
tad viparīta vyāpāraḥ praśvāsaḥ yat kauṣṭhyam vāyum nissārayati
ete vikṣepa sahabhuvaḥ vikṣepaiḥ saha ete vikṣipta cittasya eva bhavanti iti vikṣepa sahabhuvaḥ
samāhita cittasya ete na bhavanti iti yāvat
yāvat yāvat cetaḥ samādhīiyate tāvat tāvat na bhavanti iti
tābhyām eva abhyāsa vairāgyābhyām upaśamayitavyāḥ
na anyam pratipakṣam apekṣante
abhyāsa vairāgye muktvā na hi parameśvara praṇidhāyinyaḥ prabhāvaḥ bhavati iti gamyate
antarāya abhāvaḥ ca iti ukyā prāktanāt api īśvara praṇidhānāt antarāyāḥ nirudhyante
abhyāsa vairāgyābhyām tad nirodhaḥ iti uktam
tatra vairāgya viṣayaḥ pratipāditaḥ
idānīm abhyāsasya viṣayam upasaṃharan āha tad pratisedha artham eka tattva abhyāsaḥ iti
teṣām vikṣepāṇām pratiṣedhāya tat pratiṣedha artham
ekam tattvam eka tattvam
tat ca ekam tattvam vastu tvāt abhyasitum śakyam
na hi ātma ādi vastūnām śilanam vaktum śakyate
sva māhābhāgya avasthitāni hi tāni na cittamātrāṇi
vastūnām tu citta tantra tām pratiṣedhayiṣyati na ca eka citta tantram vastu ityādinā
tasmāt etat āśaṅkamānaḥ bhāṣyakāraḥ āha eka tattva ālambanam cittam abhyaset iti
sūtre api eka tattva abhyāsaḥ iti samāsāt ayam arthaḥ upāttaḥ eva
nanu na ekam cittam avasthitam asti yasya eka tattva avalambanaḥ pratyayaḥ āpadyeta
pratyayāḥ eva cittam te ca pratyayam niyatāḥ kṣaṇapraṇāśinat ca
pratyātma saṃvedyam ca pratyayānām anavasthita tvam
nā api pratyaya vyatirekeṇa avasthitam pratyayi samāna santati pati tattvāt sāt ṛṛśya nibandhanaḥ
yathā saḥ eva pradīpaḥ te eva keśāḥ iti
tat api āha pratyaham prati pratyayam pratyayī bhinnaḥ pratyayebhyaḥ yu anta paraspara bhinnebhyaḥ n anya tvāt
ekaḥ eka pratyaya svarūpa sat vartamānā aham pratyaya viṣayaḥ pratyayī bhūta bhaviṣyat kāla ahaṃpratyaya viṣayāt pratyayinaḥ bhinnaḥ bhinna pratyaya viṣaya tvāt ghaṭat paṭaḥ iva
yadi vā bhinna kāla tvāt vinaṣṭa bhaviṣyat ghaṭā Bhyām vartamānaḥ ghaṭaḥ iva
ahaṃpratyayā sarve bhinna ālambanāḥ pratyaya tvāt ghaṭa paṭa ādi viṣaya pratyaya vat iti
atra abhidhīyate sva śāstra virodhaḥ api syāt evam bruvataḥ iti āha kṣaṇikam ca yasya cittam tasya sarvam eva cittam ekāgram vikṣepa abhāvāt eva na asya iva vikṣiptam iti sarva ditta ekāgra tvāt vikṣepa prāpta bhāvāt vikṣepa pratiṣedhāya śāstra upadeśaḥ narthakaḥ syāt
asti ca citta parikarma artham maitrī ādi upadeśaḥ
sa ca virudhyeta itthaṃdharmam cittam abhyupagacchataḥ
nanu ca tava api vrtti vṛttimatoḥ abhedāt anupapannaḥ vikṣepaḥ iti tat pratiṣedha upadeśa ānarthakyam na eṣa doṣaḥ vṛtti vṛttimat tva abhyupagamāt
yadi vṛttayaḥ eva paraspara bhinnāḥ utyanta bhinnāḥ jāyeran prati artha niyatāḥ ca tatas eṣa doṣaḥ syāt
na ca evam abhyupeyate
katham tarhi vṛttimat rūpeṇa ekam aneka artham ca visaya bhedāt avasthitam ca sat asatoḥ viparyaya an abhyupagamāt iti evam ātma pakṣe samañjasatām darśayati yadi punar idam cittam vṛtti bhedena anekadhā hi prasṛtam sāṃkhya yogavādinaḥ iva tava api sarvatas sarvebhyaḥ viṣayebhyaḥ pratyāhṛtya pratyanīya ekasmin ātma ādi arthe samādhīyeta sthāpyeta tadā bhavati ekāgram iti arthaḥ
tatas yuktaḥ tat parikarmaṇe śāstra upadeśaḥ
atas na pratyakṣam smāt kāraṇāt tat parikarma viṣaya śāstra upadeśāt sāṃkhya yoga vādi vat kṣaṇika vādinaḥ api ekam aneka artham avasthitam ca cittam na prati artha niyatam vā paścāt abhyupagamanīyam
anyathā śāstra virodhaḥ syāt
yaḥ api sadṛśa pratyaya pravāham cittam ekāgram manyate sadṛśaḥ samānaḥ pratyaya pravāhaḥ yasya ekasyām santatau tat citam ekāgram
tad viparītam asamāna pratyaya pravāham vikṣiptam
tathā ca ekāgra tā vikṣepa pratiṣedhena upapadyate tad artha upadeśaḥ ca iti kutas śāstra virodhaḥ iti
itaraḥ āha na pravāha cittasya ekasya dharmiṇaḥ na abhyupagamāt
na hi pravāha citam nāma ekam atīta vartamāna bhaviṣyat pratyayānām dharmiṇam abhyupagacchati
yadi hi abhyupagacchet parityaktaḥ sva pakṣaḥ
kasmāt pravāha cittayā akṣaṇika tvāt tat eva ekam na asti yasya ekāgra tā dharmaḥ
pratyayān eva hi anyonya saṃhatān pipīlikā paṅkti kalpān asau abhyupagacchati
atha evam manyate yadi api ekam na asti tathā api sarveṣām eva pratyayānām sadṛśa pravāhāṇām ekāgra tā dharmaḥ pradīpa arciṣām iva prakāśaḥ iti tatra āha na ayugapad kāla utpatti vināśānām samāhāraḥ sambhavati
dṛṣṭāntasya ca sādhya vikala tvāt
na hi bahvīnām aiciṣām ekaḥ prakāśaḥ
prati arciṣam asya bhedāt
na ca api prakāśasya arciṣām ca ekaḥ dharmaḥ na ā mā sti
atha api manyate pravāha aṃśasya eva pratyayasya kasyacid ekāgra tā dharmaḥ yathā ekasyām pipīlikā santatau ekā api pipīlikā lohitā iti tat ca na pūrva doṣa anuṣakteḥ
sarvaḥ pratyayaḥ pravāha aṃśaḥ sadṛśa vāhī visadṛśa vāhī vā pūrvavat prati artha niyata tvāt ekāgraḥ eva iti vikṣipta citta anavadya
liptiḥ
tasmāt ekam aneka artham avasthitam ca cittam abhyupagantavyam
yadi śāstreṇa citta parikarmā upadekṣyate
kim ca yadi cittena ekena ananvitāḥ karaṇena sva bhāva bhinnāḥ pratyayāḥ jāyeran tadā brūhi katham anya pratyaya dṛṣṭasya anyaḥ pratyayaḥ smartā bhavet devadatta dṛṣṭasya iva yajñadattaḥ
anya pratyaya upacitasya vā karma āśayasya anyaḥ pratyayaḥ upabhoktā
na hi bhaviṣyat putrāḥ racita karma āśaya phalam svarga ādi prati upabhuñjīta
atha brūyāt viśiṣṭa bhaviṣyat putra vijñāna artham vinaśyat pravṛtti vijñānam ālayavijñāna saṃskāram kañcana ādhatte iti na etat evam ālaya pravṛtti vijñānayoḥ atyanta bhedāt avastu tvāt ca
yadi ālayavijñānāt na tat pravṛtti vijñānam tadā tat eva tat iti nāma mātra bhedaḥ tathā ca saṃskāra ādhāna yukta tvāt smṛti anupakṛtaḥ
lptiḥ
atha api anyat evam api anyat pravṛtti vijñānam ālayavijñāne saṃskāram na ādadhīta abhinna tvāt
yathā santati antara ālayavijñāne
kim ca yadi api saṃskāram ādhattām tathā api pravṛtti vijñāna āpādita saṃskāram ālayavijñānam deśa kāla antara akṣamam
tasya api kṣaṇika tva abhyupagamāt vinaśyat ca tāvatī eva na uttara vijñāna upkārāya paryāpnoti
deśa kāla antara vyavahitam ced tadā bhinna santāna antara janmanā api upakartavyam
atha kāla antara avasthāyi tadā kṣaṇika tva hāniḥ
kṣaṇa antaram ced avatiṣṭheta dīrgha kāla avasthāyi tve kasya syāt akṣamā
atha api pravṛtti vijñāna saṃskāra viśiṣṭasya antarāla bhāvinaḥ ātma sadṛśasya bhavisyataḥ ālayavijñānasya saṃskāram ādhāya pūrvam ālayavijñānam vanaṅkṣyati iti tat ca na saṃskāra antara abhāvāt
asti ced anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ
atha na asti ādhāraḥ tatra kim pravṛtti vijñānasya ālayavijñāna kalpanayā saṃskāra ādhānāya
yathā ālayavijñānam utpitsiṣyamāṇasya tad kālam asataḥ ālayavijñānasya saṃskāram ādhatte tathā pravṛtti vijñānam api utpitsiṣyamāṇasya tad kālam asataḥ pravṛtti vijñānasya eva saṃskāram ādhattām an apekṣya ālayavijñānam
na ca vinaśyat anyasya bhāvinaḥ tad kālam a vidyamānasya saṃskāram ādhatte iti asya dṛṣṭāntaḥ dṛśyate
na api bhāvinī eva saṃskāram kurvīta
pūrveṇa bhaviṣyat saṃskriyate bhaviṣyati ca iti viruddham
tad kālam ced asat bhaviṣyat saṃskriyate kim tulya atulya samtati kalpanena asaṃbandha aviśeṣāt sarvam sarveṇa saṃskriyeta nā api bhaviṣyat vinaśyatoḥ yugapad utpatti vinācau akṣaṇika tva prasaṅgāt
atha tulā antayoḥ iva nati unnatī yugapad pūrva vināca uttara samutpattī syātām na vastunoḥ iti ced na abhyupagama virodhāt
na hi vaināśikena utpatti vināśa kriyā vyatirekeṇa kārkam anyat iṣyate
abhyupagame ca siddhānta virodhaḥ
kim ca kriyā kārakayoḥ yāvat kriyā utpatti kārakeṇa avasthātavyam tatas ca kṣaṇika tva hāniḥ
ā na va sthāne ca kriyā artham tatas tasya upādānam anrthakam
kim ca anyat kriyāyāḥ eva kāraka tve kārakasya api kriyā tve kriyā kāraka śabdau paryāyau syātām
tatas ca aṅkuraḥ jāyate devadattaḥ jāyate iti aṅkura devadatta ūyoḥ paryāya tvam syāt
tayoḥ jani kriyā mātra tvāt
atha anya jani kriyā devadatta viśiṣṭā anyā ca aṅkura viśiṣṭā iti ced abhyupetam tarhi viśeṣeṇa kārakam na h svarūpeṇa a kiṃcid viśiṣṭam syāt
atha ucyeta sva rūpeṇa eva utpatti kriyā utpatti kriyā antarāt viśiṣṭā yathā sva lakṣaṇāni rūpa ādīni iti tat ca na bhāva abhāvayoḥ ekatva prasaṅgāt
iha aṅkuraḥ jāyate naśyati aṅkuraḥ iti ca yaḥ eva jāyate saḥ eva tatra aṅkura jananam aṅkura vināśanam iti jananam vināśaḥ iti uktam bhavati
aṅkuraḥ hi kriyā eva kārakam iti vā ucyeta
c itaḥ
atha api syāt anyā anyasya eva aṅkura janana kriyāyāḥ aṅkura vināśa kriyā iti tathā api aṅkura jananasya nitya tva prasaṅgaḥ
vināśasya anya tvāt eva
atha api nāśa janana vat vastu śabalam iti tathā api abhāvasya śabala tvam prasajyeta
katham kriyā vyatiriktasya kārakasya abhāve api nāśaḥ eva janana vināśavān jananam eva janana vināśa vat iti
na hi abhāvasya śabala tva ādi viśeṣaḥ bhāva abhāvayoḥ ca avirodhāt pratyakṣa anumāna anupapattiḥ
yat api ucyate tulā antayoḥ nāma unnāau iti tatra yuktā tulā antayoḥ eka kālayoḥ vidyamāna tvāt anyatarasya vastu antara gaurava nimittā ānatiḥ antarasya ca unnatiḥ
iha punar bhavat bhaviṣyat kālayoḥ vijñānayoḥ nāśa utpattī tulānām ā hetu vat tṛtīyasya nmitta antarasya abhāvāt eka kālam na upapadyete
vinaśyat eva vijñānam ātma sadṛśam janayati vināśena akṣaṇa tvāt
atha mṛd piṇḍaḥ yathā ghaṭam utpādayan vinaśyati tadvat iti ced tat ca na eva ghaṭa ākāreṇa pariṇata tvāt
ekā eva hi mṛd piṇḍa ghaṭa ādi bahu dharma yominī
yat ca api bījeṣu dravya antara vāsiteṣu vāsaka dravya anuvidhāyi tvam vāsya dravyasya iti tat api akāraṇam vāsya vāsakayoḥ avasthita tvāt
avasthitāni eva hi bījeṣu aṅkure ādīni vāsyante bīja vāsanena
tat anya tvāt vāsaka dravyasya api avayava an anupraviṣṭāḥ sūkṣmāḥ vidyante eva
tasmāt vidyamānāni eva aṅkura ādīni bīja vāsanayā vāsyante iti yuktam asatām śa viṣāṇa ādīnām utpatti abhāvāt
asatām ced utpattiḥ syāt vāsya vāsakayoḥ vinaṣṭa tvāt a vidyamāna tva aviśeṣe vāsaka dravya an anuvidhāyi na utpadyeta anyat vā hasta ādi
yadi vai atyanta asat eva śaśaviṣāṇa ādi utpadyeta
atas viśiṣṭam hi trayāṇām asattvam vāsite bīje
tasmāt avasthitam kārakam bhūta bhaviṣyat kāla aneka vṛtti yogi ca abhyupagantavyam
anyathā pratyaya mātram kṣaṇikam cittam iti samarthayamānasya samādhīyamānam api samarthyamānam api ākṣipati
yathā eva bahūbhiḥ api go vikāra tva ādi hetubhiḥ samīhamāne kṛta āṭopena api gomayam pāyasīkartum na śakyam tathā kṣaṇikena cittena smaraṇa ādi samarthayitum
kim ca sva ātma anubhava apahnavaḥ cittasya anya tve pratyaya mātra tve na anya dṛṣṭam anusmarati iti sva ātmanā anubvhūtam apahnuvīta
kim tu abadrākṣīḥ iti uktaḥ dṛṣṭavān api na aham adrākṣam iti bruvīta
anyena hi tat pakṣe tat dṛṣṭam dṛśyate
tat apahneve ca anubhūtasya pratipattiḥ katham yat aham adrākṣam tat aham eva spṛśāmi yat aham asprākṣam tat aham eva smarāmi iti
sā eṣa pratyaya smaraṇayoḥ eka kartṛ tve sati ghaṭanām upaḍhaukate pratipattiḥ
anyathā mad sadṛśaḥ yat adrākṣīt tat sadṛśaḥ ham tam smṛśāmi iti smarāmi iti ca syāt
sarvasya puruṣasya aham iti pratyayaḥ smṛti pratyayayoḥ kasmin sati teṣām ca pratyayānām ekasmin kartari pratyayini a bhne ca upasthitaḥ pratyakṣaḥ ca
nanu eka pratyaya viṣayaḥ eva anyaḥ smṛteḥ eka tve api kartuḥ aham pratyemi smarāmi aham iti ca na bhavitavyam pratyatā smartā iti śabda bhedāt bhedaḥ eva
tatra āha na pratyakṣa tvāt
tat eva darśayati sva anubhava grāhyaḥ ca ayam abhedāt mā aham iti pratyayaḥ
atha pratyetā smartā iti śabda bhedāt pratyaya bhedāt ca ahampratyayasya bhinna viṣaya tvam iti ced atas āha na hi pratyakṣa asya māhātmyam prāmāṇyam cakṣuṣaḥ rūpe abhibhūyate bādhyate
kim ca pratyakṣam pramāṇam ayam aham pratyayaḥ na tat smṛti pratyayānām ekasmin kartari sāmānyena vartamānaḥ
sa ced pratyakṣa pramāṇa bhūtaḥ numānena abhibhūyeta tadānīm anumānasya api pramāṇa tvam hīyeta
tad mūla tvāt anumānasya
tat etat āha pramāṇa antaram ca anumāna virodhena ca prativādi pramāṇa pratijñā doṣaḥ vyākhyātaḥ
atīta anāgata pratyaya saṃskāra ādhārāt ananyaḥ idānīntana pratyaya saṃskār ḍhāraḥ eka santāna saṃbandhi tve sati bodha ātmaka tvāt ātma svarūpāt yathā
bhūta bhaviṣyat pratyaya saṃskāra āśrayaḥ vartamāna pratyaya saṃskāra āśrayāt anyaḥ sati bodha ātmaka tvāt ātmanaḥ iva svarūpāt
vartamānā aham pratyayī mhūti abhaviṣyat pratyayibhyām abhinnaḥ eka santāna yoge sati pratyayi tvāt yathā svarūpāt
vartamāna ahaṃpratyayī bhūta bhaviṣyat pratyayibhyām abhinnaḥ eka santāna yoge sati pratyayi tvāt yathā svarūpāt
bhūta bhaviṣyat pratyayibhyām anyaḥ vartamānaḥ pratyayaḥ eka santāna saṃbandhe sati bodha ātmaka tvāt ātma rāga svarūpa ādibhyaḥ iva
bhūta bhaviṣyat pratyayebhyaḥ na anyaḥ vartamānaḥ pratyayī eka santāna saṃbandhi tve sati bodha ātmaka tvāt ātmanaḥ yathā svarūpāt
bhinna santatiṣu paraspara smṛti pratisandhāna ādi anupalambhāt eka santāneṣu ca smṛti ādi darśanāt eva siddham eka kartṛ tvam
tathā sarva pramāṇebhyaḥ garīyasā pratyakṣeṇa pramāṇena tatra na kiṃcid anumānena sādhyam
na hi kaścid kara tala lāñchana didṛkṣayā darpaṇam ā datte
tathā api vaināśika uparacita anumāna apaśadam asahamānāḥ kecid pratyanumānāni peśalāni darśayanti
tathā ca āha tasmāt ekam aneka artham avasthitam ca cittam
yasya idam nirdiśyate iti śāstra upadeśa sambandhi tvam cittasya avasthita tve hetum upadiśati
na hi vaiśīyamāṇasya ghaṭasya prakṣālana parivartana ādi saṃskāraḥ kriyate
katham citta parikarma nirdiśyate tathā ika tattva abhyāsaḥ iti ca uktam kim ca tat ekam tattvam yadi viṣayaḥ bhyāsaḥ iti tatas āha maitrī karuṇā muditā upekṣāṇām sukha duḥkha puṇya apuṇya viṣayāṇām bhāvanā tat citta prasādanam iti
maitrī mitra viṣayā bhāvanā
tādṛśīm sukhiteṣu sukham anumodayantīm asūyā ādi vaijitām
tathā duḥkhiteṣu karuṇām kṛpām anujānatīm duḥkham
puṇya ātmakeṣu muditām puṇya śīla tām anujānatīm
apuṇya śīleṣu ca upekṣām apuṇya śīla vyāpāreṣu udāsīna tām ca bhāvayet iti anuṣajyate
sarvatra evam asya bhāvayataḥ śuklaḥ iti viśuddhiḥ prāṇi upaghāta ādi varjanāt śkulaḥ dharmaḥ
tatas sa dharmaḥ iva jātaḥ cittam prasādayati
tena prasannam cittam ekāgram sthiti padam labhate
ekāgra tayā samādhīyate iti arthaḥ tat uktam prasanna cetasaḥ hi āśu buddhiḥ paryavatiṣṭhate iti
tatra upekṣāyāḥ ā kriyā rūpa tvāt dharma ahetu tve sati kim artham iha upādānam ucyate upekṣā anupādāne ca apuṇya śīleṣu api cittam vyāpāram yāyāt
tatas ca tad vyāpāra upadhāna kāluṣyāt maitrī ādi bhāvanāyāḥ na yogyam bhavati
apuṇya śīla nimitta naimittika ākāra vyāpārāt adharmaḥ vā mā saṃjaniṣṭa iti citta sthitiḥ eva upekṣā iti tasyāḥ upādānam
citta sthitiḥ ca iha samīhitā
tasmāt ittham samāhita cittasya maitrī karuṇā ādi eka tattva ālambanam cittam śīlayataḥ prāk abhihitāḥ antarāyāḥ na janiṣyante
pracchardana vidhāraṇābhyām vā prāṇasya
vā śabdaḥ maitrī ādi bhāvanā upāaya antara vikalpa arthaḥ
maitrī ādi bhāvanā ādi upāyānām anyatamena yena kenacid citta sthitiḥ sampādanīyā iti prakaraṇa arthaḥ aneka upāya pradarśanam kasyacid kvacid sukara tā abhiprāyeṇa
pracchardana vidhāraṇābhyām vyastābhyām samastābhyām vā
pracchardanam kauṣṭhyasya vāyoḥ ātamitoḥ udvamanam nāsikābhyām na sukhena
vidhāraṇam prāṇāyāme ātamitoḥ eva
yadi api pracchardanena api prāṇaḥ āyamyate tathā api bahis vṛttiḥ na nirudhyate iti vidhāraṇam prāṇāyāmaḥ iti viśeṣyate
viṣayavatī vā pravṛttiḥ utpannā sthiti nibandhanī
cittasya iti vākya śeṣaḥ
viṣayāḥ gandha ādayaḥ yasyāḥ yoga pravṛtteḥ gandha ādi saṃvedana lakṣaṇāyāḥ ālambanībhūtāḥ sa viṣayavatī iti ucyate
pravṛttiḥ nāma yoginaḥ yogam abhyasyataḥ abhimukhī bhāvam pratipadyamānasya yogasya yaḥ prathamaḥ bhimukhībhāvaḥ pratyaya kraṇaḥ yoga anuṣṭhānam pratyutsāha jananaḥ nirmadhyamānasya agneḥ iva dhūma samudbhavaḥ sā apravṛttiḥ
sā ca tādṛśī pravṛttiḥ utpannā pratyaya karaṇāt praharṣayantī yoginaḥ cittam sthitau nivadhnāti
nāsikā agre cittam dhārayataḥ gandha saṃvid prahlādana kara surabhi gandha saṃvedanam nirantara tayā sammata saṃyogam iva ācakṣāṇā jāyate
sā gandha pravṛttiḥ
tathā jihvā ādiṣu
dhārayataḥ iti sambadhyate
tāḥ etāḥ pravṛttayaḥ sthitau cittam nibadhnanti
saṃśayam vidhamanti samādhi prajñāyāḥ ca dvārībhavanti
etena raśma candra āditya graha pradīpa ādiṣu cittam dhārayataḥ hṛdaya puṇḍarīke vā dhārayataḥ vaiṣamyāt raśmi candra ādi ākārā pravṛttiḥ utpannā viṣayavatī iti eva veditavyā
yadi api śāstra anumāna ācāryebhyaḥ vagatam artha tattvam tathābhutam eva avyabhicāri svarūpam eva
teṣām anyathā bhūta a pratipādaka tvāt
tathā pi yāvat eka deśaḥ api svakaraṇa saṃvedyaḥ na bhavati pratyakṣaḥ na bhavati eka deśaḥ api tāvat sarvam parokṣam iva apavarga ādiṣu sūkṣmeṣu artheṣu na dṛḍhām buddhim utpādayati
tasmāt śāstra anumāna ācārya upoddhalana artham avaśyam kaścid viśeṣaḥ pratyakṣīkartavyaḥ
tatra śāstra ādi upadiṣṭa artha eka deśa pratyakṣa tve sati sarvam sūkṣma viṣayam api ā apavargāt śraddhīyate
etat artham evā idam cita parikarma yat etat maitrī karuṇā ityādinā paramāṇu parama mahā tva antaḥ asya vaśīkāraḥ iti evam antena prakaraṇena yama niyama āsana viśiṣṭasya citta parikarmā upadiśyate
tat etat uktam bhavati etat prakaraṇa upadiṣṭānām upāyānām anyatama anuṣṭhānāt pratyakṣīkṛta eka deśa tayā pidhmāya saṃśayam tu apavargāt dṛḍha avasthita śraddhā anādi praśānta vahis vṛtti upasthita vaśīkāra saṃjñā vairāgyam tasya tasya tṛtīya pāda upadiṣṭa pariṇāma traya ādeḥ arthasya pratyakṣi karaṇāya samartham syāt jñāna vibhūti ādi prāpi artham iti
tatas ca evam artham citta parikarmā upadiśyate iti prakaraṇa arthaḥ
tayā ca bhāṣyakāraḥ pradarśitavān etat artham evā idam citta parikarma iti evamādinā
viśokā vā jyotiṣmatī pravṛttiḥ utpannā manasaḥ sthiti nibandhanī iti prakṛtam abhisaṃbadhyate
jyotiḥ yasyām vidyate pravṛttau sā jyotiṣmatī
sā ca śokam vyapagamayati iti viśokā nāma
sā ca katham anupajāyate iti āha hṛdaya puṇḍarīke dhārayataḥ buddhi saṃvid bhavati sva rūpa sa vedanam
buddhi sattvam hi kiṃrūpam iti āha buddhi sattvam hi prabhāsvaram prabhāsana śīlam ākāśa kalpam vyāpi
yatra yasmin buddhi sattve
sthiti vaiṣamyāt iti
buddhi sattva ātmatā sāmya anāpatteḥ iti
hṛdaya puṇḍarīke eva dhārayataḥ pravṛtti jyotiṣmatī sūrya indu maṇi prabhā rūpa kāreṇa vikalpate
tathā ca asmitāyām ahaṅkāre samāpnnam syāt buddhi sattvam sva rūpeṇa sāmya āpatteḥ nistaraṅga mahodadhi kalpam śāntam anantam asmitā mātram bhavati
yatra idam uktam yatra asmitā samāpatta tam etam prakṛtam asmitā ātmānam ahaṅkāram aṇum sūkṣmam ātmānam anuvidya prāpya asmi iti evam tāvat saṃjātītaḥ iti
yat ṛṛśam ālambana svarūpam tāvat mātram sañjānīte
ahaṅkāra sva rūpreṇa eva tad ānurūpyāt avacchidyate sphuṭika maṇiḥ iva upadhāna rūpreṇa
evam dvayī viśokā pravṛttiḥ viṣayavatī ca asmitā mātrā ca
tara gandha saṃvid ādiḥ ā asmitā mātra antā sarvā viśokā eva
jyotṣmatī punar gandha saṃvid ādi pravṛtti pañcatayāt anyatra
viṣyavatī tu asmitā mātrāt prāk eva iti evam viṣaya vibhāgaḥ
yayā viśokayā jyotiṣmatyā yoginaḥ cittam sthiti padam labhate
vīta rāga viṣayam vā cittam vītaḥ rāgaḥ yasmāt pratyayāt sa vīta rāgaḥ rāga śūnyaḥ iti arthaḥ
saḥ eṣa viṣayaḥ ālambanam yasya cittasya tat vīta rāga viṣayam
vīta rāgaḥ ca pratyayaḥ prasiddhaḥ loke
rāgiṇaḥ api hi puruṣasya rāga kāraṇe api viṣaye yaḥ mātrā ādiṣu
saḥ eva pratyayaḥ tam eva pratyaye vitara āgaḥ gaṃ ālambana tvena abhyasyet na tu tasya yaḥ viṣayaḥ ālambanam
viṣayāṇām khala tvāt
tat vīta rāga pratyaya ālambana uparaktam cittam tadvat eva vīta rāgam prasannataram sthiti padam labhate
rāgāt gikhalīkṛtam hi kṛta khalīnam iva turaṅgamānam pracalati
svapna nidrā jñāna ālambanam vā
svapna jñāna ālambanam vā nidrā jñāna ālambanam vā cittam tad ākāram eva bhavati
evam svabhāvam hi cittam yat ālambate tad ākāram bhavati
svapne ca śabda ādi viṣaya śūnyam jñānam
jñānasya api svabhāvaḥ vabhāsaka tā
tatra api jñāna sva prūpam eva ālambate
na tu smaryamāṇa viṣaya svarūpam
smaryamāṇena api viṣayeṇa khalīkāraḥ dṛśyate
nidrā jñānam tu viśeṣa agrahaṇa ātmakam abhāva pratyaya ālambanam śāntam anantam anubhūyamāna acalana dharmakam
tatas ca tad ālambanam sat cittam sthiti padam labhate iti yuktam
yathā abhimata dhyānāt vā
yat eva abhimatam iti citta sthiti apekṣayā
citta sthiteḥ prakṛta tvāt
na tu sukha ādi apekṣayā
pratiṣidha tvāt ca na tu eva viṣayān prāpya dhārayeta katham cana iti
tatra labdha sthitikam karmaṇyam sat anyatra śāstrīyeṣu api sthiti padam labhate
paramāṇu parama mahā tva antaḥ asya vaśīkāraḥ
anta śabdaḥ pratyekam saṃbadhyate
sūkṣme niviśamānasya parimāṇe niviśamānasya yoginā saṃkṣipyamāṇasya
tu alpam alpataram ca krameṇa ālocayat paramāṇu antam saṃkṣipyate
sa ca cittasya saṃkṣepakoṭiḥ
tena tad antam t sthiti padam
ittham ubhaya koṭim anudhāvataḥ cittasya saṃkṣepam vistāram ca anubhavataḥ yaḥ tad virodhinā pratyaya antareṇa apratighātaḥ sa paraḥ vaśīkāraḥ
pūrvaḥ api pare eva
tathā api asya ayam viśeṣaḥ
tad vaśīkārāt paripūrṇam an avakhaṇḍitam labdha sthitikam na punar abhyāsa kṛtam parikarma apekṣate iti
pūrve tu kiyat api parikarma antaram apekṣante
tatra saṃkṣiptā viśālā vikaraṇī ca iti trayī dhāraṇā
tatra ubhaya koṭi smarśinī vikaraṇī
parama mahat tva anta spṛś viśālā
paramāṇu anta spṛś saṃkṣiptā
sā ca trayī api iha sūtra upāttā
atha labdha sthitikasya cetasaḥ atha uktānām anyatamena upāyena labdha sthitikasya kim svarūpā kiṃviṣayā vā samāpattiḥ iti tat nididarśaya idam sūtram pravavṛte kṣīṇa vṛtteḥ abhijāyasya iva maṇeḥ grahītṛ grahaṇa grāhyeṣu tad stha tad añjana tā samāpattiḥ
nanu ca samāpatteḥ viṣayam vakṣyati tṛtīya pāde parārthāt sva artha saṃyamāt puruṣa jñānam iti ādinā
samāpatti svarūpam ca saṃyama svarūpam tad kārya nirvartanena eva setsyati
tatas ca anarthakam idam sūtram na eṣa doṣaḥ pūrva ukta upāya vaśi kāraṇa arthavat tva pradarśana artha tvāt
evam hi eṣa citta vaśīkāraḥ yena grahītṛ ādi artha samāpannam cittam tad ābhāsam bhavati iti
kim ca vitarka ādi anugamāt saṃprajñātaḥ iti uktam vitarka ādi svarūpam ca iha darśayitavyam anuktāyām samāpattau vitarka ādi svarūpam āha na śakyam darśayitum samāpattiḥ dharmāḥ vitarka ādayaḥ iti
kṣīṇa vṛtteḥ iti pratyasta mita bāhya pramāṇa ādi pratyayasya iti arthaḥ
nanu sarve eva pratyayāḥ pratyastamitāḥ
sarva prati astamaye hi avasita adhikāram na sthūla sūkṣma ādikam ālambate
abhijātasya iva maṇeḥ iti dṛṣṭānt upādānam
yathā sphaṭikaḥ tat tat rūpa uparaktaḥ upāśraya ākāreṇa nirbhāsate
tathā grāhya ālambana uparaktam cittam grāhya samāpannam grāhya svarūpa ākāreṇa nirbhāsate
tathā bhūta sūkṣma uparaktam tanmātra uparaktam bhūta sūkṣma samāpannam bhūta sūkṣma svarūpa avabhāsam avabhāsate
tathā sthūla ālambana uparaktam sthūla rūpa samāpannam sthūla rūpa ābhāsam bhavati
tathā viśva bheda uparaktam viśva bheda samāpannam viśva rūpa ābhāsam bhavati
tathā api indriyeśu api draṣṭavyam
grahaṇa ālambana uparaktam grahaṇa samāpannam grahaṇa svarūpa ākāreṇa nirbhāsate
tathā grahītṛ puruṣa samāpannam buddhi bodhaka svarūpam iti arthaḥ
gṛhītṛ svarūpa ākāreṇa nirbhāsate
tathā muktapuruṣāla bana uparaktam iti
saḥ eva buddhḥ boddhā yadā viṣaya vṛttīnām na boddhā bhavati tadā sattva puruṣa anya tā khyāti mātra avasthā
yadā udāsīnaḥ muktapuruṣaḥ iti ucyate tadā hi sarva kleśa ādi muktam cittam sā eva hi puruṣasya mukta tā yā kleśa ādi vimuktiḥ cittasya
atas eva sūtre grahītṛ grahaṇam eva kṛtam
grahītā puruṣa viśeṣaḥ eva mukta puruṣaḥ iha abhipretaḥ iti
yadā yathā hi puruṣa grahaṇam eva kuryāt
parasyām vaśikāra saṃjñāyām jātāyām na punar saṃsāra yogaḥ bhavati
tathā ca uktam eva citta sattva sambandhe kleśa ādi sambandha abhāvāt sa tu sadā eva muktaḥ sadā eva īśvaraḥ iti
tasmāt muktapuruṣa ala bana uparaktam mukta puruṣa samāpannam mukta sva rūpa ākāreṇa nirbhāsate iti
yaḥ hi manyate nivṛtta sattva sambandhena eva muktena puruṣeṇ a samāpannam tad ākāram eva nirbhāsate iti tat ayuktam cittasya sva ātma pralaya prasaṅgāt
nirariśaya sūkṣmaḥ c apuruṣaḥ tad sama sūkṣmam pradhānam tad kārya krya kāryam nimittam sattvam tat cittam pradhānam puruṣam vā samāpadyamānam na sthitena svena rūpeṇa samāpattum utsahate
na hi ghaṭaḥ mṛd avasthām a parityakta svarūpaḥ samāpadyate
nanu ca kāryeṇa api yogi sattvena mahat ahaṅkārau saṃvedyau ucyete
mahati tāvat vipratipattiḥ saṃvedyate na vā iti
yadā hi saṃvedya tā grahītṛ mukta sva rūpa vat saṃbandha viśeṣaḥ upapadyate mahat ahaṅkārayoḥ api
vyaktau hi tau tatas saṃbandha viśeṣaḥ yujyate saṃbandha viśeṣāt ca yathā sva puruṣaḥ grahītṛ sva rūpaḥ ca muktaḥ ca citta vṛtti viśeṣa saṃbandhāt gṛhyate tadvat
na tu sarva ātmanā eva mahat ahaḥkārayoḥ api grahaṇam mahat tvāt
tayoḥ api tau api yadi sarva ātmanā gṛhyeyātām citta sattva mātra ātmānau jāyeyātām tathā ca sati tad viṣaya grahaṇam eva na syāt
pradhāna prurṣayoḥ tu tad saṃbandhasya ca atyantam avyakta sva rūpa tvāt na sva rūpa grahaṇam
nanu ca īśvarasya asarvajña tā yatas pradhāna puruṣa tad saṃbandhāḥ na pratyakṣāḥ iti
ucyate pradhāna puruṣa saṃbandhebhyaḥ anyat sarvam pratyakṣam iti atra tāvat avipratipattiḥ niravadhika pratyakṣa jñāna abhyupagamāt
yatra tu anumāna gośaraḥ yat tu asmākam agocaraḥ tat saḥ eva īśvaraḥ jñātum arhati
jñeyam ced asti tat sarvam asau yathā vā tathā vā jānāti iti niścayaḥ
ajñātṛkasya jñeya tva anupapatteḥ
kiñ ca yadi prakṛti puruṣau sva rupeṇa jñeya tvam ā nā padyeyātām tadā buddhi vat bhogya tā prasaṅgaḥ
tatas ca para arthaḥ api syāt paraḥ ca anyaḥ kalpyaḥ syāt
nanu puruṣāṇām anyonya bhogyatā iti na paraḥ bhoktā kalpyaḥ na etat evam sama tvāt puruṣāṇām viṣaya viṣayi tva anupapatteḥ
na hi pradīpau anyonyam uparudh rutaḥ
kiñ ca bhogyatve sukha ādi rūpa tā prasaṅgaḥ ca puruṣasya
tathā ca sati pradhānasya nirhetuka tva prasaṅgaḥ ca iti evam ādayaḥ bhūyaṃsaḥ doṣāḥ
nanu ca para arthāt sva artha saṃyamāt puruṣa jñānam iti puruṣa pratyaykṣatām vakṣyati satyam yuktam uktam
atas eva ucyate puruṣaḥ na sva rūpeṇa viṣayi bhavati iti
yena evam tatra uktam na ca puruṣa pratyayena buddhi sattva ātmanā puruṣaḥ dṛśyate
puruṣaḥ eva tam pratyayam su ālaṃbanam paśyati iti
tathā hi uktam vijñātāram are kena vijānīyāt iti iti
nanu puruṣa ālambana uparaktam cittam puruṣasya viṣayaḥ
tathā ca sati pratyakṣaḥ eva puruṣaḥ
yathā ghaṭa ālabmbana uparaktte pratyaye puruṣeṇa upalabhyamāne ghaṭaḥ pratyakṣaḥ ucyate na eṣa doṣaḥ ghaṭa vat purusasya cittena avyāpya tvāt
ghaṭa ādiḥ tu bāhyaḥ cittena vyāpyate na puruṣaḥ ānantyāt
paricchinnam hi cittam viṣayīkurvan na puruṣam viṣayiṇam anantam vyāptum utsahate
yadi puruṣam vyāpnoti pradhānam api vyāpnuyāt
tasmāt yathā darpaṇe mukham chāyā rūpeṇa gṛhyate tathā puruṣa chāyā ākāreṇa pariṇataḥ pratyayaḥ gṛhyate puruṣeṇa
tathā ca vyāsaḥ yathā darśa tala prakhye paśyati ātmānam ātmani
iti
na tu mukta anya puruṣa ākāreṇa pariṇatau dvāram asti
yadi tad ākāreṇa pariṇameta muktasya api tad svam eva iti dṛśyam syāt
na hi cittasya pariṇāmāḥ anya tvam nāma asti
su ākāreṇa hi pariṇatam puruṣaḥ na tu cittam na paśyati
sva puruṣe sva tvāt sati saṃbandhe pariṇati dvāram asti
katham tarhi sva puruṣāt anyasya sva tva asaṃbandhinaḥ grahaṇam ucyate yathā para darpaṇa dvāreṇa para mukha darśanam tathā darpaṇa sthānīya para sattva ākāra pariṇatam sva sattvam puruṣaḥ paśyan param api puruṣam jānāti
tasya ayam ātmā mama ayam iti tu anumānāt eva pratipadyate svakīyāt anyadīya sattva gata viśeṣa loggena
sattvānām ca triguṇa tvāt avaśyam viśeṣāḥ santi
puruṣāṇām tu nirviśeṣa tvāt svarūpeṇa bhedaḥ duravabodhaḥ eva
tasmāt evam abhijāta maṇi kalpasya cetasaḥ grahītṛ grahaṇa krāhyeṣu puruṣa indriya bhūteṣu tad stha tad añjana tā
teṣu grahītṛ ādiṣu tiṣṭhati iti tad stham tad stha tā viśiṣṭā yām grahītṛ ādi añjana tā tat eva āha teṣu sthitasya tad ākāra āpattiḥ samāpattiḥ iti ucyate
samyak āpattiḥ samāpattiḥ sā ca tādṛśī pratyasta mita bahis vṛtteḥ eva bhavati
yadi api vyutthita cittasya api samāpattiḥ asti
tathā api sā na samīcīnatarā rajaḥ tamobhyām citta sattvasya atyanta abhibhūta tvāt iti
sā eṣā samāpattiḥ catuṣṭayī
tatra prathamām samāpattim vyācaṣṭe śabda artha jñāna vikalpaiḥ saṅkīrṇā sa vitarkā samāpattiḥ
śabdaḥ ca arthaḥ ca jñānam ca śabda artha jñānāni teṣām vikalpāḥ śabda artha jñāna vikalpaḥ
vyāta vyālambana viṣayaiḥ vikalpaiḥ saṃkīrṇā vimmiśrā itaretara pratyaya anubuddhā sā saṃkīrṇa samāpattiḥ
nanu ca śabda artha pratyayāḥ itara itara vyāvṛtta svarūpāḥ yogī ca ekam vastu dhyeya tvena ālambate śabdam artham pratyayam vā tatra kaḥ śabda artha jñāna vikalpa saṅkaraḥ
evam eva etat
tathā api ayam eva saṃvyavahāraḥ loke yat uta avibhāgena grahaṇam
tat yathā gauḥ iti śabdaḥ gauḥ iti arthaḥ gauḥ iti jñānam iti avibhāgena loke grahaṇam dṛṣṭam
evam hi lokaḥ trayam api gauḥ iti eva vyapadiśyati
