tathā anyatara grahaṇe avaśiṣṭayoḥ api smṛtiḥ
nanu ca etat vastu na evam śabda artha saṅketa grahaṇa uttara kāla bhāvi tvāt
nanu saṅgetāt api prāk sāmānya śabdam yam kañcid adhyavasyati eva na viviktānām api grahaṇa darśanāt
vivicyamānāḥ ca anye śabda dharmāḥ gakāra ādi varṇa udātta svarita tad rutam adhi avilambita śrotra grahaṇa ādayaḥ
te na artha jñānayoḥ
tathā anye ṛtha dharmāḥ sa snā lāṅgūla kakuda khura viṣāṇa darśana ādayaḥ
tathā ca anye pratyaya dharmāḥ puruṣa grāhya ātmaka tva avabhāsa ātmaka tva saṃskāra ādhāyi tva ādayaḥ na te śabda arthayoḥ
na tena paramārthataḥ nyonya dharma saṅkara gandhaḥ api asti
tena viviktaḥ pandhāḥ teṣām
tatra yatra kvacana samāpannasya yaḥ hi eva arthaḥ samādhi prajñām upārūḍhaḥ sa ced śabda artha jñāna vikalpa anuviddhaḥ śabda artha saṅketa kṛtaḥ yaḥ itaretara smṛti anuvyādhaḥ tad viśiṣṭaḥ ced arthaḥ upāvartate sā saṅkīrṇā samāpattiḥ sa vitarkā iti ucyate
aneka janma antara śabda artha saṅketa jñāna saṃskāra viśiṣṭa tvāt yoginaḥ api prathamatarā samāpattiḥ loka pratyaya a viśiṣṭā
eṣa tu viśeṣaḥ yat labdha sthiti pada tvāt yogi cittasya samāna pratyaya pravāha te
idānīm nirvitarkā samāpattiḥ ucyate
yadā punar śabda saṅketa smṛti pariśuddhau
śabda saṅketaḥ sya ayam vācakaḥ ayam asya vācyaḥ iti samaya pratipattiḥ

tasyāḥ pariśuddhiḥ mithyātvāt vinivṛttiḥ
sā rajaḥ tamasoḥ nyak bhāvāt
śruti jñānam āgamikam anumāna jñānam laukikam te ca sāmānya viṣaye eva anumāna āgama jñāne tayoḥ vikalpaḥ hi viśeṣa adhyāropaḥ tena adhyāsena śūnyāyām yoginaḥ samādhi prajñāyām vyāvṛtta laiṅgika sāṅketika jñāna adhyāsāyām sva rūpa mātreṇa mātra grahaṇam diś deśa kāla anubhāva ādibhyaḥ api vyāvṛttaḥ iti evam artham svaiḥ eva dharmaiḥ mahīyamānaḥ tad sva rūpa mātra tayā eva tasya arthasya sva rūpa mātra tayā eva yoginaḥ prajñ
na tasmāt arthāt bahis deśa kāla ādi kiṃcid ālovayati iti arthaḥ
svam api grahaṇa ātmakam rūpam tat prajñā na nirmalatara tvāt
grāhya mātrā eva sā vibhajyate
sā ca tādṛśī nirvitarkā samāpattiḥ
nirgataḥ syāḥ nirvitarkaḥ vitarkaḥ dhyā āropaḥ
sā u syām na asti
tat etat param utkṛṣṭam śuddham pratyakṣam aparam pratyakṣam sarva sādhāraṇam purastāt vṛtti madhye paṭhitam idam yoginaḥ eva iti
tat śuta anumānayoḥ bījam
yadi api pūrvoktam api śruta anumānayoḥ bījam eva tathā api tad kārye śruta anumāne vyabhivarataḥ api na punar nirvitarka samādhi ja pratyakṣa prabhave vyabhivarataḥ iti atas āha tatas śruta anumāne prabhavataḥ iti
na ca nanu śruta anumāna jñāna sahabhūtam tat darśanam śruta anumāna jñānābhyām asamāni viṣayam iti etat
viśeṣa viṣayam hi tat darśanam sāmānya viṣaye śruta anumāna jñāne tasmāt asaṅkīrṇam pramāṇa antareṇa yoginaḥ nirvitaka jam darśanam iti tat nirvitarkāyāḥ tat iti tasmāt iti samāpatteḥ asyāḥ sūtreṇa lakṣaṇam dyotyate samṛti paru śuddhau sva rūpa śūnyā iva artha mātra nirbhāsāt nirvitarkā
śabda saṅketa śruta anumāna jñāna vikalpa smṛti pariśuddhau śabda saṅketa vikalpaḥ śruta jñāna vikalpaḥ anumāna jñāna vikalpaḥ ca saḥ eva smṛtiḥ
smaraṇena hi anyasya anya dharmaḥ adhyāropyate
na hi vastu svarūpeṇa vastu antare dhyāropayitum śakyam
nanu ca katham śruta anumite pratyakṣe adhyāropyete
nanu ca prasiddhaḥ dhyā āropaḥ tathā ca idam mayā śrutam idam mayā numitam idam iti ca paśyati
nanu tat eva tat dṛśyamānam api yat anumitam śrutam ca na sāmānya viśeṣa bhedāt
sāmānyam śrutam anumitam ca viśeṣaḥ tu pratyakṣasya viṣayaḥ
tasmin ca tad sāmānya adhyāsaḥ prasiddhaḥ eva
grāhya uparaktā yoginaḥ prajñā evam prajñā rūpam grhaṇa ātmakam tyaktvā padārtha mātra svabhāvā grāhya svarūpa āpannā iva bhavati
ivaśabdena grahaṇa ātmaka tām na jahati iti
na hi sphaṭikaḥ upādhi āśraya tāyām svām svaccha rūpa tām hāsyati
kim ca grahaṇa vyatiriktam ca grāhyam vastu antaram asti iti ca uktam bhavati
sā nirvitarkā samāpattiḥ
tathā ca vyākhgyātam
tasyāḥ hi eka buddhi upakramaḥ rtha ātmā
upakramyate ekayā buddhyā yaḥ saḥ ekaḥ buddhi upakramaḥ eka buddhi paricchedyaḥ iti
artha ātmā bodhya ātmā iti etat
gavādiḥ ghaṭa ādiḥ vā viṣayaḥ na tu bodhaḥ eva gavādi ākāraḥ viṣayaḥ aṇu pracaya viśeṣa ātmā aṇūnām tanmātra yavānām pracaya viśeṣaḥ ātmā yasya sa gavādiḥ ghaṭa ādiḥ vā ālambanam buddheḥ sa ca viṣayaḥ saṃsthāna viśeṣaḥ tathā saṃsthitāni hi tāni bhūta sūkṣmāṇi
etat uktam bhavati bhūta sūkṣmāṇām sādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ iti ātma bhūtaḥ na vyatiriktaḥ
yathā sarpasya ābhoga kuṇḍala nādi
yeṣām punar atyanta vyatiriktam anyat eva kāraṇāt kāryam teṣām kāraṇa tantra tvam kāryasya na prāpnoti
aṃśu tantraḥ hi tantuḥ tantu tantraḥ ca paṭaḥ
na ca atyanta avyatve dṛṣṭam
yathā mṛd piṇḍa tantra tā na paṭasya tantūnām vā
kim ca tad vināśa anuvināśi tvam ca na śakyam na hi kapāla vināśam anuvinaśyati paṭaḥ
atha ucyeta sambandhaḥ kāraṇam iti
paṭasya hi tantavaḥ tantūnām ca aṃśavaḥ iti sambandhaḥ tatra hetuḥ kāraṇam tat tantra tva tad anuvināśayoḥ iti
atrā ucyate caitra kṣetra ādi sambandhe api prasaṅgaḥ syāt
caitrasya api kṣetra ādi tantra tā tad anuvināśi tvam ca sambandha viśeṣāt prasajyeta
atha api syāt samavāya lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ kāraṇam iti na tasya api saṃbandha tva aviśeṣāt ahetu tvam yathā anya saṃbandhaḥ saṃbandhinoḥ anyatara tantra tva ādi ahetuḥ evam samavāya lakṣaṇasya api saṃbandha tvāt anyatara tantra tva ādau ahetu tvam eva
kiñca anyat saṃbandhasya ca saṃbandhinoḥ eva anyatara tantra tva ādi hetutve samavāyasya api samavāya antaram tasya api anyaḥ iti anavasthā prasajyeta
yathā guṇa ādīnām samavāya lakṣaṇāt saṃbandhāt dravya tantra tvam tathā samavāyasya api dravya vyatirikta tve dravya tantra tva artham samavāya antaram kalpyeta tasya api anyat tasya api anyat iti anavasthā syāt
prāk utpatteḥ abhāvāt kāryasya kāraṇena saṃbandha anupapattiḥ aviśiṣṭam ca asattvam śaśa viṣāṇasya ghaṭasya ca
tatra ghaṭena eva kāraṇasya saṃbnandhaḥ na śaśaviṣāṇa ādibhiḥ iti hetuḥ vāditavyaḥ
prāk asat na utpadyeta śaśaviṣāṇa vat
yaḥ tu tantubhyaḥ nyaḥ sa tantubhyaḥ na utpadyate tantubhyaḥ nya tvāt
yathā tantubhyaḥ ghaṭaḥ
itaraḥ āha prāk san api na utpadyate sattvāt visyamāna ghaṭa vat iti
yaḥ yasmāt ananyaḥ saḥ api tasmāt nityā na utpadyate vidyamāna tvāt sva rūpa vat iti
aparaḥ āha yadi sat na utpadyate iti sataḥ utpatti abhāvaḥ ucyeta siddha sādhya tā syāt
atha abhivyakti abhāvaḥ tadā dṛṣṭānta abhāvaḥ
yat api ucyate yaḥ yasmāt ananyaḥ iti tatra api siddha sādhya tā dṛṣṭānta abhāvaḥ ca
svarūpāt eva hi bhivyajyate na asati abhivyaṅgya svarūpe abhivyaktiḥ abhivyañjaka sahasreṇa api śakyate kartum
kiñca anyat sarva vyavahāra lopaḥ ca
katham yadā devadattasya gauḥ aśvaḥ vā prātar vidyamāna karṇa lāṅgūlaḥ punar aḍavīm gataḥ kenacid lūna karṇaḥ lūna lāṅgūlaḥ vā syāt tadā pūrva avayava vibhāgāt vinaṣṭaḥ anyaḥ tu navaḥ svāmikaḥ sañjātaḥ iti yena kenacid upādīyeta tathā ca avayava vibhāgaḥ sarvatra sambhavati iti sva svāmi sambandha ādi niyama abhāvāt aśeṣa vyavahāra lopaḥ syāt
atha brūyāt pūrva upārjita avayavaiḥ eva avayavī navaḥ pralūna karṇa lāṅgūlaḥ ārabdhaḥ iti na evam na hi mātā mitra ādi vyatirekeṇa idānīntana lūna karṇa lāṅgūla avayavi antara pratyārambhiṇaḥ dṛśyante
kim ca yasya ca kṣetre lūna karṇa lāṅgūlaḥ jātaḥ tasya eva asau syāt na pūrva āvayavikasya tad kṣetra jāta tṛṇa palāśa ādi vat
yathā ca anya kṣetra gatāni bījāni upanītāni ced tat tad bīja niṣpanna sasyam kṣetravān eva gṛhṇāti na tu pūrva bījavān
na ca asya asau pratibadhnāti vidvān api madīya bīja pariniṣpannam sasyam aham upādīya iti
tathā lūna karṇa kāṅgūlam api kṣetravān eva gṛhṇīta
na tatra madīya avayavaiḥ ārabdhaḥ yam avayavī iti
yeṣām api ekasmin gṛhīte tasmin aśve lūna karṇa laṅgūlake jāte sva kṣetre ca dṛṣṭe saḥ eva aśva dātā anyaḥ yam vitisanyaḥ yam mahattamāt aśvāt mayā dattaḥ mahattamaḥ iti hareta
haratām iti ced satva vyavahāra lopa prasaṅgaḥ śāstra kopaḥ ca
tasmāt ā nyaḥ vayavebhyaḥ kāraṇebhyaḥ ekaḥ vayavī kāryam iti siddham
yat api ucyate śabda pratyaya dharma ādi bhedāt anye iti tat api uktam
dṛśyate hi śabda ādi bhede api ananyatvam
yathā hastaḥ karaḥ pāṇiḥ iti śabda bhedaḥ ekasya pitṛ tvam putra tvam ca pratyaya bhedaḥ ekasya eva baddhaḥ punar muktaḥ sthitaḥ gataḥ ca iti kāla bhedāt
dāhaka tvam pācaka tvam iti ādayaḥ dharma bhedāḥ iti
diś deśa ādi bhedāḥ tu asiddhāḥ eva
tasmāt āha ātma bhūtaḥ iti
sa ca sva phalena vyaktena anumitaḥ
phalena udaka āharaṇa ādhāraṇa sambhavana ādinā
yasya hi phalam kāryam vyaktam upalabhyate sa asti iti niścayaḥ
anumitaḥ iti vipratipanna apekṣayā sādhāraṇa śabdena śakti rūpeṇa vā ucyate
sa tu pratyakṣaḥ eva avyaktena daṇḍa sūtra kūlāla ādi kāraka vyāpāra abhivyaktena phalena kāryeṇa ghaṭa ākhyena prāk api mṛd ādi avasthāyām astitvena anumitaḥ sa eva daṇḍa ādi kārakaiḥ sva vyañjakaiḥ abhivyajyamānaḥ prādur bhavati dharma antara udaye ca tirobhavati sā eva bhūta sūkṣmāṇām dharmaḥ vayavī iti ucyate
etat uktam bhavati aṇūnām apratyakṣa tvāt na āvirbhāva tirobhāvau yuktau
tatas tāḥ ca tau
tasmāt yaḥ āvirbhavati dharma antara udaye virodhāt tirobhavati ca āvis bhāve ca yaḥ vyañjaka ādi apekṣate saḥ vayavī iti ucyate
yaḥ ca evam dharmaḥ saḥ ṇubhyaḥ nyaḥ iti
kim ca amī api anye hetavaḥ vayavi sadbhāve saḥ ekaḥ ca mahān ca āṇīyān ca kriyā dharmakaḥ ca anityaḥ ca
pratyekam ete hetavaḥ
api ca ekaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti ghaṭa śabda vācyasya eka tvena sāmānādhikaraṇyāt
asti ca idam sāmānādhikaraṇyam yaḥ sau ekaḥ iti
na hi bahūnām aṇūnām eka tvena sāmānādhikaraṇyam upakalpete
tathā mahatvena
na ca aṇūnām amahatām mahatvena sāmānādhikaraṇyam yujyate tathā aṇīyaḥ tvena
na hi aṇūnām aṇu antara apekṣayā anīyaḥ tvam ghaṭate
sarve eva hi te ṇīyāṃsaḥ
na api ca aṇūnām aṇu tvam gṛhyate ṇubhyaḥ
aṇu tve vastu antarasya aṇīyaḥ tvam upapatsyate
kim ca kriyā dharmakaḥ ca
kriyā dharmaḥ yasya sa kriyā dharmakaḥ
phalavat vyāpāra nirvṛtti kara tvāt iti uktam bhavati
na hi aṇūnām phalavat vyāpāra nirvṛtti kara tvam yuktam
aśakya prayojya tvāt asmat ādibhiḥ
kim ca anitya tvāt
na hi aṇūnām anitya tvam gṛhyate
kim ca dṛśya tvāt
na hi aṇavaḥ dṛśyante
tathā spṛśya tvāt ca hānāt ca upādānāt ca dhāraṇāt ca iti evam ādayaḥ
tena avayavinā vyavahārāḥ kriyante na anubhiḥ iti
yasya punar ittham pramāṇa su prasiddha sattākaḥ api avastu kaḥ avayavī sa pracaya viśeṣaḥ sūkṣmam ca kāraṇam anupalabhyam aṇu ādi tasya avayavi abhāvāt atat rūpa pratiṣṭham mithyājñānam iti prāyeṇa eva visaya jñānam prāptam mithyājñānam
tatas sarvam eva jñānam śabda ādi ākāreṇa sukha ādi ākāreṇa tad jñāna ākāreṇa ca upajāyate
śabdaḥ ādayaḥ ca jñāna ākāra kara avayavi tva abhimatāḥ na abhyupagamyante
sukha ādayaḥ api viṣaya tvāt avayavi pakṣāḥ eva
tathā eva jñāna ākāra kara tvāt svarūpam api mithyā iti prāptam sarvam eva mithyājñānam
tatas ca pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ api ābhāsa tvam eva tena abhupetam tayoḥ api śabda ādi viṣaya tvāt
yat api sarvajña jñānam anitya duḥkha śūnya anātmaka tva ādi viṣayam tasya api viṣaya abhāvāt tat api mithyājñānam prāptam iti svatantrasya tīrthakarasya ca aprāmāṇyam tatra tīrthakaraḥ sahadharma abhāvaḥ ca abhyupagataḥ bhavati
śabda ādi vat pramāṇa viṣaya tva aviśeṣāt
tat etat pratipādayati samyak jñānam api kim syāt viṣaya abhāvāt
yat yat upalabhyate tat tat avayavi tvena āghnātam iti jñānasya sva ākāra samarpaka tva aviśeṣāt
tat ca sva ākāra samarpakam kiñcana nā abhyupeyate iti sarvasya ātmīkasya jñānasya tena mithyātvam āpāditam
tathā ca samyak jñānam api kim syāt yad apekṣayā mithyājñānam abhisandhīyate
yadā ca avayavinam sarva pramāṇa samyak sarva jñāna siddham apahṇute tadā na samyak jñānasya viṣayaḥ sampādayitum pāryate
yadā ca na pārasyati tadā katham abhisandadhīta sarvam mithyā iti
samyak jñānam apekṣya mithyā jñānam mithyā bhāvam āsīdati āpekṣika tvāt samyak mithyā jñānayoḥ
yaḥ ca api manate nirviṣayam jñānam samyak iti tasya api svarūpa agrahaṇāt tat astitva anupapattiḥ
gṛhyate ced viṣaya tvāt avayavi mithyātvam tad mithyātvāt ca tat jñāna mithyātvam tathā tat jānam api iti satva mithyātvam uktam pūrvam eva
api ca nirviṣaya jñāna samyaktve sarva jñānasya viṣaya an abhyupagamāt nirviṣaya tvam iti samyaktvam eva prāpnuyāt
tathā api tu sarva jñāna samyaktvāt mithyā jñānam kim syāt iti vaktavyam
atha api brūyāt yat sa viṣayam iva ābhāti tat mithyājñānam yat atyanta nirviṣayam tat samyak iti
tathā api tasya astitve pramāṇa abhāvaḥ iti uktaḥ eva doṣaḥ
tasmāt avayavī samyak jñānasya viṣayaḥ iti āha tasmāt asti avayavī yaḥ mahatvāt vyavahāra āpannaḥ samāpatteḥ nirvitarkāyāḥ viṣayībhvati iti
etayā eva sa vicārā nirvcārā ca sūkṣma viṣayā vyākhyātā
tatra bhūta sūkṣmeṣu abhivyakta dharmakeṣu tat mātreṣu eva deśa kāla nimitta anubhavau acchineṣu deśa avacchinna śabdaḥ
sarvam hi vastu deśa ādibhiḥ avacchidyamānam viṣayiṇā jñātrā saṃbandhyamānam vyavahārāya kalpate
teṣu evam bhūteṣu evaṃbhūtāḥ eva deśa ādi vikalpa abhisaṃhitāḥ eva yā samāpattiḥ sā sa vicārā iti ucyate
tatas ca sa vicārāyāḥ sa vitarka a viśeṣa tvam siddham
katham iha api adhyāsa aviśeṣāt
ayan tu viśeṣaḥ śabda saṅketa artha jñāna deśa ādi sarva adhyāsāḥ sa vitarkāyām
iha punar tanmātra sūkṣma dharmeṣu śabda saṅketasya a prasiddha tvāt viśiṣṭa nāma saṅketa jñāna anadhyāsaḥ deśa ādi adhyāsaḥ ca sūkṣma viṣaya tvam vā iti sa vitarka a viśeṣa tva siddhiḥ
tatra api eka buddhi nirgrāhyam viśiṣṭam ukta deśa ādi dharma viśiṣṭam udbhūta dharma viśiṣṭam vā bhūta sūkṣmam ālambanībhūtam na tu nirviṣayam jñānam eva samādhi prajñāyām upatiṣṭhate
yadā punar sarvathā sarva prakāreṇa sarvatas sarvatra śāntāḥ ca uditāḥ ca a vyapadeśyāḥ ca ye dharmāḥ te śānta udita a vyapadeśya dharmāḥ taiḥ anavacchinneṣu
śāntaḥ iti yaḥ vyāpāram kṛtvā uparataḥ dharmaḥ
uditaḥ iti yaḥ vyāpāram ārūḍhaḥ
avyapadeśyaḥ iti na śāntaḥ na api uditaḥ na api udbhāvayat dṛśyamāna nimittaḥ
tat yathā suvarṇasya adṛśṭa aneka āśruta ākāra upajana śaktayaḥ tāḥ a vyapadeśyāḥ dharmāḥ
taiḥ anavacchinneṣu bhūta sūkṣmeṣu sarva dharma anupātiṣu sarvan dharmān anupatanti sūkṣmāṇi sarva viśeṣa ārambhaka tvāt
sarvātmakeṣu sarvebhyaḥ viṣayebhyaḥ nanta tvāt tanmātrāṇām
tatra yā samāpattiḥ sā nirvicārā iti
nirvitarkāyāḥ yat lakṣaṇam tat sarvam iha nivicārāyām draṣṭavyam
tat darśayati evaṃsvarūpam hi tat bhūta sūkṣmam anena eva sva rūpeṇa deśa kāla nimitta anubhava ādi viśeṣa virahitena sarva ātmakena sarva dharma anupātinā ālambanībhūtam eva samādhi prajñām uparañjayati
prajñā ca sva rūpa śūnyā iva artha mātrā tadā bhavati tadā nirvicārā
tasmin nirvitarka aviśeṣā nirvicārā
tat svayam eva darśayati mahat vastu viṣayā
mahataḥ vastu mahat vastu iti samāsaḥ rāhuśiraḥ iti yathā tad viṣayaḥ yasyāḥ sā mahat vastu viṣayā sa vitarkā nirvitarkā ca sūkṣma vastu viṣayā sa vicārā nirvicārā ca iti
etayā eva sa vitarka nirvitarka ākhyayā dvayyā samāpattyā sa vicārā nirvicārā ca samāpattiḥ dvayī vyākhyātā ubhayoḥ iti sa vitarka nirvitarkayoḥ etayā eva nirvitarkayā vitarka hāniḥ vyākhyātā nirvicārā vyākhyātā iti
sa vicārā ca arthāt sa vitarkayā vyākhyātā lakṣaṇasya ubhayatra samāna tvāt
uktaḥ ca viśeṣaḥ
sa vicārā nirviārā ca samāpattiḥ sūkṣma viṣayā iti uktam
tat cintyate kim asamānam avasānam sūkṣma viṣaya tvam iti
sūkṣma viṣaya tvam ca aliṅga paryavasānam
pārthivasya aṇoḥ gandha mātra sva rūpa mātra tā iti pṛthivī samīkṣayā sūkṣmaḥ viṣayaḥ
gandha mātra svarūpa mātrasya api liṅga mātram mahat tattvam sūkṣmaḥ viṣayaḥ
tatas liṅgamātrāt mahataḥ nirvṛttāni saha ahaṅkāreṇa tat mātrāṇi layam gacchati iti liṅgam layāt vā pradhānāt liṅgāt pratyāgacchanti iti liṅgam tad viparītam aliṅgam pradhānam na layam gacchati na api anyatas lutaḥ cit layāt āgacchati
sūkṣmaḥ viṣayaḥ
na ca a liṅgāt param sūkṣmam asti
sūkṣmam nāma sthūla kārya apekṣayā kāraṇam tat ca aliṅga avasānam
na ca aliṅgāt pradhānāḥ liṅgāḥ anyat sūkṣmam kāraṇam asti
nanu puruṣaḥ iti
nanu tatra puruṣasya anāśaṅkā eva kārya kāraṇa sūkṣmatayā prakramāt na eṣa doṣaḥ puruṣasya api kaiścid kāraṇa tvasya abhyupagamāt
tadā śaṅkayai eva hi etat ucyate nanu puruṣaḥ iti
satyam aliṅga ātmaka tva m aliṅgasya saukṣmyam
kutas yatas kāraṇam a lliṅgam liṅgasya
iti
nanu puruṣaḥ
api a liṅga ātmakaḥ eva
bādham na tu liṅga apekṣayā puruṣaḥ sūkṣmaḥ
kutas yat astu liṅgasya anvayi kāraṇam puruṣaḥ na bhavati sati api aliṅga ātmaka tve
kāryasya caitanyena ananvita tvāt
kiñ ca puruṣasya api bhogya tva prasaṅgaḥ
tathā ca pārārthyam sukha duḥkha moha ātmaka tvam ca nirhetuka tvam ca pradhānasya puruṣasya
tat ca sarvapramāṇa prāṇa viprakupitam iti atas āha hetaḥ tu bhavati iti
pradhāna pravṛttau bhoktṛ tvena nimittam bhavati iti arthaḥ
atas pradhānasya saukṣmyam niratiśayam vyākhgyātam
tāḥ eva sa bījaḥ samādhiḥ
catasraḥ samāpattayaḥ bahis vastu viṣayāḥ iti bahis vastu viṣaya tvam hetuḥ samīja tve
samādhiḥ api sa bījaḥ samprajñātaḥ vitarka vicāra ānanda asmitā rūpa anugamāt samprajñātaḥ iti upavyākhyātaḥ
sthūle rthe sa vitarkaḥ nirvitarkaḥ sūkṣme rthe sa vicāraḥ nirvicāraḥ iti ca upavyākhyātaḥ vitarka ādi lakṣaṇa sūtreṇa

aśuddhi āvaraṇa mala apetasya aśuddhiḥ eva āvaraṇam tat eva malam kleśa ādikam tasmāt apetasya prakāśa ātmanaḥ buddhi sattvasya rajaḥ tamobhyām anabhibhūtaḥ svacchaḥ sthiti pravāhaḥ vaiśāradyam
yadā nirvicārasya samādheḥ vaiśāradyam idam jāyate tadā yoginaḥ bhavati adhyātma prasādaḥ ātma ādi jñāna vivekaḥ
asya eva vyākhyānam bhūta artha viṣayaḥ krama anurodhī paripāṭikayā yāvat kleśa kṣayam iti krama anurodhī sphuṭam viviktataram śuddhatara ātmakaḥ prajñā ālokaḥ tayā yathāvastu jānāti
tathā ca uktam prajñā prāsādam ārudhya na śocyaḥ śocataḥ janān
bhūmiṣṭhān iva śaulasthaḥ sarvān prājñaḥ nupaśyati
iti
ṛtaṃbharā tatra prajñā
tasmin prajñā loke dhyā ātma prasāde samāhitasya yā prajñā viveka janmā tasyāḥ viveka janmanaḥ ṛtambharā iti saṃjñā bhavati
anvarthā eva sā satyam eva vibharti na tatra viparyāsa jñāna gandhaḥ api asti
prakṣīṇa sakala viparyāsa kalmaṣasya hi jāyate
jāyamānā ca viṣaya katthaṅkam amanudati
tathā ca uktam
āgamena anumānena dhyāna abhyāsa rasena ca
tridhā prakalpayan prajñām labhate yogam uttamam
iti
yogāṅga prajñām tridhā vibhajate
tatra ekaḥ bhāgaḥ śāstra ācāra upadiṣṭa artha anusārī dvitīyaḥ tasya eva yuktyā numānena vicārya āgama artha virodhi nirākaraṇa pūrvakam tat samyak upapādana paraḥ
tṛtīyaḥ tu sat āgamaḥ anumāna samyak upapanna artha ālambanasya pratyayasya anuśīlanam rasa upayogī
tat ittham tridhā prakalpayan yogī yagam labhate
sā punar ṛtambharā prajñā sāmānya puruṣa pratyaya viṣayāt anya viṣayā iti āha śruta anumāna prajñābhyām anya viṣayā
viśeṣaḥ viśeṣāṇām anantyāt na saṅketayitum śakyate
sāmānyena hi kṛta saṅketaḥ śabdaḥ
tatas ca agṛhīta viśeṣa saṅketaḥ na viśeṣam abhidhātum jñāpayitum vā śaknoti
tathā anumānam sāmānya viṣayam eva
tat api uktam eva sāmānya avadhāraṇa pradhānā vṛttiḥ iti tathā udāharaṇena ca pratipāditam yatra prāptiḥ tatra gatiḥ
yatra aprāptiḥ tatra na bhavati gatiḥ iti anumānena sāmānya upasaṃhāraḥ
sā mānya mātram anumānena upasaṃhriyate tasmāt śruta anumāna viññāna viṣayaḥ na viśeṣaḥ kaścid asti
yadi evam na loka pratyakṣeṇa apareṇa bhūta sūkṣma gataḥ puruṣa gataḥ vā viśeṣaḥ prajñāyeta
na anyat ca pramāṇa traya vyatiriktam pramāṇam asti yena tad viśeṣam sañjānīmahe iti ced āha na ca asya sūkṣma vyavahita viprakṛṣṭasya vastunaḥ loka pratyakṣeṇa grahaṇam
na ca asya viśeṣasya apramāṇakasya ābhāḥ sti iti
pramāṇa avagamyamāna rūpaḥ hi rāja vīthīm adhirohati
tasmāt samādhi prajñā nirgrāhyaḥ eva viśeṣaḥ bhavati bhūta sūkṣma gataḥ puruṣa gataḥ vā
nanu ca te sūkṣma gatāḥ viśeṣāḥ pratyakṣeṇa avagamyante iti kim vastu tvāt avagamyante iti ced āgama anumānābhyām santi iti avagamyante eva
na ca niyāmakam kiṃcid asti pratyakṣeṇa eva nirgrāhyāḥ iti
na hi viśeṣāḥ hasta tala gatāḥ api sarve gṛhyante na anya vastu gata viśeṣāṇām pratyakṣa grāhya tvasya anumeya tvāt
katham evam manyate bhūta sūkṣmāt gatāḥ viśeṣāḥ pratyakṣa grāhyāḥ kasya cid kārya vastu viśeṣa tvāt gṛhyamāṇa sva pāṇi gata viśeṣa vat iti
tasmāt śruta anumāna prajñābhyām anya viṣayā sā prajñā viśeṣa artha tvāt iti
viśeṣa arthā hi sā
samādhi prajñā pratilambhe yoginaḥ prajñā kṛtaḥ saṃskāraḥ navaḥ jāyate
prajñā hi saṃskāra ārambhiṇī iti siddham
prajñā abhinavba tvāt tad saṃskāraḥ pratyagrataraḥ jñyate iti viśeṣaḥ
prajñānava tvam tu tasyāḥ sāmānya anya viṣaya tvāt
tat jaḥ saṃskāraḥ nya saṃskāra pratibandhī ṛtumbhara prajñā prabhava saṃskāraḥ vyutthāna saṃskāra āśayam anyam bādhate viśiṣṭi artha artha viṣaya prabhava tvāt pratibandhnāti
ā mokṣāt śete iti saṃskāra āśayaḥ
vyutthāna saṃskāra abhibhavāt vyutthāna saṃskāra āśayasya samadhi prajñā saṃskāreṇa abhibhavāt tad prabhavāḥ vyutthāna saṃskāra prabhavāḥ pratyayāḥ na bhavanti
pratyaya nirodhe vyutthāna pratyaya nirodhe samādhiḥ samprajñātaḥ iva upatiṣṭhate
tatas samādhi jā prajñā tatas prajñā kṛtaḥ saṃskārāḥ iti evam navaḥ saṃskāra āśayaḥ vardhate
tatas ca prajñā tatas ca saṃskārāḥ iti
atra āha samādhi prajñā bhavaḥ saṃskāra āśayaḥ cittasya adhikāra pravṛtti hetuḥ pratyaya prabhava tāt vyutthāna prabhava saṃskāra āśaya vat iti tathā citta saṃskāra tvāt ca iti
tat etat darśayati katham asau saṃskāra āśayaḥ cittam sa adhikāram saṃskāra upetam na iti
na eṣa doṣaḥ tad viroshi tvāt
katham te saṃskārāḥ kleśa kṣaya hetu tvāt cittam adhikāra viśiṣṭam na kurvanti
vyutthāna pratyaya prabhavānām hi saṃskārāṇām avidyā ādi kleśa hetu tvāt citta saṃskāra abhimukha bhāva kāraṇa tā
tad virodhi pratyaya prabhava tvāt tu na samādhi ja pratyaya janmanām saṃskārāṇām adhikāra ābhimukhya nimitta tā
kim ca cittam ca te sva kāryāt saṃskāra abhimukha vṛttibhyaḥ vasādayanti viramayanti
khyāti paryavasānam hi
puruṣa khyātiḥ ca jātā saṃskāraḥ ca bhavati iti viruddham
yaḥ hi vigata tṛṣṇā samuāyaḥ na asau pānīyam pipāsati
etāvat eva cittena puruṣasya karaṇīyam
na hi kaścid kṛtam karaṇīyam cikīrṣati
kim ca tasya api nirodhe sarva nirodhāt nirbījaḥ samādhiḥ iti
iti śabdaḥ parisamāpti arthaḥ
tasya api samādhi prajñā prabhavasya saṃskārasya abhinavasya nirodhe apiśabdāt saṃskāra kāraṇasya samādhi prajñāyāḥ api nirodhe sarva nirodhaḥ bhavati
uktam eva upāya dvayam para vairāgya virāma pratyaya abhyāsa ākhyam tad nirodhasya
kim punar tat sarvam ṛtambhara prajñā janita saṃskāraḥ samādhi prajñā nirodhī yathā eva tām samādhi prajñām ṛtambharām niruṇāt hi tathā eva ātmanā saha ātma sajātīyānām sva kāraṇa prajñkṛtānām saṃskārāṇām api pratibandhī nirodhāt bhavati
kasmāt nirodha jaḥ saṃskāraḥ yasmāt samādhi prajñāyāḥ tad janmanaḥ ca saṃskārasya nirodhe nirodhakaḥ samādhi prajñā janita saṃskārāt anyaḥ jāyate sa ca api yatas samādhi prajñām tad janita saṃskārān ca a tiraskṛtasya na janma pratipadyate tasmāt sa nirodha jaḥ saṃskāraḥ samādhi jān saṃskāran bādhate iti
katham punar asau nirodha jaḥ saṃskāraḥ sti iti gamyate vidyamane api sa bādhakaḥ bhavati iti āha nirodha sthiti kāla krama anubhavena iti
nirodhasya sthitiḥ tasyāḥ kālaḥ sa ca kālaḥ krameṇa anubhūyate yatas abhivardhate tasmāt tena nirodha sthiti kāla krema anubhavena nirodha citta kṛtam nirodha avastha citta kṛtam saṃskāra astitvam anumeyam
vyutthāna nirodha samādhi prabhavaiḥ vyutthāna samādhi prabhavaiḥ nirodha samādhi prabhavaḥ ca saha kaivalya bhāgīyaiḥ saṃskāraiḥ cittam avasita adhikāra tvāt svasyām prakṛtau sva kāraṇe smitāyām ahaṅkāre pravilīyate pratyastam eti
tasmāt te khyāti nirodha jnmānaḥ saṃskārāḥ yasmāt cittasya adhikāra virodhinaḥ na sthiti hetavaḥ bhavanti iti
yasmāt avasita adhikāram saha kaivalya bhāgīyaiḥ saṃskāraiḥ cittam yam puruṣam prati carita prayojanam tasmāt nirvartate
tasmin vinivṛtte puruṣaḥ sva rūpa mātra pratiṣṭhaḥ kevalaḥ muktaḥ iti ucyate citta vṛtti nivṛttiḥ eva muktiḥ iti
iti śrī govinda bhavgavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī śaṅkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śrī pātañjala yoga śāstra sūtra bhāṣya vivaraṇe
prathamaḥ samādhi pādaḥ
atha idānīm dvitīyaḥ sādhana pādaḥ ārabhyate
kaivalyasya sādhanam samyak darśanam
yoga sādhanāni ca yoga dvāreṇa samyagdarśana sādhanāni eva
tāni ca prādhānyena asmin pāde pratipādyante iti sādhana pādaḥ iti ucyate
tathā yoga sādhana anuṣṭhāna pravṛttasya ānuṣaṅgika vibhūteḥ prādhānyena pratipādanāt vibhūti pādaḥ iti ucyate tṛtīyaḥ tathā sakala yoga aiśvarya vibhūtibhyaḥ viraktasya sarva upasaṃhāra dvāreṇa kaivalyasya prādhānyena pradarśanāt kaivalya pādaḥ iti ucyate caturthaḥ
tathā samādhiḥ prādhānyena ādau iti prathamaḥ samādhi pādaḥ iti ucyate
tat etat āha uddiṣṭaḥ samāhita cittasya yogaḥ iti karmaṇi acittasya iti arthaḥ
maitrī karuṇā ādi bhāvanā ādi upā khyā ya labdhi sthiti padasya yoginaḥ para vairāgya virāma pratyayya sādhanaḥ nirbījaḥ samādhiḥ uddiṣṭaḥ
katham vyutthita cittaḥ api yoga yuktaḥ syāt iti
vikṣipta cittaḥ api katham nāma samādhi yogyaḥ bhavet iti atas idam ārabhyate
tapa ādi sādhanam anukramyate tapaḥ svādhyāya īśvara praṇidhānāni kriyā yogaḥ
nanu ca tapaḥ svādhyāya īśvara praṇidhānāni niyameṣu vadiṣyamāṇāni kim artham iha ucyante
nanu ca etat eva prayojanam yat uktam vyutthita cittaḥ api yoga yuktaḥ syāt iti
na etat asti yatra niyamāḥ paṭhyante tatra eva idam prayojanam sidhyati
atha kleśa tanūkaraṇa artham iti ced tasya api tatra eva abhidhānāt
yathā yogāṅga anuṣṭhānāt aśuddhi kṣaye iti
aśuddhiḥ ca kleśa ādiḥ
samdhi bhāvanā artham ca yogāṅga anuṣṭhānam āmnāyiṣyate eva
yathā īśvara praṇidhānāt iti
tasmāt iha tapa ādi samāmnānam anarthakam
na yogāṅga anuṣṭhānasya samyagdarśana upāyasya samyagdarśana pūrva tva pratipādana artha tvāt
sarvāṇi ca yogāṅgāni samyagdarśana upāya tvāt samyagdarśana prāk kālāni
teṣām ca niyama rka deśaḥ iha paṭhitaḥ nidarśanāya
yadi api upāya tvāt eva prāk kāla tvam arthāt siddham tathā api spaṣṭa tvam evam sati syāt iti
nanu ca evam api prāk samyagdarśanāt anantaram paṭhitavyam ucyate na samyagdarśanasya eva sākṣāt kleśa ādi pratipakṣa tvāt
avidyā hi samasta anartha mūlam
sā ca sākṣāt pratyanīka bhūta samyak darśanena nirvartyate
tapa a adeḥ tad anantram pāṭhe sati avidyā samyak darśanayoḥ vyavadhānam bhavet
tatas abhiśaṃkena kim avidyāyāḥ tapāadiḥ sākṣāt pratipakṣaḥ kim vā samyak darśanam eva iti
kim ca viṣayaḥ ca prathamam darśanīyaḥ samyagdarśana śāstrasya
sa ca kleśa karma vipāka āśaya abhibhūtaḥ puruṣaḥ
yathā roga ārtaḥ cikitsā śāstrasya viṣayaḥ
tapa ādeḥ tad anantaram samāmnāne viṣaya viṣayiṇau vyavadhīyeyātām tatas ca ayam viṣayaḥ yat ca viṣayi iti na vivicyeta
pāda ādau ca samyak darśana upāya tvam ca pratipāditam bhavati prathama pāda sambandhaḥ ca vyākhyātaḥ syāt samāhita cittasya yogaḥ uddiṣṭaḥ vyutthita cittaḥ api tapa ādi sādhanaḥ katham yoga yuktaḥ syāt iti
kiñca samādhi bhāvana kleśa tanūkaraṇa artha tvañ ca tapa ādīnām darśayitavyam
nanu parastāt eva etat vakṣyati śama ādhi siddhiḥ iśvara praṇidhānāt
kāya indriya siddhiḥ aśuddhi kṣayāt tapasaḥ
iti evam
pratyeka sādhanānām siddhim ca vakṣyati
na etat asti siddhānām iha tatra sādhana stuti artham anuvādāt
atra hi tādarthyam ucyate
tathā ca āha śama ādhi bhāvanā arthaḥ kleśa tanūkaraṇa arthaḥ ca
iti
tatra hi anūdyante sādhana stutaye
samprati sūtra akṣarāṇi vyākhyāyante tapaḥ ca svādhyāyaḥ ca īśvara praṇidhānam ca tapaḥ svādhyāyaḥ īśvara praṇidhānāni
tāni eva kriyā rūpaḥ yogaḥ
tapa ādi kriyā ca yoga artha tvāt yogaḥ iti ucyate
citta dharmaḥ hi samādhiḥ yogaḥ
tad arthaḥ ca ayam kriyā yogaḥ
tasmāt anena kriyā yogena yogī iti
tapaḥ iti kṛcchra cāndrāyaṇa ādi śīta uṣṇa ādi dvandva saha tvam
svādhyāyaḥ praṇavasya mokṣa śāstrāṇām ca upanisad prabhṛtīnām pavitrāṇām japaḥ
īśvara praṇidhānam kriyāṇām parama gurau īśvare samarpaṇam
tāsām vā phala saṃnyāsaḥ parameśvare saṃnyasanam
katham punar citta samādhānam prati viprakṛṣṭasya kāya kleśa ādi rūpasya tapasaḥ yoga tvam svādhyāya īśvara praṇidhānayoḥ tu yuktam antaraṅga tvāt yoga tvam iti tad artham āha na atapasvinaḥ yogaḥ sidhyati iti
śarīra ādi poṣaṇa abhirata cittasya atyanta śarīra ādi ātma tva darśinaḥ sukumārataraṃmanyasya na yogaḥ sidhyati iti tapasaḥ upādānam
kim ca anādi vāsanā citrā viṣaya grahaṇa vāsanābhiḥ anādi kālabhiḥ uparacita vicitra bhāvā tathā pratypasthita viṣaya jālā vartamāna kālāḥ viṣayāḥ eva jālam tena ca vartamāna viṣaya ākhyena jālena ānāyena jhaṣan iva cittam a cuddhiḥ pāśayati yā sā pratyupasthita viṣaya jalā satī yasmāt tapasā vinā sambhedam vināśam āpadyate a sambhinna aśuddheḥ cittasya kutas samādhiḥ iti tad sambhedanāya ca tapasaḥ upādānam
tat ca tapaḥ citta prasādanam samādhi antaraṅgam a bādhamānam anena āsevyam iti yogāḥ manyante
citta prasāda artha tvāt tapasaḥ tam eva ced bādheta tādarthyam eva hīyate
sa hi kriyā yogaḥ kim arthaḥ iti tasya pārārthya pratipādana artham āha samādhi bhāvanā arthaḥ kleśa tanūkaraṇa āyaḥ ca
katham punar ubhaya artha tvam iti āha sa hi āsevyamānaḥ samādhim bhāvayati
yoga aṅga sahitaḥ samādhim bhāvayati kleśāḥ ca tanū karoti
vakṣyati ca yogāṅga anuṣṭhānāt aśuddhi kṣaye jñāna dīptiḥ viveka khyāteḥ
iti
tat etat āha tanūkṛtān kleśān prasaṃkhyanena kleśa tanūkaraṇāt sañjāta samyak darśana śīlanena dagdha bīja kalpān bījāni iva dagdha prasava śaktīn atas eva aprasava dharmiṇaḥ avidyamānaḥ prasavaḥ yeṣām te aprasavāḥ aprasavāḥ ca te dharmiṇaḥ ca iti aprasava dharmiṇaḥ sarva bīja ādiṣu vā draṣṭavyam tān aprasava dharmiṇaḥ kariṣyati prasava śakti rahitān kariṣyati
teṣām tanūkaraṇa anujanmā punar kleśaiḥ a parāmṛṣṭā satva puruṣa anya tā mātra khyātiḥ samāpta adhikārā prajñā pratiprasavāya kalpiṣyate saṃsāra abhimukha tāyai punar na kalpiṣyate
yadi api śāstra ācārya upadeśena yogāṅga anuṣṭhānāt ṛte api satva puruṣa anya tā mātra khyātiḥ upajāyate tathā api na kleśa adharma ādīn atīva a tiraskṛtya sā jāyata iti punar punar kleśa ādibhiḥ parāmṛśyate iti etat darśayati punar kleśaiḥ a parāmṛṣṭā id anena
ke te kleśāḥ sva rūpeṇa kiyantaḥ vā saṃkhyayā iti saṃkhyā sva rūpa pratipādana artham sūtram praṇīyate avidyā asmitā rāga dveśa abhiniveśāḥ kleśāḥ eṣām ekaikasya lakṣaṇam sūtraiḥ eva vyākhyāyiṣyate iti na vyākhyeya tve yatnaḥ kriyate vyākhyeyam tu etāvat eva
yathā pramāṇa viparyaya vikalpa ādayaḥ paraspara bhinnāḥ na tathā kleśānām viparyayāt bhedaḥ
kintarhi viparyayasya eva ete bhedāḥ iti
kasmāt viparyaya bhāva bhāvi tvāt iti etat āha pañca viparyayāḥ iti arthaḥ
nanu ca yathā vṛtti bheda vyākhyāne pramāṇa vṛtteḥ pratykṣā anumāna āgamāḥ pramāṇāni iti tridhā bhedaḥ tatra eva vyākhyātaḥ tathā kasmāt tatra eva asya viparyayasya api bhedaḥ pañcadhā na upavyākhyātaḥ citta vṛtteḥ eva ca viparyayaḥ iti uktam
tathā ca udāhata ṃśat viṣayeṇa eka candra darśanena dvi candra darśanam bādhyate iti
na eṣa doṣaḥ kleśānām avṛttika tvāt
na hi kleśāḥ pratyaya mātrāḥ pratyaya mātrāḥ hi vṛttayaḥ
kleśāḥ tu cittasya malam yathā cakṣuṣaḥ timiram
kleśa mala viyoge cittasya viparyaya pratyaya abhāvāt
yadi hi pratyayaḥ eva viparyayyaḥ tadā yathā kleśa nirodhe api yoginaḥ smṛti pramāṇa pratyayāḥ bhavanti tathā viparyayaḥ api bhavet
na tu viparyayaḥ kṣīṇa kleśānām
tasmāt cakṣuṣaḥ iva ayathā artha grahaṇa nimittam pratyayasya malam viparyayaḥ iti ucyate
tat punar pratyaya vyatirekeṇa pratipattum ākhyātum ca aśakyam iti pratyayena eva ākhyāyate viparyayaḥ vṛttiḥ iti
tathā ca vṛttayaḥ kliṣṭa akliṣṭaḥ ca iti kleśena viśeṣitāḥ
na ca vṛttibhiḥ eva vṛttīnām viśeṣaṇam yuktam
tathā kleśa hetukāḥ iti ca vyākhgyātam
na ca vṛttayaḥ eva vṛtti hetukāḥ iti yuktam
tasmāt ca avṛtti tvāt vṛtti bheda tvena na tatra kleśāḥ vyākhyātāḥ
tathā ca uktam iti kleśānām na vṛtti tvam mala tvam eva iti abhiprāyeṇa
abheda upacāreṇa tu pratyayena sāmānādhikaraṇyam yathā dhūmaḥ malaiḥ agnim tathā jñānam etena iti
tathā eva atra api
pratyaya viparīta tvam āha te spandamānāḥ ityādinā
spandamānāḥ pratyaya dvāreṇa udbhāsamānāḥ na hi svatas teṣām calanam asti vastra ādi rāga vat
guṇa adhikāram draḍhayanti guṇānām adhikāram pravṛttim sam kartavya tvam sthirīkurvānti
na hi teṣu parispandamāneṣu kartavya tā śūnyam cittam bhavati
parīṇāmam avasthāpayanti punar punar pariṇamayanti iti yāvat
kārya karaṇa srotaḥ unnamayanti śarīrasya karaṇa ādīnām cakṣuḥ ādīnām pravṛtti srotaḥ
katham iti āha paraspara anugraha tantrī bhūtvā avidyā ādayaḥ itaretara nimitta naimittika bhāvena iti
kim ca karma vipākān ca abhinirvartayanti
karma trividham tad vipākān ca jāti āyuḥ bhogān iti
avidyā kṣetram uttareṣām prasupata tanu vicchinna udārāṇām
katham asmitā ādayaḥ viparyayāḥ iti tat pradarśayate sūtreṇa eva
avidyā kṣetram prasava bhūmiḥ ātma lābha kṣetram yathā pṛthivī tṛṇa latā gulm a vīrudhām sva ātmanaḥ na atiriktānām evam avidyātaḥ viparyayāt a vyatiriktānām asmitā ādīnām caturṇām ekaikaśas prasupta tanu vicchinna udāra tayā catur vikalpānām prasava bhūmiḥ avidyā
viparyaya pratyayāḥ hi tām āśritya ātmānam pratilabhante
tasmāt acidyā eva asmitā ādi catuṣṭaya rūpeṇa vipariṇamate
tatra kā prasuptiḥ iti
asmitā ādīnām prasuptiḥ nāma dharmaḥ ucyate na avidyāyāḥ
kāraṇa tvāt
sarva asmitā ādi vikalpeṣu anugamāt sarvadā prabuddhā eva sā na prasuptā
prasvapne vyavahāra abhāvāt
asmitā ādīnām anyatamasya prasuptau anyatamasya avasthānam avaśyam eva
anyathā kleśa antarasya udbhavaḥ eva na syāt
tasmāt asmitā ādīnām eva caturṇām prasupta ādi catur vikalpa tvam
cetasi śakti mātra pratiṣṭhānam iti asya vyākhyānam karoti bīja bhāva upagamaḥ iti
yathā bījam sat eva an aṅkurībhavat api bhūmi gatam tiṣṭhati tathā cetasyā asmitā ādayaḥ śakti rūpeṇa anabhivyakta svarūpa aṅkurāḥ vyavatiṣṭhante
tasya prabodhaḥ iti tasya kleśasya asmitā ādeḥ prabodhaḥ udbhavaḥ ālambane viṣaye sammukhibhāvaḥ sva vyañjaka añjanasya
tatra etat syāt sarvadā eva kleśasya bīja bhāva upagamaḥ prabodhaḥ ca niyamena syāt iti
tatas āha prasaṃkhyānavataḥ samyak darśana abhyāsavataḥ adagdha kleśa bījasya saṃmukhībhūte api ālambane na asau bīja bhāva upagamaḥ
dagdhasya dagdha tvāt eva kutas punar prabodhaḥ udbhavaḥ
vidyamānasya hi bījasya kṣiti jala ādi saṃyoga nimitta prāptau aṅkurī bhāvaḥ na dagdha bīja śakteḥ tathā kleśasya api
yadi evam eṣā pañcamī kasmāt avasthā na uktā iti na asādhāraṇa tvāt
na hi sarva dehinām sādhāraṇī pañcamī kleśa avasthā
yoginaḥ eva hi sā tatas nāmnā āyate
katham vā asādhāraṇī iti tatas āha tatra eva sā samyak darśana abhyāsavatī eva dagdhā na anyatra
kṣīṇa kleśaḥ kuśalaḥ caram adehaḥ iti samyak darśane ucyate yogī
tatra eva sā dagdha bīja bhāvā pañcamī kleśa avasthā
satām kleśānām tadānīm tagdham bīja sāmarthyam
yathā vidyamānānām yava ādi bījānām bharjitānām bīja sāmarthyam dagdham
viṣayasya sammukhī bhāve api na bhavati eṣām prabodhaḥ samyak darśinaḥ saṃskāra śeṣa avastha tva diṣoḥ iva lakṣya vimuktasya
uktā prasuptiḥ
kiñ ca dagdha bījānām ca kleśānām aprabodhaḥ yoginaḥ uktaḥ iti
tanu tvam idānīm ucyate pratipakṣa bhāvanā upahatāḥ pratipakṣasya śarīra ādi avadya darśana ādeḥ bhāvanayā upahatāḥ abalīkṛtāḥ manda prabhāvāḥ kleśāḥ tanavaḥ ucyante
tathā vicchidya vicchidya artha antara upajana kāla antarāleṣu sva ātmānam a pradarśayantaḥ tena tena ātmanā yena rūpeṇa pūrvam upalabdhāḥ tena eva ātmanā samudācaranti punar udbhavanti iti vicchinnāḥ
yadi vā vicchidya vicchidya viccheda kāle te vyaktena ātmanā sva rūpeṇa pūrva uttara kāla vat na samudācaranti
tatra udāharaṇam katham rāga kāle krodhasya adarśanāt
na hi rāga kāle krodhaḥ samudācarati
kutas rūpa ari śayānām vṛtti ari śayānām ca virodhāt
sa hi rāga udayāt tirobhūtaḥ nyena avyaktena ātmanā vartate iti vicchinnaḥ
tathā rāgaḥ ca kvacid dṛśyamānaḥ na viṣaya antare nā asti
kutas viṣaya virodhāt atra
pūrvatra rāgeṇa virodhāt a samudācaraṇam krodhasya
atra tu viṣayāṇām anyonya virodhāt
na hi viṣaye ekasmin upajanayati rāgam viṣaya antaram api tasya eva rāgasya utpādakam
tat yathā naḥ ekasyām striyām vcaitraḥ raktaḥ iti anyāsu viraktaḥ
kin tu tatra rāgaḥ labdha vṛttiḥ yasyām raktaḥ
anyatra bhaviṣyat vṛttiḥ anyāsu strīṣu sa hi bhaviṣyat rāga vyakti viśeṣaḥ tadā prasuptaḥ tanuḥ vā iti
nanu ca rāgaḥ kacid dṛśyamānaḥ ityāddi bhāṣyam kimartham nanu rāga svabhāva ākhyānam kttham viṣaya bhedāt labdha bhaviṣyat vṛtti svabhāvaḥ rāgaḥ iti satyam tathā api prakrānta anupayogaḥ
prakrāntam hi viccheda vyākhyānam
na ca etat viccheda vyākhyānam
nā api vakṣyamāṇa udāra vyākhyā annena sambandhaḥ
tasya nirākāṅkṣa tvāt
evam tarhi pūrva śeṣaḥ eva ayam
katham evam manyate prasupta tanu udāra tva vti atirekeṇa vicchittiḥ nāma dharmaḥ eva nā asti
katham yāvat na labdha vṛttiḥ tāvat prasuptaḥ iti uktam
pratipakṣa bhāvanā upahataḥ manda pravṛttiḥ tanuḥ iti ucyate
yaḥ ca api labdha pravṛttiḥ saḥ udāraḥ iti ākhyāyate
vicchinnaḥ nāma sa bhavati yaḥ kvacid upalabdhaḥ punar upalabhyate
yathā sarasvatī srotaḥ
na hi rāga udaye krodhaḥ kvacid api dṛśyate
tasmāt nityā na vicchittiḥ nāma dharmaḥ sti
adarśanāt
atrā ucyate yadi adarśanāt vicchedaḥ nā asti tadā rāgasya kvacid dṛśyamānasya anyatra adarśanāt abhāvaḥ stu
nanu astu eva abhāvaḥ anyatra adarśanāt
na hi
kasmāt
kvacid dṛśyamāna tvāt eva
na hi viṣaya antara abhimukhaḥ na bhavati iti dharmiṇī api cetasi nā asti
na hi cakṣuṣaḥ kadācid gaja abhimukham na bhavati iti ghaṭa abhimukha pravṛtam sat na asti
ghaṭa abhimukha darśanāt eva
tat etat āha kvacid dṛśyamānaḥ na viṣaya antare na asti iti ādi
tathā krodhaḥ api rāgeṇa udbhūtena abhibhūta tvāt vicchinna darśanaḥ bhaviṣyati sarasvatī srotaḥ vat eva
sa hi viṣaya antare prasuptaḥ tanuḥ vā
tad ābhimukhyena a dṛśyamāna viśeṣa tvāt
kaḥ punar prasupti vicchedayoḥ viśeṣaḥ
yāvatā ubhayatra a darśanam a viśiṣṭam
ucyate pravṛtti darśana prabandhasya antara avirodhinā anubaddha tvāt adarśanam vicchittiḥ adagdhasya
nanu ca evam sati na hi tadā prasuptaḥ tanuḥ vā iti viruddham pravṛteḥ adarśana prabandhaḥ hi viṣaya antareṇa dṛśyate na viṣaya anta ābhimukhyasya vivakṣita tvāt
viṣaya antara ābhimukhyam nāma yaḥ rāgasya dharmaḥ sa hi tadā prasuptaḥ tanuḥ vā
na rāgaḥ sarvadā ātmanā eva rāga kāle sarva viṣayeṣu na dṛśyate
athavā vicchina udāharaṇa antara pratipādana artham eva rāgaḥ ca kvacid ityādi bhāṣyam
katham dvi prakāraḥ vicchedaḥ te
ekaḥ tāvat pravṛtta darśana prabandhasya virodhinā bhibhavāt sarvatra adarśanam
yathā darśitam rāga kāle lrodhasya adarśanāt iti
tathā yam anyaḥ viṣaya viśeṣe dṛśyamānasya eva viṣaya antare prāpti nimittasya adarśanam
yathā caitrasya ekasyām striyām raktasya anyāsu satīṣu api rāgasya adarśanam tatra labdha vṛttiḥ anyatra na dṛśyate iti āha sa hi tadā prasuptaḥ tanuḥ vā
na hi prasuptiḥ tānavam vā vivakṣyate
yathā tathā vā bhavatu
tatra adarśanam viccheda tvena vivakṣitam
viṣaye yaḥ labdha vṛttiḥ saḥ udāraḥ
nanu ca prasupta tanu vicchinnānām kārya asamarthānām na kleśa tā
na hi prasuptaḥ tanuḥ vicchinnaḥ vā prasupti vicchitti tad niyama avasthāyām kāryam kartum kṣamate
na hi ajātaḥ śatruḥ upaghātāya alam
vicchinne vā pradeśe srotasi srātum śakyam
tasmāt avidyā kṣetram uttareṣām iti etāvat eva astu
kim taiḥ akārya kṣamaiḥ prasupta tanu vicchinnaiḥ upadiṣṭaiḥ
etat āśaṃkya āha sarve ca ete na atikrāmanti iti
na hi śatruḥ prasuptaḥ janiṣyamāṇaḥ vā na apakariṣyati
kaḥ tarhi vicchinnaḥ prasuptaḥ tanuḥ udāraḥ vā kleśaḥ
na yuktam evam bhedena vacanam
ekam eva udāharaṇam astu
na ca udāra avasthāyāḥ anyatra kāryam kariṣyati
satyam evam etat
tathā api parihāraḥ ucyate kim tu viśiṣṭānām eva eteṣām aparikti ukta kleśa tva dhamakāraṇām eva vicchinna ādi tvam
vicchinna ādi avasthāyām api na apagamat apakrtṛ tva śaktiḥ iti adoṣaḥ
tad kāle kārya akṣama tvam iti ced na pratipakṣa vidhāna artha tvāt vacanasya
na hi śatroḥ a dṛśyamānasya prasuptasya janiṣyamāṇasya vā na prativighātavyam
śrūyate ca indraḥ pratipakṣa mayena diteḥ garbham bhinat iti
tatra kāraṇam svayam eva prakaṭayati yathā eva pratipakṣa bhāvanātaḥ nivṛttiḥ tathā eva sva vyañjaka añjanena viṣaya ādinā abhivyaktaḥ iti
yasmāt te punar abhivyaktāḥ punar ca tirohitāḥ punar api abhivyañjiṣyante ca tasmāt prasuta ādi avasthāḥ api pratipakṣa vidhānāya vaktavyāḥ eva kleśa tva anatikrānta tvāt
idānīm upasaṃharati sarve eva amī kleśāḥ avidyā bhedāḥ
kasmāt yasmāt sarveṣu asmitā ādiṣu avidyā pratarati udbhūtā dṛśyate
kiñca yat avidyayā vastu ākāryate prakalpate tat anuśerate tad viṣayāḥ upajāyante kleśāḥ rāga ādayaḥ
yathā strī ādi piṇḍe heye api bhogyaḥ yam iti avidyayā parikalpayā ātma abhimānam kṛtvā rajyate
dharma jñāne viparītam prarikalpya dveṣṭi
katham punar tat eva anuśerate iti yasmāt viparyāsa pratyaya kāle eva upalabhyante
itas ca avidyā bhedāḥ yasmāt kṣīyamāṇām avidyām anu kṣīyante iti
avisyā a praṇāśa anupraṇāśinaḥ hi kleśāḥ asmitāḥ ādayaḥ
na hi asatyām avidyāyām kaścid api kleśaḥ sambhavati
tatra avidyā svarūpam āha ucyate
kim punar avidyā svarūpa ākhyāne prayojanam tat svayam eva bhāṣyakṛt ākhyāsyate avidyā mūlam asya kleśa santānasya ityādinā
ajñāte ca kleśa santāna mūla svarūpe tat mūla unmūlanam na śakyam kartum iti tat svarūpam ākhyāyate
anitya aśuci duḥkha anātmasu nitya śuci sukhya ātma khyātiḥ avidyā
katham anitye kārye nitya khyātiḥ nityam iti viparyaya buddhiḥ yathā dhruvā pṛthivī dhruvā sa candra tārakā amṛtāḥ divaikasaḥ iti
nanu ca etasmāt mantrāt pṛthivī ādīnām dhru tvam pratīyate
tatra katham eṣām kārya tvam ucyate āpekṣika tvāt adoṣaḥ
manuṣya ādi apekṣayā pṛthivī ādayaḥ dhruvāḥ
kārya tvam anitya tvam ca sarva pramāṇa siddham śrutiṣu vacanāt dyaiḥ āsīt na pṛthivī na antarikṣam iti ādiṣu siddham
tathā aśucau parama bīja bhatse parama udvega kare tyanta ghṛṇā āspade kāye
katham sya bīmatsaka tvam iti āha rathānāt aśuciḥ garbhāśaya sthāna tvāt aśuciḥ
bījāt aśuciḥ śkla śoṇita bījaḥ hi kāyaḥ
upaṣṭambhāt vāta pitta śleṣma upaṣṭambhāt
teṣām ca aśuci tvam prasiddham
niṣyandāt prasveda mūtr purīpa ādi mala aja sna niṣyandāt
nidhānāt api maraṇāt
mṛta saṃbandhinām daśa aha ādi āśauca smaraṇam
nanu ca svabhāvataḥ yadi āśuciḥ kāyaḥ tasya śauca vidhānam anarthakam prāapnoti iti atas āha kāya modheya śauca tvāt iti
śāstrataḥ ādhātavyam eva śaucam asmin na svatas sti iti yāvat
yat vā karaṇāni buddhi sattva ādīni sattva ātmaka tayā śucīni ādheyāni asmin iti tad śuci tvāt asya api śaucam
buddhi sattva ādi ādheya viprayoge ca atyanta aśuci tva darśanāt
tasmāt piṇḍa tā hi aśucim viduḥ
piṇḍita grahaṇam viparyasta dhiyām śuci tva grahaṇa khyāpana artham
aśucau śuci khyātiḥ dṛśyate
viparīta cetasām
nanu eva śaśāāka lekhā kamanīyā iyam kanyā amṛta avayava nirmitā iva candram iva nismṛtā jñāyate nīlotpala patra akṣī bhāva garbhābhyām locanābhyām jīva lokam samāśvāsayantī iti kasya kena abhisaṃbandhaḥ bhavati iti
kva śarīra ādi yāthātmyam kva bhavati evam aśucau kvacid śuci viparyāsaḥ iti
etena apuṇye puṇya pratyayaḥ yathā saṃsāra mocakānām tathā eva anarthe ca artha pratyayaḥ vyākhyātaḥ yathā taskarāṇām
tathā duḥkhe sukhya khyātim vakṣyai pariṇāma tāpa saṃskāra duḥkhaiḥ guṇa vṛtti virodhāt ca duḥkham eva sarvam vivekinaḥ iti
tatra sarvasmin saṃsāre duḥkhe sukha khyātiḥ avidyā
tathā anātmani ātma khyātiḥ cetana acetateṣu gavādu ghaṭa ādiṣu bhoga adhiṣṭhāne vā śarīre puruṣa upakaraṇe vā manasi anātmani ātma khyātiḥ iti
atra ucyate kasya punar manasi anātmanu ātma khyātiḥ iti nanu manasaḥ eva khyātiḥ kim codyate yāvatā avidyā viparyayaḥ citta vṛttiḥ iti hi uktam
cittam eva prāpta caitanya upagrahaṇa rūpa tvāt ātmānam cetanam abhimanyate aham draṣṭṛ śrotṛ vā aham idam mama iti ca aviśeṣeṇa
tathā etat atra etasmin arthe uktam vyaktam avyaktam vā pradhāna ādikam śarīra indriya ādi viṣaya viśeṣa paryantam kiṃcid vyaktam ānubhāvikam kiṃcid ānumānikam āgamikam avyaktam vā sattvam ātma tvena abhipratītaḥ pratipannaḥ tasya sampadam anunandati tasya vyakta avyakta ātmakasya ātma tvena avagatasya sampadam samṛddhim vibhūtim anu nandati anu hṛṣyati ātma sampadam manvānaḥ sampannaḥ ham anayā sampadā mama eṣā sampad iti manyamānaḥ
tasya vyāpadam tasya kṣayam anu śocati mama eṣā vyāpadā aham eva iti
sa sarve eva abhimānāḥ apratibuddhim ajñaḥ iti
eṣā catuṣpadī bhavati avidyā
nanu ca apuṇye puṇya khyātiḥ puṇye apuṇya khyātiḥ iti ābhyām saha ṣaṭpadī tvam na catuṣu eva pādeṣu yathāsaṃbhavam antar bhāvāt
avidyā mūlam prabhava bījam asya kleśa santānasya abhiniveśa anta kleśānām anavarata pravartanasya
kim ca karma āśayasya ca trividhasya bhoga lakṣaṇa vipāka traya sahitasya sakalasya saṃsārasya iti arthaḥ
tasyāḥ ca avidyāyāḥ amitra goṣpada vat vastu satatvam vastu antara tvam vijñeyam
kim artham idam ucyate
yāvatā viparīta khyātiḥ iti vastu sata tvam uktam eva
ayam abhiprāyaḥ avidyā iti samāsaḥ yam tatpuruṣaḥ sa ca uttara padārtha pradhānaḥ vā syāt yathā rāja puruṣaḥ iti
yat vā pūrva padārtha pradhānaḥ ardhapiṣpalī iti
tatra yadi pūrva padārtha pradhānaḥ tadānīm vidyāyāḥ iti yatra eva vidyā prasaṅgaḥ vṛtti sāmānyāt tatra eva smṛtya vṛtti antara ādau pratītiḥ iti anirdhārita viśeṣa tvaḥ ṛthaḥ prajñayeta
yā tu viparīta khyātiḥ pūrva uktā avidyā iti sā pāribhāṣikī syāt
tatas kaḥ doṣaḥ syāt avidyā śabda śravaṇe sandehaḥ syāt
kim prasiddhaḥ eva śabda arthaḥ paribhāṣitaḥ śāstra saṃvyavahāra artham yathā loke yeṣu artheṣu prasiddhani padāni tāni sati sambhave tad arthāni eva sūtreṣu iti avagantavyam
iti
atha āśabda arthaḥ eva yathā i kaḥ guṇa vṛddhī DuNF
iti
tatas ca aniścite padārthe na avidyā śabdena vyavahāraḥ kriyeta
atha uttara padārtha prādhānyam samāna adhikaraṇa tvāt nīlotpala vat tatra api nīlotpala śabda artha ayoḥ avirodhāt viśeṣya viśeṣaṇa bhāvena saṃbandhaḥ yuktaḥ
iha nañā nivṛttiḥ ucyate
vidyā śabdena api vidyā
tatra yadi uttara padasya artham pradhānam prati guṇa bhūtaḥ nañ tasya eva uttara padārthasya abhāvam kuryāt tadā tat guṇa tvam eva hīyate
na api itarasya prādhānyam
yaḥ hi kiñcid nirvartayitum anuprasthitaḥ nirvartyam eva vyāpādayet na tasya nirvartyam prati guṇa tvam
na api nirvartyasya pradhāna tā tadvat
tasmāt pradhāna vaśa vartinā guṇena bhavitavyam iti vidyāyām eva iti kevalaḥ nañ nitya anuvādī iti vidyā mātram pratīyeta
tat etat evam kṛtvā ucyate
tasyāḥ ca amitra goṣpada vat vastu sata tvam vijñyetam iti
yathā amitraḥ na mitra abhāvaḥ yathā pūrva padārtha prādhānye ardhapippalī iti
na mitrāmātram
yathā uktam uttara padārtha prādhānye pradhāna vaśa vartinā guṇena bhavitavyam na pradhāna vināśena iti
tathā ca uktam a brāhmaṇam ānaya iti ukte brāhmaṇa mātrasya ānayanam prāpnoti iti nañ vārtike

evam amitraḥ iti
evam avidyā ādi
yathā vā agoṣpadam na goṣpada abhāvaḥ na goṣpada mātram kin tu deśaḥ eva tābhyām goṣpada abhāva goṣpada mātrābhyām anyat vastu antaram
katham evam
yāvatā goṣpada mātram tad abhāvaḥ ca śrūyate ucyate atas eva prayoga sāmarthyāt atyanta a goṣpada artha pratītiḥ
katham nañaḥ tāvat bhāva viruddhaḥ rthaḥ yena ca saha prayujyate tat abhāvam āha
tatas ca a goṣpadam iti goṣpada prasaktaḥ rthaḥ goṣpada mātram goṣpada viruddhaḥ ca iti trayaḥ rthāḥ pratibhānti
tatra yadi goṣpada mātram bhavet tadā nañaḥ prayogaḥ narthakaḥ eva
anya abhāva anuvādī ced goṣpade nañ syāt evam api anarthakaḥ eva
atha goṣpada prasaṅga yuktaḥ rthe tathā api nañ mukhye rthe pravṛttaḥ syāt gobhiḥ atyanta āsevita tvasya an ukta tvāt
yatas sevita tve bhaviṣyati api triṣu api kāleṣu śabda prayogaḥ yuktaḥ syāt
mukhyaḥ ca arthaḥ nāma sa bhavati yatra gobhiḥ sevitam na bhūtam na vartate na api bhaviṣyati
tasmāt sati sambhave nañ arthaḥ saḥ eva yuktaḥ iti na sevita prasaṅgaḥ nā api sevita mātraḥ iṣyate
go sevita viruddhaḥ eva deśaḥ goṣpada śabdena abhidhīyate
katham punar nīlotpala vat viśeṣya viśeṣaṇa bhāvaḥ ekasya bhāva abhāvayoḥ virodhāt
tat abhāva pratipādana mātreṇa saṃvyavahāra anupapatteḥ yasmin vastuni tad abhāvaḥ ucyate tat eva vastu antaram pratīyate
tat uktam goṣpadam sevita a sevita pramāṇeṣu iti
atra asevita grahaṇe punar kriyāmāṇe ca bahuvrīhiḥ ayam vijñāyate avidyā māna sevitaḥ sevitaḥ iti
tasmāt evam avidyā na pramāṇam na ca pramāṇa abhāvaḥ
kin tu viparītam jñāna antaram iti
dṛś darśana śaktyoḥ eka ātma tā iva asmitā
adhunā asmitā ākhyam viparyayam ācaṣṭe dṛś darśanam upalabdhiḥ puruṣaḥ saḥ eva śaktiḥ
dṛśyate nena iti darśanam sā eva śaktiḥ antaḥkaraṇa adhyavasāya svarūpā
tayoḥ dṛś darśana śaktyoḥ upalabdhi adi avasāya svarūpayoḥ eka ātma tā iva ekaḥ ca asau ānanda mahā udanvat taraṅgāyamāṇaḥ ātmā ca tasya bhāvaḥ eka ātma tā
iva śabdena atyanta vivaktatām ācaṣṭe
eka sva rūpa āpattiḥ iva asmitā kleśaḥ ucyate
yasmin aham pratyaye citta puruṣayoḥ vivekāḥ na upalabhyate saḥ yam aham pratyayaḥ asmitā ākhyaḥ kleśaḥ ucyate
pūrvatra tu puruṣa upakaraṇe antaḥkaraṇe na ātmani ātma khyātiḥ iti viparīta darśanam eva avidyā iti uktam
iha tu punar buddhi puruṣayoḥ aviśeṣa darśanam eka svarūpa āpattiḥ iva darśanam asmitā iti viśeṣaḥ
tat etat uktam bhavati bhoktṛ bhogya śaktyoḥ atyanta viviktayoḥ atyanta asaṅkīrṇayoḥ avibhāga prāptau iva satyām bhogaḥ kalpate
bhoga hetuḥ asmitā abhidhāna kleśaḥ iti arthaḥ
sati hi aham paratyaye sukhitaḥ ham duḥkhiaḥ ham iti sukha duḥkha ādi sambandhaḥ bhavati
tasmāt etat evam iti
sva rūpa pratilambhe tu tayoḥ viveke na aham mama iti sva rūpa upalabdhau satyām buddhi puruṣayoḥ kaivalyam eva avimiśra tā eva bhavati
kutas bhogaḥ iti kāraṇe hi aviśeṣa aham pratyaya ātmani sati kāryam bhogaḥ tasmin asati kāraṇe na bhogaḥ iti
na hi manasi cetanāvat tvam an adhyāropya sukhi tvam duḥkhi tvam vā śakyam pratyetum
aham pratyaya viṣayaḥ hi sukha duḥkha pratyaya adhikaraṇam
aham sukhī duḥkhī ca aham iti sāmānādhikaraṇyāt
tasmāt asmitā ākhyaḥ haṅkāraḥ bhoga hetuḥ
tathā ca uktam buddhitaḥ param puruṣam buddhitaḥ sakāśāt vibhat ktam vilakṣaṇam anyam
kaiḥ guṇaiḥ vibhāgaḥ iti āha ākāra śīla vidyābhiḥ ākāreṇa vṛtti ārūpyeṇa śīlena buddhi pratisaṃvedi tathā
vidyayā caitanya svarūpa tayā
athavā ākāreṇa śuddha ananta svarūpa tvena śīlena apariṇāmi tvāt apratisaṃkrama tvena vidyayā citi śakti svarūpa tayā
tat etaiḥ dharmaiḥ buddhitaḥ vibhāgaḥ
tathā buddheḥ api ākāreṇa sukha duḥkha moha ātmaka tvena śīlena prakhyā pravṛtti sthiti ātmanā vidyāyā sarva artha adhyavasāya ātmaka tvena puruṣāt vibhāgaḥ
ittham anyonyam ākāra vibhaktam puruṣam a paśyan kuryāt tatra tasyām buddhau ātma buddhim ātma pratyayam mohena lokaḥ iti
vidyā śīla ākāraiḥ atyanta vibhaktayoḥ buddhi puruṣayoḥ avibhāgaḥ iva tat darśanam iti anena aṃśena udāharaṇam
yat tu vihaktam a paśyan kuryāt atra ātma buddhim iti
sā pūrva uktā eva avidyā
yat vai amitāyāḥ avidyā bheda tvāt sarvam udāharaṇam iti
apaśyam kuryāt iti puruṣa sva rūpa adarśanam avidyāyāḥ asmitāyāḥ ca hetuḥ kāraṇam cittasya daṣṭṛ dṛśya uparakta tā
puruṣasya tu adarśanam draṣṭṛ tvāt eva
sukha anujanmā sukha anuśayī rāgaḥ
anu janma anu utpattiḥ yasya saḥ
sukha anuśayī tathā duḥkha anuśayī iti anyeṣām pāṭhaḥ
sukha anuśayī rāgaḥ duḥkha anuśayī dveṣaḥ iti te vyācakṣate sukham anubhavitum śīlam asya sa sukha anuśayī tathā duḥkha anuśayī iti
ubhayadhā api anujanmatā eva
tat eva tācchīlyam
tathā ca vakṣyati dharmāt sukham sukhāt rāgaḥ iti
katham iti tat āha sukha abhijñasya sukhe ābhijñānam abhijñā yasya sa sukha abhijñaḥ sukham yaḥ upalabdhavān tasya sukhya abhijñasya sukha anusmṛtiḥ pūrvaḥ sukham pūrva anubhūtam anusmaran sukhe hlāde tad sādhane vā agaru candana ādau anurajyate
tatra yaḥ sau gardhaḥ saḥ ucyate tṛṣṇā lobhaḥ rāgaḥ iti
duḥkha anujanmā duḥkha anuśayī dveṣaḥ
duḥkham uktam yena abhihatāḥ prāṇinaḥ tat upaghātāya prayatante iti
duḥkha abhijñasya iti pūrvavat hi ākhyānam
duḥkha anusmṛtiḥ pūrvaḥ duḥkhe tad sādhane vā sa taskaraḥ ādau yaḥ manyuḥ ujjihāsā uddhātum icchā krodhaḥ sa dveṣaḥ
rāgeṇa tulyam vyākhyānam sarvam
sva rasa vāhī viduṣaḥ api tathā rūḍhaḥ abhiniveśaḥ sva rasena svabhāvena cittasya avidyā mātreṇa boddhum pravartitum śīlam asya
bahateḥ akarmakasya api darśanāt yathā nadī vahati iti
atha vā sva rasam svabhāvam boddhum śīlam asya sva rasa vāhī samyak darśanasya api
api cabdāt aviduṣaḥ eva yuktaḥ maraṇa atrāsaḥ ātma uccheda māninaḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ
samyak darśanasya ātma anuccheda māninaḥ yuktaḥ iti
tathā vimṛḍhyatara buddhiṣu ātma uccheda darśiṣu ayam abhiprāyaḥ maraṇa trāsaḥ rūḍhaḥ bhiniviṣṭaḥ sthiraḥ yathā tathā iva viduṣaḥ api ātma anuccheda darśi tvāt ayuktaḥ api rūḍhaḥ
kasmāt punar ayam maraṇa trāsaḥ sva rasena eva rūḍhaḥ iti yatas sarvasya prāṇinaḥ iyam ātma āśīḥ nityā bhavati yat asau maraṇam mā anvabhūvam ucchedam mā prāpam
iyam āśiḥ vā bhūyāsam guṇaiḥ śubha ātmabhiḥ sampatsīya iti na taiḥ viyogaḥ bhūyāt iti
mūḍheṣu bhoga sampadām ātmanāḥ ca anucchedaḥ prārthanīyaḥ
kim etayā śiṣā avagamyate iti āha na ca ananubhūta maraṇa dharmakasya bhavti eṣā ātma āśīḥ iti
etayā ca ātma āśiṣā pūrva janma anubhavaḥ pratīyate
tat etat uktam bhavati na hi an anubhūte sukhe bhavati prārthanā nā api an anubhūte duḥkhe tat parihāra vāñchā bhavati iti
yena api pratyakṣa anumānābhyām ananubhūtam maraṇa duḥkham tasya api anayā ātma āśiṣā pūrvaḥ maraṇa anubhavaṅ pratīyate saḥ api na antareṇa janma iti janma anubhavaḥ
tayā pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ janma maraṇa anubhavaḥ na ādiḥ iti mataḥ
sa ca ayam abhiniveśaḥ kleśaḥ kṛmeḥ api jāta mātrasya iti
maraṇa anubhava kāraṇam ācaṣṭe pratyajṣa anumāna āgamaiḥ asambhavitaḥ maraṇa trāsaḥ uccheda dṛṣṭi ātmakaḥ ātma bhoga uccheda pratipatti hetuḥ pūrva janma anubhūtam maraṇa duḥkham anumāpayati
yathā ca ayam atyanta mūḍheṣu dṛśyate kṛmi prabhṛtiṣu kleśaḥ tathā viduṣaḥ api vijñāta pūrva apara antikasya api pūrva antikam bandhaḥ apara antikam muktiḥ
jñāta janma maraṇa antikasya vā rūḍhaḥ
kasmāt punar mūḍhasya iva viduṣaḥ rūḍhaḥ iti tatas āha samānā hi kuśa lālu śalayoḥ vidviduṣoḥ maraṇa anubhavāt iyam vāsanā maraṇa bhaya vāsanā
kleśa mūlaḥ karamāśayaḥ sati mūle tad vipākaḥ iti vakṣyate
tasmāt te kleśāḥ hātavyāḥ
hāna artham ca te pradarśitāḥ
tad avahānau ca upāyam vakṣyati dhyāna heyāḥ tad vṛttayaḥ iti
tatra na jñāyate kiṃviṣayaḥ dhyāna prayogaḥ kim dagdha bīja karma kleśa viṣayan kim sarva viṣayaḥ iti
idam sūtra īm ārabhyate te pratiprasava heyāḥ sūkṣmāḥ iti
te pañca kleśāḥ dagdha bīja kalpāḥ yoginaḥ carita adhikāre cetasi pralīne saha tena aṣtam gacchanti
etat uktam bhavati samyak darcana abhyāsa anala dagdha bīja sārarthyānām kleśānām kṛta aśeṣa puru sa prayojanasya cetasaḥ pratiprasavena eva pralayena eva pralaya utpatteḥ na dhyāna sādhana apekṣā
na hi dagdham dāham apekṣate piṣṭam vā peṣaṇam iti
cetaḥ tu sādhita pruruṣa artha tvāt
sthiti prayonana abhāvāt ca svayam eva nirvartate
kīdṛśānām punar dhyāna ādi sādhana aprekā iti atas ucyate sthitānām tu bīja bhāva upagatānām iti
dhyāna heyāḥ tad vṛttayaḥ
kleśānām yāḥ vṛttayaḥ sthūlāḥ tāḥ kriyāḥ yogena tapaḥ svādhyāyaḥ īśvara praṇidhāna ākhyena sthūla pratipakṣeṇa tanūkṛtāḥ pūrvam
tatas idānīm tanūkaraṇāt bīja śakti avasthāḥ prasaṃkhyānena samyak darśana śīlanataḥ naipuṇa viśeṣeṇa dhyānena mahatā balīyasā pratipakṣeṇa hātavyāḥ tatas api yāvat sūkṣmīkṛtāḥ
kim uktam bhavati yāvat dagdha bīja kalpāḥ yāvat nirbījīkṛtāḥ iti
tat kim iva iti yathā vastrāṇām sthūlaḥ malaḥ pūrvam nirchūyate pañcāt sūkṣmaḥ malaḥ snehana ādi nimittaḥ yatnena ca upāyena kṣāra ādi viśiṣṭa upāyena apanīyate tathā su alpa pratipakṣāḥ tapaḥ svādhyāya īśvara praṇidhāna yama niyama ādi yoga aṅga anuṣṭhāna ādi pratipakṣāḥ sthūlāḥ vṛttayaḥ kleśānām
sūkṣmāḥ tu mahā pratipakṣāḥ iti
sūkṣmāḥ bīja śakti apekṣāḥ iti
kim artham punar kleśa hānāya prayatate iti āha yatas kleśa mūlaḥ karma āśayaḥ dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa janma vedanīyaḥ
kleśāḥ avidyāḥ ādayaḥ mūlam janma kāraṇam yasya karma āśayasya sa kleśa mūlaḥ karma āśayaḥ iti
ā karma phala pradānāt antaḥkaraṇe śete iti karama āśayaḥ śukla kṛṣṇa ātmakaḥ
dṛṣṭam ca adṛṣṭam ca dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭe janmanī tayoḥ vedanīyam anubhavanīyam phalam yasya sa dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa janma vedanīyaḥ karama āśayaḥ
yaḥ dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa karma anubhavitavya phalaḥ karamāśayaḥ sa kleśa mūlaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ
yasya puṇya auṇya rūpasya karma āśayasya yasmin janmani niṣpattiḥ tasya tasmin eva janmani vedanīyam phalam sa dṛṣṭa janma vedanīyaḥ yasya tu janmāntare vedanīyam phalam saḥ dṛṣṭa janma vedanīyaḥ karma āśayaḥ iti
bhāṣyam idānīm vyākhyāyate tatra puṇya apuṇya karma āśayaḥ lobha krodha moha prabhavaḥ iti kleśa mūla tvam tasya ācaṣṭe
puṇya karma āśayaḥ lobha prabhavaḥ yathā svarge vā atra vā śubham phalam anubhaiṣyāmi iti krodha prabhavaḥ yathā viśvāmitrasya ambāyāḥ ca
moha prabhavaḥ yathā draupadyāḥ kumbhakarṇasya ca
apuṇya karma āśayaḥ api lobha vrabhavaḥ yathā carmaṇī dvīpanim hanti kuñjaram hanti dantayoḥ
karṇasya śāstra jñāna lobhāt aniṛta vacane
krodha prabhavaḥ yathā brahmahatyā
bhārate bhāve api aśvatthāmnaḥ ca
moha prabhavaḥ yathā saṃsāra mocaka ādīnām nahuṣasya ca
asmitā avidyā yoḥ lobha krodha mohaiḥ pratyekam
katham aham adhikṣiptaḥ smi iti krudhyati
aham sukham anubhaviṣyāmi iti
aham muhyāmi iti muhyati
avidyā api sarvatra eva viparīta darśana lakṣaṇā sambadhyate
na hi asatyām avidyāyām asmitā ādīnām sambhavaḥ sti
rāgaḥ tu lobhaḥ eva
dveṣaḥ tu krodhaḥ
abhiniveśaḥ vimohe eva antarbhavati
yat tu mohaḥ punar avidyā iti tat avidyā ika sāmānyāt uktam
lobha krodha mohāḥ tu paraspara nirapekṣāḥ dharma adharma utptti dvāram
tathā ca vakṣyati lobha krodha moha pūrvikāḥ iti
sa dṛṣṭa janma vedanīyaḥ ca sa lobha krodha moha prabhavaḥ karma āśayaḥ d ṛṣṭa janma vedanīyaḥ ca adṛṣṭa janma vedanīyaḥ ca
katham punar karmaṇām sva rūpa nimitta tulya tve kasyacid dṛṣṭa janma vedanayi tvam kasyacid adṛṣṭa jana vedanīya tvam ca iti āha yathā tīvra saṃyogena tīvra udyamena mantra tapaḥ samādhibhiḥ yathā prasiddha rūpaiḥ tīvra saṃvega anuṣthitaiḥ nirvartitaḥ īśvara devatā mahā ṛṣi mahā anubhāvānām ārādhanāt vā
īśvaraḥ uktaḥ devatāḥ āditya ādayaḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ bhṛgu ādayaḥ mahā anubhāvāḥ dharma jñāna nirata matayaḥ ete eva vā tat eṣām vā tīvratara ārādhana pariniṣpanaḥ sadyas paripacyate sa tasmin eva janmani
yathā nandīśvara kumārasya
tathā tīvra kleśena lobha ādi prakarṣeṇa bhīta vyādhita kṛpaṇeṣu visrambha upagateṣu mahā anubhāveṣu vā tapasmiṣu jñāna dharma nirata matiṣu tapasviṣu punar punar ābhīkṣṇyena kṛta u pakāraḥ sa ca api pāpa karma āśayaḥ sadyas paripacyate phalati
yathā nahuṣasya
loke api kṣetra bīja saṃskāra viśeṣeṇa vṛkṣa ādi phala sannikarṣaḥ prasiddhaḥ vṛkṣa āyurveda prasiddhyā
tathā kriyāsu phala sannikarṣa viprakarṣa darśanam gami paci ādiṣu tīvra manda anuṣṭhāna viśeṣataḥ
tatra puṇya karma āśayasya udāharaṇam āha yathā nandīśvaraḥ kumāraḥ manuṣya pariṇāmam svakam hitvā maheśvara ārādhana pariniṣpannena tīvratara kleśa anuṣṭhānena janmanā devatā tvena pariṇataḥ
tathā puṇya karma āśayasya udāharaṇam
sa devānām indraḥ
sa svakam pariṇāmam hitvā tīvratara moha anuṣṭhāna jane karma āśayena tiryaktvena pariṇataḥ iti
krodha ādīnām tu yathāsaṃkhyam dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa janma vedanīya tvena udāharaṇāni vyākhyātāni pūrvam eva
etena ca manda mandatara lobha ādi kleśa anuṣṭhāna janmānau puṇya pāpa karma āśayau adrṣṭa janma vedanīyau vyākhyātau loka vat eva
tatra api tāvat ucyate
tatra nārakāṇām na asti yaiḥ naraka prāpti artham eva karma anuṣṭhitam brahmahatyā guru dāra gamana ādhi lakṣaṇam teṣām nārakāṇām nāraka tvasya āśu bhāvi tvam āśritya teṣām nārakāṇām na asti dṛṣṭa janma vedanīya phalaḥ karama āśayaḥ yena phalam ārabhyate
katham punar nārakāṇām karma ārambhaḥ tiryak devatānām ca manuṣyāṇām hi karma adhikāraḥ eṣā ca karma bhūmiḥ na naraka ādiḥ iti ucyate na nahuṣa ādīnām karma darśanāt
śrūyate ca śaka rataḥ api vṛtra ādi vadhena brahmahatyā prāptiḥ yoga ādi anuṣṭhāna śravaṇam ca
yat manuṣyāṇām karma adhikāraḥ iyam karma bhūmiḥ iti tat kṣipra phala siddhi apekṣam
tat uktam kṣipram hi mānuṣe loke siddhiḥ bhavati karma jā
iti
vyāsena kīṭa upākhyāna vara smaraṇāt ca tiraścām api karma upapattiḥ
kiñ ca deha indriya ādimataḥ kriyā upapatteḥ
kriyāṇām ca kāya vāc manaḥ prabhavānām phala āra bhaka tvam kleśa pūrvaka tvāt
kṣīṇa kleśānām api samyak darśinām api na asti adṛṣṭa janma vedanīyaḥ karama āśayaḥ kleśa abhāvāt eva
na hi vīta rāgaḥ jātaḥ dṛśyate
kleśānām karma ārambhe iva karma phala ārambhe api hetu tvāt
kṣīṇa kleśasya api jñāna prāpteḥ prāk ārabdhaḥ dṛṣṭa janma vedanīyaḥ sambhavati karamāśayaḥ pravṛtti phala tvāt mukta śara vat iti
kiñ ca sati mūle tad vipākaḥ jāti āyuḥ bhogāḥ
mūlam hi karmaṇām kleśaḥ
asmin sati mūle kleśesu satsu iti arthaḥ
tasya lobha krodha prabhavasya puṇya apuṇya karma āśayasya vipākaḥ phala niṣpattiḥ a tad vipākaḥ
kim punar tat phalam iti āha jāti āyuḥ bhogāḥ
bhāṣyam satsu kleśeṣu karma āśayaḥ vipāka ārambhī bhavati na ucchinna kleśa mūlaḥ iti mūlasya vyākhyānam
tatra satsu kleśeṣu karma āśayaḥ vipāka ārambhi iti asya dṛṣṭāntam āha yathā tuṣa avanaddhāḥ śāli taṇḍulāḥ adagdha bīja bhāḥ
tuṣa avanaddhāḥ api kadācid dagdha bīja bhāvāḥ na praroha samarthāḥ bhavanti dagdha bīja bhāvāḥ api vyapanīta tuṣāḥ na prarohāya alam bhavanti
ubhayathā ca dārṣṭāntika pratipādana aṛtham dṛṣṭānta vikalpaḥ
katham tathā karṃ āśayaḥ vipāka prarohī bhavati kleśa upabandhaḥ tuṣa avanaddha śāli taṇḍula vat
na apanīta kleśaḥ na dagdha kleśa bīja bhāvaḥ vā iti
apanīta tuṣāli taṇḍula vat na vipāka prarohī
yogāṅga annuṣṭhāna kleśa kṣaya pūrva samyagdarśanānām yoginām na apnīta kleśaḥ api ā na panīta tuṣa dagdha bīja śakti śāli vat yogāṅga anuṣṭhāna praṇāli kevala samyagdarśana anala dagdha bīja sāmarthyaḥ na vipāka prarohī bhavati
tathā ca vyāsaḥ sāṃkhyānām yoginām ca prthak mokṣam darśayati
bījāni agni upadagdhāni na rohanti yathā punar
jñāna dagdhaiḥ tathā kleśaiḥ na ātmā sampadyate punar
iti
R 
tathā yogaiścaryam atikrāntaḥ yogī mucyeta iti ādi
vakṣyati ca atra api prāpta aprāpta aiśvarya yogayoḥ kaivalyam
kati prakāraḥ sau vipākaḥ iti āha sa ca vipakaḥ trividhaḥ jātiḥ āyuḥ bhogaḥ iti
tatra idam vicāryate
kim punar vicāra phalam ucyate ekaekena prāṇinā viruddha phalāni bhūyiṣṭhāni ekasmin eva janmani karmāṇi kriyante
tat yathā śarīra jaiḥ karma doṣaiḥ yāti sthāvara tām naraḥ
vācakaḥ pakṣi mṛga tām mānasaiḥ antya jāti tām
svarga arthāni ca tāvat anutiṣṭhanti
naraka prāpīṇi ca karmāṇi
tatra ekasya brahma hti ādi karmaṇaḥ neka janma kāraka tvam śrūyate śva sūkara khroddrāṇām ityādi smṛteḥ
atha viruddha deśa kāla nmimitta vipākānām karmaṇām eka janma ārambhe viruddha vipāka tādarthyam hīyeta
tatas ca tādarthya codanāḥ karmaṇām bādhyeran
atha janma ārambhi tvam karmaṇām asaṃkhyeya tvāt kenacid eva phalam ārabdham na anyaiḥ iti tatra niyama anupapattiḥ kena ārabdhaḥ kena vā na iti
tathā ca kartṛṇām karma phalam utsāha vibhaṅgaḥ syāt abhyudaya niśreyasa pravṛttiṣu
atha anyatamena ārmbhe vināśaḥ eva anyeṣām iti tathā api saḥ eva doṣaḥ kim vinaṣṭam kim ārambhakam iti aniyamāt
atha avināśe eva tathā api avaśiṣṭasya ārambha kāla abhāvaḥ mokṣa abhāvaḥ ca iti
tasmāt pravṛtti nivṛtti śāstra arthavatva pratipādana artham idam vicāryate
kim ekam karma ekasya janmanaḥ kāraṇam svarga ādi prāpti nimitteṣu bahuṣu karmasu satsu
karma anekam janma ākṣipti iti prathamā vicāraṇā
viruddha pakṣa dvaya ālambinī hi vicārāṇā ekā eva syāt
dvitīyā vicāraṇā kim anekam karma anekam janma nirvartayati viruddha phalam a viruddha phalam vā atha anekam karma ekam janma nirvartayati viruddha phalam a viruddha phalam vā
kim ca atas na tāvat ekam karma ekasya janmanaḥ kāraṇam
kasmāt bahuṣu karmasu satsu ekam eva karma janma ekam na ārabhate iti
yadi ekasya eva janma ārabhi tvam tadā anādi kāla pracitasya saṃsāra anādi tvāt ekaikena puruṣeṇa asaṃkhyeyam ekaikasmin janmani karma pracīyate
viruddha phalam a viruddha phalam ca
tatra avaśiṣṭasya janma ārambhi karma vyatiriktasya asaṅkhyeyasya aneka janma antara pracitasya karmaṇaḥ sāmpratasya ca vartamāna janma pracitasya anārabdha kāryasya phala krama aniyamāt kim pūrva janma upacita karma rāci gatasya kasyacid eva bhaviṣyat janma ārmbhi tvam āhosvit idānīntana janma karma rāśi gatasya kasyacid iti phala kramaḥ na anāśvāsaḥ lokasya
kim pūrva janma karmaṇā duṣṭena a duṣṭena vā phalam ārabdhavyam atha idānīntana karmaṇā duṣṭena a duṣṭena vā iti avisrambhāt na kaścid agnihotra ādi kurvīta
na api mokṣāya samīheta iti anāśvāsaḥ prasaktaḥ sa ca aniṣṭaḥ
idānīm prathama vicāraṇāyām dvitīyam pakṣam nirākaroti na ca ekam karma anekasya janmanaḥ kāraṇam
kasmāt ekaikasmin tāvat janmani anekam karma anuṣṭhīyate tatra ekam eva ced karma anekasya janma vipākasya janma pariṇāmasya nimittam bhavet tatas avaśiṣṭasya ārabdha kāryāt anyasya vipāka kāla abhāvaḥ prasaktaḥ sa ca api aniṣṭaḥ
phala krama aniyamaḥ ca iti pūrva doṣaḥ api
na evaṃbhūtam aniṣṭam abhyupagantavyam
yat tu brahmahatyā ādi karmaṇām ekaikasya aneka janma ārambhi tvam tasya śāstra gocara tvāt brahmahatyā ādi viṣaya tvam eva abhyupagamyate
dvitīya vicāraṇāyām idānīm prathamaḥ pakṣaḥ nirākriyate na ca anekam karma anekasya janmanaḥ kāraṇam
kasmāt evam na abhyupagamyate tat ucyate tat eva anekam janma yugam na sambhavati ekasya anīśvarasya
tatas ca krameṇa ca ācyamāne kim ekam anekam janma ārabhate iti
tathā ca pūrva doṣa anuṣaṅgaḥ sarvatra prathama doṣa anuṣaṅgaḥ phala krama aniyamāt anāśvāsaḥ iti
tasmāt evam pakṣa traya anupapattau idānīm siddhāntam upasaṃharati janma janma maraṇayoḥ antare madhye kṛtaḥ puṇya pāpa karma āśayaḥ aviruddha janma vedanīyaḥ
tasya tridhā viniyogam vakṣyati tasmāt aviruddha phalasya eva puṇya apuṇya karma āśayasya ayam ucyate
pracaya vicitraḥ tulya atulya aneka karma pracita tvāt pravcayena vicitraḥ
kiñcid karma kasyacid karmaṇaḥ pradhānam api kasya cid anyasya upasarhanam upasarhanam api pradhānam iti evam aneka sa karma śabalimnā avasthitaḥ
prāyaṇa abhivyaktaḥ yathā bīja kṣetra saṃskāra saṃyogaḥ ṅkura bhāva abhivyakti kāraṇam tathā prāyaṇam api aviruddhānām karmaṇām abhivyakti nimittam
ekapradhadṛkena ekalolībhāvena samuccitaḥ ekībhūtaḥ ekam eva janma karoti
tat ca janma tena eva karmaṇā labdha āyuṣkam bhavati
tasmin āyuṣi tyena eva karmaṇā bhogaḥ sampadyate yena janma āyuṣī kṛte
yathā yena bījena aṅkuraḥ nirvṛttaḥ tena eva phala puṣpa ādayaḥ api
tena ca karmaṇā bhoga āyuḥ nirvṛttiḥ bhavati eva iti avadhāryate
na punar anyasya āyuḥ bhoga ādi nimittasya putra paśu kāma ādi yāga ādeḥ putra āyuḥ ādi prāpteḥ hetu tvam nirākriyate
itarathā hi sarva śruti smiṛti viprakopaḥ syāt
tasmāt tena eva karmaṇā iti janma mātram ārahya kṛta kārya tvāt vinivṛtti āśaṅkā niṣedha mātram kriyate
asau karma āśayaḥ janma āyuḥ bhoga hetu tvāt trayaḥ vipākāḥ janma ādayaḥ yasya sa tri vipākaḥ abhidhīyate
ayam aikabhāvikaḥ karma āśayaḥ uktaḥ ekaḥ eva janma prayojanaḥ eka bhavikaḥ
dṛṣṭa janma vedanīyaḥ tu eka vipāka ārambhī yathā putra grāma ādi kāma yāgaḥ
dvi vipāka ārambhī vā bhoga āyuḥ hetu tvāt
yathā āyuḥ ādi kāma yāgaḥ
tri vipāka ārambhī vā nandīśvara nahuṣa vat
nanu ca nandīśvara nahuṣayoḥ dṛṣṭa janma vedanīya tvam tri vipāka ārambhi tvam ca viruddham
dṛṣṭam hi janma nindi īśvarasya manuṣya tvam
yat punar nandīśvarasya deva tvam nahuṣasya ca ajagara tvam tat dvayam api adṛṣṭam na hi manuṣya tve eva deva tvam saṃvedyam nandīśvarasya na api deva tve eva nahuṣasya ajagara tvam saṃvedyam iti katham tri vipāka ārambhi tvam ca iti
na eṣa doṣaḥ
dṛśyamāna jāti viśiṣṭam eva śarīram tayoḥ jāti antara tvena pariṇatam
na ca yathā nyeṣām dṛṣṭa jāti viśiṣṭa śarīra upamardena jāti antara upādāna niṣeka ādi nimitta apekṣayā jāti antara prāptiḥ tathā nandīśvara nahuṣayoḥ
tasmāt tri vipāka ārambhi tvam dṛṣṭa janma vedanīya tvam ca iti udāhṛtam
tatra trividhaḥ karma rāśiḥ dṛṣṭa janma vedanīyaḥ ca adṛṣṭa janma vedanīyaḥ ca
dṛṣṭa janma vedanīyaḥ tu aniyata vipākaḥ
kadācid bhoga hetuḥ iti eka vipākaḥ
kadācid bhoka āyuḥ hetu tvāt dvi vipākaḥ
kadācid jāti ātuḥ bhoga hetu tvāt tri vipākaḥ nandīśvara nahuṣayoḥ iva
adṛṣṭa janma vedanīyaḥ tu dvividhaḥ niyata vipākaḥ ca aniyata vipākaḥ ca
niyata vipākaḥ tu pradarśitaḥ tasmāt janma prāyaṇa antare kṛtaḥ iti ādinā
yaḥ tu aniyata vipākaḥ sa trividhaḥ vakṣyate
idānīm tu karma vipāka janitaḥ vāsanā rāśiḥ aparaḥ ākhyāyate kleśa karma vipaka anubhava nirvartitābhiḥ kleśa anubhavaḥ ca karma anubhavaḥ ca vipāka anubhavaḥ ca kleśa karma vipaka anubhavāḥ taiḥ nirvartitābhiḥ vāsanābhiḥ saṃskāraiḥ anādi kāla saṃmūrcchitam idam cittam citrīkṛtam iva paṭa kuḍya ādi vat sarvatas matsya jālam granthibhiḥ iva ātatam vyāptam
atha ekaikasmin janmani aneka bhava pūrvikāḥ vāsanāḥ karmaṇi vipāke ca tat bhāvena vyāpriyante
na hi vāsanāyāḥ karma vipāka anaṅga bhāve sati jāta mātrasya pṛṣadaṃś dārakasya vṛṣa yuvānam prati sphurita parikopasya avaskandanam jāghaṭīti
na ca sakṛt anubhava vāsanā mātra tayā tena śakyam bhavitum
yaḥ tu ayam karama āśayaḥ yaḥ tu ayam janma prāyaṇa antare kṛtaḥ pradhāna upsarjanī bhāvena tri vipāka ārambhī eṣaḥ eva aika bhavikaḥ uktaḥ
na dṛṣṭa janma vedanīyaḥ na api aniyata vipaktiḥ adṛṣṭa janma vedanīyaḥ na api ca vāsanāḥ
tāsām tāvat svarūpam ye saṃskārāḥ smṛti hetavaḥ tāḥ vāsanāḥ tāḥ ca anādi kālīnāḥ saṃsārasya kleśa karma vipaka anubhava rūpasya anādi tvāt
yaḥ tu asau ānanda mahā udanvat taraṅgāyamāṇaḥ eka bhavikaḥ karama āśayaḥ pūrva uktaḥ tasya apavādaḥ ucyate ukedeśasya
katham sa niyata vipākaḥ ca a niyata vipākaḥ ca
kaḥ sau niyata vipākaḥ yaḥ prāyaṇa abhivyaktaḥ kāryam ārabhate
saḥ eva ca eka bhavikaḥ
yaḥ tu saḥ dṛṣṭa janma vedanīya tva sāmānye sati api aniyata vipākaḥ
kasmāt niyata vipākena virodhāt
na ca ayam eka bhavikaḥ virodhāt eva
yat tu asya eka bhavika tvam uktam yaḥ tu asau eka bhavikaḥ karma āśayaḥ iti tat adṛṣṭa janma vedanīya tva sāmānyena
nanu ca yadi evam janma prāyaṇa antare kṛtaḥ puṇya pāpa karma āśayaḥ pracaya vicitraḥ pradhāna upasarjana bhāvena avasthitaḥ prāyaṇa abhivyaktaḥ ekapraghattena sammūrcchitaḥ eka janma karoti iti evamādi niyamaḥ virudhyeta
kutas prāyaṇasya sarva pūrva karma abhivyañjaka tvāt āśaya ādhāra upamardena ca āśaya antara utpatteḥ mānuṣyaka āśaya ādhāre pūrvam daivata airyagyona āśayānām samavasthānam tad ādhāra upamardana kāle ca prāyaṇe sādhāraṇe sarva karma abhivyakti kāraṇe daivatairyadyona āśayānām kasyacid eva abhivyaktiḥ na itareṣām iti na asti hetuḥ
na hi sva gocara āpannam vyaṅgyam eka deśa parityāgena abhibyanakti pradīpaḥ
atrā ucyate na etat yuktam karma ānarthakya prasaṅgāt
bahu prakārāṇi hi karmāṇi paraspara viruddhāni kriyante
yaḥ hi svarga artham karma kṛtavān saḥ eva paśu krāma ādi artham karma anuṣṭhāya punar brahmahatyām vā sthāvara ādi prāpti artham vā balavat karma anutiṣṭhet tatra naraka sthāvara ādi prāptasya na hi paśu grāma ādi lābha saṃbhavaḥ
tatas ca tad karmaṇām ānarthakyam prasajyeta
atha tatra api grāma ādi lābha sukham bhavati iti ced na hi grama kāmaḥ iti ukte grāma sukha tvam abhipretam
na hi grāma sukham prāptaḥ grāmam prāptavān
kim ca sarva śāstra viprakopaḥ ca syāt
adṛṣṭānām ca svarga naraka ādīnām sukha duḥkha mātra prasaṅgaḥ
tatas śeṣeṇa iti śṣa sadbhāva jñāpana śruti smiṛtayaḥ bādhyeran
tasmāt nityā na sarvam karma prāyaṇe bhivyajyate
atyanta viruddhānām karmaṇām ānarthakya prāpteḥ
karma śāstra ānarthakye ca mokṣa śāstre api anāśvāsa prasaṅgaḥ
abhivyañjakānām api kasyacid abhivyañjaka tvam kasyacid na iti dṛśyate vyabhicāraḥ
yathā cakṣuṣaḥ rūpa abhivyañjaka tve api caitra ulūka cakṣuṣoḥ ahar rātrayoḥ itaretara vyabhicāraḥ
ālokasya ca samāne sarva cakṣuḥ sahakāri tve na ulūka cakṣuḥ sahakāri tvam
ekasmin ca strī ādi piṇḍe sukha duḥkha mohānām sarveṣām abhivyakti nimitte api kasyacid eva abhivyaktiḥ
tatra karma ādi apekṣayā virodhāt adoṣaḥ iti ced iha api virodhāt anabhivyaktiḥ sarva karmaṇām
na ca api bīja ādhāre kṣetre upamardyamāne jala ādi nimitta saṃyoge sati api tat gatānām bījānām biruddha jātīyānām aṅkura ādi kārya ārambhi tvam
evam mānuṣyakālīna āśaya ādhāre api upamardyamāne na viruddha jātīya devatā airyagyona āśayānām sarveṣām yugapad vṛtti lābhaḥ
na ca prāyaṇam eva karmaṇām abhivyañjakam
dṛṣṭa janma vedanīyānām bhoga arthānām darśanāt
yeṣām prāyaṇam eva abhivyañjakam teṣām sarveṣām bhavatu abhivyaktiḥ iti ced na virodhāt daivata airyagyona mānuṣyaka āśayānām
prāyaṇānām ca bhūta bhaviṣyat kāla viśeṣaiḥ vi śeṣa upapatteḥ na sarva karma abhivyañjaka tvam
prāyaṇa viśeṣa śravaṇāt ca prāyaṇa bhedaḥ yathā yam yam vā api smaran bhāvam tyajati ante kalevaram iti
smaraṇa viśeṣa bhedāt prāyaṇa bhedaḥ
tasmāt nityāḥ na sarva karma abhivyañjaka tvam prāyaṇasya
anyathā viśeṣaṇa ānarthakya prasaṅgāt
na ca smaraṇa ādi viśeṣaṇena prakṛtasya anyathātvam nāśaḥ vā syāt
tad nāśa anyathātva karaṇe hi smaraṇasya prakṛta krma sahakāri tvam na syāt
svatantram hi smaraṇam syāt
tathā ca anuṣṭhita karma nairarthakyam bhavet
kim ca kalala ādi avasthāsu bhṛtānām mokṣa prasaṅgaḥ
karma anārambhāt
tāsām karma tvam api iti ced na karaṇa a vyūhāt
karaṇeṣu hi vyūhiteṣu karmaṇām vṛttilābhaḥ phala tvam ca na tadā tad vyūhaḥ upapadyate
svapna vat iti ced na
tatra api karma anabhyupagamāt
śrutiḥ ca  sa yat tatra kiṃcid paśyati an  anvāgataḥ tad SNM tena tad SINe bhavati iti  karmaṇā svapna darśana jena asambandham SAM darśayati
na kaścid svapnaiḥ aparādhavān asti
brahmahatyā ādi karaṇa darśanāt
atha skanna prāyaścitta ādi darśanāt na iti ced na retaḥ skandana nimitta tvāt prāyaścittasya
tasmāt yadi api svapna ādi avasthāyām iva kalala ādi avasthāsu phalam abhyupagamyate tathā api karaṇa vyāpāra abhāvāt svapna avasthā vat eva phala mātram tat na karma kartṛ tvam iti mokṣa prasaṅgaḥ eva garbha prasṛtānām āpatitaḥ iti
tasmāt nityāḥ na sarva karma abhivyañjaka tvam prāyaṇānām teṣām ca iti atas idam ucyate tatra adṛṣṭa janma vedanīyasya eva ayam niyamaḥ janma prāyaṇa antare kṛtaḥ iti evamādi bhāṣyeṇa tri vipāka ārambhi tva niyamaḥ uktaḥ na tu adṛṣṭa janma vedanīyasya aniyata vipākasya
kasmāt yaḥ tu adṛṣṭa janma vedanīyaḥ aniyata vipākaḥ tasya trayī gatiḥ
katham kṛtasya avipākasya vināśaḥ nāśa kālam aprāptasya eva nāśaḥ
yathā prāyaścitta ādinā pratiṣiddhasya kṛtasya nāśaḥ
pradhāna karmaṇi āvāpa gamanam pradhāna karmaṇi niyata vedanīye āvāpa āpattiḥ pradhāna karma phala a tiraskāreṇa svayam api manda mandam phalam madhyamā anupraviśya
yathā sakaleṣu taṇḍuleṣu vipaśyamāneṣu asakalāḥ api taṇḍula kaṇāḥ uptāḥ alpīyāṃsam arthyam sādhayanti eva
niyata vipāka pradhāna karma abhibhūtasya vā api avasthānam niyata vipākam yat pradhāna karma prārabdha phalam tena abhibhūtasya nyak kṛtasya viruddha deśa kāla nimitta vipāka tvāt avasthānam
yathā vijigīṣamāṇayoḥ anyatareṇa pravṛtta rājyena abhibhūtasya itarasya avasthānam deśa kāla nimitta apekṣayā
tatra kṛtasya avipakkasya nāśaḥ yathā iha eva tapaḥ svādhyāya yoga ādi lakṣaṇasya śuddhasya udayāt prāyaścitta ādi lakṣaṇasya ca kṛṣṇasya aśuddhi rūpasya hiṃṣā ādi lakṣaṇasya prāk eva vṛttilābhāt nāśaḥ
iha eva iti tu avivakṣitam
janma antare api prāc vṛtti lābhāt nāśa upapatteḥ
yathā kaunakhya ādi nimitta pāpa viśeṣāṇām kaunakhya ādi cihnaiḥ avagamya prāyaścittena nāśaḥ kriyate
tat etat tantra antara para siddhena udāharaṇena vyācaṣṭe yatra idam uktam dve dve ha vai karmaṇī śukla kṛṣṇe janmani janmani sādhakasya puruṣasya adhikṛtasya
ekaḥ rāciḥ svādhyāya ādi puṇyena kṛtaḥ puṇya kṛtaḥ apahanti itaram apuṇyena kṛtam rāśim
atha vā puṇya kṛtaḥ puruṣasya śukla karma rāśiḥ kṛṣṇa karma rāśim apahanti
tat tasmāt su accha karmāṇi svakīyāni karmaṇi śuklāni sakṛtāni kartum
kutas yatas iha eva atra eva tava śarma ukham śāntim kavayaḥ vedayante karma vipāka vibhāga jñāḥ jñāpayanti
pradhāna karmaṇi āvāpa gamanam udāharaṇena pradarśyate su alpa saṅkaraḥ alpīyān doṣa avakāraḥ
kutas sa parihāraḥ parihāra sahitaḥ
parihāram apekṣate na tu parihṛtaḥ
parihāra śakti upāya vijñāna samāna āśrayaḥ iti arthaḥ
sa pratyavamarśaḥ sa pratyavekṣaṇaḥ
katham akāryam mayā kriyate kadā nu nistariṣya abhi etat na punar kariṣyāmi iti āpadi pravṛttasya akāryam kuvataḥ prāṇa sthiti ādi nimittam
kuśalasya karma phala doṣa parihāra ādi vibhāga viśārad asya viduṣaḥ
na ayam apakarṣāya na ayam su alpaḥ saṃkaraḥ puṇya phalāt pravṛttāt bahutarāt apakraṣṭum apakṛṣya ca sva kārye niyoktum paryāptaḥ
atha vā kuśalasya karmaṇaḥ eva na ayam apakarṣāya paryāptaḥ
kasmāt kuśalam hi me
sādhakaḥ evam manyate
śubham yasmāt mama bahu anyat asti yatra ayam yasmin bahuni śubhe ayam saṅkaraḥ āvāpa gataḥ svarge api apakarṣam alpam kariṣyataḥ iti
niyata vipāka pradhāna karma abhibhūtasya vā api
katham iti duṣṭa abhiprāyaḥ praśnaḥ
katham pravṛtta rājyena aparasya apravṛtta rājyasya abhibhavaḥ yuktaḥ nimitta bhedena rājya pravṛtteḥ
iha tu nimittam abhivyañḥjakam maraṇam sarveṣām karmaṇām tulyam tasmin tu nimitte sati sarveṣām karmaṇām vṛttilābhaḥ yuktaḥ iti pradhāna karma ābha bhavaḥ na yuktaḥ itarasya iti manyate
tatas ca avāpa gamanam eva astu iti
atrā ucyate tatra adṛṣṭa janma vedanīyasya eva aviruddha deśa kāla vipāka ādi nimittasya niyata vipākasya puṇya apuṇya rūpasya anekasya karmaṇaḥ samānam maraṇam abhivyakti kāraṇam uktam
na tu dṛṣṭa janma vedanīyasya putra grāma ādi viṣayasya aniyata vipākasya vā adṛṣṭa janma vedanīyasya yathā kṛta vyākhyānasya
yat tu adṛṣṭa janma vedanīyam aniyata vipākam tat naśi ṛṛdāpām vā abhibhūtam vā ciram api upāsīta udādīta yāvat samānam a viruddham tulya jātīyam abhivyañjakam nimittam karma
samāna jātīyam hi karma vipacyamānam etat abhimukham karoti
tad vipākasya eva tasya aniyata vipākasya karmaṇaḥ vipākasya eva
deśa kāla nimitta an avadhāraṇāt kasmin vā deśe kasmin vā nimitte kasmin kāle vā tat karma vipāka abhimukham bhavīyati iti an avadhāraṇāt
iyam gatiḥ citrā durjñānā ca bhavati
citrā nāśa āvāpa abhibhava ādi vaicitryāt
durjñānāḥ deśa kāla nimitta an avadhāraṇāt
nanu ca adṛṣṭa janma vedanīyasya prāyaṇe bhivyaktasya ekam eva janma karoti iti eka janma āraṃbhi tvam uktam tat idānīm bādhyeta iti ced na upapādita uttara tvāt adṛṣṭa janma vedanīyasya niyata vipākasya eva ayam niyamaḥ iti
na tasya utsargasya asmāt aniyama apavādāt nivṛttiḥ iti
katham na nivṛttiḥ eka bhavikaḥ karma āśayaḥ durjñānaḥ iti evam na aniyata vipākasya api eka janma ārambhi tvam na pratiṣiddham iti arthaḥ
atha vā utsargasya apavādāt nivṛttiḥ iti matvā naimabhavikaḥ karma āśayaḥ durjñānaḥ iti anena nañ saṃbadhyate
yasmāt utsargasya eka deśasya apavādaḥ nirvartakaḥ na sarvasya tasmāt nityāḥ niyata vipākaḥ eka bhavikaḥ karama āśayaḥ su jñānaḥ eva
aparaḥ kalpaḥ iha karma gatiḥ prakṛtam tasya ayam apavādaḥ eka bhavikaḥ karma āśayaḥ durjñānaḥ iti
tatra iti śabdaḥ hetvarthe
yasmāt hetoḥ autsargikasya karma gatiḥ tathā jñātavyā eva
durjñānāḥ iti duḥkhena jñeya tvam ucyate kleśena
karma āśayaḥ upavyākhyātaḥ dṛṣṭa janma vedanīyaḥ ca adṛṣṭa janma vedanīyaḥ ca
tasya api trividhāḥ vipākāḥ jāti āyuḥ bhogāḥ hlāda paritāpa phalāḥ puṇya apuṇya getu tvāt
hlādaḥ sukham paritāpaḥ duḥkham hlādaḥ ca paritāpaḥ ca hlāda paritāpau tau phalam yeṣām te hlāda paritāpa phalāḥ
tathā puṇyam ca apuṇyam ca puṇya apuṇye te eva hetū yeṣām te puṇya apuṇya hetavaḥ
teṣām bhāvaḥ puṇya apuiṇya hetu tvam tasmāt puṇya puṇya hetu tvāt
te jāti āyuḥ bhogāḥ puṇya hetukāḥ sukha phalāḥ
apuṇya hetukāḥ duḥkha phalāḥ
yathā idam duḥkham pratikūla ātmakam evam viṣaya sukha kāle api duḥkham asti eva pratikūla ātmakam yoginaḥ
katham viṣaya sukha kāle yoginaḥ suḥkham asti
tathā pūrvatra ca uktam duḥkhe sukha khyātim vakṣyati iti
tat uppādayate pratipādyate
tatra ca etat na pratipāditam
duḥkhasya karma kārya tvāt krama antaram yuktam iti bahu vaktavya tvāt ca
pariṇāma tāpa saṃskāra duḥkhaiḥ guṇa vṛtti virodhāt ca duḥkham eva sarvam vivekinaḥ
pariṇatiḥ pariṇāmaḥ taptiḥ tāpaḥ saṃskrtiḥ saṃskāraḥ tāpaḥ ca saṃskāraḥ ca tāpa saṃskārau pariṇāmaḥ ca tāpa saṃskārau ca pariṇāma tāpa saṃskārāḥ te eva duḥkhāḥ duḥkha nimittāni etaiḥ pariṇāma tāpa saṃskāra duḥkhaiḥ h getubhiḥ sarvam eva duḥkham
kim tat sarvam kleśāḥ duḥkha kāraṇa tvāt eva hetoḥ
karmāṇi hlāda paritāpa phala tvāt
jāti āyuḥ bhogāḥ ca kleśa ādīnām āśraya niomitta viṣayāḥ ca duḥkha hetu tvāt iti etat sarvam eva duḥkham
kim sarvasya eva na iti āha vivekinaḥ iti kleśa ādīnām vibhāga vivekaḥ yasya vidyate sa vivekī
tasya kleśa karma vipaka abhijñasya ca sarva duḥkha tva upapādaka pratipādaka hetu abhidarśinaḥ iti arthaḥ
na itarasya anittham daiśinaḥ
tasya tu tapti mātram duḥkham
tat api aham tapye iti ātma tvena pratipdyamānaḥ tatra api saṃśayāna u sau mama idam duḥkham iti etāvat mātram api viviṅkte
yadi hi etāvat api antaram viviñcīta tatas duḥkha sādhanam api etat duḥkha sādhana m iti manvīta
tathā ca sarvam idam duḥkham iti titikṣet iti saḥ api vivekī syāt
tasmāt yadi api tāpa kāle duḥkha mātram paśyanti tathā api na tad sādhana ādi sarvam duḥkham iti manyante nirvivekinaḥ
yasya punar pariṇāma duḥkha hetu darśanam tasya vivekinaḥ sarvam eva duḥkham
tatra tāvat pariṇāma duḥkha tām vyāṣaṣṭe sarvasya ayam rāga anuviddhaḥ sarvasya iti anena sarva prāṇi prasiddha tvāt avyabhicāri pratyakṣa avagamya tvam darśayati
cetana acetana adhīnaḥ putra puśu hiraṇya ādi sādhana āyattaḥ sukha anubhave iti sukha anubhava kāle rāgaḥ manaḥ vyāpāraḥ tad viśiṣṭaḥ hi sukham anubhavati
sa sarvaḥ vyāpāraḥ kleśa upasaṃhita tvāt dharma adharma hetuḥ
tat pūrvaḥ ca prārabdha phalaḥ upabhujyate bhoga kāle ca aparaḥ upacīyate
tatas ca kleśa mūlaḥ karamāśayaḥ sati mūle tad vipākaḥ iti upapannam bhavati
tathā sukha velāyām sukha pratyanīka bhūtāni duḥkha sādhanāni upalabhmānaḥ dveṣti tathā sukha upabhoga paripālana vyagratara mānasaḥ muhyati ca iti dveṣa moha pūrva vyāpāra janitaḥ api asti asti karama āśayaḥ
athavā dveṣa mohau eva vyāpāra rūpau iti tad kṛtaḥ eva
tathā yaḥ ca asau sukha upabhohgaḥ sa na an upahatya na an upahiṃsya bhūtāni upabhogaḥ sambhavati iti
eva upaghāta hetu tvāt upahantṛ tvena vivakṣitaḥ iti samāna kartṛkatvam
anyaḥ api madīyam evā upabhokṣyate iti manyate tatra api sarva upbhoga sāmarthya yuktam dhanam iti tasmin upādīyamāne dhruvam para pīḍā syāt
kim uta pīḍayitvā eva yat upādīyate
tatas ca hiṃsā kṛtaḥ api asti karama āśayaḥ śārīraḥ
tad upādāna vyāpārasya śarīra nirvartya tvāt
evam ekasmin upabhoga kāle bahudhā karma āśayaḥ lobha krodha moha nimittaḥ upacīyate
tathā ca rāga dveṣa moha viśiṣṭa tvāt aneka mukha karma āśaya viśiṣṭaḥ sukha anubhavaḥ pariṇamānaḥ san anubandhe duḥkhībhavati iti pariṇāma duḥkha tā iti ucyate
vivekinaḥ tu evam paśyataḥ suklha anubhava kāle api duḥkham asti eva
tat yathā viṣa dighatām jñātvā dadhyodanam bhuñjānasya
taraḥ ca sarvam suḥkham eva avidyā tvāt viṣaya sukhasya
aviveka pratyaya ātmakaḥ hi viṣaya sukha anubhavaḥ
tat etat āha viṣaya sukham ca avidyate uktam iti
kva uktam iha eva paryāya śabdena atyanta vi vi bha ktayoḥ atyanta asaṅkīrṇayoḥ aviveka prāptau iva satyām bhogaḥ kalpate
sva rūpa pratilambhe tu tayoḥ kaivalyam eva bhavati kutas bhogaḥ iti iti anena bhāṣyeṇa
yat vā sūtrakāreṇa ukta ūm upariṣṭāt pratyaya aviśeṣaḥ bhogaḥ iti
avidyā ca pariṇamamānā sarvam anartham karoti
tatas ca duḥkha bīja tvāt duḥkham eva viṣaya sukham
