vyādhi nimitta tvāt svādutaram api bhakṣyamāṇam
viṣaya sukham ca avidyā iti asya eva arthasya tantra siddham udāharaṇam
yā tu laulyāt īpsayā tṛṣṇātaḥ sakāśāt anupaśānti anuparitas tat duḥkham
tat uktam ṅā asti tṛṣṇā samam a suḥkham a tṛṣṇā samam sukham iti
nanu ca upabhogena eva vaitṛṣṇyam bhavati upabhoga ante
upabhogaḥ ca sukham bhaviṣyati
tatas āha na ca indriyāṇām bhoga abhyāsena śakyam vaitṛṣṇyam kartum
kasmāt atas āha yatas bhoga abhyāsam anuvuvardhante indriyāṇām rāgāḥ
tathā ca uktam jātu kāmaḥ kāmānām upabhogena
baviṣā kṛṣṇa vatsā iva bhūyas eva abhibardhate
iti
kauśalāni naipuṇāni ca bhoga abhyāseṣu indriyāṇām anu vivardhante
yadi api manaḥ kauśala pūrvakam indriyāṇām kauśalam tathā api dṛśyate eva bhikṣā kṣvā dīnām indriyasya api kauśalam
tasmāt anupāyaḥ sukhasya bhoga abhyāsaḥ iti bhoga abhyāsāt nivṛttiḥ eva sukham
sa khalu ayam vṛścika bhītaḥ iva āśīvipepeṇa daṣṭaḥ yaḥ sukha arthī viṣaya ananvavasitaḥ anvavabaddhaḥ anupravṛttaḥ nuvyavasitaḥ vā yathā manda viṣāt vṛścikāt upajāta bhītiḥ paṭureṇa āśīviṣeṇa grastaḥ mahattaram duḥkham abhiprapadyate
tathā yam agra duḥkha ābhāsāyāḥ pariṇāma mahā sukhāyāḥ nivṛttaḥ duḥkha buddhyā bhītaḥ san apāre mahati duḥkha paṅke magnaḥ iti eṣā pariṇāma duḥkha tā sukhasya pratikūlā sukha avasthāyām api yoginaḥ
sa hi yogī pravṛtta veparhunā eva hladayena pratiniyata vedanīyasya karmaṇaḥ balīyaḥ tvāt anubhuṅkte sukham
sarvam duḥkham vivekinaḥ
atha tāpa duḥkha tā vyākhyāyate sukha upabhogaḥ tu pariṇamamānaḥ san anubandhe vijñāt viṣa digdha svādu dadhi odana upabhoga vat duḥkhī bhavati svarūpataḥ punar avidyā rūpaḥ api
iha punar svarūpataḥ eva duḥkha tā tāpasya rati kula ātmaka tvāt
katham sarvasya dveṣa anuviddhaḥ dveṣa anugataḥ cetana acetana sādhana adhīnaḥ śatru kaṇṭaka ādi sādhana āyattaḥ tāpa anubhavaḥ pūrva vat eva adharma phalam anu bhavati apūrvaḥ ca upacīyamānaḥ tatra asti dveṣa jaḥ karamāśayaḥ
tena c duḥkhena paritapyamānaḥ sukha sādhanani candana ādīni prārthayamānaḥ kāyena vācā manasā ca parispandate ceṣṭate
tat ca parispandanam para anugrahāya para pīḍanāya vā bhavati
tatas para anugraha pīḍābhyām dharma adharmau upacinoti
sa ca dharma adharma ākhyaḥ karma āśayaḥ lobhāt mohāt ca prabhavati iti eṣā tāvat tāpa duḥkha tā drāghīyasī viprasṛtā
evam paśyataḥ vivekinaḥ sarvam eva āśraya viṣaya nimittaiḥ duḥkham iti
adhunā hlāda paritāpa anubhava janita saṃskāra duḥkham ucyate kā punar saṃskāra duḥkha tā sukha anubhavāt sukha saṃskāra ācayaḥ duḥkha anubhavāt api duḥkha saṃskārāt śayaḥ
sukha duḥkhayoḥ rāga dvsṣa anuviddha tvāt tad saṃskāra āśayau api rāga dveṣa anuviddhau evam karmaṇaḥ vipāke jāti āyuḥ bhoha ākhye nubhūyamāne bhavataḥ
tatas api sukha duḥkha anubhava saṃskāra āśayaḥ yathā nairantaryeṇa sukha duḥkha anubhavaḥ tathā eva tad anubhava saṃskārau api rāga dveṣa anuviddhau nirantara tayā bhavataḥ
tau ca saṃskāra hetukam saṃskāra duḥkham tathā ca tad saṃskāra duḥkha tā
na hi a smaran upabhogāya kriyāyāḥ sādhanam upādatte
smṛteḥ ca saṃskāra nimitta tvam upapāditam
yadi api saṃskārasya svarūpataḥ duḥkhatā nā asti tathā api saṃskārasya duḥkha hetutām jānataḥ viveinaḥ sattā mātreṇa duḥkha tvam bhakṣita mātra viṣa vat
iti am etaiḥ pariṇāma tāpa saṃskāra hetubhiḥ sarvam eva duḥkham iti anādi duḥkha rotaḥ yoginam eva pratikūla ātmaka tvāt uddhejayati
nanu ca itarasya api pratikūla ātmakam eva kasmāt na tam udvejayati
na atyanta kleśa ādi kāluṣyāḥ viveka kiṇīkṛta cetaḥ tvāt itaram uddhejayati
na pratikūlā ātmaktā prabhāvyate
yaḥ hi dayitām uṣṭi ghātam mudgara abhighāta deśīyam api mastakena pati icchati
putrasya vā mūtra purīṣam urasā dhārayati
asau ānanda mahā udanvat taraṅgāyamāṇaḥ sva ātmani api na vātitarām sva ātmānam api na vetti tarām
na hi tasya tat pratikūla ātmakam
rāgam eva hi tat itarasya pratipattṛ tvāt abhivardhayati tarām
nanu ca yoginaḥ api tad samānam nimittam kasmāt tam uddhejayati iti
uddhejayati eva tam
kasmāt akṣi pātra kalpaḥ hi saḥ
prasanna tvāt virakta tvāt iti arthaḥ
tasmāt nityāḥ na samānam nimittam tasya yatas sau vidvān iti
na hi viduṣaḥ kleśa ādi kāluṣyāḥ viveka kiṇīkṛta cetaḥ tvam
na ca tad kiṇīkṛta cetaḥ tva tiraskārāt ṛte vidvat tā
tasmāt akṣpātra kalpa tvāt vidvāṃsam eva uddhejayati na itaram
tatra dṛṣṭāntābhyām vidvat aviduṣoḥ antaram ācaṣṭe yathā ūrṇā tantuḥ ati mṛdu sparśaḥ api akṣi pātre nyastaḥ sparśena dūkhyati svaddhatara tvāt akṣi pātrasya tathā yoginam viviktatara prajñānam akaluṣa hṛdayam udvejayati duḥkham
saḥ evā ūrṇā tantuḥ anyeṣu gātreṣu kṣiptaḥ kharatara saṃsparśena api na duḥkhayati tathā na itaram pratipattāram duḥkham pīḍayati kleśa ādi kiṇīkṛta cetaḥ tvāt kaṭhinatara itara gātra avayava kalpaḥ hi saḥ
tat idam āha evam etāni duḥkhāni akṣi pātra kalpam yoginam eva kliśnanti na itaram pratipattāram
itarasya tu pratipattuḥ itara gātra avayava svabhāva tām darśayan āha itaram tu iti
tāpāḥ anuplavante iti evam antena vākya samaptiḥ
sva kāraṇa upahltam duḥkha prāpti nimittaiḥ cetana acetana ādibhiḥ upahṛtam upanītam buddhi vṛtti dvāreṇa puruṣasya karmatām āpāditam duḥkham upāttam tyajantam śarīra tyāgena anyatra ca tyaktam punar anyam śarīra ādi laksaṇam eva duḥkha samudāyam upādadānam anādi vāsanā citrayā avidyayā vittavṛttyā srvatas nuviddham iva
itaram pratipattāram kim viśiṣṭam hātavya ahaṅkāra mamakāra anupātinam
kārya karaṇeṣu tat dharmeṣu ca kriyā guṇa phaleṣu viparyayeṇa pratipattiḥ ahagkāraḥ mamakāraḥ tu teṣu bāhyeṣu ca cetana acetaneṣu mama iti pratyayaḥ
tau ca viparyaya tvāt samasta kleśa karma vipāka bīja tvāt ca hātavyau
na hi rāga ādayaḥ karma vipākāḥ vā samudācaranti
tasmāt dhātavyau tau tau anupatitum śīlam asya iti hātavya ahaṅkāra mamakāra anupātī tam
jātam jātam anya gātra avayava kalpam bāhya ādhyātmika ubhata nimittāḥ bāhyam bhūtāni ca ādhyātmikam kāryam kāraṇam ca bāhya ādhyātmikāni ca nimittam yeṣām te bāhya ādhyātmika ubhaya nimittāḥ
tri parvāṇaḥ bāhya ādi nimittam eva tri parva tvam
bhūta bhaviṣyat vartamāna tvam vā tri parva tvam
vakṣyati ca heyam duḥkham anāgatam iti yat vā kleśa karma vipaka ātmaka tvam
yat vā pariṇāma tāpa saṃskāra duḥkha tvam
atas te tri parvāṇaḥ tāpāḥ anuplavante anuṣajyanti
ta me evam avivekam pratipattāram anādi duḥkha srotasā uhyamānam ātmānam ca duḥkha srotasi magnam tathā bhūta grāmam ca dṛṣṭvā yogī sarva duḥkha kṣaya karam samyak darśanam śaraṇam prapadyate iti
nanu ca yogi tvāt eva samyak darśanam pratipannaḥ
ucyate yogāṅga anuṣṭhānāt eva yogi tvam ṛte api samyak darśanāt
tasmāt samyak darśana sādhana tvam yogasya darśayati
yogam yoga phalam ca eva duḥkham paśyan samyak darśana eka śaraṇam pratipadyate
tathā ca vakṣyati tad vairāgyāt api doṣa bīja kṣaye kaivalyam iti
itas ca sarvam duḥkham vivekinaḥ kutas ca guṇa vṛtti virodhāt ca api
nanu ca kimartham sūtre pṛthak bibhakti kriyā yāvatā pariṇāma tāpa saṃskāra guṇa vṛtti virodhaiḥ iti eva kartavyam
na eṣa doṣaḥ
sukha duḥkha anubhava tad vāsanāḥ sarva jana prasiddhāḥ iti pariṇāma tāpa saṃskāra duḥkhaiḥ iti nirdiṣṭāḥ
tad kāraṇa vibhāga jñāna viśāradasya eva viveka prakarṣavataḥ guṇa vṛtti virodhāḥ vijñeyāḥ iti pṛthakkaraṇam
sarva duḥkha hetu tva sāmānyāt tu eka sūtra vinyāsaḥ
guṇāḥ sattva ādayaḥ teṣām vṛttayaḥ guṇa vṛttayaḥ tāsām virodhāt guṇa vṛti virodhāt
te ca guṇāḥ antaḥkaraṇa ādi ākāra sanniviṣṭāḥ
teṣām guṇa pradhāna bhāvena abhinna pariṇāma tvāt ca viruddha vṛtti tvam bhavati
anyatama vṛttiḥ udbhavantyā nyatama vṛttyā abhibhūyate
evam trayāṇām api anyonya vṛtti tiraskāraḥ itaretara vṛtti udbhāvi tvam ca
na sukha duḥkha moha ātmakānām guṇānām anytama vṛttilābhaḥ nyatama an anusaṃhitaḥ
tatas etat siddham bhavati yadā duḥkha ātmakam rajaḥ udbhavati tadā duḥkha tvāt eva tad vṛtteḥ na duḥkham iti vaktavyam
sattva tamasoḥ api rajaḥ nugatiḥ asti eva iti tayoḥ api duḥkha tvam eva
sattva tamaḥ pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ api rajaḥ vyāpāra anuja tvāt duḥkha tvam eva sarvasya iti
etat upavyācaṣṭe prakhyā pravṛtti sthiti śīlābhiḥ vṛttibhiḥ guṇāḥ paraspara anugraha tantrāḥ api paraspara upakārya upakāraka bhāvena taila varti agni vat śāntam sāttvikam ghoram rājasam mūḍham tāmasam pratyayam triguṇam eva ārabhante
tare tarayoḥ aṅga bhāvena anugata tvāt yadā sāttvikaḥ śāntaḥ pratyayaḥ udbhūyas saḥ nantaram eva udbubhūṣatā tamaḥ nu saṃhitena ghoreṇa rājasena pratyayena hanyate
yadā ca rāsasaḥ ghoraḥ pratyāyaḥ itara guṇa anugataḥ udbhūtaḥ bhavati saḥ eva udbubhūṣatā tāmasena pratyayena mūḍhena sattva anugatena sāttvikena vā hanyate
tathā tāmas pītara pratyāyābhyām paryāyeṇa
tathā sāttvikena itarau iti anaḥ yoni udaya abhibhava pravṛttayā guṇāḥ
kasmāt yatas phalam guṇa vṛttam guṇa svabhāva tvam citta ākāreṇa guṇāḥ sanniviṣṭāḥ iti kṣipra pariṇāmam cittam uktam
kva tantre
kasmāt punar guṇāḥ virudhyante iti
aneka atiśayānām ekatra asambhavāt
yathā apavarake tamaḥ prakāśayoḥ atiśayavatoḥ evam antaḥkaraṇa ākāra sanniveśinām sukha duḥkha moha rūpāṇām prakāśa pravṛtti niyama vṛttīnām guṇānām rūpeṇa sukha ādinā vṛttyā vā jñāna ādi lakṣaṇayā yugapad atiśayaḥ na sambhavati
sāmānyānām tu avirodhāt avyakta rūpāṇām ati vyaktaiḥ saha vṛtti yuktā
tena rūpa atiśayāḥ vṛtti atiśayāḥ ca virudhyante
sāmānyāni tu atiśayaiḥ saha vartante iti ucyate
yadā sukha rūpa atiśayaḥ tadā na duḥkha rupa atiśayaḥ māṃha rūpa atiśayaḥ vā
tathā itara atiśaye na itara atiśayaḥ
tathā jñāna vṛtti atiśaye na lobha pratyaya vṛtti atiśayaḥ
tathā anyatama vṛtti aticaye na anyatama vṛtti atiśayaḥ
evam ete guṇāḥ itara itara upāśraya upārjita sukha duḥkha moha pratyayāḥ
sattvena rajaḥ tamaḥ aupāśrayeṇa upārjitaḥ sukha pratyayaḥ
rajasā api sattvatamaḥ aupāśrayeṇa upārjitaḥ duḥkha pratyayaḥ
tamasā api sattva rajaḥ upāśrayeṇa upārjitaḥ moha pratyayaḥ
tatas sarve sarvakāryāḥ bhavanti
yadi evam ayam pratyayaḥ sāttvikaḥ tāmasaḥ yam rājasaḥ ca ayam iti viśeṣaḥ kaḥ iti āha guṇa pradhāna bhāva kṛtaḥ tu eṣām viśeṣaḥ iti
pradhāna upsarjana tayā saṃjñā lābha alābhau
yathā pāñcabhautika tve api pārthivam taijasam āpyam iti
yatas evam guṇa vṛtti virodhaḥ tasmāt sarvam eva duḥkham vivekinaḥ iti
guṇa vṛtti virodhāt iti etat para vairāgya artham
katham pariṇāma tāpa saṃskāra duḥkhaiḥ iti dṛṣṭa ānuśravika viṣaya vitṛṣṇasya eva sarvasya duḥkha pratipādana artham pṛthak vibhaktikam kṛtam
na hi tatra duḥkha tvam a paśyataḥ vairāgyam upakalpyate iti
etat tu guṇa vṛtti virodhāt ca iti guṇānām paraspara virodhi vṛtti tvena duḥkha pratipādanāt tebhyaḥ vyakta avyakta dharmakebhyaḥ param vairāgyam upakalpyate iti evam artham
tathā ca atra api pradhāna upasarjana bhāvena sarve sarva rūpāḥ bhavanti iti vyakta avyakta dharma tvam pratipāditam
evam ca kṛtvā sūtre api guṇa vṛtti virodhāt ca iti pṛthak paṭhitam
pariṇāma tāpa saṃskāra duḥkha dharma tvāt tasya etasya mahataḥ guṇa gauṇa lakṣaṇasya duḥkha samudāyasya prabhava bījam avidyā
tasyāḥ ca samyak darśanam abhāva hetuḥ pratipakṣa tvāt
bhūta artha āśraya tvāt vidyāyāḥ abhūta artha āśraya tvāt ca avidyāyāḥ vidā eva abhāva hetuḥ
yathā sat viṣayeṇa eka candra darśanena asat viṣayasya aneka candra darśanasya bādhanam
saha duḥkha nidānena kleśa karma vipaka lakṣaṇena sarvam duḥkham iti upapāditam
anena duḥkhena yaḥ duḥkhī vivekī saḥ etasya samyak darśana śāstrasya viṣayaḥ adhikṛtaḥ na itaraḥ duḥkhasya eva pratipattṛ tvāt iti etat dṛṣṭāntena pratipipādayiṣyan āha yathā cikitsā śāstram catur vyūham rogaḥ roga hetuḥ ārogyam bhaiṣajyam iti bhaiṣajyasya śāstrasya ārogyasya prayojanasya viṣayaḥ
evam idam api śāstram catur vyūham eva yathā saṃsāraḥ saṃsara hetuḥ mokṣaḥ mokṣa hetuḥ
tatra duḥkha bahulaḥ saṃsāraḥ heyaḥ
pradyāna puruṣa saṃyogaḥ heya hetuḥ
saṃyogasya ātyantikī nivṛttiḥ hānam
hāna upāyaḥ samyak darśanam iti ete catvāraḥ vyuhāḥ
yathā cikitsā śāstram roge roga hetau ca ārogye ca tad prayojanake bhaiṣasye ca catuṣtaye svarūpa pratipādanāya vyūhitam tatas eva ca roga ādayaḥ asya catvāraḥ vyūhāḥ iti catur vyūham tathā asya śāstrasya
duḥkha bahulaḥ saṃsāraḥ heyaḥ avidyā hetukaḥ ca pradhāna puruṣa saṃyogaḥ hetuḥ sa nimittasya saṃsārasya hānam samyagdarśana śāstrasya prayojanam tathā samyagdarśanam ca iti catvāra vyūhāḥ asya api iti catur vyūham śāstram
eṣu vā rtheṣu caturdhā vyūhaḥ syaḥ iti catur vyūham
tatra hātuḥ svarūpam iti
nanu draṣṭā dṛśi mātraḥ iti hātṛ lakṣaṇa sūtre etat viditavyam
na eṣa doṣaḥ śāstra ārambha prayojana pratipipādayiṣuṇā kleśa ādikaḥ samastaḥ duḥkha avasānaḥ saḥ asya śāstrasya viṣayaḥ upapāditaḥ
tasya vivekinaḥ śāstram atas param ārabhyante
etat ca prathama sūtre pradarśitam
ārambhyamāṇasya śāstrasya samyak darśanam eva prayojanam
tat ca saṃsāra duḥkha nirvarṇana anantaram avasara prāptam pratipādayitavyam iti etat ucyate
tatra hātuḥ svarūpam iti
hātā puruṣaḥ tasya svarūpam upādeyam vā heyam vā na bhavati
kutas etat evam heya upādeya vyatikekeṇa vastu adarśanāt
yathā loke sukham tad kāraṇam ca upādeyam duḥkham tad kāraṇam ca heyam evam ayam api puruṣaḥ vastu tvāt anyatara dharmā bhavitum arhati iti abhiprāyaḥ
kim atas yadi evam atas etat bhavati hāne tu asya uccheda vāt aprasaṅgaḥ iti
yadi asau heya tva dharmā tatas eṣa hātavyaḥ
hāne tu asya kim syāt ātma uccheda vāt aprasaṅgaḥ syāt
atas kaḥ doṣaḥ syāt doṣam kaivalya pāde pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ
kim ca anyat asya hātṛ antarasya kiñca anyatarasya abhāvāt dhānā anupapatti tvam
svayam eva ātmanaḥ ātmā hātā iti ced na svātmani kriyā virodhāt bheda abhāvāt ca
heyāt ātmanaḥ ātmana hātā ced anyaḥ tadā
yaḥ yaḥ hātā tasya api heya tvāt
na ca yugapad dvyoḥ hātroḥ saṃbhavaḥ ati
bhinna kāla bhāvinoḥ tu heya hātṛ tva anupapattiḥ
hātuḥ ca heya tva abhyupagame tasya anavasthita tvāt dheya sambandha anupapattiḥ
hātuḥ anavasthita tve ca svayam eva heya tva pratipatteḥ hātuḥ hānāya udyama ānarthakya prasaṅgaḥ
hāna phala anupapattiḥ ca na hi baddhasya svarūpa nāśaḥ eva phalam
mokṣaḥ hi tasya phalam
na api mriyamāṇaḥ api jñāta kṣaṇa antara maraṇaḥ sva rūpa vināśam icchati
vināśasya atha prāpta tvāt evam anavasthitaḥ ced dhātā na sva rūpa hānam icchet artha prāpteḥ hānasya
yathā ca hātuḥ nitya tvam tathā sūtre kaivalya pāde ca vyākhyāsyāmahe
tasmāt nityāḥ na heya tva dharmā puruṣaḥ
saṃsāraḥ tu mahat ādi vyaktiḥ duḥkha bahulaḥ heyaḥ
tat tulya dharmakaḥ puruṣaḥ na bhavati iti arthaḥ
tad tulya dharmaka tve tasya uccheda vāt aprasaṅgaḥ iti
astu tarhi upādeyaḥ yathā sukha artham sukha kāraṇam dravyam
na etat evam
kasmāt upādāne tu asya hetuvāda prasaṅgāt tasya dravya ādi upādāna phalena sambandhaḥ sa ced upādīyeta tat nirhetukam asya upādānam syāt
anyasya upādātuḥ abhāvāt
na hi paṭaḥ paṭena eva upādīyate
anyasya hi anyat upādeyam
upādātṛ antara sambhave hi tad anavasthā prasaṅhaḥ saḥ api anyena upādīyate saḥ api ca anyena iti
kim ca pārārthya prasaṅgaḥ ca
anyasya hi hetoḥ anyat upādīyate sattva ādi lakṣaṇasya pradhānasya upādāne puruṣaḥ hetuḥ abhyupeyate yathā ghaṭāya mṛd piṇḍa upādāne kilālaḥ hatuḥ
sa ced puruṣaḥ pradhāna upādāna hetuḥ pradhāna vat upādīyeta tasya api sattva ādi dharma tvam syāt upādeya tvāt mṛd piṇḍa vat
tatas asya pradhānasya nirhetukam kārya artham upādānam prāpnoti
atha īśvara artham upādeyaḥ puruṣāṇām vā paraspara artham iti ced bhogyatva acetana tva pariṇāmi tva ādi doṣa sāmagrī prasajayeta tasmāt nityā nā api pradhāna dharmakaḥ puruṣaḥ iti upādāne ca hetuvāda prasaṅgaḥ iti ucyate
tat uktam hetuḥ tu apuruṣaḥ bhavati iti
tasya ca upādāne ahetuḥ pradhāna vṛttiḥ nirhetukī syāt
na ca svayam sva artham śakyam vijñātum
prakāśa ādiṣu sva artha tvāt adarśanāt
ubhaya pratyākhyāne heya tva upādeya tva pratyākhyāne
śāśvata vāda prasaṅgaḥ ātma nitya tva vāda prasaṅgaḥ
yadi api pradhānasya upādeyasya api śāśvata tvam tathā api vikāra ātmanā tat aśāśvatam eva
aneka ātmaka tvam aśuci tvam avidyā tvam parārtha tvam iti evamādayaḥ doṣāḥ pradhāne
puruṣāṇām api tathātve sati anirmokṣa prasaṅgaḥ
bandhaḥ mokṣayoḥ tad hetvoḥ ca vidyā avidyayoḥ svarūpa avyatirekāt bandha muktayoḥ ca nirviśeṣa tva prasaṅgāt
tasmāt dheya upādeya tva pratyākhyānena śāśvata vādaḥ iti etat eva samyak darśanam
yathā cikitsya vyatirikta roga ādi catuṣṭayam antareṇa cikitsā śāstram ārogya prayojanam catur vyūham na saṃbhavati tathā idam api hātṛ svarūpa vyatirikta heya ādi catuṣṭayam antareṇa samyagdarśana śāstram hāna phalam catur vyūham na sambhavati iti heya ādi catuṣṭaya pratipādanena tat etat śāstram catur vyūham abhidhīyate
katham heyam duḥkham anāgatam duḥkham atītam atikrāntam vartamānāt janmanaḥ utikrānta janma lakṣaṇam duḥkham tad upabhogena ativāhitam atinītam na heya pakṣe vartate
svayam eva hīna tvāt
vartamānam ca yat janma lakṣaṇam sva kṣaṇa upabhoga ārūḍham svam vartamānam bhoga viśiṣṭam kṣaṇam adhvānam upabhujyam ān ātmaka tvena ārūḍham tat duḥkham na kṣṇā antare heya tām āpadyate
svayam eva bhogena hīnam na hānāya kṣaṇa antaram apekṣate
tasmāt yat eva anāgatam prāyaṇa anantara bhāvi janma duḥkha lakṣaṇam duḥkham tat eva akṣi pātra kalpam yoginam kliśnāti iti tat eva heyam samyak darśanena hānīyam ucyate
bhaviṣyat janma abhāvāya eva yatitavyam
na vartamāna duḥkha nirodhāya
hi samyak darśanam aśakti aviniyoga tvāt anarthakam syāt
mukta bāṇa vat pravṛtta phala tvāt vartamāna duḥkhasya
bhaviṣyati punar apravṛtta tvāt bīja nirodhaḥ upakalpate iti samyak darśana arthavat tvam
sva viṣayaḥ hi samyak darśanasya saḥ iti
tat etat śāstram catur vyūham abhidhīyate iti uktam ekaḥ caturṣu vyūhaḥ pratipāditaḥ heyam duḥkham anāgatam iti
idānīm dvitīyaḥ vyūhaḥ tasya duḥkhasya kāraṇam hetuḥ pratinirdiśyate
nanu nirdiṣṭam eva duḥkha kāraṇam iti tathā eva upasaṃhṛtam ante tasya etasya mahataḥ suḥkha samudāyasya prabhava bījam avidyā iti
satyam evam
kin tu duḥkha svarūpa mātram tad kāraṇa svarūpa mātram ca pūrvam nirdiṣṭam
na ca tad svarūpa mātre iti tat kāraṇam nirdiśyate
draṣṭṛ dṛśyayoḥ saṃyogaḥ heya hetuḥ
draṣṭā buddheḥ pratisaṃvedī puruṣaḥ vakṣyamāṇa lakṣaṇaḥ
pratisaṃveditum śīlam asya sa pratisaṃvedī
kasya buddheḥ iti
dṛśyā buddhiḥ antaḥkaraṇam pratyaya rūpeṇa
nanu ca api viṣayāḥ dṛśyāḥ eva iti atas āha sattva upārūḍhāḥ sarve dharmāḥ śabda ādayaḥ buddhi sattvam upārūḍhāḥ buddhi pratyaya ākārāḥ eva dṛśyāḥ na svatas
svatas ca dṛśya tve jñāta ajñāta viṣaya tvam puruṣasya syāt
sadā jñāta viṣaya tvam ca puruṣasya nyānena sthāpyate
tasmāt buddhi upārūḍhāḥ eva sarve dharmāḥ dṛśyāḥ
tat etat dṛśyam ayaskānta maṇi kalpam ayasaḥ api kriyā arthena eva upakartā yaskānta maṇiḥ yathā tathā puruṣasya puruṣa arthena dvividhena bhoga apavarga lakṣaṇena upakartṛ tvāt iva svam dṛśi rūpasya citta tva rūpa mātrasya
katham svam iti atas āha karma viṣaya tvam āpannam karma eva viṣayaḥ karma viṣayaḥ karma tva āpattiḥ eva
viṣayaḥ dṛśi rūpasya dṛśya tām āpannaḥ iti etat
katham bhūtam sat karma viṣaya tām āpadyate iti tad viśeṣaṇa artham āha anya svarūpeṇa pratilabdha ātmakam iti
anya sva rūpeṇa a sva para puruṣa rūpeṇa ādi rūpeṇa ca pratilabdha ātmakam pratilabdha viśeṣa rūpam pratilabdha puruṣa śabda ādi viśeṣa svabhāvam puruṣa sva rūpeṇa labdha ātmakam sat dṛśya tvena karmatām āpannam apavarga arthena svam bhavati
śabda ādi ākāreṇa labdha ātmakam sat dṛśya tvena karmatām āpannam bhoga arthena svam bhavati
nanu katham svatantrasya svatvam
na hi kiñcid svatantram svayam vyāpriyamāṇam anyat apekṣate
yat api sva vyāpāra anuniṣpādi puruṣa artha rūpam tat api svabhāvāt eva
na puruṣa niyoga kārī
tasmāt svatantrasya sataḥ svatvam na yuktam iti atas āha svatantram api puruṣa aṛtha dvaya kartṛ tvena parārtha tvāt paratantram
tatas ca svam eva
tayoḥ drak darśana śaktyoḥ iti
draṣṭṛ dṛśyayoḥ iti upkramya dṛś farśana śaktyḥ iti upasaṃhāraḥ buddhi puruṣa saṃyogasya buddhi utpatti anantara bhāvi tvāt ādimattvam āśaṅkya tad anādimattva pradarśana artham kriyate
dṛś darśana śaktyoḥ anādiḥ saṃyogaḥ
darmiṇām nitya tvāt nitya sambandha upapatteḥ tad śaktyoḥ api draṣṭṛ dṛśya tva lakṣaṇaḥ na ādiḥ saṃyogaḥ rtha kṛtaḥ puruṣa artha prayojava vaśaḥ iti arthaḥ
tathā ca sati anādi tve api prayojana nivṛttau saṃyoga nivṛttiḥ upapadyate
karmiṇām tu sva rūpa saṃyogaḥ sattā mātreṇa na prayohjana kṛtaḥ iti nityaḥ eva
dharma mātrābhiḥ tu anityābhiḥ anityaḥ saṃyogaḥ
sa tu buddhi puruṣa saṃyogaḥ heya hetuḥ duḥkhasya kāraṇam iti arthaḥ
tathā ca uktam tantre tad saṃyoga hetu vivarjanāt tayoḥ buddhi puruṣayoḥ saṃyogaḥ tasya hetuḥ avidyā yad vivarjanāt
katham vivarjanam vidyayā samyak darśanena tad pratipakṣeṇa nirvartanāt
tasmāt tad saṃyoga hetu vivarjanāt ātyantikaḥ tyantāya prabhavati duḥkha pratīkāraḥ
kaḥ sau yat samyagdarśi tvam
katham etat iti prasiddham dṛṣṭāntam āha tat yathā pāda talasya bhedya tā sukha māratara tvāt
kaṇṭakasya bhoktṛ tvam karkaśa svabhāva tvāt
tad saṃyogaḥ viśiṣṭaḥ duḥkha hetuḥ iti artha siddham
tatra kaṇṭaka vyathā duḥkhasya parihāraḥ kaṇṭake padā pādena anadhiṣṭhānam
etat dvayam yaḥ veda bhedya bhettṛ dvayam parihāra dvayam vā yaḥ veda loke sa tatra anyataram parihāram ārabhate
sa tatra prati kāram āramamāṇaḥ bheda jam kaṇṭaka bheda janitam duḥkham na āpnoti
tathā iha api puruṣaḥ sattva dvāreṇa kaṇṭaka sthānīyam pradhānam tayoḥ viśiṣṭaḥ saṃyogaḥ vidya mātra viśeṣebhyaḥ dṛśyebhyaḥ nirapekṣa tā samyagdarśanena prayojana abhāvam buddhvā puruṣasya avikriya tvāt kaṇṭaka adhiṣṭhāna vat śarīra ārambhiṇaḥ vā karmaṇaḥ niyata vedanīya tvāt avvaśyam phala dāyi tvam buddhvā a prārthita upanatānām śabdaḥ ādīnām samyagdarśana vyavahitena sattvena bhogaḥ
evam parihāram sañjānānaḥ kaṇṭakabheda duḥkha parihāram iva saṃsāra duḥkham na āpnoti
kasmāt etat evam iti tri tva upalabdhi sāmarthyāt
pradhāna puruṣa saṃyoga tri tva upalabdhi sāmarthyāt
evam hi vijñānasya sāmarthyam dṛśyate pāda tala kaṇṭaka tad saṃyogeṣu ajñānasya ca tri tva anupalabdheḥ duḥkha hetu tvam dṛśyate eva
etam artham pracikhyāpayiṣan āha atra api tāpakasya rajasaḥ
yadi api pradhānam kaṇṭaka sthānīyam tāpakam tathā api rajasaḥ duḥkha ātmaka tvāt rajaḥ dvāreṇa eva pradhānasya tāpaka tvam iti ucyate tāpakasya rajasaḥ iti
tasya rahjasaḥ karma bhūtam sattvam eva tapyam
kasmāt chidi kriyā vat tapi kriyāyāḥ karma stha tvāt
karmaṇi hi tapi kriyā vartate na rajasaḥ tāpakasya viṣayiṇi puruṣe
tapteḥ ca phalasya puruṣa viṣaya tvāt
na hi paraśuśdhettari sva ātmani vā vartate chidiḥ vā phalam viṣaye eva chedye kāṣṭha ādau
evam puruṣasya eva taptiḥ karmaṇi sattve vartamānā phalam rajaḥ ca kāṣṭha ādau iva paraśuḥ sattve eva puruṣasya dṛśye vartate
itas ca puruṣe tapi kriyā na vartate
apariṇāmi tvāt draṣṭu
tapiḥ api hi karma vikriyā
yathā chedanasya phalam chedyasya karmaṇaḥ dvaidhī bhāvaḥ vikriyā tadvat
na apariṇāmini niṣkriye kṣetrajñe
apariṇāmi tvam ca sadā jñāta viṣaya tvena sādhayiṣyati
yadi evam puruṣaḥ ced na tapyate puruṣa artham pradhānam pravartate iti etat anupapannam
vṛtti sārūpyeṇa ukta uttara tvāt
tat eva idam ucyate darśita viṣaya tvāt

tasmāt dṛśikarmaṇi sattve tapye tad ākāra anurodhī tad ākāra anuvartī
tad ākāra anurodhi tvam tat dṛśi sannidhau bauddhasya pratyayasya dṛśi rūpa avabhāsa tā
yathā lākṣā rasa sannidhau sphaṭihkasya lākṣā ākāra avabhāsa tā tathā puruṣaḥ api tapyate iti upacaryate
dṛśya svarūpam ucyate
nanu ca draṣṭṛ dṛśyayoḥ iti uktam pūrva sūtre
tatra krama prāpta sannidhānam dṛṣṭṛ svarūpam eva pūrvam vaktavyam
na eṣa doṣaḥ
dṛśya sva rūpa avagama pūrvaka tvāt draṣṭṛ sva rūpa avabodhasya
dṛśyasya hi sva ātma vyatirikta draṣṭṛ artha tvāt vyatirikta draṣṭṛ sadbhāva siddhiḥ
atas eva prādhānyāt pūrva sūtre draṣṭuḥ pūrva nipātaḥ kṛtaḥ
tat lakṣaṇe tu artha kramaḥ vivakṣyate
prakāśa kriyā sthiti śīlam bhūta indriya ātmakam bhoga apavarga artham dṛśyam
prakāśaḥ ca kriyā ca sthitiḥ ca prakāśa kriyā sthitayaḥ
prakāśasya abhyarhita tvāt pūrva nipātaḥ
bahuṣu ca aniyamāt sthiti kriyā śabdayoḥ aniyamaḥ iti kriyā śabdasya pūrva nipātaḥ
tāḥ eva śīlam yasya tat prakāśa kriyā sthiti śīlam
prakāśanam kriyā katham tad śīlam sattvam syāt rajaḥ hi tat śīlam sthiti śīlam vā tamaḥ katham iti
nanu ca svarūpam eva tad prakāśanam sthitiḥ ca
na
sva rūpa mātre śīla śabda ayogāt
na hi mṛṣ aṅga śīlaḥ mārdaṅgikaḥ
mṛṣ aṅga vācana śīlaḥ hi saḥ ucyate
na hi vyāpāra śūnye kvacid api śīla śabdaḥ prayujyate
nanu ca sthiti prakāśau api sattva tamasoḥ svarūpam
tat etena eva gamyate sva rūpe śīla śabdaḥ prasaṃkṣyate iti
ucyate na svarūpe sarvatra śīla śabda prayoṅaḥ
iha api rajasi duḥkha svarūpe kriyā śīlam iti kriyayā samprayujya śīla śabda vyapadeśaḥ
sthiti prakāśau api vyāpāra rūpau abhipretau
atha matam kriyā api rajasaḥ svarūpam eva iti na pradhāna avasthāyām sāmya abhyupagamāt guṇānām
yadi kriyā rajasaḥ sva rūpam abhaviṣyat
pradhānasya api kriyāvat tvam guṇa sāmya avasthāyām abhaviṣyat
kārya avasthāyām hi kriyāvat tvam abhyupagamyate na pradhāna velāyām
tasmāt nityāḥ na svarūpa abhiprāyeṇa śīla śabda prayogaḥ
tatra akriyā śīlayoḥ api sattva tamasoḥ nityam kriyā śīlena rajasā saṃyogāt rajaḥ kriyayā eva kriyāvat tvam sthiti prakāśayoḥ api iti tad kriyā upacāreṇa prakāśa śīlam sattvam sthiti śīlam tamaḥ iti vyapadiśyate
sthiti prakāśayoḥ ātmalābhasya rajaḥ kriyā pūrva tvāt calatoḥ eva abhivyakteḥ tācchīlyam sattva tamasoḥ ucyate
tatra prakāśa śīlam yat tat sattvam
kriyā śīlam pravṛtti śīlam rajaḥ
sthiti śīlam varaṇa śīlam niyama śīlam tamaḥ iti ete guṇāḥ paraspara uparakta pravibhāgāḥ paraspareṇa uparaktaḥ pravibhāgaḥ bhedaḥ yeṣām guṇānām te paraspara uparakta pravibhāgāḥ
yathā prakāśa śīlam iti sattvam ucyate
rajaḥ kriyā uparañjanāt sarva avabhāsa samarthasya api sattvasya niyata prakāśa tvam tapa auparakta tvena
tathā rajasaḥ api pravṛtti abhivyaktiḥ sattva uparāgeṇa
niyata pravṛtti tvam tu tamauparāgeṇa
tathā tamasaḥ api sthiti abhivyaktiḥ sattva uparāgeṇa
sthiti śīla tvam rajaḥ oparāgeṇa
sthitiḥ tu svatas eva
rajasaḥ api pravṛttiḥ svatas
sattvasya api prakāśaḥ svatas eva ittham eva anyeṣu api kāryeṣu sattva ādīnām itaretara uparāgaḥ draṣṭavaḥ
saṃyoga viyoga dharmāṇaḥ
saṃyogaḥ ca viyogaḥ ca saṃyoga viyogau tau dharmau yeṣām te saṃyoga viyoga dharmāṇaḥ
kasmin cit kārye ārabhyamāṇe guṇa pradhāna bhāvena anyonyam saṃyujyante
tathā eva ārabdha kārya virodhi dharma antara udaye parasparam viyujyante
itaretara upāśrayeṇa upārjita mūrtayaḥ mahat ādi stamba paryantāḥ mūrtayaḥ itaretara upāśrayeṇa upārjitāḥ yaiḥ te itaretara upāśrayeṇa upārjita mūrtayaḥ
parasparataḥ bhinnāḥ api paramārthataḥ nyonyataḥ nye api
asambhinna śakti pravibhāgāḥ atyante vyāvṛtta kārya ārambha ābhimukhya sāmarthya prabhedāḥ
etat uktam bhavati ekasmin kārye ārabdhavye tyanta vyatiṣakta paraspara śaktayaḥ kārya ārambha kāle pṛthaktvena an upalakṣyamāṇa śakti pravibhāgāḥ iti
tulya jātīya atulya jātīya śakti bheda anupātinaḥ
sāttvikānām sattvam tulya jātiḥ rājasānām rahaḥ tulya jātiḥ tāmasānām tamaḥ iti ca
paraspara apekṣayā tu bhinna jātīya tvam
tulya jātīya atulya jātīyānām śakti prabhedam anupatitum śīlam yeṣām te tulya jātīya atulya jātīya śakti prabheda anupātinaḥ
na hi sāttvike vā rājase tāmase vā prārabdhavyasya trayāṇām śakti prabheda anupātam antareṇa kārya ārambhaḥ sambhavati
yadi evam sarva śakti prabheda anupāti tvāt ekaikasya kārya ārambhe tulyam prādhānyam iti atas āha pradhāna velāyām upadarśita sannidhānāḥ sarve
ekaikasmin prādhānyena sva kārya ārambhiṇi tad kāle api sannidhānam upasarjana bhāvena upadarśitam iti pradhāna velāyām upadarśita sannidhānāḥ
na hi sarveṣām yugapad prādhānyam
sama pradhāna tve hi pradhānam eva bhaveyuḥ na kārya ārambhi tvam
atha ucyate katham punar ekasmin prādhānena kārya ārambhiṇī itara astitvam avagamyate iti
tat ucyate guṇa tve ca upasarjana bhāve ca vyāpāra mātreṇa pradhāna upalakṣyamāṇena vyāpāra mātreṇa
pradhāna antar nītena na hi pradhānasya antar nītaḥ vyāpāraḥ itarayoḥ upasarjana bhāvena asannidhāne saṃbhaviṣyati iti pradhāna vyāpāreṇa anumita astitvāḥ
puruṣa artha itikartavya tā prayukta sāmarthyāḥ puruṣa arthaḥ bhoga apavargau tasya iti kartavya tā yathā yathā artha niṣpattiḥ tathā tathā prayuktam kārya ārambhim prati sāmarthyam yeṣām te puruṣa artha itikartavya tā pratyukta sāmarthyāḥ
sannidhi mātra upakārāṇiḥ vikāra pratyaya rūpa sannidhi mātreṇa puruṣa asya upakuruvanti iti sannidhi mātra upakāriṇaḥ
ayaskānta maṇi kalpāḥ
pratyayam vṛttim jñānam antareṇa ekatamasya vṛttim sthiti lakṣaṇām samastām
pradhāna śabda vācyāḥ bhavanti
na eva triguṇī vyatirekeṇa anyat pradhānam nāma asti
te eva guṇāḥ sāmya avasthāḥ pradhāna eka śabda abhidhānīyakam pratipadyante
vaiṣamyam bhajantaḥ vikāra śabda abhidheyāḥ vṛttimantaḥ bhavanti
etat dṛśyam iti ucyate
tat etat dṛśyam bhūta inriya ātmakam bhūta ātmakam indriya āmakam ca
katham tad ātmaka tvam iti āha bhūta bhāvena pṛṭhivī ādinā sūkṣma sthūlena sūkṣmeṇa tanmātra rūpeṇa sthūlena viśeṣa arūpreṇa
dvividhaḥ hi bhūta bhāvaḥ tanmātra rūpaḥ viśeṣa rūpaḥ ca
vipariṇamate sthla sukṣma bhāvam āpadyate
indriya bhāvena indriya rūpeṇa śrotra ādinā sūkṣma sthūlena vipariṇamate
sūkṣmeṇa ahaṅkāra rūpeṇa sthcūlena śrotra ādi rūpeṇa
tat tu dṛśyam na aprayojanam
sarvatra eva pravṛtteḥ prayojana darśanāt
api tu prayojanam ūri kṛtasya aṅgīkṛtya pravartate
kim punar dṛśya pravṛtti prayojanam iti āha bhāga apavarga artham hi dṛśyam puruṣasya agni ādi pratipatti vat
kau oubaḥ tau bhoga apavargau iti āha tatra iṣṭa aniṣṭa guṇa svarūpa avadhāraṇam avibhāga āpannam iṣṭānām agaru candana sparśana di lakṣaṇānām aniṣṭānām pratikūla ātmakānām kṛpāṇa kaṇṭaka ādi smarśana rūpāṇām guṇānām svarūpa avadhāraṇam svarūpa avagamaḥ svarūpa adhyavasānam
tasya viśeṣaṇam avibhāga āpannam puruṣa pratyaye na ayam puruṣaḥ idam sattvam iti avibhāga tām gatam
prāpta caitanya upagraha rūpa tvāt bauddhasya pratyaysya
saḥ ittham bhūtaḥ puruṣasya bhogaḥ iti ākhyāyate
tasmāt bhoga svarūpāt pratyayāt vivicya dṛśi rūpasya svarūpa avadhāraṇam bhoktṛ svarūpāt avadhāryamāṇāt uttarakālam api apavṛttasya viśeṣa abhāvāt apvargaḥ iti ucyate
sarvadā sva rūpa pratiṣṭyhaḥ hi tadā saḥ iti
vṛtti sārūpyam itaratra viśeṣaḥ iti
dvayoḥ bhoga apavargayoḥ atiriktam anyat tṛtīyam darśanam na asti
yāvat avidyā tāvat iṣṭa aniṣṭe staḥ iti bhogaḥ eva
puruṣasya tu aheya anupādeya svarūpa tvāt tad avadhāraṇe kutas bhogaḥ iti bhoga rūpasya avidyā lakṣaṇasya pratyayasya pratipakṣaḥ pratyayaḥ puruṣa avadhāraṇam yasmāt etat atas etat darśana dvaya vyatirekeṇa tṛtīyam arśana antaram na kalpayitum śakyate
tathā ca uktam ayam tu khalu evam samyagdarśī triṣu guṇeṣu ukta lakṣaṇeṣu kartuṣu sarva vyāpāra nirvṛtti kareṣu akartāri ca guṇa dharma vilakṣaṇe puruṣe caturthe tad kriyā sākṣiṇi guṇa kriyāsu upadraṣṭari sandhi kriyā sākṣi bhūta upadraṣṭṛ vat upānīyamānān antar klaraṇa lakṣaṇaiḥ guṇaiḥ prāpyamāṇān darśita viṣaya tvāt sarva bhāvān upapannān gauṇān eva bauddha pratyaya ākāreṇa pariniṣpnnān paśyan upalabhamānaḥ n
na asti eva anyat samyak darśanam iti manyate
tāvatau bhoga apavargau buddhi kṛtau buddhi nirvartikau buddhau eva vartamānau
anya kṛtasya api anyatra vṛttiḥ dṛṣṭā yathā rajaka kṛtaḥ vastra rāgaḥ iti katham puruṣe apadiśyete iti tau buddhau eva vartamānau puruṣe padiśyete iti kutas etat sa hi tat tat phalasya bhoktā iti smyak mithyā pratyayoḥ upalabdhā iti
dṛṣṭāntena vyākhgyātam artham nigamayati yathā vijayaḥ parājayaḥ vā iti
buddheḥ eva artha aparisamāptiḥ bandhaḥ iti
yāvat samāptau kartavyau bhogāḥ apavargau iti buddhiḥ manyate tāvat bandhaḥ
tad artha avasāyaḥ mokṣaḥ
tasyāḥ eva buddheḥ artha avasāyaḥ kartavya samāptiḥ
yadā ātma vilakṣaṇam bandha mokṣa asambandhinām puruṣam īkṣite na asya kartavyam asti iti sa kartavya avasāyaḥ buddheḥ mokṣaḥ iti
etena ūha apoha kriyāḥ yathā nyāya avadhāraṇa abhiniveśāḥ puruṣe dhyā āropita sadbhāvāḥ iti jñeyāḥ
pratyaya tva aviśeṣāt buddhi dharmāḥ buddhau eva vartamānāḥ buddhi kṛtāḥ puruṣe dhyāropita sadbhāvāḥ puruṣaḥ gṛhṇāti puruṣaḥ dhārayati iti evam eva puruṣe adhyāropyante
grahaṇam śabdaḥ ādīnām śrotra ādibhiḥ upādānam
gṛhītānām a vismaraṇam dhāraṇam
dhāritasya sāmānya viśeṣa avadhāraṇam vijñānam
vijñātasya eva punar tat gata viśeṣa avabubhutsayā ūhanmūhaḥ ūhitasya viruddhānām dharmāṇām vyudasanam apohaḥ
viṣayesu pravṛttiḥ kriyā
vākya viṣayaḥ vṛtti viśeṣaḥ cittasya vacanam
yaḥ yaḥ nyāyaḥ yathānyāyam yasya ca vastunaḥ tathā eva avadhāraṇam yathā nyāya avadhāraṇām
tatra punar punar samyak pratyaya avicalanāya yaḥ cittasya abhiyogaḥ saḥ abhiniveśaḥ
te ete grahaṇa ādayaḥ puruṣe dhyā āropita sadbhāvāḥ
sa hi tat phalasya bhoktā iti grahaṇa ādi phalasya upalabdhā iti
dṛśyānām guṇānām yathā vyākhyāta ātmanām svarūpa bheda avadhāraṇa artham tattva avasthā bheda avadhāraṇa artham idam sūtram ārabhyate viśeṣa aviśeṣa liṅga mātra aliṅgāḥ guṇa parvāṇaḥ
viśeṣāḥ ca aviśeṣāḥ ca liṅga mātram ca aliṅgaḥ ca na liṅgati kutas cit na āgacchati pradhāna ākhyaḥ arthaḥ iti pacāt yat sarva dhātubhyaḥ iti yaugikaḥ san abhidheya liṅgam bhajate
yaḥ vā liṅgam na vidyate liṅgam avagamanam paricchedaḥ pratyakṣeṇa pradhāna ākhyasya arthasya asau aliṅgaḥ iti bahuvrīhiḥ
te ca viśeṣa ādayaḥ puruṣa abhiprāyam pālayanti bhoga apavarga pradānena pūrayanti vā vikārān svān iti piparteḥ anyebhyaḥ api dṛśyante iti kartari vanipratyayaḥ
tathā ca sati yat na antam a kartari tat napuṃsakam
yat tu na antum kartari tat sarva liṅgam bhavati yathā berudṛśvā merudṛśvani iti
tatas ca viśeṣa ādayaḥ parvāṇaḥ
keṣām te sambandhinaḥ iti guṇānām parvāṇaḥ guṇa parvāṇaḥ
keṣāṃcid ayam eva pāṭhaḥ viśeṣa aviśeṣa liṅga mātra aliṅkāni guṇa parvāṇi iti
tatra ākāśa vāyu agni jala bhūmayaḥ bhūtāni
śabda tanmātra ārabdham ākāśam sparśa tanmātreṇa śabda sparśa lakṣaṇena ārabdhaḥ vāyuḥ
rūpa tanmātreṇa śabda sparśa rūpa lakṣaṇena ārabdhaḥ gniḥ
rasa tanmātreṇa śabda sparśa rūpa rasa catuṣṭaya lakṣaṇena apāarabdhāḥ
gandha tanmātreṇa śabda sparśa rūpa rasa gandha pañcataya lakṣaṇena bhūmiḥ ārabdhā
nanu ca nityam ākāśam prāk utpatteḥ vināśa kālam ca viśeṣa abhāvāt
yaḥ yaḥ autpattimān tasya tasya pṛthivyā ādeḥ prāk utpatteḥ vināśa uttara kālam ca viśeṣaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ
tathā ākāśam yadi utpattimat syāt prāk utpatteḥ vināśa uttara kālam ca bhvet viśeṣaḥ
na ca saḥ sti tasmāt ākācam anutpattikam
atha avakāśa dāna abhāavaḥ viśeṣaḥ iti ced na mūrtimataḥ nyasya abhāvāt tulyam nitya tve api anitya lakṣaṇa abhāvāt ca nityam ākāśam
na āgama virodhāt
tasmāt vai etasmāt ātmanaḥ ākāśaḥ sambhūtaḥ iti āgama virodhaḥ
smṛti virodhaḥ ca
avakāśam kurvati tad upacāraḥ iti ced na vāyu ādiṣu api upacāra prasaṅgāt
ākāśāt vāyuḥ sambhūtaḥ eti eka vākya tvāt
prāk utpatteḥ viśeṣa abhāvāt anityaḥ na bhavati iti ca bruvatā viśeṣa abhāvāt nitya tvam iti uktam bhavati
tathā ca sati ātma ādīnām api bandha mokṣa upalabdhi ādi viśeṣa abhāvāt sataḥ vaiśeṣikasya anitya tva prasaṅgaḥ tathā paramāṇu ādīnām ca anitya tvam prasajyeta
atha api utpattimataḥ eva prāk ūrdhvam ca viśeṣa bhāva abhāvau vivakṣitau iti ced na ākāśasya utpatti abhyupagama prasaṅgāt
atha ākāśa utpatti vādinā aviśeṣaḥ vaktum na śakyate iti ced na puruṣa artha sādhana asādhana tva viśeṣāt
sarvagata tvāt iti ca asiddhaḥ hetuḥ
asarvagatāni kāka cit ākāśa manāṃsi anityāni ca svārtha abhāve parārtha tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat
utpattimanti ca pradhā anupuruṣābhyām anya tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat
evam ākāśam utpattimat anityam ca bāhya indriya viṣaya tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat
bhūta tvāt ca pṛthivī vat
anitya dravya saṃyoga uta ādi aguṇa tvāt
pṛthivī ādi vat
vcikitsā nivartya prakopa kara tvāt vāyu vat
nabhaḥ ca prakopaḥ cikitsā nirvartanīyaḥ cikitsaka prasiddhim upārūḍhaḥ
etena anitya sādharmyam vyākhyātam
etāni ca bhūtāni śabda sparśa rūpa rasa gandha tanmātrāṇām aviśeṣāṇām viśeṣāḥ
śānta ghora mūḍha ādi aneka viśeṣavat tvāt viśeṣāḥ
śānta ādi avhāvāt ca aviśeṣāḥ tad mātrāṇi
tathā śrotra tvac cakṣuḥ jihvā ghrāṇāni śabda ādi viṣaya buddhi artha tvāt buddhīndiryāṇi sva viṣaya buddhibhiḥ eva anumitāni
vāc pāṇi pāda pāyu upasthāni karmendriyāṇi vacana ādi kriyā nirvartakāni tad animitāni eva
na vāda ādīni karmendriyāṇi siddhāni iti ced na śruti prasiddha tvāt
indriyāṇi prakṛtya sarveṣām vedānām vāc eka ayanam ityādi śruteḥ
smṛtiṣu ca sarvatra eva vidhi pratiṣedha viṣaya pravṛtti nivṛttima tvāt ca śrotra ādi vat indri atvam
na vākya capalaḥ na pāṇi pāda capalaḥ ityādeḥ vidhi pratiṣedha viṣaya pravṛtti nivṛttimat tva siddhiḥ
tathā vāgāḍīni indriyāṇi kauśalavat tvāt cakṣuḥ ādi vat
sarva gātreṣu ca indriya śaktiḥ karaṇa vṛttyāḥ sandarśanāt iṣyate eva
vāgguda prabhṛtīnām sarpa ādīnām mūka ṣaṇḍānām ca mukham eva upastha indriyam
ekādaśam manaḥ sarva artham atīta anāgata vartamāna viṣaya artham buddhīndriya karmendriya viṣaya artham ca
etāni ekādaśa indriyāṇi asmitā smitā asmi iti pratyayaḥ sa ca lakṣaṇam yasya saḥ smita lakṣaṇaḥ smitā pratyayena hi lakṣyate liṅgyate ṣaṣṭham a viśeṣa ākhyam tattvam ahaṅkāraḥ
tasya aviśeṣasya viśeṣāḥ etāni guṇānām aviśeṣa ākāra saṃsthitānām sattva ādīnām eṣa ṣodaśakaḥ viśeṣa pariṇāmaḥ sattva bahulā pṛthivī grāhya tvāt
tām a sattve api eṣām guṇa pradhāna kṛtaḥ viśeṣaḥ
karaṇāni prakāśa tvāt sattva bahulāni manaḥ ṣaṣṭhāni tu buddhīndriyāṇi prakāśa prādhānyāt sattva bahulāni
kriyā prādhānyāt rajaḥ bahulāni
ṣaṭ aviśeṣāḥ
tat yathā śabda mātram sparśa mātram iti dvi lakṣaṇasya api pradhānena vyapadeśaḥ
tathā rūpa mātram iti tri lakṣaṇasya api pradhānena vyapadeśaḥ
tathā uttarayoḥ api mātra śabdaḥ śānta ghora ādi viśeṣa vyāvartana arthaḥ
eka dvi tri catur pañca lakṣaṇa bhedāḥ śabda tattva eka lakṣaṇaḥ śabda tanmātra bhedaḥ
śabda sparśa lakṣaṇaḥ sparśa tanmātra bhedaḥ iti evam ekaika ādhikyena uttaratra api draṣṭavyam
ṣaṣṭhaḥ ca aviśeṣaḥ smita mātraḥ śabda ādi tanmātra apekṣayā ṣaṣṭhaḥ indriyāṇām ekādaśānām aviśeṣaḥ
ete sattva mātrasya astitva mātrasya liṅga mātrasya mūrti mātrasya pradhānasya amūrtasya prathamā mūrtiḥ iyam yathā bījasya aṅkurībhāvaḥ
ātmanaḥ vastu rūpasya mahataḥ sarva viśeṣa aviśeṣebhyaḥ mahā tvāt ṣaṣ aviśeṣa pariṇāmāḥ ṣaṣ aviśeṣāḥ eva pariṇāmāḥ sattva ādīnām mahat rūpa avasthitānām amī aviśeṣa pariṇāmāḥ
yat tat param sūkṣmam aviśeṣebhyaḥ liṅgamātram mahat tattvam tasmin ete sattā mātre mahat tvāt mahati avasthāya kāraṇa svarūpe mahati avasthāya vivṛddhi kāṣṭhām pṛthivī ādi viśeṣa anta tām anubhavanti
pratisaṃsṛjyamānāḥ ca pratilīyamānāḥ ca aviśeṣāḥ tasmin eva sattā mātre liṅga mātre mahati ātmani avasthāya avyaktam prati yānti
kim viśiṣṭam nissattā asattvam viśeṣa aviśeṣa dharma rahitam
nissad asat iti avyaktāt īṣat vikṛtam iti sat aviśeṣebhyaḥ sūkṣmataram iti ca asat sat ca asat ca sat asat iti mahat tattvam ucyate
tat dharma rahitam avyaktam nissad asat iti
eṣa teṣām guṇānām sattva ādīnām liṅgamātraḥ pariṇāmaḥ yasmin avasthāya vivṛddhi kāṣṭhām pratilayam ca pratiyānti a viśeṣāḥ
nissatta sattam ca avyaktam ca yat sa teṣām eva guṇānām aliṅga pariṇāmaḥ
paraḥ ca na sūkṣmaḥ vasthā antara pariṇāmaḥ sti guṇānām
sūkṣma viṣaya tvam ca aliṅga paryavasānam iti hi
aliṅga tvāt eva aliṅga avasthāyām na puruṣa arthaḥ hetuḥ
aliṅga avasthā nimittam na puruṣa arthaḥ hetuḥ na aliṅga avasthā puruṣa artha prayuktā iti arthaḥ
tat etat vyācaṣṭe na aliṅga avasthāyām ādau puruṣa artha tā kāraṇam
kasmāt punar tad avasthā puruṣa artha prayuktā na bhavati iti tatas āha yasmāt na asyām puruṣa artha tā kāraṇam vidyate svayam api na asau puruṣa artha tā mahat ādi vat asaṃvedya tvāt īśvarāṇām api
yatas ca etat evam tasmāt nityā vyākhyāyate
yaḥ hi puruṣa artha prayuktaḥ saḥ nityaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yathā pṛthivyādiḥ
na ca eṣā pradhāna avasthā puruṣa artha prayuktā iti nityā vyākhyāyate
trayāṇām tu avasthā viśeṣāṇām viśeṣa aviśeṣa liṅga mātrāṇām ādau puruṣa artha tā mahat ādi avasthā puruṣa artha prayuktā
sa ca arthaḥ sa ca puruṣa arthaḥ hetuḥ nimittam kāraṇam iti anityāḥ vyākhyāyante mahat ādyaḥ tisnaḥ vasthāḥ
guṇāḥ tu sarva dharma anupātinaḥ sarva vikāra anupātinaḥ
yathā sarpaḥ prāṃśu tva sarpaṇa kuṇḍala tva ādi viśeṣa anupātī tathā viśeṣa ādi tattva anupātinaḥ guṇāḥ piṇḍa pratyaya anupātinaḥ ca na pralīyante na upajāyante
yathā sarpaḥ kuṇḍala ādi tve pralīyamāne na pralīyate tat upajane ca na upajāyate tathā eva guṇāḥ api
yathā ca ghaṭa piṭhara ādiṣu pralīyamāneṣu jāyamāneṣu ca mṛd na pralīyate na api jāyate
guṇāḥ vyaktibhiḥ eva dharmaiḥ eva atīta anāgata vyaya āgam avayībhiḥ tri lakṣaṇābhiḥ guṇa anvayībhiḥ guṇa upādāna kāraṇābhiḥ upajana apāya dharmakāḥ iva utpatti pralayavantaḥ iva pratyavabhāsante na sva rūpeṇa vinaśyanti jāyante vā
etasya eva arthasya dṛṣṭāntam āha devadattaḥ
kasmāt yena asya mriyante gāvaḥ iti
gavām eva maraṇāt tasya daridrāṇam na sva rūpa hānāt iti samaḥ samādhiḥ tulyaḥ carocaḥ dṛṣṭāntena dārṣṭāntikasya devadatta daridrāṇa vat eva guṇa anugatābhiḥ vyaktibhiḥ mahat ādibhiḥ guṇa virmarda ba vaucitrya kṛtābhiḥ vivardhamānābhiḥ guṇānām āḍhya tā tat pralaye ca teṣām daridrāṇam na sva rūpeṇa apacayaḥ upacayaḥ vā iti tulyaḥ samādhiḥ iti
sarvasya pradhāna kārya tve sati viśeṣāḥ aviśeṣāḥ vā kasmāt anantaram na upajāyante iti tat āha liṅgasya aliṅgam pratyāsannam yathā mūlam vṛkṣasya pratyāsannam bīje saṃsṛṣṭam mūlam eva prathamataram vivicyate na vṛkṣasya uttara avasthā
evam tatra pradhāne tat liṅgam saṃsṛṣṭam saṃlīnam prathamam vīdyate āvirbhavati na uttare viśeṣāḥ viprakṛṣṭa tvāt eva
tat eva āha krama anatipatteḥ krama anatikramāt
na hi loke kasyacid utpadyamānasya krama atilaṅghanam asti
tathā ṣaṭ aviśeṣāḥ pūrva uktāḥ liṅga mātre pratyāsanna tvāt saṃsṛṣṭa tvāt vivicyante
kasmāt iti āha pariṇāma krama niyamāt
tathā teṣu aviśeṣeṣu bhūta indriyāṇi
tad mātreṣu bhūtāni saṃsṛṣṭāni vivicyante
asmitā mātre indriyāṇi manaḥ sahitāni
tathā ca ukta purastāt
na viśeṣebhyaḥ prāk uktebhyaḥ ākāśa ādibhyaḥ param tattva antaram asti
na viśeṣāṇām anyaḥ tattva antara pariṇāmaḥ iti arthaḥ
etat eva āha viśeṣāṇām na asti tattva antaram iti tattvam hi nāma sādhāraṇam sarva prāṇa dhāriṇām mahāpralaya sthāyi
na evam lakṣaṇam pṛthivī ādibhyaḥ utpadyamānam anyat asti

teṣām tu viśeṣāṇām dharma lakṣaṇa avasthā pariṇāmā vyākhyāyiṣyante tṛtīya pāde
vyākhgyātam dṛśyam avadhṛtam dṛśyam
yat artham ca dṛśyate tasya idānīm draṣṭuḥ svarūpa avadhāraṇa artham idam ārabhyate draṣṭā dṛśi mātraḥ śuddhaḥ api pratyaya anupaśyaḥ draṣṭā dṛśyasya yathā vyākhyāta rūpasya upalabdhā puruṣaḥ
tasya idam lakṣaṇam dṛśi mātraḥ śuddhe api pratyaya anupaśyaḥ ca iti
punastāt ākhyātam tadā draṣṭuḥ svarūpe vasthānam vṛtti sārūpyam itaratra iti ca tat eva dvayam iha pratipādyate
pratisaṃvedī buddheḥ puruṣaḥ iti upapādayiṣyāmaḥ iti tat ca atra upapādyate
dṛśiḥ darśanam upalabdhiḥ tāvat mātraḥ dṛśi mātraḥ
yatas evam tasmāt śuddhaḥ
śuddhaḥ api san asau bauddhasya pratyayasya anupaśyaḥ dṛśi mātra tvāt eva
tasmāt tam anupaśyan tad sva rūpaḥ bhavati
dṛśi sannidhau vṛtteḥ dṛśi sva rūpa avabhāsa tā draṣṭuḥ vṛtti sārūpyam
dṛśi mātrasya eva a vikriyā ātmakasya sataḥ asya bauddha pratyaya anudarśanam yasmāt tasmāt ca svarūpa pratiṣṭha tā ca siddhā
pratyaya anupaśye iti
etat tu tat astitva anumānam
katham ghaṭa ādīnām dṛśyānām sva rūpa vyatiriktena anyena dṛśya tva darśanāt tat prakāśakānām ca āloka ādīnām vyatirikta dṛśya tvāt sarva artha avabhāsakānām api pratyayānām sva rūpa vyatirikta dṛśya tvam dṛśya tvāt avagamyate ghaṭa ādi tad āloka ādi vat iti
yasmāt ca bauddham eva pratyayam anupaśyati tam ca paśyati eva na kadācid sva visayam pratyayam na paśyati tasmāt dṛśi mātraḥ
mātra grahaṇam dharma antara nirvartana artham
etena draṣṭuḥ dṛśiḥ iti etat nirvartitam iddha ādi samāna āśraya tvam ca nirvartitam dṛśeḥ eva draṣṭṛ tvāt
tat etat ucyate dṛśi mātraḥ iti dṛś śaktiḥ eva dṛś darśanam tat eva śaktiḥ dṛś śhaktiḥ
na api anyaḥ dṛkchaktimān asti
sā eva śaktiḥ dṛś iti
tatra mātra śabda artham vyācaṣṭe viśeṣeṇa aparāmṛṣṭā iti arthaḥ
viśeṣeṇa kenacid icchā ādinā guṇaiḥ guṇa dharmaiḥ ca aparāmṛṣṭaḥ
sa puruṣaḥ buddheḥ pratiṣaṃveditum śīlam asya iti pratisaṃvedī
bauddha pratyaya upalabdhi svabhāvaḥ iti arthaḥ
puruṣaḥ buddheḥ pratisaṃvedī dṛśi mātraḥ śuddhaḥ ca iti katham gamyate iti āha sa buddheḥ na sarūpaḥ na atyantam virūpaḥ iti
na samāna lakṣaṇaḥ na api atyanta vidharvā iti etat
asarūpa tayā dṛśi mātra tvam śuddha tvam ca āha
na atyanta virūpaḥ iti vṛtti sārūpya tām āha
katham punar na sarūpa tā iti ucyate na tāvat sarūpaḥ
kasmāt kaḥ hetuḥ
buddheḥ tāvat svarūpam vaidharmya darśana artham āha jñāta ajñāta viṣaya tvāt pariṇāminī buddhiḥ iti
kaḥ punar asau buddheḥ iṣayaḥ yaḥ jñātaḥ ca a jñātaḥ ca
yena bāhya ākāreṇa pariṇatā buddhiḥ sa jñātaḥ
yena ākāreṇa na pariṇatā saḥ jñātaḥ
yadi na pariṇameta apariṇamamānā ced viṣayam vikhyāpayet sadā eva viṣayi tvam buddheḥ syāt
tasmāt jñāta ajñāta viṣaya tā pariṇāmi tvam khyāpayati
pariṇāminī buddhiḥ jñāta ajñāta viṣaya tvāt
dīpa cakṣuḥ ādi viṣaya vat
tad vilakṣaṇaḥ puruṣaḥ sadā jñāta viṣayaḥ
sarvadā hi jñātaḥ eva puruṣasya svaḥ viṣayaḥ
tasmāt sadā jñāta viṣaya tvam puruṣasya apariṇāmi tvam paridīpayati
sadā asiddham puruṣasya iti āśaṅkya āha kasmāt kaḥ hetuḥ na hi iti hi śabdaḥ prasiddha avadyotana arthaḥ
buddhiḥ ca nāma buddhiḥ iti bauddha pratyayaḥ puruṣasya viṣayaḥ syāt agṛhītā gṛhītā ca iti
sarvadā ca gṛhītaḥ eva bauddhaḥ pratyayaḥ
tad avyabhicāreṇa eva puruṣasya vyatirikta tva siddhiḥ
tasmāt puruṣasya sadā jñāta viṣaya tvam
tatas ca apariṇāmi tvam iddham
apariṇāmī puruṣaḥ iti pratijñā
sadā jñāta viṣaya tvāt iti hetuḥ
vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ buddhi ādiḥ
nanu ca buddhyā vyavasitam artham puruṣaḥ cetayati buddheḥ ca sarvaḥ viṣayaḥ jñātaḥ ca ajñātaḥ ca puruṣasya api samānaḥ
jñāta ajñāta viṣaya tvam buddhyāḥ vyavasita artha upalambhi tvāt
tasmāt puruṣasya api pariṇāmi tvam jñāta ajñāta viṣaya tvāt buddhi vat eva
na eṣa doṣaḥ
buddheḥ eva puruṣa viṣaya tvāt
buddhiḥ eva hi bāhya artha ākārā puruṣasya viṣayaḥ na arthaḥ kevalaḥ svarūpeṇa
tasmāt nityā na jñāta ajñāta viṣayaḥ puruṣaḥ
buddhiḥ tu sadā eva jñātā eva iti na pariṇāmi tvam puruṣasya
nanu ca buddhyā vyavasitam artham puruṣaḥ cetayati iti kaścid āha
tat katham ucyate na taiḥ api apariṇāmi tvasya abhyupagamāt puruṣasya
buddhyā vyavasitam artham iti etat uktam bhavati buddhi ākāram cetayati buddhi vyavasāya ākāra āpannam artham cetayati iti
anyathā hi teṣām pariṇāmi tva parārtha tva saṃhatyakāri tva ādayaḥ buddhi dharmāḥ sarve eva prasajeyuḥ
atha apariṇāmi tve darśana anupapattiḥ iti ced na darśanasya eva puruṣa svarūpa tāt
yaḥ hi puruṣa pariṇāmi tvam abhimanyate saḥ idam pra draṣṭavyaḥ kim pariṇāmena kriyate iti
sa ced abhidadhīta darśanam iti
sa pratyabhidhānīyaḥ puruṣasya darśanam eva rūpam atas pariṇāma ānarthakyam iti
sa ced pratibrūyāt na puruṣasya upalabdhiḥ bhogaḥ kasmāt tarhi vikriyā eva bhogaḥ iti
sa punar vaktavyaḥ tathā api vikriyāvat tvāt anitya tvam upanatam śarīra ādi vat eva
atha api pratibhāṣeta sva ātmani vikriyā na anitya tva kāraṇam syāt kim tu avasthā antara bhāvi kriyā hi kāraṇam anitya tvasya iti
sa punar pratibhāṣitavyaḥ vikriyā avasthāyāḥ eva avasthā antara tvāt
pūrvam avikṛtasya vastunaḥ punar vikriyā avasthā antaram
kim ca viṣaya abhyupagame ca vikriyā eva tāvatā niyamaḥ pāryate na kartum
na ca api sva ātmani vikriyamāṇānām vajra vaidūrya ādīnām anitya tvam na asti
na ca vikriyā janitasya eva darśanasya dṛśya viṣaya tvam na nityasya darśanasya iti niyama hetuḥ asti
vikriyā eva upalabdhiḥ na vikriyā janitā iti ced na śarīra ādīnām vikriyāvatām upalabdhi prasaṅgāt
tasmāt dṛśi mātraḥ evā apariṇāmī ca sadā jñāta viṣaya tvāt puruṣaḥ iti siddham
tasya ca ntya upalabdhi sva rūpa tve api dṛśya bauddha pratyaya bhāva abhāva kṛtaḥ yam vyapadeśaḥ paśyati darśayiṣyati dadarśa iti ca
savitṛ ādi pakāśana vyapadeśa vat
yathā savitā prakāśayiṣyati prācīkaśāt iti ca prakāśya bhāva abhāva kṛtaḥ vyapadeśaḥ
śuddha tva ādayaḥ hetavaḥ abuddhi ādayaḥ dṛṣṭāntāḥ
i taḥ ca a sarūpaḥ
sarva artha adhyavasāyi tvāt dhora śānta ādi samasta artha avasāyi tvāt triguṇā buddhiḥ śrotra ādi vat
guṇānām tu upadraṣṭā iti upadraṣṭṛ tvam hetuḥ
atriguṇaḥ purusaḥ iti pratijñā
vaidharmyeṇa abuddhi ādiḥ eva triguṇa tvāt ca asarūpaḥ
astu tarhi virūpaḥ eva
tatas ca atyanta virūpa tvāt bhoga anupapattiḥ iti
atrā ucyate na atyantam virūpaḥ
kasmāt kaḥ tra hetuḥ na hi śuddhasya buddhi svarūpa virūpasya aśuddha bauddha pratyayāt atyanta vairūpya siddhaye hetuḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ
na buddhi pratyaya sākṣi tvasya siddha tvāt
yatas śuddhaḥ api asau bauddham pratyayam anupaśyati tat ca bauddha pratyaya anudarśanam sādhitam
anupaśyati iti viṣaya kāra pariṇāme sati bauddham pratyayam paśyati iti arthaḥ
tam anupaśyan api na tad ātmā na triguṇaḥ
tad ātmakaḥ iva śānta ghora mūḍha vyavasāya rūpaḥ iva pratyavabhāsate
tasmāt nityāḥ na atyanta virūpaḥ pravṛtti sārūpyāt
tatra yat uktam buddheḥ pratisaṃvedī puruṣaḥ iti upapādayiṣyāmaḥ iti tat upapāditam
tathā ca tad sārūpyam ādarśitam
tathā uktam tantre apariṇāminī bhoktṛ śaktiḥ dṛś haktiḥ yathā vyākhyāta rūpā apratisaṅkramā ca pariṇāminī arthe bauddhe pratyaye pratisaṅkrāntā iva pratyaya viṣaya tvāt tad vṛttim anupatantī iva asyāḥ buddheḥ vṛttim anupatantī iva draṣṭṛ tvāt upalabhmānā
bauddhaḥ pratyayaḥ jāyamānaḥ eva dṛkśhakteḥ karmatām āpadyate
tam anupatanti upalabhamānā bhoktṛ śaktiḥ tasyāḥ ca prāpta caitanya upagraha rūpāyāḥ prāptam caitanya upagraha rūpam puruṣa upagraha rūpam yayā buddhi vṛttyā āsāditam pāvaka upagraha rūpa tapta loha piṇḍa vat dṛśi karma tvāt eva anukāra mātra tayā buddhi vṛtti sārūpya mātra tayā buddhi vṛtti a viśiṣṭā jña vṛttiḥ iti jñaḥ eva upalabdhiḥ eva vṛttiḥ iti ākhyāyate
tad arthaḥ eva dṛśyasya ātmā tad śabdena draṣṭā dṛśi mātraḥ śuddhaḥ yathā adhigata ātmā pratyāmnāyate
tad arthaḥ asmai tad arthaḥ tad prayojanaḥ dṛśi karma tva arthaḥ iti arthaḥ
bhoga rūpeṇa apavarga rūpeṇa ca
kaḥ sau iti āha dṛśyasya ātmā pradhānasya ātmā svarūpam svarūpa lābhaḥ iti
nanu catur vyūha tvam vyācikhyāsitam kimartham etat aprakṛtam ucyate
na eṣa doṣaḥ
ātyantika duḥkha nivṛtti prayojanasya prakṛta tvāt
katham dṛśya tādarthya lābha avadhāraṇena ātyantikī duḥkha viratiḥ uktā bhavet iti
ucyate yadi dṛśya sva rūpa pratilṃbhaḥ tad arthaḥ eva tadā aśeṣa tad artha viratau punar kṛtārtha tvāt kārya abhāvāt ātyantika dṛśya viraktiḥ syāt
tasya punar pravṛttau prayojana abhāvāt
na hi kṛtam eva punar karaṇīyakam upāśnute
atha tu sva arthaḥ api dṛśyasya ātma lāmhaḥ bhaviṣyat atas sva arthasya bhāvāt punar punar pravartiṣyata
tatas ca na ātyantikī nivṛttiḥ
tasmāt tādarthyam
dṛśya ātma lābhasya svārtha abhāvaḥ ca dṛśyasya bhogya tvāt odana ādi vat siddhaḥ acetana tvāt saṃhatya kāri tvāt ca
tat āha dṛśi rūpasya puruṣasya karma viṣaya tām āpannam dṛśyam iti
iti śabdaḥ hetvarthe
tad arthaḥ eva dṛśyasya ātmā abhavati sva rūpam bhavati iti arthaḥ
puruṣa arthaḥ eva pradhānasya ātmalābhaḥ dṛśi karmatā āpatteḥ odana ādi vat
sūtra prayojanam ācaṣṭe idānīm tatas ca tādarthyasya niyata tvāt kāraṇāt puruṣa rūpeṇa pratilabdha ātmakam prāpta caitanya upagraha rūpam sat bhoga apavarga artha tāyām kṛtāyām puruṣeṇa na dṛśyate
bhoga apavarga vyatirekeṇa kartavya abhāvāt
sūtra sambandham karoti yam puruṣam prati caritārtham dṛśyam tam prati dṛśi karma tām naḥ āpatsyate iti sva rūpa hānam atas ca sva rūpa hānāt asya vināśaḥ prāptaḥ
na tu vinaśyati sarva ātmanā
kasmāt kaḥ hetuḥ pradhānānām prati puruṣam bahu tvāt kṛtārtham prati naṣṭam eva iti manyate
kṛtārtham prati naṣṭam api anaṣṭam tat anya sādhāraṇa tvāt
kṛtārtham yam puruṣam prati bhoga apavarha nirvartanena kṛta prayojanam tam ekam puruṣam prati punar kārya karaṇa rūpeṇa a pravartanāt bhāva abhāvayoḥ aviśeṣāt naṣṭam api
asya vyākhyānam nāśa prāptam api iti
anaṣṭam tad anya puruṣa sādhāraṇa tvāt
yān prati akṛtārtham tān prati a naṣṭam
katham a naṣṭam iti āha kuśala puruṣān prati nāśa prāptam bhoga apavarga pradānena kuśala puruṣān prati kṛta prayona jam
akuśala puruṣān prati akṛtārtham bhoga apavargayoḥ kartavyayoḥ a kṛta tvāt teṣām akuśalānām dṛśeḥ te eva dṛśiḥ tasyāḥ karma tām dṛśya tām āpannam labhate eva puruṣa rūpeṇa puruṣa nirvhāsa tayā ātma rūpam iti
atas ca sādāraṇa tvāt ekam eva pradhānam pṛthivī ādi vat
kārya karaṇānām ca abhinna tvāt puruṣāṇām nānātvam siddham
sukha duḥkha nānātvāt ca puruṣa bheda siddhiḥ
atas ca dṛś darśana śaktyoḥ nitya tvāt anādiḥ saṃyogaḥ vyākhyātaḥ
tathā ca uktam tantre dharmiṇām anādi saṃyogāt guṇānām puruṣāṇām ca anādi saṃyogāt dharma mātrāṇām mahat ādi kārya kāraṇa antānām api puruṣaiḥ anādiḥ saṃyogaḥ dharmibhiḥ dharmāṇām abhinna tvāt
dṛśyam avadhṛtam
draṣṭā ca avadhṛtaḥ
draṣṭṛ dṛśyayoḥ saṃyogaḥ heya hetuḥ iti ca uktam
sa ca saṃyogaḥ vadhārayitavyaḥ kīdṛśaḥ iti
tatas ca saṃyuoga sva rūpa avadhāraṇa artham idam sūtram pravavṛte sva svāmi śaktyoḥ sva rūpa upalabdhi hetuḥ saṃyogaḥ
sva svāmi śaktyoḥ buddhi puruṣayoḥ svarūpa upalbadheḥ hetuḥ kāraṇam
yasmin sati tayoḥ sva rūpam upalabhyate vadana darpaṇayoḥ iva sa tayoḥ sva rūpa upalabdhi hetuḥ
saṃyogaḥ dṛṣṭṛ dṛśya sva rūpa kārya anumeyaḥ iti arthaḥ
pramāṇam ca atra sva saṃyoga pūrvikā buddhi puruṣayoḥ sva rūpa uplabdhiḥ viṣaya viṣayi sva rūpa upalabdhi tvāt īkṣaṇa darpaṇa sva rūpa uplabdhi vat
yā kācid sukha duḥkha upalabdhiḥ vivāda gocara āpannā sā sukha suḥkha hetu saṃyoga oūrvikā sukha duḥkha upalabdhi tvāt candana kānṭaka sukha duḥkha upalabdhi vat
tat āha puruṣaḥ svāmī dṛśyena svena svayā buddhyā bhoga apavarga darśana artham saṃyuktaḥ
darśana prayuktaḥ eva saṃyogaḥ iti arthaḥ
tasmāt saṃyogāt darśana pratyuktā dṛśyasya upalabshiḥ aviśiṣṭā yā sa bhogaḥ
yā tu draṣṭuḥ sva rūpa upalabdhiḥ viviktā sā u pavargaḥ
yasmāt darśana kārya dvaya prayuktaḥ saṃyogaḥ tasmāt darśana kārya avasānaḥ saṃyogaḥ tena puruṣa saṃyoga vat darśanam viyogasya kāraṇam iti uktam
guṇa puruṣa antara darśanam pradhāna puruṣa viyogasya kāraṇam iti uktam kāryasya darśanena paryavasita tvāt
saṃsāri saṃsāra hetu yāthātmya darśanam duḥkha duḥkhi saṃyoga hetu nivartakam duḥkhi duḥkha hetu yāthātmya viṣaya tvāt rogi roga hetu yāthātmya darśana vat
avidyā draṣṭṛ dṛśyayoḥ saṃyoga kāraṇam duḥkha nimitta saṃyoga hetu tvāt rogga hetu saṃyoga nimitta mithyājñāna vat
draṣṭṛ dṛśya saṃyogaḥ mithyā jñāna pūrvakaḥ duḥkha hetu tvāt rogi roga hetu saṃyoga vat
yasmāt duḥkhi duḥkha hetu yāthātmya viṣayam darśanam tasmāt tad anyathā viṣayasya adarśanasya pratidvandvam iti adarśanam saṃyoga nimittam iti uktam tasya hetuḥ avidyā iti
duḥkha nimitta tvāt ca saṃyogasya
yasmāt adarśanam eva nivartayati darśanam na anyat kāryam karoti tasmāt na atra darśanam mokṣa kāraṇam adarśana abhāvāt eva artha adarśana kāryasya duḥkha hetoḥ bandhasya abhāvaḥ sa mokṣaḥ
na punar bandha abhāva vyatirekeṇa bhāvayitavyaḥ mokṣaḥ
tatas ca mokṣasya nitya tva siddhiḥ
darśanasya bhāve draṣṭṛ dṛśya viṣayasya darśanasya bhāve tad viṣayasya adarśanasya nāśaḥ
darśana adarśanayoḥ ekatra virodhāt timi ura ravi kiraṇa jālayoḥ iva
atas darśanam kaivalya kāraṇam uktam viveka khyātiḥ aviplavā hāna upāyaḥ iti
kim ca idam adarśanam nāma nanu ca uktam avidyā eva
sā ca amitra goṣpada vat iti vidyā viparyayeṇa vyākhyātā
satyam evam kin tu śāstra gatāḥ vikalpāḥ darśayiṣyante sva abhimata pakṣa niścīṣayā
para parikalpita vastu khaṇḍimānam āpādayatā hi nija abhimata nirūpita vaḥ tu draḍhimānam atitarām ānīyate
kim ca idam iti sarvaiḥ eva vikalpaiḥ vakṣyamāṇaiḥ abhisaṃbandhanīyam
kim guṇānām ahikāraḥ iti sāmānyena paripṛṣṭasya viśeṣa paryanuyogaḥ
adhikṛtiḥ adhikāraḥ guṇānām pravṛttiḥ
nanu guṇānām adhikārasya katham adarśana āśaṅkā ucyate artha dvāreṇa bhavati eva adarśanam adhikāraḥ
yāvat hi guṇānām pravṛttiḥ tāvat bandhaḥ
bandha kāraṇam avidyā iti sthiti sthairyam ānīyate
śavda dvāreṇa api darśanāt anyat adarśanam yadā bhavati eva tadānīm āśaṅkā
guṇa adhikāraḥ hi darśanāt anyaḥ eva iti
āhosvit dṛśi svarūpasya svābinaḥ darśita viṣayasya sittasya anutpādaḥ
iha tu pūrva padārtha pradhāna tvam adarśanasya gṛgītvā śaṅkyate
cittasya anutpādaḥ prāk utpatteḥ darśanasya abhāvaḥ
kim uktam bhavati anutpādaḥ iti atas āha svasmin dṛśye tu artha dvāreṇa eva āśaṅkā
aprayojanavataḥ hi prayojanam avaśya kṛtyam iti
kim arthavat tā guṇānām bhoga apavargābhyām yā guṇānām arthavat tā tat adarśanam iti
atra tu artha dvāreṇa eva āśaṅkā
prayojanavataḥ hi prayojanam avaśya kṛtyam iti
kaḥ punar eṣu pakṣeṣu doṣaḥ ucyate yadi adhikāraḥ guṇānām adarśanam vidyā ānarthakyam prāptam
na hi asmin pakṣe vidyā pratyanīka bhūtā syāt adarśanasya
yasmāt vidyākārayoḥ avirodhaḥ atas ca nirmokṣaḥ prasaktaḥ
punar punar prayojanavat tayā pravṛtti saṃbhavāt
guṇa arthavat tā adarśanam iti pakṣe api eṣaḥ eva doṣaḥ
tathā cittasya anutpāda pakṣe api eṣaḥ eva
anutpādaḥ hi darśana abhāvaḥ tasya ca avastu tvāt vidyayā nivṛttiḥ anupapannā iti
abhāve hi sati pratyanīka vidhānam anarthakam eva
atha avidyā sva cittena saha niruddhā iti
atra hi avidyāyāḥ adarśanasya ca kenacid aṃśena bhedam manyamānaḥ vikalpayati
katham aniruddhā hi avidyā dṛśyamāna tvāt darśanam eva
yā tu niruddhā cittena saha pralīnā sva kāraṇe
sva cittasya utpatti bījam utpatti kāraṇam sā na dṛśyate iti adarśānam iti abhimānaḥ
tatas ca anirodha avasthāyāḥ darśana tva prasaṅgaḥ iti duṣṭaḥ eva ayam pakṣaḥ syāt
atha tu nirodha anirodha avasthāyoḥ api adarśanam eva tathā sati abhimata siddhiḥ iti adoṣaḥ eva
kim sthiti saṃskāra kṣaye gati saṃskāra abhibyaktiḥ
kim etat adarśanam iti na saṃbadhyate
katham tarhi saṃbandhaḥ ucyate tatra avidyā sva citta saha niruddhā cittasya utpatti bījam iti uktam tatas idam arthā siddham cittam sva kāraṇe nirudhyate punar ca utpadyate iti
tatas ca idam api siddham arthāt cittasya kāraṇam api sthityā gatyā ca vartate iti
tatas ca etad vispaṣṭīkaraṇa artham pṛcchati
sthiti arthaḥ guṇānām sāmya avasthā hetuḥ saṃskāraḥ sthiti saṃskāraḥ
tasya kṣaye sthiti saṃskāra kṣaye gatiḥ mahat ādi tā ākāreṇa pravṛttiḥ tad arthaḥ saṃskāraḥ gati saṃskāraḥ tasya abhibyaktiḥ iti
yadi sthityā gatyā ca vartate tatas kaḥ doṣaḥ syāt tat udāharaṇena darśayati yatra idam uktam pradhānam sthityāḥ eva vartamānam vikāra akaraṇāt mahat ādi ākāreṇa apariṇāṃāt apradhānam syāt
yatas pradhatte vikārān iti pradhānam
tena vikārāṇām a pradhātṛ tvāt apradhānam syāt
tathā gatyai eva vartamānam nityam vikāra rūpeṇa eva vartamānam vikāra nitya tvāt na vikārān pradhatte iti kāraṇa tva hāneḥ apradhānam syāt
ubhayathā vṛttiḥ gatyā sthityā ca vartanam vṛttiḥ yasya pradhānasya tat ubhayathāvṛtti vyavahāram pradhāna tva vyavahāram kāraṇa tva vyavahāram labhatet
na anyathā pradhāna tvam pradhānasya
kāraṇa antareṣu api puruṣaḥ īśvara paramāṇu ādiṣu para kalpiṣu samānaḥ carcaḥ tulya viṣayaḥ nyāyaḥ prakṛtaḥ eva adunā nirūpyate
darśana śaktiḥ eva adarśanam iti eke
darśanasya śaktiḥ anabhivyakta avasthā bīje iva anabhivyakta aṅkura avasthā tat etat adarśanam iti eke manyate
kutas pradhānasya ātma prakhyāpana arthā prakhyāpanam darśanam ākhyāyamāna rūpa tā tasyai tat adarśanam iti śruteḥ
asmin pakṣe tat eva anabhivyakta ātmakam śakti rūpam adarśanam tat eva ca abhivyaktam darśanam iti svātmani virodha anupapatteḥ darśanāt adarśanasya nivṛtti anavakāśaḥ
lptiḥ
tathā darśana antaram sarva bodha samarthaḥ bodha ātmaka tvāt prāk pravṛtteḥ pradhāna pravṛtteḥ prāṅ na paśyati darśana ātmakaḥ api san puruṣaḥ iti
sarva kārya karaṇa kriyā samartham dṛśyam pradhānam na tadā prāk pravṛtteḥ paramārtham api sat dṛśyate iti ubhayasya pradhāna puruṣayoḥ adarśanam dharmaḥ iti eke manyante
atra api ubhayoḥ api prāk avasthā eva adarśanam uttara kāla avasthā ca darśanam iti pūrva doṣaḥ sthitaḥ eva
dṛśyasya ātma bhūtam a vyatirkitam api puruṣa pratyaya apakṣām puruṣa ākāreṇa puruṣasya na dṛśyate
puruṣa ākāra viśiṣṭa tayā vā puruṣasya dṛśyate iti puruṣa pratyaya apekṣam adarśanam puruṣasya dharma tvena bhavati
tat etat spaṣṭayati puruṣasya anātma bhūtam api dṛśya pratyaya apakṣam dṛśya pratyayaḥ jñānam tat apekṣam katham puruṣa ākāreṇa adarśanāt saṃkareṇa vā darśanāt antaḥkaraṇa pratyaya apekṣam puruṣa anātma bhūtyam api puruṣa adharva tvena eva adarśanam ābhāsate
tathā ca sati dṛśya dharmaḥ eva ayam iti adoṣaḥ
sarva vikalpa pakṣa khyāpana arthaḥ upanyāsaḥ
darśanam jñānam tat eva jñānam adarśanam iti kecid manyante
samāsasya uttara padārtha prādhānyam ūrīkrtyā ayam vikalpaḥ
etasya doṣaḥ avidyā sūtre eva vyākhyātaḥ
ete śāstra gatāḥ vikalpāḥ darśana antara gatāḥ vikalpāḥ
tatra vikalpa bahu tva māram etat na bahu tva mātreṇa artha siddhiḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ
yasya tu buddhi puruṣa saṃyoga hetu tvam tasya adarśanam na tvam yuktam darśana virodhāt
tathā ca vyākhgyātam iti na atra punar prayatyate
sarva puruṣāṇām guṇa saṃyoga aviśeṣaḥ
guṇaiḥ saṃyogaḥ sarveṣām aviśiṣṭaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ tathā api asādhāraṇa viṣayaḥ tu pratyātmam viśiṣṭaḥ tu pratyak cetanasya bauddha pratyaya anudarśinaḥ sva buddhi saṃyogaḥ
sa ca asādhāraṇaḥ sva buddhi saṃyogaḥ yena bhavati tat eva adarśanam
tasya hetuḥ avidyā
tasya sva svāmi śakti svarūpa upalabdhi hetoḥ saṃyogasya hetuḥ kāraṇam avidyā viparyaya jñāna vāsanā iti arthaḥ
nanu ca viparyayaḥ mithyājñānam a tat rūpa pratiṣṭham iti uktam
tathā anitya aśuci duḥkha anātmasu nitya śuci sukha ātma khyātiḥ avidyā iti uktam
atra katham viparyaya jñāna vāsanā iti ucyate
na eṣa doṣaḥ avidyā kārya tvāt vāsanāyāḥ sā eva avidyā iti ucyate
pralīneṣu api kāraṇeṣu sāmya avasthāyām api satyām avidyā vasanā punar punar pravṛttau pradhānasya hetuḥ bhavati
na punar viparyayaḥ prāk buddhi utpatteḥ abhāvāt pravṛtti kāraṇam iti tat vāsanā eva pradhāna puruṣa asaṃyogasya kāraṇam iti ākhyāyate
tat mā eva āha viparyaya jñāna vāsanā avasitāḥ na kārya niṣṭhām kārya smāptim
kārya niṣṭhām āha puruṣa khyātim iti
tām buddhiḥ na prāpnoti
puruṣa khyāti paryavasānā hi buddheḥ karaṇīyavat tā
sa adhikārā karaṇiyavatī punar punar āvartate viparyaya jñāna vāsanā vaśāt
sā tu buddhiḥ puruṣa khyāti paryavasānā kārya niṣṭhām prāpnoti
punar api tat eva spaṣṭayati carita adhikārā nivṛtta adarśana bandhanā karma vipāpayoḥ adarśana mūla tvāt adarśanam eva bandhanam
adarśana nivṛttau ca bandha nivṛtteḥ bandha kāraṇa abhāvāt bandha kāraṇasya adarśanasya abhāvāt na punar āvartate
atra kaścid paṇḍaka upākhyānena uddhaṭṭayati
paṇḍakaḥ ṣaṇḍaḥ
sa kila mugdhayā bhāryayā abhidhīyate
katham āryaputra me bhaknī apratyavatī kim artham na aham apratyavatī asmi iti
tām āha mṛtaḥ te ham apratyam utpādayiṣyāmi iti
tadhā idam vidyamānam jñānām citta nivṛttim na karoti naṣṭam kariṣyataḥ iti kā pratyāśā
ayam uddhaṭṭayituḥ abhiprāyaḥ avidyā ced buddhi puruṣa saṃyogasya kāraṇam tasyāḥ ca vidyā nivṛtti hetuḥ tatas ca vidyā mānāyām vidyāyām tad virodhin avidyā nivartate
na tu vidyā utpatti anantaram api citta nivṛttiḥ
tatra yathā eva satyām vidyāyām na citta nivṛttiḥ tathā naṣṭyām api vidyāyām na nivartsyati tarām idānīm ṣaṇḍāt iva mṛtāt apatya upattiḥ
atas eva kāraṇāt avidyā api na saṃyoga kāraṇam
atra ācārya deśīyaḥ parihāram vakti
ācārya deśīya grahaṇam pūrvapakṣasya asāra tva prakhyāpana artham
uddhaṭṭanena eva pratyuttaram
nanu buddhi nivṛttiḥ eva mokṣaḥ
katham adarśana kāraṇa bhāvāt buddhi nivṛttiḥ
tat ca adarśanam bandha kāraṇam darśanāt nivartate tad nivṛttiḥ eva mokṣaḥ
kimartha asthāne vibhramaḥ
pradhāna puruṣa saṃyogasya duḥkha hetoḥ avidyā kāraṇam iti vistareṇa pratipāditam
tatas ca darśanāt adarśana nivṛtti upapatteḥ pūrvapakṣam asāram manyate
nanu ca uktam vidyā anantaram eva buddhiḥ na nivartyate iti
ucyate
vidyayā tāvat cat avidyā nivartate eva
na atra vibhramaḥ kāryaḥ tasyām tu nivṛttāyām buddhi nivṛttiḥ ca bhavati eva punar buddhi saṃyogasya avidyā vyatirekeṇa kāraṇa antara abhāvāt
tatas ca buddhi nivṛttiḥ eva mokṣaḥ
yat tu vidyā anantaram eva buddhiḥ na nivartate iti tat akāraṇam
kasmāt nimitta naimittikayoḥ aneka prakāra darśanaṭ
yathā takṣa ādi nimittāḥ prāsāda ādayaḥ takṣa ādiṣu uparateṣu api na nimitta viratyā viramanti
bhagnasya ca drumasya ca drumasya bhaṅga anantaram eva viśeṣāt adarśanāt
tathā cittasya api vimukta sāyaka vat ārabdha saṃskāra aparikṣayāt tad saṃskāra apekṣayā kiṃcid kālam darśanena eva avastya hānam iti
tathā ca śrutiḥ tasya tāvat eva ciram iti
catvāraḥ vyūhāḥ prakṛtāḥ
tatra heyam duḥkham heyam duḥkham anāgatam iti uktam
roga sthānīya ekaḥ vyūhaḥ vyākhyātaḥ iti arthaḥ
heya kāraṇam ca sa nimittam saṃyoga ākhyam uktam
dvitīyaḥ vyūhaḥ roga hetu sthānīyaḥ heya hetuḥ tu avidyā nimitta sahitaḥ pradhāna puruṣa saṃyogaḥ upavarṇitaḥ
ukta parikīrtanam ca sopapattika ukteḥ tad viṣaya āṅkṣā nivṛtti artham
atas param hānam ārogya sthānīyam mokṣa śāstra prayojanam vaktavyam
vakṣyamāṇa saṃkīrtanam ca śrotṛ buddhi samādhāna artham
tad abhāvāt saṃyoga abhāvaḥ hānam tat dṛśeḥ kaivalyam
tat iti pūrva prakṛtāyāḥ avidyāyāḥ prtyavamarśaḥ
tasya adarśanasya avidyāyāḥ abhāvāt abhāvaḥ ātyantikaḥ bandhana uparamaḥ iti arthaḥ
etat hānam ārogya sthānīyam
tat dṛśeḥ kaivalyam tat eva hānam ātyantikaḥ bandhana uparamaḥ dṛśeḥ puruṣasya kaivalyam
asya vyākhyānam puruṣasya a miśrī bhāaḥ punar asaṃyogaḥ guṇaiḥ iti arthaḥ
padārtham vyākhyāya vākya artham idānīm darśayati duḥkha kāraṇa nivṛttau duḥkha uparamaḥ hānam
tadā sva rūpa pratiṣṭhā ah puruṣaḥ iti uktam sva rūpa pratiṣṭhā vā citi śaktiḥ iti
nanu ca aniyata vipākasya karmaṇaḥ sadbhāve katham hānam syāt punar aniyata vipāka karmaṇā śarīrasya ārambhaḥ iti
na abhihita pratividhāna tvāt
samyak darśanena kleśa bījasya dāhāt karmaṇām anārambhaka tvam uktam dagdha bīja bhāva apanīta tuṣa śalita pḍula nidarśanena
tasmāt na viduṣaḥ kāraṇa abhāvāt śarīra ārambhaḥ
uktaḥ tṛtīyaḥ vyūhaḥ ārogya sthānīyaḥ hānam nāma
adhunā caturtham vyūham bhaiṣasya sthānīyam upācikhyāsan āha hānasya kaḥ prāpti upāyaḥ iti
nanu c katham hānasya prāpti upāyaḥ iti yāvatā na eṣa hānam avastu tvāt prāpyam
bandhana uparamaḥ eva hi hānam

samyak hyātau satyām avidyā nivṛttiḥ iti hānam avastu api prāpyam iti upacaryate
viveka khyātiḥ aviplavā hāna upāyaḥ
kā punar viveka khyātiḥ iti āha sattva puruṣa anya tā pratyayaḥ sattva puruṣayoḥ yā avabodhaḥ iti arthaḥ sā tu viveka khyātiḥ anivṛtta mithyājñānā na sthirībhavati na kārya kṣamā iti
tathā ca uktam yathā na virājate
tathā pajha kaṣāyasya vijñānam prakāśate
tathā kāma grāha gṛhītasya jñānam api asya na plavaḥ

yadā tu mithyājñānam dagdha bīja bhāvam dagdha bīja tvāt eva bandha prasavam kārya ārabhā kṣamam sampadyate tadā vidhūta kleśa rajasaḥ kleśāḥ eva rajaḥ vidhūtam yasya tat vidhūta kleśa rajaḥ tasya sattvasya rāga dimala a kalaṅkitasya parasyām vaśīkāra saṃjñāyām vartamānasya jñāna prasāda mātre vartamānasya
tat eva anuvadati viveka pratyaya pravāhaḥ viveka jñāna nirantara bhāvaiḥ nirmalaḥ bhavati
sā aviveka khyātiḥ itthaṃbhūtā satī aviplavā bhavati
yadā evam aviplavā viveka khyātiḥ tatas mithyājñānasya dagdha bīja bhāva upagamaḥ virudha tvāt
punar ca āpravaḥ mithyājñānasya dagdha bīja bhāva upagamāt eva
tathā ca uktam bījāni agni upadagdhāni na rohanti yathā punar

sā ca tādṛśī viveka khyātiḥ mokṣasya mārgaḥ hānasya upāyaḥ iti arthaḥ
utpanna samyak darśanasya samyak darśana utpattau sva anubhava pratyaya liṅga prakaṭīkaraṇa artham āha tasya saptadhā prānta bhūmiḥ prajñā
tasya iti pratyudita khyāteḥ pratyutpanna samyak darśanasya pratyāmnāyaḥ pratyavamarśaḥ
saptadhā iti aśuddhi āvaraṇa mala apagamāt
aśuddhiḥ eva avadharaṇam kleśāḥ karmāṇi ca tat eva malam tasya apagamāt vittasya pratyaya antara anutpāde mama aham iti ca viruddha pratyaya antarāṇām anutpattau
saptadhā iti asya vivaraṇam sapta prakārā eva prajñā buddheḥ vivekinaḥ bhavati
tān sapta prakārān krameṇa ācaṣṭe yathā parijñātam heyam sarvam duḥkham heyam jñātam upapattibhiḥ
na asya parijñātavyaḥ duḥkha prakāraḥ
kṣīṇāḥ heya hetavaḥ iti bahuvacana prayogāt kleśāḥ karmāṇi ca abhidhīyante
na punar eṣām kleśa karmaṇām alpam api bhāvāt asti
etena api prānta bhūmi tvam eva uktam
ittham ca pratyupasthita samīcīna pratyayasya kṣīṇa kleśa tvāt na kṣetavyam asti
kṛtakarṇīyaḥ aham iti ca samyak darśana paripāka liṅga pratyayaḥ upāvartate
yathā rogātuḥ asya roga hetu kṣaye nīrogaḥ ham na punar bhaiṣajyam asti iti pratyayaḥ
evam eva ṣa dvitīyaḥ prajñā prakāraḥ uktaḥ
sākṣāt kṛtam nirodha samāpattiḥ hānam
hāna pratyāsanna tvāt hāna tulya rūpa tvāt ca niodha samādhiḥ eva hānam iti ākhyāyate
tat ca sākṣāt kṛtam anubhava viṣaya tām ānītam
tat idam kaivalyam paryavasitam kaivalyam kartavyam iti ca prajñāyate
eṣaḥ api prānta bhūmi prajñā prakāraḥ tṛtīyaḥ ākhyātaḥ
bhāvitaḥ samyak abhyastataraḥ viveka khyāti rūpaḥ hāna upāyaḥ
samyak darśanam yathāvat upasthitam iti niścitā ced prajñā vivekinaḥ jāyate saḥ eṣa caturthaḥ prajñā prakāraḥ
iti eṣā catuṣṭayī kārya vimuktiḥ kāryāt kartavyāt vimuktiḥ yasyāḥ prajñāyāḥ sā kārya vimuktiḥ catur rūpā prajñā puruṣa artha kartavya tā iti arthaḥ
atha vā kāryasya vimuktiḥ nivṛttiḥ kārya vimuktiḥ
sā ca catuṣṭayī kārya vimuktiḥ iti samāptam vākyam
prajñā iti pareṇa saṃbadhyate
katham prajñā pra yuktam viveka khyāti yuktam vittam prajñā cittam tasya vimuktiḥ pralayaḥ prajñā citta vimuktiḥ
sā trayī
tathā ca vakṣyati puruṣa artha śūnyānām guṇānām pratiprasavaḥ kaivalyam iti
tatra kārya vimuktiḥ catuṣṭayī
puruṣa artha śūnyatvam pūrvam uktam
idānīm buddhi guṇāt nivṛttiḥ
puruṣa artha kartavyānām puruṣa aṛtha śūnyānām pratiprasavaḥ prajñā citta vimuktiḥ trayī vyākhyāyate
yathā carita adhikārāḥ nivṛtta kartavyāḥ buddhi guṇāḥ sattva ādayaḥ buddhi ākāra avasthitāḥ pralaya abhimukhāḥ
kim iva giri śikhara kūṭa cyutāḥ iva grāvāṇaḥ niravasthānāḥ kartavya abhāvāt sva kāraṇe ahaṃkāre pralaya abhimukhāḥ saha tena buddhi saṃsthānena kāryeṇa atha vā sva kāraṇena ahaṅkāreṇa kuśalam puruṣam prati sva kāraṇam api avyakta bhāvam pratipadyate iti saha tena astam gaddhanti iti ucyate
eṣā prathamā prajñā citta vimuktiḥ
na ca eṣām pratipralīnānām puruṣam prati punar asti utpādaḥ prayojana abhāvāt
vumuktam hi caturvidham kāryam
eṣā dvitīyā prajñā citta vimuktiḥ
etasyām avasthāyām caritārtha guṇa pralaya avasthāyām guṇa sambandha atītaḥ guṇa saṃbandhaḥ draṣṭṛ dṛśya lakṣaṇaḥ tam atītaḥ
sva rūpa mātra jyotiḥ dṛśi sva rūpa mātram evam jyotiḥ
puruṣaḥ kevalī śuddhaḥ iti tṛtīyā prajñā citta vimuktiḥ iti
etām samavidhām prānta bhūmim prāntāḥ pragata avaṣanāḥ bhūmayaḥ avasthāḥ yasyāḥ tām prānta bhūmim prajñām anupaśyan samyak darśana liṅga paripāka bhūtām īkṣamāṇaḥ puruṣaḥ kuśalaḥ iti ākhyāyate kuśalaḥ iti saṅketaḥ
