kutas kauśala tasya iti āha guṇa atīta tvāt iti
guṇān atītaḥ hi kuśalaḥ
siddhā viveka khyātiḥ samadhigatā viveka khyātiḥ saptavidha prānta bhūmi prajñā phala avasānā hānasya upāyaḥ iti
na ca siddhiḥ antareṇa sādhanam iti atas idam viveka khyāti siddhi sādhana artham ārabhyate yogāṅga anuṣṭhānāt aśuddhi kṣaye jñāna dīptiḥ ā viveka khyāteḥ
yogāṅga anuṣṭhānāt eva viveka khyātiḥ iti guru upāsana dharma prabhṛtikebhyaḥ api viveka khyāteḥ siddhiḥ iti atas eva
kim tarhi sādhana mātram antareṇa na bhavati eva iti avadhārayiṣyate
na punar yogāṅga anuṣṭhānam eva sādhanam yogāṅga anuṣṭhānāt tu bhavati eva viveka khyāti siddhiḥ iti
tathā ca ācāryaiḥ uktam yogaḥ tattva jñāna arhaḥ iti
yogāṅgāni abhidhāyiṣyamāṇāni teṣām anuṣṭhānam yogāṅga anuṣṭhānam tasmāt aśuddheḥ kleśa ākhyāyāḥ kṣayaḥ tad kṣaye dīptiḥ prakarṣaḥ
iti āha ā viveka khyāteḥ bhavati iti upaskāraḥ
svayam eva bhāṣyakāraḥ spaṣṭataram vivṛṇoti yogāṅgān anuṣṭhau abhidhāyiṣyamāṇāni
teṣām anuṣṭhānāt pañca parvaṇaḥ viparyayasya aśuddhi rūpasya kṣayaḥ nāśaḥ tad kṣaye samyak darśanasya abhivyaktiḥ dīptiḥ
katham etat bhavati iti āha yathā yathā ca sādhanāni anuṣṭhīyante tathā tathā tanu tvam aśuddhiḥ āpadyate
tathā ca manuḥ abiṣiṣṭa prāṇāyāmaiḥ dahet doṣān dhāraṇābhiḥ ca kilbiṣān
pratyāhāreṇa saṃsargān dhyānena anaiścarān guṇān
iti
yathā yathā ca aśuddhiḥ kṣīyate tathā tathā tad kṣaya krama anurodhinī divasakarasya iva śiśira avasāne jñānasya dīptiḥ vivardhate
sā khalu iyam vivṛddhiḥ prakarṣam anubhavati
kim avasānam tat āha ā viveka khyāteḥ
tasya vyākhyānam ā guṇa puruṣa sva rūpa viveka jñānāt iti arthaḥ
sattva puruṣa anya tā khyāti paryavasānā eva śuddhiḥ
ca iti eva
tatra kāraṇa prasaṅgena śāstra prasiddhāni kāraṇāni vyācaṣṭe kati ca etāni kāraṇāni śāstre bhavanti nava eva iti āha
tat yathā tāni ślokena eva kathayati utpatti sthiti abhivyakti vikāra pratyaya āptayaḥ
viyoga anyatva dhṛtayaḥ kāraṇam navadhā smṛtam
iti
tad praviveka artham udāharaṇāni prastāviṣyante
tatra utpatti kāraṇam manaḥ bhavati vijñā jasya manasaḥ hi vṛttiḥ jñānam yathā jala mūrmāṇām
sthiti kāraṇam sthiteḥ kāraṇam manasaḥ puruṣa aṛtha tā
bhoga apavarga artha tvena hi mānasaḥ sthitiḥ
śarīrasya yathā sthiti kāraṇam āhāraḥ
abhivyakteḥ kāraṇam rūpasya ālokaḥ
tadā rūpa jñānam
na hi ālokena anabhivyakte rūpe
vikārasya kāraṇam manasaḥ viṣaya antaram
viṣaya antara sannidhānena hi manaḥ vikriyām āsīdati
yathā agniḥ pākasya
yaḥ pāka ākhyaḥ vikāraḥ tasya pākasya vikāra rūpasya agniḥ kāraṇam yathā
pratyaya kāraṇam dhūma jñānam agni jñānasya
pratyayasya phalavataḥ pramāṇasya kāraṇam iti arthaḥ
pūrvatra tu bhavati vijñānasya iti jñānasya upādānakāraṇam vivakṣitam
prāpti kāraṇam yogāṅga anuṣṭhānam viveka khyateḥ dharmaḥ iva sukhasya
tat eva aśuddheḥ viyoga kāraṇam paraśuḥ iva chedyasya
anya tva kāraṇam yathā suvarṇakāraḥ suvarṇasya
suvarṇam hi bhittvā vardhamānakam anyam karoti
tathā vardhamānakam bhittvā anyat ābharaṇa antaram karoti
tathā iti
evam ekasya svī iti pratyayasya api avidyā kāraṇam mūḍha tve
dveṣaḥ tasya eva strī pratyayasya duḥkha tve kāraṇam
tathā rāgaḥ sukha tve
tathā tasya eva mādhyasthye heya upādeya śūnyatāyām viveka yuktam jñānam kāraṇam
evam ekaḥ strī pratyayaḥ suvarṇā vat anekadhā mūḍha tva duḥkha tva sukha tva mādhyasthya ādi bhedaiḥ bhidyate
dhṛteḥ kāraṇam
dhāraṇam dhṛtiḥ tasyāḥ kāraṇam śarīram indriyāṇām
na hi śarīram a prāpya indriyāṇi dhṛtam labhante
tāni ca idriyāṇi tasya śarīrasya dhṛti kāraṇam bhavanti
indriya vṛtti dvāreṇa hi śarīram dhriyate
tathā mahābhūtāni ākāśa ādīni śarīrāṇām dhṛti kāraṇam
mahābhūta ārabdhāni hi śarīrāṇi brahma ādi stamba avasānāni
tāni ca parasparam upakārya upakāraka tva dvāreṇa dhṛti kāraṇam
tathā sarveṣām padārthānām tairyagyauna mānuṣa daivatāni dhṛti kāraṇam
kutas paraspara artha tvāt tairyagyaunam mānuṣa daivatayoḥ vāhana dohana haviḥ ādibhiḥ upakurvat dhṛti kāraṇam
tathā mānuṣam ijyā rakṣāṇa ādibhiḥ daivata airyagyaunayoḥ dhṛti kāraṇam
tathā daivam itarayoḥ śīta uṣṇa pravarṣāṇa ādinā dhṛti kāraṇam
evam varṇa āśramāṇām api anyonya upakāreṇa dhṛti kāraṇa tvam
paraspara upāśrayeṇa hi jagat akhilam api dhriyate
evam nava eva kāraṇāni iti kāraṇa antaram pratiṣedhati
tāni ca yathā rtha saṃbhavam yaḥ yaḥ rtha saṃbhavaḥ padārtha antareṣu api anudāhṛteṣu tathā yojyāni
yogāṅga anuṣṭhānam tu dvidhā eva kāraṇa tvam labhate
tathā ca vyākhyātam
kāni punar tāni yogāṅgāni yeṣām anuṣṭhānam dvidhā kāraṇa tvam labhate iti
tatra yoga aṅgāni avadhāryante yama niyama āsana prāṇāyāma pratyāhāra dhāraṇāḥ dhyāna samādhayaḥ ṣṭa aṅgāni
nanu ca yoga śāstra antareṣu āsana ādīni eva ṣaṣ aṅgāni
tat yathā ṣaṣ aṅgaḥ yogaḥ ucyate ityādi
kiñ ca sākṣāt āsana ādīni eva samādheḥ upakurvanti na yama niyamau
na eṣa doṣaḥ
yama niyamavatoḥ yoga adhikāra upapatteḥ na hi yathā kāmacāriṇām yoga adhikāraḥ
na a virataḥ duścaritāt na a śāntaḥ iti śruteḥ
tathā yeṣām tapaḥ brahmacaryam yeṣu satyam pratiṣṭhitam ityādi ca atharvaṇe
tathā gītāyām brahmacāri vrate SLNe sthitaḥ SNPaPsM
iti
tasmāt yama niyamayoḥ api aṅga tvam
yama niyamayoḥ ca yamasya prādhānya khyāpana artham
yamasya hi prādhānyam sarvatra siddham
yama niyama yuktasya adhikṛtasya yoginaḥ āsana ādi aṅgānām pūrva pūrve sthira pada prāptasya uttarottara anuṣṭhānam prāptam
na hi prathamam sopānam an āruhya uttaram āroḍhum śakyam
yat anyatra ucyate sthāna āsana vidhānāni yogasya vidhayaḥ api vā
vyākṣepa janakāḥ sarve na te yogasya hetavaḥ
sarva doṣa parityāgaḥ samādhiḥ ca iti tat dvayam
yoga hetuḥ syāt bhavati vā anyat na vā bhavatu anyat na vā bhavet
iti
tad samādhi sarva doṣa parityāgayoḥ prādhānyāt tat stuti artham na āsana ādi aṅga pratiṣeda artham
yathākramam eṣām yama ādīnām anusṭhānam svarūpam ca vakṣyāmaḥ svarūpe hi anavagate na anuṣṭhātum śakyam iti
tatra teṣu yama ādiṣu prathamam yamāḥ vyākhyāyante ahiṃsā satya asteya brahmacarya aparigrahāḥ yamāḥ
tatra ahiṃsā sarvathā sarva ātmanā sarva prakāreṇa sarva bhūtānām an abhidrohaḥ sarva bhūtānām sthāvara jaṅgmānām pīḍanam
yama niyamānām ahiṃsā pradhāna bhūtā kāya vāc manasaiḥ sarva ātmanā karaṇīyā iti darśayati uttare ca yamāḥ satya ādayaḥ tad mūlāḥ ahiṃsā prayojanāḥ ahiṃsā arthāḥ tad siddhi para tayā eva ahiṃsāt siddhi tat paratvena pratipādyante
kim uktam bhavati iti āha karaṇāya upādīyante ahiṃsā śuddhi pratipādanāya upādīyante
tathā hi uktam sa khalu ayam brāhmaṇaḥ yathā yathā bahūni vratāni samāditsate tathā tathā pramāda kṛtebhyaḥ hiṃsā nidānebhyaḥ hiṃsā mūlebhyaḥ hiṃsā kāraṇebhyaḥ nivartamānaḥ tām eva avadāta rūpām ahiṃsām karoti iti
satya ādi aneka vrata upādānāt anyeṣām aviruddha vratānām ca upādānāt hiṃsā kāraṇāt nivṛ tasya hiṃsā kāraṇāt uparata parisphuraṇasya ahiṃsā kāraṇa abhāvāt upajāyate
yathā bhikṣā ādi vrata anuṣṭhāne kṛṣi ādi hiṃsā nidāna nivṛttiḥ
satyam yathā yathā anumitam yathā śrutam tathā vāc manaḥ ca iti
tat satyam
etat uktam bhavati abhra antaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ yathā artha avagamaḥ sañjātaḥ tam avagamam tathā eva paratra saṃkramayitum vā āṅga nasābhyām tathā eva pravartanam satyam iti
tat eva āha paratra sva bodha saṃkrāntaye vāc uktā
sā yathā vagata arthā api yadi na vañcitā
yathā satyam eva para vipralambhana artham prayuktam deśa kāla ādi apekṣayā kvacid anṛtāyate yathā yidhiṣṭhirasya aśvatthāmā hataḥ sa kuñjaraḥ iti
bhrāntāḥ vā yathā satyam iti manyamānaḥ eva vadati
pratipatti vandhyā vā rotuḥ pratipādanāya aparyāptā yathā sandigdham vākyam agṛhyamāṇa prakaraṇa ādi viśeṣam
kaṣṭa śabdaḥ vai aja avayaḥ ityādiḥ
tasmāt evamādi doṣa rahitā eṣā vāc ṛju manaḥ sahacāriṇī sarva bhūta upakāra artham pravṛttā satyatām āskandati
na bhūta upaghātāya pravṛttā yathā artha bala ādhānā api satya tām āpadyate
yadi api uktena prakāreṇa nirdoṣā api abhidhīyamānā bhūta upaghāta parā eva syāt na satyam bhavet na hi prāṇi ghāta ālambinī api satya tvam pratipadyate
pāpam eva bhavet
tat eva āha tena puṇya ābhāsena puṇya pratibimbakena satya kauśika vacana deśīyena kaṣṭam tamaḥ prāpnuyāt
tasmāt parīkṣya sarva hitam satyam brūyāt
uktam ca satyam brūyāt priyam brūyāt na crūyāt satyam apriyam
priyam ca na anṛtam brūyāt eṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ
iti steyam a śāstra pūrvam dravyāṇām paratas svīkaraṇam spṛhā nimittam
yat steyam tad pratiṣedhaḥ tu na spṛhālūnām sambhavati iti tasya eva steyasya pratiṣedhaḥ tu
saḥ a spṛhā rūpam asteyam ucyate
brahmacaryam gupta indriyasya puruṣasya abrahmacarya artha vāc manasā ādi vṛtti śūnyasya iti
viṣayāṇām ārjana rakṣaṇa kṣaya saṅga hiṃsā doṣa darśanāt a svīkaraṇam an upādanam a parigrahaḥ
na punar a sāmarthyena a svīkaraṇam
iti ete yamāḥ
anya dharmāṇām jāti deśa kāla ādi avacchedena anuṣṭhānāt iha api tathā prasaṅgaḥ iti tat pratiṣedhāya āha ete tu iti
ete tu ahiṃsāḥ ādayaḥ mahāvrata saṃjñāḥ saṃnyāsavatām anuṣṭhānīyāḥ kīdṛśāḥ te mahāvrata nāmāni iti jāti deśa kāla sama yāna vat hināḥ sārvabhaumāḥ mahā vratam
mahat ca tat vratam ca mahā vratam
mahat tvam ca sārvabhauma tvam
katham punar jāti ādi anavat hinna tvam eṣām iti anavat heda pratipādanāya vyatirekeṇa ahiṃsām udāharati tatra ahiṃsā jāti avacchinnā matsya bandhakasya matsyeṣu eva na anyatra matsya jāteḥ hiṃsā
sā ca matsya jāti avācchinnā matsya bhūmim an aśnuvānā vartate iti asārvabhaumī eva
sā eva ahiṃsā deśa avacchinnā katham na tīrthe prayāga ādau haniṣyāmi iti
tīrtheṣu ahiṃsā ca tīrthāt anyam deśam na vyaśnute iti asārvabhaumī
sā eva ca kāla avacchinnā yathā na caturdaśyām na puṇye hani iti
caturdaśī ādi kālāt anyam kālam na iti sā api a sārvabhaumī
tribhiḥ api jāti deśa kālaiḥ uparatasya tasya eva matsyabandhakasya samaya avacchinnā samayaḥ kartavya tā niyamaḥ katham deva brāhmaṇa artham haniṣyāmi na anyathā iti śrāddha ādi samaya bhūmim an aśnānā vartate iti sā api na sārvabhaumī yathā ca kṣatriyasya yuddhe eva hiṃsā na anyatra iti samaya avacchinnasya eva udāharaṇam
ye ete yamāḥ jāti deśa kāla samayaiḥ anavaddhinnāḥ ahiṃsā ādayaḥ te sarvathā eva paripālanīyāḥ sarva bhūmiṣu jāti ādiṣu sarva viṣayeṣu sarva prāṇiṣu sarvathā vinā vyabhicāreṇa te ca ittham viśiṣṭāḥ sārvabhaumāḥ mahāḥ vratam iti ucyante
śauca santoṣa tapaḥ svādhyāya īśvara praṇidhānāni niyamāḥ
tatra śaucam mṛd ādi janitam ādi śabdāt udakam ca
medhya abhyvaharaṇāni ca ghṛta payā adīni bhakṣaṇāni
caśabdāt medhya darśana śreavaṇa ādīni ca
bāhyam etat śaucam
ābhyantaram ucyate citta malānām kāma krodha ādīnām tat pratipakṣa bhāvanā salilaiḥ ākṣālanam
santoṣaḥ sannihita sādhana āśvāsāt sannihitāt āśvāsa nimittāt adhik sādhana anupāditsā sannihita mātrāt atṛptau satyām api alaṃpratyayaḥ
tapaḥ dvandva sahanam
dvandvaḥ ca jighatsā pipāse
jighatsā attum icchā
jighatsā pipāse alpīyaḥ pāna aśana nimitte tapaḥ
śīta uṣṇe a pratikriyamāṇe alpa pratikriye vā tapaḥ
sthāna āsane tiṣṭhet ahani rātrau āsīta iti smṛtiprasthānam
kāṣṭha mauna a kāṣṭha maune
kāṣṭha maunam hasta prayoga ādi rahitam
a kāṣṭha maunam hasta ādi prayoga yuktam sambhāṣaṇa ādi rahitam
vratāni ca eṣām yoginām yathā yogam yathāsambhavam
homa ādi viruddha dharma viruddha pratiṣedha artham yathā yogam iti āha
kāni tāni kṛcchra ādīni
kṛcchram prājāpatya ādi
tri aham prātar tri aham sāyam tri aham adyāt a yācitam
upoṣaṇam tri aham iti
cāndrāyaṇam yava madhya pipīikā madhya ādi
ekaikam vadhayet grāsam ityādi smṛtiḥ
sāntapanam go mūtram gomayam kṣīram dadhi sarpiḥ kuśa udakam
eka rātra upavāsaḥ ca kṛcchraḥ sāntapanaḥ amṛtaḥ
etāni eva dravyāṇi tris abhyastāni mahāsāntapanam
ādi grahaṇam parāka ādi pratyupādāna artham
svādhyāyaḥ mokṣa śāstra adhyayanam up niṣad ādi adhyayanam praṇava japaḥ vā
pratyak cetanā adhigamaḥ api antarāya abhāvaḥ ca iti
tatra yama niyamānām viruddhāḥ tarkāḥ vitarkāḥ taiḥ bādhane sati pratipakṣān bhāvayet abhidhāsyamānena prakāreṇa
a pratibhāvyamānāḥ hi vitarkāḥ yoginam hiṃsā ādiṣu praṇidhāpayeyuḥ
yadā asya brāhmāṇasya vitarkāḥ hiṃsā ādayaḥ jāyeran
tatra ahiṃsā ādi vitarkāḥ ye vā hiṃsā ādayaḥ te vitarkāḥ kīdṛśāḥ iti tatra ahiṃsāyāḥ vitarkaḥ hiṃsā haniṣya abhyapakāriṇam iti
tathā satyasya anṛtam vadiṣyāmi iti viruddhaḥ pratyayaḥ vitarkaḥ
tathā eva asteyasya vitarkaḥ dravyam asya svīkariṣyāmi iti
tathā brahmacaryasya vitarkaḥ dāreṣu ca asya gamiṣyāmi iti
tathā eā parigrahasya vitarkaḥ parigraheṣu ca asya svāmī bhaviṣyāmi iti
asya iti etat sarvatra hiṃsā ādiṣu anugama pratipādana artham
dravyam asya svīkariṣyāmi iti para dravyasya ātma saṃbandha karaṇam
parigraheṣu ca asya svāmī iti para saṃbandhiṣu eva dreavyeṣu svayam svāmī iti
yathā kumāra narapati saciva ādīnām
ittham unmārga hāriṇā vitarka jvareṇa dīptena bādhyamānaḥ tad pratipakṣān bhāvayet
katham bhāvayet iti ghoreṣu saṃsāra aṅgāreṣu pacyamānena mayā abhyupagataḥ sarva bhūta abhayta pradānena yoga dharmaḥ
sa khalu aham tyaktvā vitarkān hiṃsā ādīn punar tān ādadānaḥ tulyaḥ śva vṛttena iti
śunaḥ iva yasya saḥ śvavṛttaḥ
śva vat vā vṛttaḥ śva vṛttaḥ
tena tulyaḥ iti bhāvayet
yathā śvā vānta avalehī tathā tyaktasya punar ādānam kurvan iti upaskāraḥ
tena puruṣeṇa tulyaḥ ham iti
tathā katham aham bhaveyam na yuktam etat iti bhāvayet
iti evam ādi sūtra antare api niyama sūtre api yojyam
śauce ādīnām pratyekam vitarkāḥ draṣṭavyāḥ śaucam na kariṣyāmi iti ādayaḥ
bhāṣye tu yamānām eva pradarśanam teṣām avaśya kartavya tvāt akaraṇe ca doṣa gauravāt atyādara artham
vitarkāṇām svarūpam bhedaḥ prabhava hetuḥ phalam ca sūtreṇa eva pradarśyate vitarkāḥ hiṃsā ādayaḥ iti svarūpam
kṛta kārita anumoditāḥ iti bhedaḥ
lobha krodha moha pūrvakāḥ iti prabhava hetuḥ
mṛdu madhya ahi mātrāḥ iti manda madhya uttama doṣa tvam
duḥkha ajñāna ananta phalāḥ iti pratipakṣa bhāvanam
phalam vā tena eva vyākhyāyate
tatra hiṃsā eva ekā udāhriyate sarveṣām pradarśanāya
sā kṛtā kāritā anumoditā iti trividhā
kṛtā sva vyāpāreṇa
kāri tā prayojya vyāpāreṇa
anumoditā pareṣām vyāpāreṇa manasā nau jñātā
ekaikā punar tridhā
katham lobhena māsa carmā sthi rthī mṛgam hanasti
krodhena apakṛtam anena iti
mohena dharmaḥ me bhaviṣyati iti
evam ete nava bhedāḥ
ekaieka tvena sya punar tridhā bhedaḥ
katham lobha krodha mohāḥ punar tridhā mṛdu madhya adhimātrāḥ iti
ekaikam punar tridhā bhavati mṛdu mṛduḥ madhya mṛduḥ tīvra mṛduḥ iti
tathā mṛdu madhyaḥ madhyamdhyaḥ tīvra madhyaḥ iti
tathā mṛdu tīvraḥ madhya tīvraḥ tīvra tīvraḥ iti
evam ekāśīti bhedā hiṃsā bhavati
sā ca punar ekāśīti bhedā api satī niyoga vikalpa samuddaya bhedāt asaṅkhyeyā
yathā niyoga bhedaḥ kaścid iti uktaḥ san anyam niyuṅkte yathā rājñaḥ
sa ca api niyuktaḥ param sa ca api param iti
te ca sarve niyuktāḥ samuddayena vikalpena vā hiṃsanti
tathā mūla niyoktā api niyojya eṅaḥ saṃhatya vikalpya ca hiṃsām anutiṣṭhati iti
vadhya ghātaka ādi prāṇi bhedasya asaṅkhyeya tvāt iti
evam anṛta ādiṣu api yojyam
kṛta kārita anumodita ādi yojyam
te khalu amī vitarkāḥ duḥkha ajñāna ananta phalāḥ
duḥkham ca ajñānam ca duḥkha ajñāne te eva anantam phalam yeṣām te duḥkha ajñāna ananta phalāḥ
duḥkham eṣām anantam phalam
ajñānam ca eṣām anantam phalam
tasmāt etān vitarkān manasā api na upekṣayet iti pratipakṣam bhāvayet
tatra hiṃsyasya tri prakārā pīḍā pratipādyate tat bheda dvāreṇa phala bheda pradar Vana artham
tathā ca hiṃsakaḥ vadhyasya vīryam ākṣipati
ghātaka rūpa avalokana bhartsana ādinā trastasya vīryam ākṣipya śastra ādi nipātanena duḥkhayati
tatas jīvitāt api mocayati
prāṇebhyaḥ viyojayati
tasya vīrya ākṣepāt asya hiṃsituḥ cetana acetanam paśu kṣetra ādikam upakaraṇam kṣīṇa vīryam bhavati
śastra ādi nipātana duḥkha utpādāt hiṃsā viśeṣāt naraka tiryak preta ādiṣu duḥkham anubhavati
tathā jīvita vyaparopaṇāt pratikṣaṇam ca jīvita atyaye vartamānaḥ janma maraṇa antare vartmni pratikṣaṇam maraṇam icchan api duḥkha vipākasya niyata vedanīya tvāt avaśya anubhavitavya tvāt katham cit eva ucchvas iti
yadi ca kathaṃcid puṇya avagamāt prabhūta puṇya avagatā alpīyasī hiṃsā bhavet tatra puṇya bhūmnā sukha prāptaḥ san api bhavet alpa āyuḥ āvāpa gata hiṃsā doṣeṇa
ittham anṛta ādiṣu api yathāsaṃbhavam hiṃsāyām uktam yojyam
evam vitarkāṇām hiṃsā ādīnām ddhāyām iva anugatam vipākam aniṣṭam bhāvayet na vitarkeṣu manaḥ praṇidadhīta
pratipakṣa bhāvanā heyāḥ vitarkāḥ yadā ca sytut aprasava dharmiṇaḥ aprasavāḥ ca te dharmiṇaḥ ca iti aprasava dharmiṇaḥ
yadā yoginaḥ manasi nā utpadyante nikṛtta mūlāḥ santaḥ tadā tat kṛtam yama niyama sthairya kṛtam aiśvaryam yoginaḥ siddhi sūcakam ahiṃsā ādi phala siddhi jñāpakam jāyate iti yoga siddhi phalam avasthitam eva
anyat api yoga aṅga stutaye aiśvaryam anuṣaṅga jātam ucyate
katham ekaikasya api ahiṃsā ādīnām sthiratva liṅgam īdṛśam yajña ādi dharma phalaiḥ api asamānam pratyakṣataḥ upalabhyate kim aṅga saṃhatānām yoga siddhi kara tvam iti
tat etat pratidarśayati tat yathā ahiṃsā pratiṣṭhāyām ahiṃsā sthira tve a vitarka prādur bhāve
tad sannidhau vaira tyāgaḥ
śāśvatika vicveṣiṇām api sarpa nakula ādīnām tasya ahiṃsakasya sannidhau vaira tyāgaḥ bhavati
satya pratiṣṭhāyām satya sthaiḥ ye kriyā phala āśraya tvam yajña ādi kriyā phalānām āgamanam prāptiḥ bhavati
satya vādi vākyāt iti śeṣaḥ
katham adhārmikaḥ api dhārmitaḥ bhūyāḥ iti ukte tad vacanāt dhārmikaḥ bhavati
yathā dharme asya ramatām manaḥ iti devaiḥ uktaḥ kuṇḍadhāra ārādhī brāhmaṇaḥ dhārmikaḥ babhūva
tathā svargam prāpnuhi iti uktaḥ svargam prāpnoti
yathā viśvāmitreṇa uktaḥ svargam prāpnuhi iti triśaṅkuḥ svargam prāpa
kim bahunā
amodhā asya vāc bhavati
asteya pratiṣṭhāyām a smṛhāyām
tatas kim asya bhavati stnā upasthānam bhavati sarva diś sthāni asya upatiṣṭhante ratnāni ātmānam darśayanti
brahmacarya pratiṣṭhāyām vīrya lābhaḥ
brahmacarya lābhāt apratighāt guṇān utkarṣayati
apratibandhān ātmanaḥ upapādayati
sarva śubha artha pravṛttiṣu aprativaddha vīryaḥ bhavati
na kenacid pratighātena vivadhyate iti arthaḥ
kiñca vinayeṣu śiṣyeṣu yogyeṣu vā sādhuṣu jñānam ādhātum samarthaḥ bhavati yathā bhagavān vyāsaḥ sam jñeye jajñe
a parigraha sthaiḥ ye janma kathantā sambodhaḥ
janmanaḥ kathaṃbhāva bodhaḥ asya bhavati
kim svid itam sama mama janmanaḥ kim sa tattvam katham svid itam kena prakāreṇa svid kim bhaviṣyāmaḥ uttarakālam kim vā na bhaviṣyāmaḥ bhaviṣyantaḥ vā ke bhaviṣyāmaḥ katham bhaviṣyāmaḥ iti evam asya pūrva apara anta madhyeṣu bhūta bhaviṣyat vartamāneṣu ātma jijñāsā samyak darśanasya pūrva rūpam sva rūpeṇa upāvartate
sva ātma viṣaya ālocanam ayatnena pravartate
na anyeṣām parigraha santāpa vitānita tṛṣām yatnena api jāyate
yameṣu siddhayaḥ uktāḥ
idānīm niyameṣu vakṣyāmaḥ śaucāt sva aṅga jugupsā paraiḥ a saṃsargaḥ
sva aṅga jugupsayā śaucam ārabhamāṇaḥ kāya avadya darśī śarīra garhya tva darśī kāyān abhiṣvaṅgī yatiḥ bhavati
kim ca paraiḥ a saṃsargaḥ bhavati
kāya svabhāva avalokī svam api kāyam jihāsuḥ mṛd jala ādibhiḥ ākṣālayan api kāya śuddhim apaśyan katham para kāyaiḥ atyantam eva aprayataiḥ saṃsṛjyate iti
kim ca anyat bhavati
sattva śuddhi saumanasya aikāgrya indriya jaya ātma darśana yogya tvāni ca asya bhavanti
pūrvasya pūrvasya sthairyāt uttarasya āvirbhāvaḥ
katham śuceḥ sattva śuddhiḥ
tatas saumanasyam tatas ekāgryam tatas ca indriya jayaḥ tatas ca ātma darśana yogya tvam buddhi sattvasya bhavati iti atas śauca sthairyāt adhigamyate etat sarvam
tatas ca iyam śauca siddhiḥ eva
santoṣāt anuttamaḥ sukha lābhaḥ
santoṣa vitarka anutpattau anuttamaḥ na vidyate smāt anyaḥ uttamaḥ
tathā ca uktam yat ca kāma sukham loke yat ca aihikam yat ca divyam mahat sukham
deva ādi sambandhi

kāya indriya siddhiḥ aśuddhi kṣayāt tapasaḥ
nirvartyamānam eva tapaḥ hinasti aśuddhi āvaraṇam kim aṅga nirvartitam iti abhi mānaḥ prāyaḥ
tad āvaraṇam ala upagamāt kāya siddhiḥ aṇima ādyā
mātā pitṛ ādi saṃbandha jam kāyam alam baijam cāra ādi jam ca sarvam tapasā nighātayiṣyate
tatas ca aṇima ādi kāya siddhiḥ
tathā viṣaya ādi samparka jam indriyāṇām adharma ādi āvaraṇam malam tapaḥ srotasvinī srotasā kṣālyate
tathā indriya siddhiḥ dūrāt śravaṇāt yā
svādhyāyāt iṣṭadevatā samprayogaḥ
devāḥ ṛṣayaḥ siddhāḥ ca ye iṣṭāḥ te svādhyāya śīlasya darśanam gacchanti kāryeṣu ca asya upadeśa ādiṣu vartante
samādhi siddhḥ īśvara praṇidhānāt
īśvara arpita sarva bhāvasya samādhiḥ siddhi ati
yayā samādhi siddhyā sarvam īpsitam avitatham jānāti
tathā deśa antar kāla antare ca asya prajñā yathābhūtam jānāti
uktāḥ saha siddhibhiḥ yama niyamāḥ
idānīm āsana ādīni vakṣyāmaḥ tatra sthira sukham āsanam
sthiram sukham ca āsanam
yasmin āsane sthirasya manaḥ gātrāṇām upajāyate sthira tvam duḥkham ca yena na bhavati tat abhasyet
tat yathā śāstra antara prasiddhāni nāmāni padmāsana ādīni pradarśyante
tatra śucau deva nilaya giri guhā nadī pulina ādau jvalana salila a samīpe jantu vivarjite śmake śuciḥ samyak ācamya parame īśvaram abhivandyān ca yoge īśvarān ātma gurūn ca praṇipatya caula jina kuśa uttaram aduḥkha karam prāc mukhaḥ udak mukhaḥ vā viṣṭaram adhiṣṭhāya anyatama deśām āsanam nirbadhnīyāt
tatra padmāsanam nāma savyam pādam upasaṃhṛtya dakṣiṇa upari
tathā eva dakṣiṇam savyasya upariṣṭāt
ca viṣṭabhya āsikā agra nihita dṛṣṭiḥ samudraka vat api hita uṣṭha sampuṭaḥ dantaiḥ danta agram aparāmṛśan muṣṭi mātra antara viprakṛṣṭa cibuka uraḥ sthalaḥ rājat danta antara nihita rasana agraḥ hastau pāṇyoḥ upari kacchapakam brahmāñjalim vā kṛtvā sakṛt āsthāpita ettham saṃsthānaḥ punar punar śarīra avayava śarīra vinyāsa viśeṣa parityakta prayatnaḥ san yena āsīt tat padmāsanam
etat ca sarvam anyeṣām āsanānām api tulyam
kaścid eva viśeṣaḥ
tathā dakṣiṇam pādam savyasya upari kṛtvā hastam ca dakṣiṇam savya hastasya upari nidhāya yena āste tat bhadrāsanam
anyat samānam
tathā kuñcita anyatara pādam avani vinyasta apara jānukam vīrāsanam
ucyamānaḥ eva viśeṣaḥ sarvatra
dakṣiṇam pādāṅguṣṭham parigṛhyāt dṛśyam kṛtvā tathā savyam pādāṅguṣṭhum dakṣiṇena ūru jaṅkgenāt dṛśyam parihṛhya yathā ca pārṣṇibhyām vṛṣaṇayoḥ apīḍanam tathā yena āste tat svastikam āsanam
samagulphau samāṅguṣṭhau prasārayan samajānū pādau daṇḍavadyena upaviśet tat daṇḍāsanam
na yogapaṭṭasam stham vā sa upāśrayam
ājānu prasārita bāhu śayanam paryaṅka āsanam
krauñca niṣadanam hasti niṣadanam uṣṭra niṣadanam ca krauñca ādi niṣadana saṃsthāna sādṛśyāt eva draṣṭavyam
bhūmau nyastoḥ ujaṅghanam sama saṃsthitam
sthita prasrabdhiḥ
anyena api prakāreṇa svayam utprekṣya sthita prasrabdhiḥ
anāyāsaḥ yena bhavati tat api āsanam sthitaprasrabdhī nāma
yathāsukham ca yena rūpeṇa āsīn asya sukham bhavati tat yathāsukham
ādi śabdāt anyat api yathā ācārya upadiṣṭam āsanam draṣṭavyam
tat āsana jaya abhyupāyaḥ idānīm upapādyate prayatna śauthilya ānantya samāpattibhyām
bhavati iti vākya śeṣaḥ
āsanam dṛḍha niṣpannam bhavati iti upaskāraḥ
prayatna uparamāt āsana bandha uttara kālam prayatna akaraṇāt vā siddhi ati
yena na aṅgamejayaḥ bhavati
yena prayatna uparameṇa
prayatnena hi aṅgam kampayati
yena acalita āsanaḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ
ānantye vā samāpannam
anantam viśvam ananta bhāvaḥ ānantyam tasmin samāpannam vyāpya viśva bhāvam sthitam cittam āsanam nirvartayati draḍhayati
tatas dvandva anabhighātaḥ
tatas āsana sthirībhāvāt
idam dṛṣṭam ānuṣaṅgikam
yat śita uṣṇa ādibhiḥ dvandvaiḥ na abhibhūyate
kiñ ca prāṇāyāma ādi yogya tā ca bhavati
katham tasmin sati śvāsa paśvāsayoḥ gati vicchedaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ
sati āsane dṛḍhe bāhyasya vāyoḥ ācamanam cvāsaḥ
yathā santata tvāt udakam nālena ākṛṣyate tathā santata tvāt nāsikā puṭa nālābhyām apāna vāyu saṃbandhaḥ bahis vāyuḥ ākṛṣyate tad ākarṣaṇam śvāsaḥ
tathā kauṣṭhya vāyoḥ niścāraṇam
prāṇa vṛtti sambandhaḥ hi kauṣṭhyaḥ vāyuḥ
tasya bahis nissāraṇam praśvāsaḥ
tayoḥ gati vicchedaḥ
kim uktam bhavati atas āha ubhaya abhāvaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ iti
sa tu trividhaḥ bāhya abhyantaraḥ tambha vṛttiḥ deśa kāla saṃkhyābhiḥ paridṛṣṭaḥ dīrgha sūkṣmaḥ
sa bāhya vṛttiḥ abhyantara vṛttiḥ stambha vṛttiḥ ca
yatra śvāsa pūrvakaḥ gati abhāvaḥ sa bāhya vṛttiḥ
bāhyasya vāyoḥ antar praveśanam prati vṛttiḥ yasya sa bāhyavṛttiḥ
tasmāt sa bāhyaḥ
bāhyam anye pūrakaḥ iti ācakṣate
yatra praśvāsa pūrvakaḥ rati abhāvaḥ saḥ ābhyantara vṛttiḥ
ābhyantarasya vāyoḥ bahis nissāraṇam prati vṛttiḥ yasya saḥ ābhyantara vṛttiḥ
tasmāt saḥ ābhyantaraḥ
tam recakaḥ iti ācakṣate
tṛtīyaḥ tu stambha vṛttiḥ
tatra ubhaya abhāvaḥ ācamana niścāraṇayoḥ abhāvaḥ
sa tu sakṛt prayatnāt prabhavati
yathā tapte nyastam upale jalam sarvatas saṃkocam āpadyate tathā sakṛt prayatnāt prāṇa ādi vṛttayaḥ saṃkocam upayānti iti āha dvayoḥ yugapad gati abhāvaḥ iti
trayaḥ api ete deśena paridṛṣṭāḥ iyān asya deśaḥ iti
yathā bahis vṛtteḥ antar ācamyamānasya nāsikā agra prabhṛti āpādāṅguṣṭham deśa vyāptiḥ
evam antar vṛtteḥ bahis niścāryamāṇasya vāyoḥ pādāṅguṣṭha prabhṛti ā nāsikā agram deśa vyāptiḥ
stambha vṛtteḥ ā mastakā pādatala vyāptiḥ
atha vā bahis api vitasti ādi krameṇa deśa vyāptiḥ asti eva
kālena paridṛṣṭāḥ kṣaṇānām iyattā avadhāraṇena iyantaḥ kṣaṇāḥ prāṇāyāmena ativāhitāḥ iti
tathā paridṛṣṭāḥ etāvadbhiḥ śvṣāsa praśvāsaiḥ atītaiḥ paridṛṣṭaḥ prathama uddhātaḥ
yathā nirodha kṣubhitānām vāyūnām sakṛt mūrdhānam uddhasya nivṛttiḥ prathamaḥ uddhātaḥ
saḥ eva mṛduḥ
punar ca sakrt uddhata nigṛhītasya vāyoḥ tāvadbhiḥ praśvāsaiḥ atītaiḥ paridṛṣṭaḥ dvitīyaḥ id hātar prāṇāyāmaḥ madhyamaḥ iti ucyate
tathā tṛtīyaḥ etāvadbhiḥ śvāsa praśvāsaiḥ paridṛṣṭaḥ tṛtīyaḥ uddhātaḥ
saḥ eva ca tris uddhātaḥ tīvraḥ iti
tathā vāyūnām dīrgha tvam anda tva āpatteḥ sūkṣmam ca bhavati
bāhya ābhyantara viṣaya ākṣepī caturthaḥ bāhyasya viṣayāḥ pādāṅguṣṭha ādayaḥ
bāhyaḥ hi vāyuḥ ācabhyamānaḥ ntardeśān vyāpnoti ākṣipati
ābhyantarasya viṣayāḥ bhūmi ādayaḥ
sa ca bahis niścāryamāṇaḥ bhūmi ādīn deśa kāla saṅkhyā paridṛṣṭān vyāpnoti ākṣipati
sa bāhya abhyantara viṣayāk caturthaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ
deśa kāla saṅkhyābhiḥ bāhya vastu viṣayaḥ paridṛṣṭaḥ ākṣiptaḥ vyāptaḥ
tathā ābhyantara viṣayaḥ paridṛṣṭaḥ deśa kāla saṅkhyā paridṛṣṭān vyāpnoti ākṣipati
sa bāhya ābhyantara viṣaya ākṣepī caturthaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ
bāhya vastu viṣayaḥ paridṛṣṭaḥ ākṣiptaḥ vyāptaḥ
tathā ābhyantara viṣayaḥ paridṛṣṭaḥ deśa kāla saṅkhyābhiḥ ākṣiptaḥ vyāptaḥ
ubhayathā dīrgha sūkṣmaḥ
bāhya ābhyantara viṣaya ākṣepeṇa ubhayathā dīrgha sūkṣma tva āpannaḥ
kim uktam bhavati iti āha tat pūrvakaḥ ubhatya viṣaya ākṣepa pūrvakaḥ
bhūmi jayāt ubhaya vṛtti vāyu bhūmi jaya krameṇa ubhayoḥ prāṇa apāna vṛttyoḥ bāhya abhyantarayoḥ gati abhāvaḥ caturthaḥ
tṛtīya caturthayoḥ ubhaya bṛtti sāmānyāt aviśeṣa tvam āśaṅkya āha tṛtīyaḥ tad viṣaya anālocitaḥ sakṛt ārabdhaḥ eva gati abhāvaḥ deśa kāla saṅkhyābhiḥ paridṛṣṭaḥ dīrgha sūkṣmaḥ
caturthaḥ tu śvāsa praśvāsayoḥ ātamitoḥ viṣaya avadhāraṇāt krameṇa vā yat gati abhāvaḥ caturthaḥ iti ayam viśeṣaḥ tṛtīya caturthayoḥ
tatas kṣīyate prakāśa āvaraṇam
prakāśaḥ āvriyate yena tat prakśāvaraṇam karma
prāṇāyāmān abhyasyataḥ yoginaḥ viveka jñānam āvriyate yena tat viveka jñāna āvaraṇīyam karma
yat tu ācakṣate śāstra antare mahā moha mayena indrajālena prakāśa śīlam sattvam āvṛtya tat eva akārye viniyuṅkte iti
yat āvriyate viparyaya jñāna mahā indrajālena tat eva sattvam āvaraṇa karmaṇā sarva akārye viniyujyate
tat prāṇāyāma abhyāsāt asya prakāśa āvaraṇam karma saṃsāra nibandhanam durbalam bhavati
na kevalam durbala bhāvaḥ eva pratikṣaṇam ca kṣīyate
tathā ca uktam bhavati anyat api prāṇāyāma abhyāsāt
dhāraṇāsu vakṣyamāṇāsu yogya tā manasaḥ prāṇāyāmāt eva pracchardana vidhāraṇābhyām vā prāṇasya iti vacanāt tābhyām hi manasaḥ sthiti sampattiḥ uktā
atha kaḥ pratyāhāraḥ pratyāhāra viśeṣam abhidhitsamānaḥ praśnena upakramate
sva viṣayāt indriyāṇām pratyāharaṇa mātram pareṣām pratyāhāraḥ
atra punar viśeṣavān ucyate sva viṣaya asamprayoge cittasya sva rūpa anukāraḥ iva indriyāṇām pratyāhāraḥ iti
svaiḥ svaiḥ śabda ādibhiḥ viṣayaiḥ indriyāṇām śrotra ādīnām saṃyoga abhāve viṣaya doṣa darśanāt dhyāyinām sva viṣayāt nirvartitānām citta sva rūpa anukāra tā iva
yoginaḥ cittam yat akāra tām bhajate tat citta sva rūpa anukāra tā iva iti
etat uktam bhavati citta nirodhe cittavat ruddhāni na upāya antaram jaya artham
citta nirodhāt eva tāni nirudhyante
yathā madhukara rājānam śruti akṣaram etat
madhukara rājam iti arthaḥ
makṣikāḥ utpatantam anūtpatanti niviśamānam anu niviśante
tathā eva indriyāṇi citta nirodhe niruddhāni iti eṣa pratyāhāraḥ
tatas pratyāhāra sthairyāt paramā vaśya tā indriyāṇām bhavati
iti śabdaḥ samāpti arthaḥ
yāsām ca vaśyatānām madhye pratyāhāra sthairyāt paramā vaśyatā jāyate tāḥ ucyante śabda ādiṣu indriya jayaḥ avyasanam punar punar anāsaktiḥ vā iti kecid āhuḥ
vyasanam iti nirbravīti saktiḥ vyasanam
katham vyasyati kṣipati enam pratipattāram śreyasaḥ sakāśāt iti vyasanam
a viruddhā pratipattiḥ vā
viruddhānām vā śabdaḥ ādīnām apratipattiḥ vaśya tā iti
tasya eva vyākhyānam nyāyyaḥ śāstra anujñātaḥ śabda ādiṣu saṃyogaḥ sva icchyā
teṣu a viruddheṣu yadi icchati pravartate na vai iti evam anye manvate
rāga dveṣa abhāve sukha duḥkha śūnyam heya upādeya tva varjitam śabda ādi jñānām vaśya tā iti eke
madhymāyām tu api na vāryate iti viśeṣaḥ
paramā tu iyam sarvāsām uktānām iyam paramā vaśyatā indriyāṇām yat yasmin citta niruddhāni indriyāṇi na itara indriya jaya vat pūrva uktāsu indriya vaśyatāsu upāya antaram apekṣante jaya artham asyām punar na prayatna kṛtam upāya antaram apekṣante yoginaḥ
iti śrī govinda bhgavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya paramahāṃsaparvrājaka ācāryasya śrī śaṅkara bhagavataḥ kṛtau śrīpātāñjala yoga śāstra sūtra bhāṣya vivaraṇe
dvitīyaḥ sādhana pādaḥ
uktāni pañca bahiraṅgāni sādhanāni samprajñātasya yogasya
adhunā antaraṅgam dhāraṇā dhyāna samādhi sama ākhyam sādhana trayam tasya eva abhidhīyate
bahiraṅga antaraṅga tva bhedāt eva hi bahiraṅga sādhana vyākhyānena eva pādaḥ parisamāpitaḥ
saṃhatya kāri tvāt ca sādhana trayasya pṛthak vacanam
bahiraṅga sādhana abhidhāna anantara paryupasthāpita antaraṅga sādhana pratipādanena pāda sambandhaḥ vyākhyātaḥ
asmin ca pāde vibhūtayaḥ prādhānyena pradarśyante iti ca ṛthak tvāt ā
etat eva hi samākhyā lābhe kāraṇam avādiṣma
dhāraṇā vaktavyā
pratyāhāra anantaram krama upanīta sannidhānā dhāraṇā abhidhānīyā
deśa bandhaḥ cittasya dhāraṇā
deśabandhanam deśabandhaḥ
kasya cittasya
svayam eva ca sarvam vyācaṣṭe nābhi cakre nābhi deśaḥ cakram iva
sarve vāyavaḥ avayavāḥ tatra cakrībhūtāḥ iti nābhi cakram
hṛdayam puṇḍarīka ākāram
mūrdha jyotiṣi
mūrdhanāḍī dvāram prabhāsvara tvāt jyotiḥ iti ākhyāyate
nāsikā agre jihvā agre iti evam ādiṣu deśeṣu bāhyeṣu ca viṣayeṣu candra āditya ādiṣu cittam badhyate
tasya cittasya iti evam ādiṣu apracalita rūpeṇa yā vṛttiḥ sā dhāraṇā iti ucyate
vṛtti mātreṇa iti
tat deśa pratyaya mātreṇa vikṣepa śūnyatayā vartate iti
tatra pratyaya eka tāna tā dhyānam
tasmin deśe dhāraṇā vṛtti viṣaye nābhi cakra ādau
dhyeya ālambanasya dhyeyaḥ deśa ādi tad ālambanasya
pratyayasya eka tāna tā sadṛśa pravāhaḥ tulya pratyayānām pravāhaḥ eka ākāraḥ pratyaya santānaḥ pratyaya antareṇa vijātīyena aparāmṛṣṭaḥ anākīrṇaḥ
tat dhyānam
dhāraṇā tu tasmin eva dhyeye tad avasthasya eva cittasya tad viṣaya vikalptaiḥ pratyaya antaraiḥ parāmṛṣṭā api
yathā sūrye dhāryamāṇasya tat gata parimaṇḍala tīvratara dīdhiti tva ādi pratyayeṣu api dhāraṇā eva
vṛtti mātreṇa tatra eva vartamāna tvāt cittasya
dhyānam punar na tu tathā
bhinna jātīya pratyaya antara aparāmṛṣṭaḥ eka pratyaya pravāhaḥ eva hi dhyānam
tat eva artha mātra nirbhāsam sva rūpa śūnyam iva samādhiḥ
tat eva dhyānam tulya pratyaya pravāha rūpam svām eka pratyaya santāna tām iva hitvā dhyeya ākāra nirbhāsam dhyeya ākāra vat avabhāsate
pratyaya ātmakena svena grahaṇa ātmanā sva rūpeṇa śūnyam iva
yathā sphaṭika dravyam upadhāna avabhāsam sva rūpa śūnyam iva
yadā bhavati dhyeya svabhāva āveśāt kāraṇāt cittasya tadā tat eva dheānam samādhiḥ iti ucyate
nanu ca yogaḥ samādhiḥ iti aṅgī pūrvam uktaḥ
iha aṅgaḥ yogasya samādhiḥ iti ākhyāyate
kaḥ punar atra aṅga aṅginoḥ bhedaḥ iti ucyate yogaḥ samādhiḥ iti citta sthiti viśeṣaḥ vivakṣitaḥ
iha tu pratyaya santānasya eva dhyeya svabhāva āveśāt dhyeya ākāra tvam aṅgam iti viśeṣaḥ
tat etat dhāraṇā dhyāna samādhi trayam yat vyākhyānam tat ekatra ekasmin deśe pariniṣpannam sat sāṃyamaḥ iti ucyate
tat āha eka viṣayāṇi trīṇi sādhanāni saṃyamaḥ iti ucyate
tat asya trayasya ittham krameṇa abhiniṣpannasya yatra yatra saṃyamaḥ śrūyate jetavya jayāya vā tatra tatra trayam etat praveditavyam iti evam artham etasya trayasya asmin śāstre paribhāṣā iyam saṃyamaḥ iti
vakṣyati ca pariṇāma traya saṃyamāt atīta anāgata jñānam sthūla svarūpa sūkṣma anvaya arthavat tva saṃyamāt bhūtajayaḥ iti ca
tat jayāt prajñā lokaḥ
tasya saṃyamasya jayāt sthira tva āpādanāt abhīpsita artha abhivyañjana samarthaḥ pradīpa āloka deśīyaḥ samādhi prajñāyāḥ bhavati ālokaḥ
yathā yathā saṃyamaḥ sthira padaḥ bhavati tathā tathā samāhi prajñā sthirapadī bhavati
yena samādhi prajñā lokena vyavahita viprakṛṣṭa ādi vastu nirbhāsana samarthena yoginaḥ kara tala kalitam iva abhimatam artham avalikayanti
tasya bhūmiṣu viniyogaḥ
tasya saṃyamasya bhūmiṣu bāhya ādhyātmikeṣu dhyāna ālambana bhūtāsu vakṣyamāṇāsu pariṇāma traya ādiṣu viniyogaḥ prayogaḥ kartavyaḥ
tad bhūmi jaya sākṣāt prayojana arthinā tasya saṃyamasya jita bhūmeḥ jitāyāḥ bhūmeḥ yatra bhūmau yoginaḥ saṃyatāyām saṃyamaḥ labdhaḥ tasyāḥ jitāyāḥ bhūmeḥ anantarā yā bhūmiḥ tatra saṃyamasya pūrva bhūmi jaya anantaram viniyogaḥ karaṇīyaḥ
tat yathā pṛthivī ādīnām sthūla svarūpa sūkṣma anvaya arthavattva bhūmiṣu krameṇa jetavyāsu sthūāyām bhūmau saṃyamam kṛtvā tad jaya anantaram svarūpe eva anantare saṃyamaḥ viniyojanīyaḥ
na anantaram sva rūpam vyatilaṅghya sūkṣma ādi bhūmiṣu saṃvidadhīta
kasmāt evam na hi ajita adhara bhūmiḥ anantarām bhūmim vilaṅghya prānta bhūmiṣu uparitanīṣu bhūmiṣu saṃyamam labhate
yadi ca anantarām bhūmim a jitvā prānta bhūmiṣu saṃyamam viniyuṅkṣeta tam eva saṃyamam na labhate
tatas ca tat alābhaḥ eva doṣaḥ
tad alābhāt ca saṃyama abhāvāt ca kutas tatra saṃyama viṣaye prānta bhūmau iti arthaḥ
prajñā lokaḥ
nimitta abhāvāt
na hi asati taila varti jvalana abhisannipāte pradīpa ālokaḥ
jita uttara bhūmikasya jita uttarātma ādi bhūmikasya yoginaḥ na adhara bhūmiṣu para citta jñāna ādiṣu saṃyamaḥ yuktaḥ
kasmāt tad arthasya ātma ādeḥ uttara bhūmeḥ apakṛṣṭa para citta jñāna ādi bhūmi vaiparītyena anyathā eva adhigata tvāt
para citta jñāna ādibhiḥ saṃkīrṇam asamādhi gata viveka ātmaka tvāt
tatra hi jita uttara bhūmi saṃyamasya parakīya citta ālambana tve saṃkīrṇa citta ākāra tā yogi cittasya api syāt iti na yuktaḥ
tatra ātma ādeḥ arthasya anyathā eva vivikta tayā adhigata tvāt
anyeṣām vyākhyānam arthasya
anyathā eva adhigata tvāt ātma ādi uttara bhūmi samādhi gamanena eva adhara para citta jñāna ādi bhūmeḥ arthasya adhigata tvāt iti
asmin pakṣe adhara bhūmiṣu saṃyamaḥ narthakaḥ iti vaditavyam abhaviṣyat na na yuktaḥ iti
na yuktaḥ iti etat asamīcīnam iva dṛśyate
bhūmeḥ asyāḥ iyam anantarā abhūmiḥ iyam anantaram jayanīyā iti katham avabhotsyate iti āha tatra yogaḥ eva upādhyāyaḥ
yogaḥ pūrva dhūmau saṃyama lābhaḥ
tena eva ānantaryam avagamyate
katham evam hi uktam yogena yogaḥ jñātavyaḥ
pūrva saṃyama lābhena yogena anantaraḥ toga viṣayaḥ prajñānīyaḥ
sa ca yogaḥ saṃyamaḥ tyogāt eva eva pravartate vivicyate
yathā eva januṣā andhakasya sopāna paṅktim ārurukṣataḥ prathama sopāna pratilabdha pada sparśa pratyayena anantara sopāna jñānam upaploṣyate tathā yogaḥ yogāt pravartate
yatas evam tasmāt saḥ ittham jānan apramattaḥ tu yogī yogena yuktaḥ san yogeṣu yoga aiśvarya phaleṣu ramate ciram iti
trayam antaraṅgam pūrvebhyaḥ
dhāraṇā dhyāna samādhi trayam antaraṅgam pūrvebhyaḥ pañcabhyaḥ sādhanebhyaḥ yama ādibhyaḥ samprajñātasya yogasya
tatra antaraṅga grahaṇam pūrva sādhana asampattau api atra trayaḥ ādaraḥ karaṇīyaḥ iti evam artham
vinā api hi yama ādi sādhana pañcataya sampad anena janma antara vihita saṃskāra āveśa vaśāt eva videha prakṛtila yānam iva dhāraṇā ādi traya sampattyā yogaḥ upakalpyate
dhāraṇā ādi trayeṇa vinā na yogaḥ saṃbhavati kasyacid
tad vyāpāra nairantarya saṃvāda ātmaka tvāt dhāraṇā ādhi trayasya
yagasya citta sampatti rūpa tvāt
yadā tu jñāna vairāgya sampattiḥ tadā na kiṃcid anyat dhāraṇa ādi api apekṣyate
tathā ca maṅki piṅgalā prabhṛtīnām anuśrūyate vairāgyāt eva samasta siddhiḥ
tathā ca uktam sthāna āsana vidhānāni iti pūrvatra śloka dvayam
tat api u bahis aṅgam nirbījasya tat api etat antar aṅgam api sa bījasya yogasya bahis aṅgam bhavati nirbījasya yogasya
kasmāt tad abhāve bhāvāt
tasya sa bīja antaraṅga sādhana trayasya abhāve api puruṣa sarva viśeṣa apekṣayā nirbīja yogasya bhāvāt bahiraṅga tvam
kecid ati samīcīna darśanāḥ janmani iva saṃskārāt paraktāḥ
teṣām para vairāgya virāma pratyaya saṃśīlana ādi samīkṣayā nirbījaḥ samādhiḥ upajaniṣyate eva
na hi teṣām dhāraṇā ādi samīkṣaṇam
tathā ca uktam uktaḥ samāhita cittasya yogaḥ vyutthita cittaḥ api katham yoga yuktaḥ syāt iti atas idam ārabhyate iti
tathā bhava pratyayaḥ videha prakṛti layānām iti
atha nirodha citta kṣaṇeṣu nirodha yuktam cittam yeṣu kṣaṇeṣu nirudhyate te nirodha citta kṣaṇāḥ teṣu nirodha kāle iti arthaḥ
kṣaṇeṣu iti bahuvacanam atīta anāgata vartamāna vṛtti tva pradarśana artham
nirodhasya tri kṣaṇam kṣaṇaḥ hi nirodha dharmam anvīyamānam cittam nirudhyate
calam guṇa vṛttam gauṇam cittam guṇa vṛttam calam iti avaśyam bhāvī tasya bāhya vṛttibhyaḥ nirudhyamāna cittasya pariṇāmaḥ
na hi a pariṇamamānasya cittasya puruṣa vat kauṭasthye nirodhaḥ upakalpate
tatas ca āha kīdṛśaḥ tadā nirodha pariṇāmaḥ iti
vyutthāna nirodha saṃskārayoḥ abhibhava prādur bhāvau nirodha kṣaṇa citta anvayaḥ nirodha pariṇāmaḥ
vyutthānam vividham utthānam calanam pratyaya ākāreṇa cittasya
tad upajanitaḥ saṃskāraḥ cittasya dharmiṇaḥ dharmaḥ
na sa pratyaya ātmakaḥ
tathā nirodha janmā saṃskāraḥ apratyaya ātmakaḥ cittasya eva dharmaḥ
sa ca vyutthāna saṃskāraḥ pratyaya ātmakaḥ iti sa pratyaya nirodhe na nirudhyate
vyutthāna pratyaya nirodhe na abhibhūtaḥ
pratyaya nirodhāt ca nirodha jaḥ saṃskāraḥ sañjāyate
tayoḥ vyutthāna nirodha saṃskārayoḥ dharmiṇi citte vartamānayoḥ abhibhava prādurbhāvau bhavataḥ
kim tāca āvirbhāva tirobhāvau aniyamena bhavataḥ na
katham tarhi
vyutthāna saṃskārāḥ hīyante sva kārya akṣama tvam upāśnuvate
nirodha saṃskārāḥ ādhīyante
tau ca abhibhava prādurbhāvau nirodha kṣaṇam cittam dharmi tvena na vā iti sa tayoḥ abhibhava prādurbhāvayoḥ cittena anugamaḥ nirodha pariṇāmaḥ cittasya
tat etat abhihitam bhavati ekasya cittasya pratikṣaṇam idam saṃskāra anyathātvam vyutthāna saṃskāra abhibhavena nirodha saṃskāra prādurbhāvena saṃskāra anyathātvam
vyutthāna saṃskārāṇām api hīyamāna tayā sati api sambandhe prādurbhavatā nirodhena eva balavat tvāt nirodha pariṇāmaḥ iti samākhyātam
tadā nirodhyamānam bāhyebhyaḥ pratyayebhyaḥ saṃskāra śeṣam cittam iti vyākhgyātam virāma pratyaya abhyāsa pūrvaḥ saṃskāra śeṣaḥ nyaḥ iti
kim etena āha nirodha avasāna tvāt pratyaya abhāva avasāna tayā pariṇāmasya nirodha pariṇāmaḥ iti
samprajñāta avasthāyām
api pratyayāḥ na vivakṣitāḥ kim tu prati kṣaṇa saṃskāra anyathātvam eva vivakṣyate
yathā niruddhabhūmini cetasi vidyamānaḥ
api samādhiḥ na vivakṣyate
nirodha mātrasya vivakṣita tvāt
tathā sa bīja avasthāyām api saṃskāra anyathātva mātram eva vivakṣitam
na pratyayāḥ samādhiḥ ekāgra tā ca iti
tasya cittasya nirodha pariṇāmam anugacchataḥ praśānta vāhi tā saṃskārāt
nirodha saṃskāra pāṭava apekṣā nirodha saṃskārasya pāṭavam draḍhimā draḍhimā tad apekṣā praśānta vāhi tā cittasya bhavati
sā praśānta vāhitā kiyantam kālam iti āha tam saṃskāram nirodha saṃskāram ārabhya yāvat vyutthāna dharmiṇā vyutthaānam dharmaḥ byutthāna janita tvāt yasya tena saṃskāreṇa nirodha dharma saṃskāraḥ na ābhbhūyate tāvantam kālam asya praśānta vāhitā
nirodha saṃskāra samudayāt iti
kṣaya udayau cittasya samādhi pariṇāmaḥ
sarva artha tā bhoga apavarga artha yogya tā vicitra tā citta dharmaḥ
vakṣyati draṣṭṛ dṛśya uparaktam cittam sarva artham iti
ekāgra tā api cittasya dharmaḥ śānta udita pratyayoḥ sāmyam samādhīyamānasya cittasya sarva artha tāyāḥ kṣayaḥ bhavati
tirobhāvaḥ iti arthaḥ
na hi kiṃcid vidyamānam vinaṅkṣyati
ekāgratāyāḥ udayaḥ bhavati
āvirbhāvaḥ iti arthaḥ
na a vidyamānam utpadyate
tayoḥ kṣaya udayayoḥ dharmi tvena anugatam cittam
pūrva sūtrāt anvaya grahaṇam iha api sannidhīyate
sarva artha tāyāḥ kṣayam ekāgra tāyāḥ ca udayam niyamena anvīyamānam cittam samādhi prādhānyena pariṇamate
yaḥ
asau cittena sarva artha tā ekāgra tā kṣaya udayayoḥ anugamaḥ sa samādhi pariṇāmaḥ
samādheḥ ca ekāgra tā bhūmau vyākhyātam yaḥ tu ekāgre cetasi sa bhūtam artham pradyotayati iti
tat eva āha tat idam cittam apāya upajanau sva ātma bhūtau a vyatiriktau tayoḥ dharmayoḥ sarva artha tā ekāgra tayoḥ anu bhavāḥ gamāt samādhīyate
sa cittasya samādhi prādhānyāt samādhi pariṇāmaḥ
tatra punar samādhi kāle śānta uditau tulya pratyayau cittasya ekāgra tā pariṇāmaḥ
samāhita cittasya niruddha bāhya vṛtteḥ pūrvaḥ pratyayaḥ śāntaḥ tirobhūtaḥ
uttaraḥ tad sadṛśaḥ uditaḥ prādurbhūtaḥ
samādhi cittam samāhāna viśiṣṭam samādhi avastham
samādhi cittam ubhayoḥ śānta uditayoḥ pratyayoḥ anugatam
punar tathā eva yathā pratyayaḥ ādyaḥ śāntaḥ uttaraḥ tad sadṛśaḥ upajātaḥ sa ca śāntaḥ punar anyaḥ uditaḥ sa śāntaḥ punar ca anyaḥ uditaḥ iti evam ā samādhi bhreṣāt vyutthāna saṃskāreṇa yāvat samādhiḥ vibhraṃśate
sa khalu ayam dharmiṇaḥ cittasya pratikṣaṇam sat ṛṛśa śānta udita pratyayayoḥ anugamaḥ ekāgra tā pariṇāmaḥ
tatra yāvat bāhya vṛtti nirodhāt ārabhya cittasya saṃskāra pariśeṣa tā tāvat nirodha pariṇāmaḥ
tathā bāhya pratyaya nirodhāt prabhṛti ā prāk aśeṣa pratyaya nirodhāt aśeṣa pratyaya nirodha uttarakālam ca ekāgra tā udaya abhāvāt tāvat samādhi pariṇāmaḥ
tathā samāhi pariṇāma kāle eva śānta uditayoḥ tulyayoḥ saṃbhavāt ekāgra tā pariṇāmaḥ
uttara uttara pariṇāmasya iti krameṇa trayaḥ api pariṇāmāḥ vyākhyātāḥ
kim anena pariṇāma anvākhyānena prayojanam ucyate calam guṇa vṛttam gauṇam ca samastam pariṇāma dharmakam anavasthitam iti vairāgya bhāvanā artham
tathā pariṇāma traya saṃyamāt atīta anāgata jñāna artham ca etat anvākhyānam
etena bhūta indriyeṣu dharma lakṣaṇa avasthā pariṇāmāḥ vyākhyātāḥ
etena pūrva uktena citta pariṇāmena
kiṃcid śiṣṭena dharma lakṣaṇa avasthā rūpeṇa dharma rūpeṇa lakṣaṇa rūpeṇa avasthā rūpeṇa ca
bhūta indriyeṣu bhūteṣu pṛthivī prabhṛtiṣu sthūleṣu indriyeṣu śrotra ādiṣu yeṣām tattva antara pariṇāmaḥ na asti
dharma pariṇāmaḥ lakṣaṇa pariṇāmaḥ vasthā pariṇāmaḥ ca uktaḥ veditavyaḥ
cittasya anavasthita tvena gamyamānena pariṇāmena bhūta indriyāṇām pariṇāmasya pariṇāmasya prakāra traya yoginaḥ citta pariṇati vat asu vijñāna tvāt atideśaḥ kriyate
nanu ca ariṇāmāḥ cittasya abhihitāḥ
na tu dharma lakṣaṇa avasthā pariṇāmāḥ
kutas tatra atideśaḥ iti abhihita tvam eṣām darśayati tatra vyutthāna nirodhayoḥ dharmayoḥ abhibhava prādur bhāvau dharmiṇi citte dharma pariṇāmaḥ
etasmāt hi dharma bheda vacanāt dharma bhedam avādiṣma
tayoḥ ca vyutthāna nirodhayoḥ abhibhava prādurbhāva vacanāt lakṣaṇa avasthā pariṇāmau api ca avādiṣma eva
katham vartamāna lakṣaṇāt atīta lakṣaṇam abhisampadyamānaḥ dharmaḥ abhibhūyate
yaḥ ca anāgata lakṣaṇāt vartamāna lakṣaṇam abhisampadyamānaḥ sa prādur asti
tat abhibhava prādur bhāva vacanāt ca pratikṣaṇam durbala rūpaḥ vasthā pariṇāmaḥ uktaḥ bhavati iti āha lakṣaṇa pariṇāmī kūṭasthaḥ iti ucyate
sa khalu nirodhaḥ anāgata lakṣaṇam adhvanam hitvā dharma tvam nirodha dharma tvam an atikrāntaḥ asatkārya ārambhāvāt
asatkārya ārambhe hi tri kāla tvam ekasya vastunaḥ na upapadyate na api kāla traya paricchedyasya tri lakṣaṇasya abhāvāt
atas ucyate dharma tvam an atikrāman eva vartamānam lakṣaṇam pratipannaḥ yatra yasmin vartamāne lakṣaṇe asya sva rūpeṇa abhivyaktiḥ eṣaḥ asya nirodhasya anāgata adhva samīkṣayā dvitīyaḥ dhvā
yadā tu vyutthānam vartamānam lakṣaṇam ārokṣyati tadā adhvānam tṛtīyam prāpsyati iti sa tṛtīyaḥ dhvā bhaviṣyati eva
syāt etat vartamāna lakṣaṇa pratipattau nirodhasya tri adhvam na asti iti atas āha na ca atīta anāgatābhyām lakṣaṇābhyām viyuktaḥ
kutas yena saḥ eva anāgataḥ vartamānaḥ u tītaḥ ca iti
tathā vyutthānam tri lakṣaṇam tribhiḥ adhvabhiḥ atīta anāgata vartamānaiḥ yuktam vartamāna lakṣaṇam hitvā dharma tvam an atikrāntam yathā nirodhe nirodhini dharme vartamānam adhvānam a hisampadyamāne atīta lakṣaṇam adhvānam pratipannam
eṣaḥ u asya vyutthānasya vartamānam prathamam adhvānam abhisamīkṣya dvitīyaḥ dhvā
dvitīye tu paryāye eva adhvā dvitīyaḥ bhaviṣyati
na ca anāgata vartamānābhyām lakṣaṇābhyām viyuktam
punar vyutthānam nirodha saṃskāreṇa upasampadyamānam anāgata lakṣaṇam adhvānam hitvā dharma tvam an atikrāntam vartamāna lakṣaṇam pratipannam
yatra asya sva rūpeṇa abhivyaktau satyām vyāpāraḥ sva kārya āpādana sāmarthyam
eṣaḥ asya sva rūpeṇa abhivyaktau satyām vyāpāraḥ sva kārya āpādana sāmarthyam
eṣā u asya anāgatā abhisamīkṣyā dvitīyaḥ dhvā
na ca atīta anāgatābhyām lakṣaṇābhyām viyuktam
yathā cittam vyutthāna nirodha dharmābhyām na yujyate
evam punar nirodhaḥ evam punar vyutthānam iti eṣa lakṣaṇa pariṇāmaḥ citta dharmayoḥ vyutthāna nirodhayoḥ
tathā avasthā pariṇāmaḥ paridṛśyate
katham nirodha kṣaṇeṣu nirodhe vartamāne nirodha saṃskārāḥ balavantaḥ bhavanti
saṃskāra balavat tvena nirodha balavat tvam api
durbalāḥ vyutthāna saṃskārāḥ tatas eva vyutthāna durbala tvam api
tathā vyutthāna lakṣaṇe vyutthāna saṃskāra balīyaḥ tvam nirodha saṃskāra durbala tvam iti evam pratikṣaṇam dṛḍha durvala avatthābhyām yujyamānānām dharmāṇām avasthā pariṇāmaḥ
tatra kena rūpeṇa kasya pariṇāmaḥ iti darśayati dharmiṇaḥ dharmaiḥ pariṇāmaḥ
yathā cittasya dharmiṇaḥ nirodha vyutthāna ādi dharmaiḥ
dharmāṇām tri adhvanām lakṣaṇaiḥ pariṇāmaḥ
yathā nirodha ādi citta dharmāṇām anāgata ādi lakṣaṇaiḥ
lakṣaṇānām api avasthābhiḥ pariṇāmaḥ
yathā vartamāna ādi lakṣaṇānām dṛḍha durbala tva ādi avasthābhiḥ
iti evam dharma lakṣaṇa avasthā pariṇāmaiḥ a śūnya lakṣaṇam a śūnya rūpam guṇa āvṛttam avatiṣṭhete
calam guṇa vṛttam
etat eva tu guṇa svabhāvyam pravṛtti kāraṇam sakala vyāpāra kāraṇam uktam guṇānām sattva ādīnām iti
etena cetasi prasiddhena dharma lakṣaṇa avasthā pariṇāma triyena bhūtyā indriyeṣu dharma dharmi bhedāt trividhaḥ pariṇāmaḥ veditavyaḥ
paramārthataḥ tu ekaḥ eva pariṇāmaḥ
katham dharmi svarūpa mātraḥ hi dharmaḥ
na hi dharmi parihāreṇa dharmaḥ nāma pṛthak asti
nā api dharma parityāgena lakṣaṇam nāma pṛthak bhāvyate
na api lakṣaṇa vyatirekeṇa avasthānām pṛthaktvam bhavati
tena dharmi vikriyā eva eṣā dharma dvārā dharma bheda dvāreṇa tridhā prapañcyate
katham punar dharmi vikriyā eva eṣā
na punar iti tatas āha tatra dharmasya ghaṭa ādeḥ dharmiṇi mṛd ākhye vartamānasya adhvasu atīta anāgata vartamāneṣu bhāva anyathātvam eva pratyaya anyathātvam atītaḥ ghaṭaḥ vartate anāgataḥ iti ca dharmiṇi vartamānasya eva
saḥ eva dharmasya āvirbhāva tirobhāva anyathātvam
na dravya anyathātvam tat eva mṛd dravyam dharmi antaram ca
udāharaṇam paridarśayati yathā suvarṇa bhājanasya anyathā kuṇḍala ādi bhāvena kriyāmāṇasya bhāva anyathātvam svastika kuṇḍala ādi saṃsthāna anyatvam
na suvarṇa dravya anyathātvam iti
aparaḥ āha asatkārya samārambha abhimānī dharma abhyadhikaḥ dharma vyatiriktaḥ dharmī dharmaḥ ca a vidyamānaḥ anyaḥ ca anyaḥ ca samudāyiṣyate
na punar ekaḥ dharmī dharmeṣu bhūta bhaviṣyat vartamāneṣu dharma a vyatiriktaḥ nvayī iti
yadi anvayī dharma anabhyadhikaḥ dharma avyatiriktaḥ pūrva tattvāt pūrva pūrva dravya svarūpāt an atikrāman pūrva apara avasthā bhedam atīta ādi avasthā bhedam anugatitaḥ anugataḥ syāt tatas ca eṣa doṣaḥ prasajati sa dharmī tava abhimataḥ kauṭasthyena api parivarteta apariṇāmmi tve varteta
atra aha ayam adoṣaḥ
kasmāt ekānta anabhyupagamāt ātyanta kauṭasthya vināśayoḥ dharmiṇaḥ
yadi atyantam kūṭasthaḥ dharmī syāt ātma vat tatas ca asmāt dharmiṇaḥ dharmāṇām abhedāt kauṭastham prasajyate iti doṣaḥ syāt
na tu dharmiṇām guṇānām atyanta kauṭastham abhyupagamyate
pariṇāmi nitya tvam hi guṇānām vadiṣyati
atha vā dharma dharmiṇoḥ ekānta bheda an abhyupagamāt
ekāntena hi dharmibhyaḥ nvayibhyaḥ dharmiṇām ā bhedam kauṭasthyam prāpnuyāt
atyanta bhede vā dharmāṇām atyanta vināśaḥ syāt
na tu atyanta bheda abhedau abhyupayiṣyete
tasmāt na kauṭastgya doṣaḥ iti
katham kauṭasthya abhāvaḥ iti āha tat etat vailokyam vyakteḥ apaiti na kūṭastham
kasmāt nitya tva pratiṣedhāt
kārya tvāt eva hi nitya tvam pratiṣiddham
atha ati nta vinaṣṭam iti ced āha apetam api asti vināśa pratiṣedhāt
kāraṇasya nitya tvāt tad abhedāt ca kāryasya atyanta vināśaḥ pratiṣiddhaḥ eva
tatas ca yat ucyate kaiḥ cit viruddha hetvābhāsa udāharaṇam etat iti katham yathā asau vikāraḥ vyakteḥ apaiti nitya tva pratiṣedhāt apetam api asti iti atra nitya tva pratiṣedhāt iti ayam hetuḥ apetaḥ api asti iti anena siddhāntena virudhyate
katham vyaktiḥ ātma lābhaḥ apāyaḥ pracyutiḥ yadi ātma lābhāt pracyutaḥ nitya tva pratiṣedhaḥ na upapadyate
yat tu vyakteḥ apetasya api vikārasya astitvam tat khalu nitya tvam iti
nitya tva pratiṣedhaḥ nāma vikārasya ātmalābhāt pracyutiḥ
yadā ātmalābhāt pracyuvate tat anityam
yat asti na pracyuvate
astitvam ca ātma lābhāt pracyutiḥ ca iti viruddhau etau dharmau saha na sambhavataḥ
saḥ yam hetuḥ yam siddhāntam āśritya pravartate tam eva vyāhanti iti viruddhaḥ hatuḥ iti
na ayam doṣaḥ
vastūnām vyakta avyakta dharmaka tva abhyupagamāt
yathā hi ghaṭa ādi vidyamānaḥ api san agāre na upalabhyate
na ca tāvatā asau na asti iti śakyam pratijñātum
āloka upāyena hi vyajyate
tathā idam trailokyam kāraṇe saṃsṛṣṭam vidyamānam eva anabhivyakta ātmaka guṇa svabhāva tayā puruṣa artha nimittena āviṣkriyate
tathā eva ca gati saṃskāra kṣaye sthiti saṃskāra abhivyaktau kāraṇam prati saṃsṛjyamānam vyakteḥ apaiti
yathā dīpa āloka tirodhāne vidyamānaḥ api ghaṭa āt iha santam asau aṣṭambhāt vyakteḥ apasarati tathā atra api mahat ādayaḥ dharmāḥ tri adhvānaḥ saṃsarga visarga dharmāṇaḥ na tu sattva ādayaḥ dharmiṇaḥ
tatas trailokyam mahat ādi stamba paryavasānam sattva ādīnām dharma bhūtam na abhivyakti dharmakam sat atyanta niruddha sūkṣma dharma samudāyāt vyakti sthūla dharma rūpeṇa na gṛhyate iti ucyate tat etat trailokyam vyakteḥ apaiti iti
na punar darmi svarūpeṇa apāyaḥ
tathā ca dharmi rūpeṇa nitya tvāt ucyate tad apetam api asti iti
tat evam vyakti rūpaḥ ca śakti rūpaḥ ca ekaḥ dharmī vyakti rūpeṇa ca tasya anitya tvam śakti rūpeṇa ca nitya tvam iti katham eṣa virodhaḥ syāt
na hi devadattaḥ calana ādi vyāpāreṇa sarvadā gṛhyamāṇaḥ calana ādi virāme viraṃsyati
calanam eva hi tirodhīyate
tasmāt avyakta avasthita ghaṭa ādi vat
vyaktiḥ api svakīya dharma antara samīkṣayā dharmiṇī
sā ca dharmi rūpeṇa nityā dharma rūpeṇa anityā abhyupeyate
evam vikāreṣu dharma dharmi bhedaḥ anavasthitaḥ iti anavasthā api iṣyate eva
tatra vyakteḥ apaiti iti anena na virudhyate nitya tva pratiṣedhāt iti ayam hetuḥ
na api apatā īm api asti iti anena virodhaḥ
ubhayoḥ bhinna viṣaya tvāt
na api vināśa pratiṣedhāt iti ayam apetam api asti iti anena virudhyate
yathā bāhyāt api asti devadattam
tat etat a nirjñāya para abhiprāyam virodha udāharaṇa tva apādānam andhadarpaṇīya vṛttāntam udbhāvayati
yathā kila kaścid andhaḥ svām adarśana śaktim an avadhārya sva artham ādarśam upājayati tadvat etat ābhāti
api ca yadi api ekatra eva vyaktau śaktau vā nitya tvam anitya tvam ca adhyāropya tvam pakṣa siṣādhayiṣayā bravīthāḥ evam api viruddha udāharaṇa tvam na sambhavati viparītā sādhanāt
katham apetaḥ api asti iti nitya tva pratiṣedhāt iti ucyate
nitya tva pratiṣedhāt iti anitya tvāt iti uktam bhavati
apetasya api astitvam nitya tvam ucyate
nitya tvasya viparītam anitya tvam
na ca pakṣasya anitya tvasya anitya tvam hetuḥ bhavati yaḥ viparītam sādhayan nitya tvam virundhīta
na hi aniṣṭam a sādhayan viruddha tām iyāt
atha api nitya tva pratiṣedhaḥ nāma ātma lābhāt pracyutiḥ iti evam api śabda bhda mātram na artha bhedaḥ
ātma lābhāt pracyutiḥ anitya tvam iti ekaḥ rthaḥ
atha api nitya tva upapatti abhāvāt iti avalambethāḥ evam api nitya tva pratiṣedhāt iti ayam śabdaḥ ekasyām śuktikāyām nitya tva upapatti abhāvāt iti asya arthasya vācakaḥ
atha api vācakaḥ iti āropya pratibhāṣeta evam api śakti vyakti dharma dharmi bheda rūpeṇa na nitya tvam anitya tvam ca iti ukyam eva samādhānam
etena vyakteḥ api asti vināśa pratiṣedhāt iti virodha udbhāvanam prati ākhyātam
evam avasthite vyakteḥ apetasya pratyakṣeṇa anupalbhyamānasya katham astitvam yāvatā na asti nabhaḥ kusuma vat iti
atrā ucyate anupalabdhiḥ asiddhaḥ hetuḥ
anumāna āgamābhyām upalabdheḥ
yat etat vyaktam etat prāk utpatteḥ api asti yatas utpadyate
asat ced na utpadyeta caśa viṣāṇa vat eva
kim ca asataḥ sattve sataḥ ca asattve sarvatra naḥ āśvāsyuḥ
kim ca anupalabdheḥ ced asattvam mukta ātma kāraṇa ādīnām ca prāk upalambhāt ūrdhvam ca astitvam kena lahyate tathā na sataḥ vidyate bhāvaḥ na abhāvaḥ vidyate sataḥ
iti āgamaḥ
pratyakṣa anupalabdhiḥ ca na asattvasya kāraṇam
atha vyakteḥ eva vikārp vidyamānaḥ ced kutas na upalabhyate iti āha sākṣāt kāraṇe saṃsargāt asya saukṣmyam atas nupalabdhiḥ
na a sattvāt
idānīm bhūta indriyāṇām lakṣaṇa pariṇāmaḥ idam ucyate lakṣaṇa pariṇāmaḥ dharmaḥ yathā mṛdaḥ ghaṭa ādiḥ adhvasu atīta ādiṣu dharmaḥ
kim uktam bhavati atīta lakṣaṇa yuktaḥ na punar asattvam āpannaḥ
itarābhyām ca anāgata vartamānābhyām a viyuktaḥ
kāraṇasya mṛdaḥ vartamāna tvāt tatra saṃsṛṣṭasya ghaṭasya vidyamāna tve yuktaḥ vartamānena lakṣaṇena ghaṭaḥ
tathā bhaviṣyan api ghaṭaḥ mṛdaḥ eva anāgataḥ san bhaviṣyati iti anāgata lakṣaṇena api a viyuktaḥ tathā vartamānaḥ vartamāna lakṣaṇa yuktaḥ atīta anāgatābhyām lakṣaṇābhyām a viyuktaḥ
tathā anāgataḥ anāgata lakṣaṇa yuktaḥ vartamāna atītābhyām lakṣāṇābhyām a viyuktaḥ atīta anāgata lakṣaṇayoḥ mṛd ātmaka tvāt ghaṭasya vyavahitena api atīta lakṣaṇena aviyogaḥ
katham eka lakṣaṇa yuktaḥ dharmaḥ lakṣaṇābhyām aparābhyām a viyuktaḥ iti aviyogasya dṛṣṭāntam āha yathā puruṣaḥ ekasyām striyām raktaḥ na śeṣasu viraktaḥ bhavati
śeṣāsu tu bhūta bhaviṣyat lakṣaṇa yuktaḥ rāgaḥ
sataḥ ca avināśāt asataḥ ca anutpatteḥ iti hi pratipāditam
atra lakṣaṇa pariṇāme sarvasya dharmasya sarva lakṣaṇa yogāt adhva saṃkaraḥ paurdoṣaḥ codyate
katham yaḥ hi bhaviṣyati sa vartate atītaḥ ca
tena atīte vartamāna bhaviṣyat tvam vartamāne atīta bhaviṣyat tvam bhaviṣyati ca atīta vartamāna tvam iti evam anyonya adhva saṃkaraḥ
tasya parihāraḥ ayam ucyate dharmiṇaḥ mṛd ākhyasya dharmāṇām miṇḍa ghaṭa kapālānām dharma tvam dharma antarāt ca abhinna tvam aprasādhyam
sati ca dharma tve tad bhede ca lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ api siddhaḥ vācyaḥ
katham yathā piṇḍa avasthāyām anāgata lakṣaṇa yuktaḥ ghaṭaḥ na vartamānaḥ na api atītaḥ
yadi api mṛd tva bhaviṣyat tva samīkṣayā atīta vartamānābhyām api a vi yuktaḥ
tathā vartamāna lakṣaṇa yuktaḥ na atītaḥ na api anāgataḥ
yadi api atīta anāgata lakṣaṇābhyām hīyamāna jāyamānābhyām lakṣaṇābhyām api vi yuktaḥ
tathā piṇḍa kapāla ādiṣu yojanīyam
tasmāt āha na vartamāna samayaḥ eva asya ekam lakṣaṇaḥ dharmasya
kim tarhi prakāreṇa uktena tri lakṣaṇa tvam
atas na adhvānaḥ saṃkīryante
evam hi na cittam rāga dharmakam iti na citte dharmiṇi rāga ādīnām dharma tve tad bhede ca siddhe
kasmāt krodha kāle rāgasya a samudācārāt
na hi krodha kāle rāgaḥ sva kāle iva samudācarati
krodha kāle hi rāgaḥ atītaḥ na āgataḥ vā
tathā krodhaḥ api rāga kāle
yadi hi vartamāna samaye eva ekam lakṣaṇam abhaviṣyat kodha kāle na asti
kim ca trayāṇām lakṣaṇānām yugapad ekasyām lakṣaṇasya vṛttau virodhāt na asti sambhavaḥ
krameṇa lakṣaṇānām krameṇa sva vyañjaka anjanasya ghaṭa ādi sva vyañjaka añjanasya anyatam asya kaṣaṇasya bhavet sambhavaḥ
uktam ca rūpa atiśayāḥ vṛtti atiśayāḥ ca virudhyante
vartamāna rūpa vṛtti atiśayaiḥ yukte ghaṭe ca piṇḍa ādi vyakti rūpa atiśayāḥ virodhāt na saṃbhavanti
atas eva atīta anāgata rūpāḥ dharmi sāmānya anugata tvena avirodhāt atiśayaiḥ saha vartante
tasmāt adhvanām asaṃkaraḥ
yathā rāgasya eva kvacid samudācāraḥ iti na tadānīm anyatra abhāvaḥ rāgasya
kin tu kevalam sāmānyena citta rūpeṇa samanvāgataḥ atītaḥ na āgataḥ api san iti asti tadā tasya rāgasya bhāvaḥ
tathā lakṣaṇasya iti
nanu ca piṇḍa kapālayoḥ atīta anāgata tvāt ghaṭa avasthāyām abhāvāt ca tābhyām mṛd ākhyasya dharmiṇaḥ api atīta anāgata tvam iti dharmiṇi piṇḍa kapālayoḥ abhāvaḥ iti kṛtvā dharmāṇām piṇḍa kapāla ādīnām adhva traya anupapattiḥ iti pariśaṅkamānaḥ kathayati na dharmī tri adhvā
mṛd ākhyaḥ hi dharmī piṇḍakpāla atīta anāgata tvena na atītaḥ na agataḥ vā
sarva dharmeṣu mṛd abhijñānā anu pra vṛtteḥ
kim tarhi dharmāḥ piṇḍa ādayaḥ tri adhvānaḥ ghaṭa kāle piṇḍa kapālayoḥ adarśanāt
tasmāt adhva traya ayogaḥ na dharmāṇām pariśaṅkanīyaḥ
te dharmāḥ lakṣitāḥ piṇḍa ādayaḥ tri adhva tvena abhilakṣitāḥ tām tām avasthām dṛḍha durbala tva ādikām prāpnuvantaḥ nyatvena navaḥ ghaṭaḥ purāṇaḥ ca iti anena pratinirdiśyante vasthā antarataḥ
na dravya antarataḥ mṛd atiriktāt
yathā ekā rekhā śata sthāne śūnya dvayena tṛtīya sthāne śatam bhavati
sā eva ca daśa sthāne ekena śūnyena dvitīya sthāne daśa
sā eva prathama sthāne ekā
yathā vā ekatve api strī mātā ca utyate duhitā ca sā eva anya apekṣayā svasā ca
tat evam avasthā antarāt eva śabda pratyaya ādi bhedāḥ
na dharma dharmi bhedena
tasmāt yat ucyate paraiḥ śabda pratyaya lakṣaṇa dharma kāla ādi bhedaḥ hetuḥ kārya kāraṇa bhede iti saḥ nena anaikāntikīkṛtaḥ
avasthā pariṇāme tṛtīye smin kauṭasthya prasaṅga doṣaḥ kaiścid uktaḥ
katham kauṭasthya prasaṅgaḥ adhvānaḥ vartamāna ādayaḥ sva vyāpāreṇa sthi tāḥ
katham yadā dharmaḥ ghaṭaḥ piṇḍa avasthāyām sva vyāpāram na karoti tadā anāgataḥ
yadā karoti tadā vartamānaḥ ayam
yadā kṛtvā nivṛttaḥ tadā atītaḥ
tatra saḥ eva dharmaḥ kṛtaḥ kriyamāṇaḥ kariṣyamāṇaḥ nija vyāpāra upārūḍhaḥ dharmi tva ātma bhūtaḥ eva avasthāpitaḥ
na vyatirikta rūpaḥ
tena dharmiṇām guṇānām nitya tvāt nitya tva avyatirekāt dharma lakṣaṇa avasthanām kauṭasthyam prāpnoti iti doṣaḥ ucyate
na asau doṣaḥ kasmāt guṇi nitya tve api guṇānām vimarda vaicitryāt udbhava abhibhava tva vicitra tayā puruṣa vat ekānta kūṭastha tā nā iṣyate guṇānām
pariṇāma abhyupagamāt
na ca anavarata pariṇatīnām api paraspara vimarda a trirekeṇa dravya antara bhāva āpattiḥ iti na kauṭasthyam
katham vimarda vaicitryam iti āha yathā saṃsthānam śarīra ādikam ādi mat kāraṇavat dharma mātram kāraṇasya ātma bhūtam avyatiriktam vināśi tirobhāva dharmakam dharma antara samudaye
keṣām saṃsthānam iti ā mā ha śabdaḥ ādīnām avināśinām
evam liṅgam mahat ākhyam ādimat kāraṇavat dharma mātram vināśi guṇānām avināśinām ātma bhūtam
tasmin mahat ādi dharma mātre vikāra saṃjñā na guṇānām vimarda vicitra tayā vināśi tvam guṇa asvarūpeṇa nitya tvam iti
tatra āharaṇam mṛta dharmī piṇḍa ākārā piṇḍa ākārāt ākāra antaram ghaṭam upasampadyamānaḥ dharmataḥ pariṇamate
ghaṭa ākāraḥ na agatam lakṣaṇam hitvā vartamāna lakṣaṇam pratipadyate iti lakṣaṇataḥ pariṇamate
tathā ghaṭaḥ nava purāṇa tām pratikṣaṇam anubhavan avasthā pariṇāmam pratipadyate iti dharmiṇaḥ api mṛd ādeḥ dharma antaram piṇḍa ādikam avasthā
dharmī piṇḍa kapāla ādi rūpa avasthām āsīt iti
tatas ekaḥ eva pariṇāmaḥ bhedena upadarśitaḥ iti
evam api mṛdaḥ anyeṣu api śarīra indriya ādiṣu yojyam
te ete dharma lakṣaṇa avasthā pariṇāmāḥ dharmi svarūpam an atikrāntāḥ iti ekaḥ eva dharmiṇaḥ pariṇāmaḥ sarvān dharma lakṣaṇa avasthā pariṇāmān viśeṣān abhimpavate
kutas yena avasthitasya dravyasya pūrva dharma nivṛttau dharma antara utpattiḥ pariṇām iti dharmī pariṇām eva iti śakyam pratipattum
kaḥ punar asau dharmī yasmin avasthite dharma antara virāme dharma antara udayaḥ pariṇāmaḥ iti
tatra śānta udita avyapadeśya dharma anupātī dharmī
śānta uditān a vyapadeśyān ca dharmān anupatitum śīlam yasya saḥ nvayī bhinneṣu abhinna ātmā dharmī iti vyapadiśyate
dharmaḥ nāma yogyatā avacchinnā śaknoti raśaṇā kuṇḍala ādi bhāvam āpattum iti yā suvarṇasya dharmiṇaḥ kuḍala tva ādikā śāktiḥ saḥ eva dharmaḥ
sa ca avyaktaḥ api san dharmiṇi phala prasava bheda anumita sadbhāvaḥ
yathā deśa antare kāla antare ca tāḍaṅka ādikām phalam kanka piṇḍaḥ prasūyate
tad phala prasava bheda darśānena anya ananyān api prakāra anyam prasavitum vibhavati iti tasmin dharmiṇi phala prasava bheda anumita sadbhāvaḥ
ekasya dharmiṇaḥ anyaḥ ca anyaḥ ca dharmaḥ iti anena ekasya dharmiṇaḥ dharma asāṃkhya tvam āha
tatra yaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ sa vartamānaḥ svam vyāpāram udaka āharaṇa ādikam anubhavan dharma antarebhyaḥ śāntebhyaḥ ca a vyapadeśyebhyaḥ ca bhidyate
yadā tu sāmānyena dharmi rūpeṇa samanvāgataḥ bhavati atha tadā dharmi sva rūpa mātra tvāt dharmi sva rūpa ātma bhūta tvāt saḥ viśeṣataḥ kena vā bhidyate
vyāpāra adhirūḍha rūpāṇām eva bhedaḥ na kāraṇa samuanugama nirīkṣita ātmanām iti arthaḥ
ke punar śāntāḥ uditāḥ a vyapadeśyāḥ vā te khalu dharmiṇaḥ dharmāḥ śāntāḥ ye kṛtvā vyāpāram paratāḥ
sa vyāpārāḥ uditāḥ ṭe ca anāgata lakṣaṇasya samanantarāḥ
tathā vartamānasya anantarāḥ atītāḥ
kimartham atītasya anantarāḥ na bhavanti
sa santi iti arthaḥ pūrva paści bhā bhāvāt
yaḥ yasya paścāt bhavati sa tasya paścimaḥ nantaraḥ
itaraḥ ca tad apekṣayā pūrvaḥ
tat iha paścibhā bhāvāt eṣa svayam api pūrvaḥ na bhavati iti pūrva paścibhā bhāvāt atītasya anantarāḥ na santi
yathā anāgata vartamānayoḥ pūrva paścima tā na evam atītasya
tasmāt na tasya asti samanantaraḥ
yaḥ tu ayam pāṭhaḥ tad anāgate eva samanantarībhavati vartamānasya iti na tasya prakṛtena sambandhaḥ
tasmāt tad anāgataḥ eva samanantaraḥ bhavati atītasya iti ayam eva pāṭhaḥ
artha upapatteḥ
katham yadā vyutthāna saṃskāraḥ nirodha saṃskāreṇa ādyaḥ abhibhūyate tadā vartamānam adhvanam hitvā vyutthāna saṃskāraḥ utītam adhvānam upasampadya punar anāgataḥ san vartamānībhavati iti asamanantaraḥ api anāgataḥ eva samanantarībhavati atītasya iti ucyate
atīta anāgatayoḥ lakṣaṇayoḥ dharmāṇām dharmi svarūpa mātrā viśeṣāt
atha avyapadeśyāḥ ke tad avyapadeśya abhipradarśana artham āha sarvam sarva ātmakam iti
katham tatra uktam jala bhūmyoḥ pāriṇāmikam rasa ādi vaiśvarūpyam sthāvareṣu dṛṣṭam
yathā rasaḥ ekaḥ eva ikṣu śṛṅka geraka ādiṣu madhura kaṭuka tva ādi vaiśvarūpyam pratipadyate
tathā rūpasya śukla kṛṣṇa tva ādi vicitra rūpa tvam
evam gandha ādiṣu api
tathā sthāvarāṇām jaṅgameṣu rasa ādi vaiśvarūpyam
sthāvarāṇām upayuktāṇām jaṅgameṣu rasa lohita ādi viśva bhedaḥ
tathā jaṅgamānām sthāvareṣu upayuktānām vṛkṣa āyurveda prasiddham rasa ādi vaiśvarūpyam
evam sthāvarāṇām sthāvareṣu jaṅgamānām jaṅgameṣu iti evam jāti anucchedena sattva ādi avināśena sarvam sarva ātmakam
aṅguli śikhare loka trayam api asti
tathā ca aṅguṣṭhāt asṛjat brahmā romakūpebhyaḥ iti ādi śruti smṛti śata prasthānam
yadi sarvam sarva ātmakam tadā sarvam sarvatra upalabhyeta sammati viprayoga janmā ca śokaḥ mā pra ti vartiṣṭa ityādeḥ uttaram pathati deśa kāla ākāra nimitta apabandhāt deśa ādīnām apabandhaḥ avabandhaḥ tasmāt na samāna kālaṃ ātmanām sarva vastūnām abhivyaktiḥ
kasya cit kvacid eva deśe kāle ca kena cit eva ākāreṇa tanubhṛtām ca dharma ādi nimitta abhisamīkṣayā kvacid evā abhivyaktiḥ yathā rāhu prabhṛtīnām
etena eva sammati viprayoga nimitta śoka ādi upapattiḥ
atas ekaikasmin atilaṅghita saṃkhyā gocara tvāt dharmāḥ na śakyāḥ vyapadeṣṭum
ya teṣu śānta udita avyapadeśyeṣu abhivyakta anabhibyakteṣu dharmesu anupātī sāmānya viśeṣa ātmā sattva ādi śabda ādi rūpeṇa saḥ nvayī dharmī
yasya tu vadinaḥ dharma mātram eva idam niranvayam bāhyam ādhyātmikam ca yasya ca jñāna mātram eva tasya dharmāṇām kṣaṇa praṇāśi tvāt samāna kālānām ca bhoktṛ bhogya tva ādi saṃbandha anupapatteḥ bhoga abhāvaḥ
sambandha abhāvam darśayati kasmāt anyena kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ anyat vijñānam akartṛ bhaviṣyat katham bhoktṛ tvena adhikriyeta
kartuḥ ca phala abhipravṛtteḥ phalena saṃbandhaḥ yujyate
anyaḥ kartā phalena ca anyaḥ sambadhyate iti virudhyate
smṛti abhāvaḥ ca
kṛta karaṇīya ādi viṣaya smṛti abhāvaḥ ca
anya dṛṣṭasya smaraṇam anyasya na asti iti
na hi caitra dṛṣṭasya vasumitraḥ smarati
vastu pratyabhijñānāt ca yasmāt tat eva idam iti vastu pratyabhijānīmaḥ tasmāt sthitaḥ nvayī dharmī dharma anyathātvam dharmaiḥ anyathātvam abhyupagataḥ pratipannaḥ
na tu svarūpeṇa anyathātvam
yathā rucaka ādi bheda anugatam api kanakam eva iti pratyabhijānīmaḥ
tasmāt na idam dharma mātram niranvayam iti
idānīm pariṇāma bhede hetuḥ ucyate siddhe hi bhede pariṇāma traya saṃyamaḥ prayoktuḥ upakalpeta
yatas kayācid liṅga dvārā atīta ādiṣu matiḥ upajanayitum śakyate na anyathā iti krama anya tvam pariṇāma anya tve hetuḥ
ekasya dharmiṇaḥ citta ādeḥ ekaḥ eva pariṇāmaḥ iti prasakteḥ dharma ādīnām dharmta bhedāt iti pariṇāma bheda siddhaye hetuḥ eṣaḥ ucyate krama anya tvam
kramaḥ anatarabhāvaḥ tasya anya tvam bhedaḥ
trayaḥ hi kramāḥ anyonya vidharmāṇaḥ upalakṣyante lakṣaṇa avasthā kramābhyām anyaḥ dharma kramaḥ

dharma lakṣaṇa kramābhyām anyaḥ vasthā kramaḥ
yat ca teṣām anya tvam prasiddha mārgam adhirūḍham tat krama kāryāṇām pariṇāmānām anumāpakam anya tve hetuḥ
tat yathā mṛd dharmī cūrṇa mṛd iti cūrṇa ādibhiḥ dharmaiḥ ayugapad kāla janmabhiḥ krama vartibhiḥ paiṇamate
sarvatra mṛd grahaṇeṇa dharmiṇaḥ mṛd ākhyasya paraspara lakṣyamāṇa bheda cūrṇa piṇḍa ghaṭa kapāla kaṇa ādi dharma anugamam pratipādayati
cūrṇasya anantaraḥ piṇḍaḥ piṇḍasya anantaraḥ ghaṭaḥ ghaṭasya anantarāṇi kapālāni kapālānām kaṇāḥ anantarāḥ iti dharmaḥ eva cūrṇa mṛd piṇḍa mṛd ghaṭa mṛd kapāla bṛt kaṇa mṛd iti kramaḥ dharma antarasya kramaḥ
na lakṣaṇam na api avasthā
yathā yaḥ yasya dharmasya samanantaraḥ dharmaḥ sa tasya kramaḥ
katham piṇḍaḥ ghaṭaḥ upajāyate iti piṇḍa rūpā mṛd ghaṭībhavati iti arthaḥ
piṇḍaḥ ghaṭaḥ upajāyate iti ucyate
na punar piṇḍaḥ dharmaḥ dharma antarātma tām pratipadyate
piṇḍa dharma vimardanena tad virodhī tad anantaram ghaṭa ākhyaḥ dharmaḥ upajāyate
dharma pariṇāmaḥ ca dvividhaḥ tulya pariṇāmaḥ ca atulya pariṇāmaḥ ca
yathā piṇḍaḥ ghaṭaḥ upajāyate iti atulya piṇḍasya ghaṭa ādhi dharmaiḥ mṛd ākhyaḥ dharmī pariṇamate saḥ atulya dharma pariṇāmaḥ
yāvat ca ghaṭasya janmanaḥ prabhṛti ā kapāla āpatteḥ tāvat ghaṭa rūpeṇa eva pariṇamate mṛd iti sa tulya dharma pariṇāmaḥ
idānīm lakṣaṇa pariṇāma kramaḥ ucyate lakṣaṇa pariṇāma kramaḥ ghaṭasya anāgatāt lakṣaṇāt vartamāna bhāvaḥ
tathā piṇḍasya virodhi dharma udaye vartamānāt atīta bhāvaḥ kramaḥ
na atītasya asti kramaḥ
dharme hi vartamāna lakṣaṇasya samanantaram yat lakṣaṇam sa lakṣaṇa kramaḥ
na ca atīta lakṣaṇasya samanantaram lakṣaṇam asti
kasmāt pūrva apara tāyām hi satyām samanantara tvam
sā ca atītasya na asti
tasmāt dvayoḥ eva anāgata vartamānayoḥ lakṣaṇayoḥ kramaḥ
atītasya krama abhāva pratipādane prayojanam kṣaṇa tad kramayoḥ saṃyamāt iti atra bhaviṣyati
tathā avasthā pariṇāma kramaḥ ghaṭasya abhinavasya prānte avasāna avasthāyām purāṇātā dṛśyate
sā ca kṣaṇa paramparā nupātinā krameṇa abhyūhyamānā pratikṣaṇam abhinava bhāva parimardanena purāṇa tā sañjaniṣyate
sā ca prānteṣu parām vyaktim āpāditā
madhye tu sūkṣma tayā na vibhāvyate
tena madhya avasthāyām san api kramaḥ na lakṣyate
prānta kāla abhivyakti liṅgena anumāyiṣyate yena iyam purāṇa tā parām vyaktim upaprāpitā saḥ yam kramaḥ iti
na hi ghaṭe pariniṣpann mātre prati kṣanā janmā api purāṇa tā gṛhyate
tathā ca vadiṣyati kṣaṇa pratiyāgī pariṇāma apara anta nirgrāhyaḥ kramaḥ iti
tasmāt dharma lakṣaṇa kramābhyām avasthā kramasya anya tvāt dharma lakṣaṇa pariṇāmābhyām viśiṣṭaḥ yam tṛtīyaḥ pariṇāmaḥ
te ete kramāḥ dharma dharmi bhede sati pratilabdha svarūpāḥ
vivakṣite tu dharma dharmiṇoḥ abhede tatra krama bhedaḥ na labhyate
dharmaḥ api dharmī bhavati anya dharma apekṣayā
guṇabhyaḥ nyatra dharma dharmi tvam nāma na vyavasthitam
mahat ādīnām api aviśeṣa apekṣayā dharmi tvam
aviśeṣāṇām ca viśeṣa apekṣayā viśeṣāṇām ca śānta udita apekṣayā iti
yadā tu paramārthataḥ dharmiṇī abheda upacāra dvāreṇa abhidhīyate dharmaḥ tadā yam eka tvena eva kramaḥ pratyavabhāsate
tatra cittasya dvaye dvīdhāḥ dharmāḥ paridṛṣṭāḥ ca a pariḍṛṣṭāḥ ca upalabdhāḥ ca anupalabdhāḥ ca
ke te iti āha tatra pratyaya ātmakāḥ rāga dveṣa moha ādayaḥ paridṛṣṭāḥ
vastu mātrāḥ sva rūpeṇa vidyamānāḥ kārya yoginaḥ aparidṛṣṭāḥ
te ca sva viṣaya vṛtti sadbhāvaiḥ saptā eva bhavanti
te katham avagamyante iti anumānena prāpita vastu mātra sadbhāvāḥ kārya aliṅgena avagata sadbhāvāḥ
sva rūpeṇa tu na anīśvaraiḥ upalabhyante
tatas ca eka eka tvena ucyante
nirodha dharma saṃskārāḥ
nirodhaḥ uktaḥ dharmaḥ iti dharma adharmau
saṃskārāḥ vāsanā rūpāḥ
pariṇāmaḥ ukta lakṣaṇaḥ
atha jīvanam iti dharma ādi apekṣayā sakala karaṇa vṛttiḥ prāṇa lakṣaṇā yena citta dharmeṇa bhavati sa jīvanam iti ucyate sā iṣṭā vyāpāraḥ śaktiḥ sāmarthyam cittasya dharmāḥ
darśana varjitāḥ apratyakṣāḥ
iti ete sapta nirodha ādayaḥ citta dharmāḥ aparidṛṣṭāḥ ucyante
ete trayaḥ pariṇāmāḥ dharma lakṣaṇa avasthā rūpāḥ yoginaḥ upātta sarva sādhanasya yama ādi sakala sādhanasya sthiratara saṃyamasya atīta anāgata pratupa sthita bubhutsita artha pratipattaye saṃyamasya viṣayaḥ upakṣipyate
trayaḥ api ekaḥ viṣayaḥ saṃyamasya

pariṇāma traye tāvat saṃyamaḥ karaṇīyaḥ yāvat samādhi prajñā lokaḥ
sa ca yad viṣaye upasthitaḥ tam viṣayam yathābhūtam pratyakṣa tām āpādayati
sūkṣmam vyavahitam atītam anāgatam viprakṛṣṭam vā yam uddiśya prāpaṇa abhiprāyeṇa sūkṣma ādiṣu saṃyamaḥ kriyate tadā saḥ rthaḥ vaśyatām yoginaḥ upayāti
bhavati
dhāraṇā dhyāna samādhi trayam ekatra saṃyamaḥ uktaḥ
tena saṃyamena pariṇāma trayam sākṣātikriyamāṇam atīta anāgata jñānam teṣu pariṇāmeṣu sampādayati
sakala padārthānām pariṇāmi tvāt teṣām ca atīta ādi yogāt kāla traya yukta samasta padārtha viṣaya pariṇāma traya saṃyamena sarvam pratyakṣībhavati
tathā pratikṣaṇa pariṇāma dharmakam anavasthitam viśvam īkṣamāṇasya vairāgyam jāyati
ayam anyaḥ saṃyama viṣayaḥ upakṣipyate sarva śabda artha pratipatti arthaḥ śabda artha pratyayānām itaretara adhyāsāt saṃkaraḥ tat pravibhāga saṃyamāt sarva bhūta ruta jñānam sampadyate
tatra kaḥ śabdaḥ kaḥ vā arthaḥ pratyayaḥ vā saṃkaraḥ ca kinnīmittaḥ katham ca teṣām pravibhāgaḥ iti
tatra kim vāc uccāryaḥ śrotra grāhyaḥ sa śabdaḥ uta arthāmtaram kim vāc eva tad vyatiriktaḥ vā iti tācat vicāryate vāc tāvat na śabdaḥ
kasmāt vāc varṇeṣu eva arthavatī
vā iti varṇa abhivyañjakam aṣṭasu sthāneṣu viṣaktam indriyam varṇa abhivyakti mātra prayojana upakṣayam na tāvat arrha abhibyaktau śabda abhivyaktau vā vyāpāram karoti
tathā śrotram ca na svayam śabdaḥ na api śabda viṣayam
kasmāt dhvani pariṇāma mātra viṣayam hi tat
dhvaniḥ iti sāmānyam varṇa avarṇa rūpam
tasya viśeṣaḥ pariṇāmaḥ akāra ādi varṇa ātmakaḥ kāka ādi vāśitā ātmakaḥ ca mūḍha karaṇa vyaṅgyaḥ
tat dhvani pariṇāma mātra prakāśa avasānam śrotram na artha śabdayoḥ vyāpriyate
nanu ca śrotra grāhyaḥ eva śabdaḥ
na artha pratyāyaka tvāt
artham yaḥ sampratyāyayati sa śabdaḥ
kaḥ punar asau padam
tat punar nāda anusaṃhāra buddhi nirgrāhyam nādānām dhbanīnām śrotra viṣaya bhūtānām pratyekam pratyayini saṃskāram ādhāya nirvartamānānām antyena dhvaninā yā samupasthāpitā buddhiḥ sā nāda anusaṃhāra buddhiḥ prathama dhvani krama anusaṃhāra āsādita saṃskārasya pratyayinaḥ cittasya jāyate tayā ekayā buddhyā ayam nirgṛhyate
tat padam tat ca pratyakṣa tvāt rūpa ādi vat na anya pramāṇa apekṣam
nanu ca gakāra aukāra visarjanīyāḥ iti bhagavān upavarṣaḥ
tat na avācaka tvāt
katham samudāya asambhavāt
samudāya asambhavaḥ ca eka samaya asambhavi tvāt
na hi gakāra uccāraṇa kāle aukāra visarjanīyau
na api aukāra uccāraṇa kāle gakāra visarjanīyau
nā api visarjanīya pravṛtti velāyām itarayoḥ samavasthānam iti varṇa samudāya asambhvāt avācaka tvam
yathā eva varṇānām yugapad samaya anavasthānam evam saṃskārāṇām smṛtīnām ca tad janitānām ayugapad kāla tvāt avācaka tvam
smṛti upayoga artha tvāt ca saṃskārasya anubhūta viṣaye eva upayogāt pratyāyasya ca apūrva tvāt
api ca saṃskārāṇām vācaka tva abhyupagame śabdāt artha pratipattiḥ pūrvāparībhūtam bhāvam ākhyātena ācaṣṭe dharmasya śabda mūla tvāt an apekṣyam syāt iti prasiddhiḥ apahnūyate
atha api varṇa bhāva bhāvi tvena smṛti saṃskārayoḥ api śabda tvam upacaryeta
na etat api tad bhāva bhāvi tvam nāma tasmin eva sati bhavati asti abhāvaḥ eva yatra tatra syāt
na ca tat ca varṇānām śabda tve siddhe bhavet
tu śrīḥ ādau ātma abhimānāt avivekāt a tasmin api tad buddhim iti na sarvatra vastu nirṇaye hetuḥ bhavati
api ca vāc śrotra vyāpāre eva sati artha pratipattiḥ iti tasya avyabhicārāt tad bhāva bhāvi tve śabda tvam prāpnoti
tasmāt antyaḥ varṇaḥ na vācakaḥ varṇa tvāt ādya varṇa vat
tathā tad smṛti saṃskārāḥ na vācakāḥ smṛti saṃskāra tvāt ādya varṇa smṛti saṃskāra vat
yadi ca antyaḥ varṇaḥ pūrva varṇa janita saṃskāra sahitaḥ vācakaḥ iti ucyate na etat evam
kasmāt antya varṇa uccaraṇa mātrāt eva artha pratyaya prasaṅgāt
katham atīta divasa uccarita gakāra ādi varṇa āhita saṃskāraḥ hi samastaḥ śrotā
tatra antyaḥ vrṇa uccāraṇa mātrāt arthaḥ pratīyeta
atha api niyama artham ādya varṇa uccāraṇam iti ced na pūrva varṇānām paścima barṇena atulya kāla tvāt sāhāyaka abhāve niyama anupapattiḥ
tava api varṇānām pada vyañjaka tve niyama artham pūrva varṇāḥ uccāra etavyāḥ iti doṣaḥ eva iti pada vyañjaka tva kalpanātaḥ varṇānām eva vācaka tvam yuktam iti ced na varṇānām buddhau svakīya saṃskāra ādhāna mātra abhyupagamāt
uccarita pradhvaṃsamāna varṇa saṃskāra paraṃparā upacitāyām hi buddhau padam nirbhāsate
etat eva hi varṇānām pada vyañjaka tvam na padam prati dīpa vat sākṣāt pravartate
na buddhau dharmi dvāreṇa saṃskārānām eka āśraya avasthānāt anyonya upakārya upakāraka bhāvaḥ samīcīnataraḥ
iṣṭa aniṣṭa viṣaya upalabdhi smṛti icchā dveṣa ādi vat
na kadācid antyena varṇena pūrva varṇānām tadīya smṛti saṃsārāṇām vā sambandhaḥ upakalpate
atha mama api a saṃskāra paramparā upacita buddhi utpādaka tvena eva varṇānām vācaka tvam iti ced na abhyupeta parivarjanāt
yadi tāvat varṇa aneka saṃskāra viśiṣṭā buddhiḥ artha viṣayā vā pada viṣayā vā tathā api padārtha pratipattiḥ iti vādhyeta
tasmāt eka buddhi viayaḥ varṇa vyatiriktaḥ śabdaḥ bhyupagantavyaḥ
tena pūrva varṇa janita saṃskāra sahitaḥ ntyaḥ varṇaḥ tad smṛtiḥ saṃskāraḥ vā na vācakaḥ
saṃskāra sāhāyaka apekṣa tvāt buddhi vat
evam gate katham varṇānām artha viṣayaḥ pada viṣayaḥ vā vyāpāraḥ na asti iti āha varṇāḥ eka samaya asambhavi tvāt
eka kāla sambhavi tvam ca vācaḥ krama varti tvāt
atas paraspara niranugraha ātmānaḥ kasyacid abhisambandhasya abhāvāt itaretara nirupakārāḥ
te padam an upasaṃspṛśya an upasthāpya kañcana pade vyāpāram avhidhāya āvis bhūtāḥ ca tirobhūtāḥ ca vyastāḥ vā samastāḥ vā na pada ātmānam apāṅga vikṣepeṇa api parāmṛśanti
pratyekam apada svarūpāḥ yugapad anavasthānāt samudāya ātmanā api apada svarūpāḥ eva
kim aṅga punar pratyekam anarthakānām avasthitānām iti
varṇaḥ punar ekaikaḥ sarva abhidhāna śakti pracitaḥ
abhidhīyate yaiḥ tāni abhidhānāni padāni teṣām sarveṣām abhidhānānām padānām abhivyañjikābhiḥ śaktibhiḥ pracītaḥ arāṇām ekaikaḥ iva nābhau
tat yathā gakāraḥ kovarga agni gagana ādi sarva pada abhidyotana sāmarthya pracitaḥ
sahakāri varṇa antara pratiyogi tvāt
yathā gauḥ iti agniḥ iti īkāra pratiyogī
tasmāt aneka varṇa antara upādhi sambandhāt pratipadam vaiśvarūpyam iva āpannaḥ
uttaraḥ ca varṇaḥ pūrveṇa viśeṣe pada viśeṣa pradyotane avasthāpitaḥ
pūrvaḥ ca uttareṇa madhyamaḥ api pūrva uttarābhyām
evam bahavaḥ varṇāḥ krama anurodhinaḥ viśiṣṭa kramam ānupūrvīm anurudhyamānāḥ
artha saṅketena amī asmin arthe etad krama āvalmbinaḥ iti antaḥ iti saṅketaḥ samayaḥ tena artha saṅketena avacchinnāḥ
varṇa saṅketa dvāreṇa padam saṅketyate
varṇa avyabhicarita cāritram asādhāraṇa varṇa krama apekṣita saṅketa samayam hi padam
varṇa saṅketaḥ eva tasya saṅketaḥ
iyantaḥ ete varṇāḥ sarva abhidhāna śakti paricyutāḥ viśiṣṭa sāsnādimmat artha pratipādaka asādhāraṇa pada avabhāsana vyāpāra para tvāt eva apara pada antara pratipādaka śakti antarebhyaḥ paricyutāḥ nivṛttāḥ itaretara viśeṣa viniyoga para vaśa āveśāt udāsīna pada antara prakāśana śaktayaḥ gakāra aukāra visarjanīyāḥ sāsnādimantam artham avadyotayanti padam abhivyañjayantaḥ
tat eṣām artha saṅketena avacchinānām abhihitena nyāya mārgeṇa hvani kramāṇām viśiṣṭa anuparipāṭi samāyoginām ittham krama viśeṣa krama labdha janmanām varṇānām sambandhaḥ yaḥ ekaḥ buddhi nirbhāsaḥ buddheḥ nirbhāsaḥ tat padam bhūmiḥ bhūmiṣum eva bhūmikā iva vācakam vācyasya na varṇāḥ
varṇa dvāreṇa tu saṅketyate
tat padam ekam ekam api yat vastu sa avayavam ghaṭa ādi tat aneka buddhi viṣayam dṛṣṭam na tu padam tathā
tat eka buddhi viṣayam sarva loka pratyakṣam
varṇāḥ punar aneka tvāt ayugapad kāla janmānaḥ eka buddhi viṣaya tām na samupāśnuvate
yaḥ tu evam ekabuddhi nirgrāhyam anumānena nirācikīrṣati tasya pratyakṣa virodhinī pratijñā syāt
evam eka prayatna ākṣiptam varṇa krama janma pratyupanīta saṃskāra nimitta buddhi paripāka abhisamīkṣayā paścim a buddhau jhaṭiti parisphuritam a vibhāgam avayava śūnyam atas eva a kramam a vrṇa ātmakam antya vara pratyaya vyāpāra upasthāpitam ādya varṇa vyāpāra paramparā anugṛhīta paścima varṇa grahaṇa mātra pratyudbhāsitam
paratra para buddhi pratipipādayiṣayā varṇaiḥ eva abhidhīyamānaiḥ abhidhātṛbhiḥ śrūyamāṇaiḥ ca śrotṛbhiḥ anādi vāc vyavahāra vāsanā anuviruddhyā loka buddhyā siddha vat saṃpratipattyā pratīyate
na api anā adi saṃsāra cakra maṇḍale parivartate
śabdāt eva artha pratipattiḥ pūrvakaḥ vyavahāraḥ tad vāsanā vāsitayā loka dhiyā siddha vat pratīyate iti laukikānām sammugdha ākāra pravartita vyavahāra mātra carita prayojanānām ātmani iva pade vipratipattiḥ
tasmāt padam varṇa vyatiriktam eka buddhi nirgrāhya tve sati pratyāyaka tvāt pradīpa vat
artha pratipattau ca kāraṇa tvāt pradīpa vat buddhi vat ca
na varṇāḥ padam ekena kartā krameṇa prayujyamāna tvāt karaṇa tvāt ca vāsī vṛkṣa ādāna ādi vat
atra kaścid āha
varṇāḥ vā dhvanataḥ vā api sphoṭam na pada vākyayoḥ
vyañjanti vyañjaka tvena yathā dīpa prabhā ādayaḥ
sattvāt ghaṭa ādi vat ca iti sādhanāni yathāruci
laukika vyatirekeṇa kalpitaḥ rthe bhavanti hi
laukika vyavahāreṇa all the mss
na arthasya vācakaḥ sphoṭaḥ varṇebhyaḥ vyatirekataḥ
ghṭa ādi vat na dṛṣṭena virodhaḥ dharmya siddhitaḥ
pratiṣedhāt tu yaḥ varṇān
dṛṣṭa bādhaḥ bhavet tasya śaśi candra niṣedha vat
varṇa utthā vā rtha dhīḥ eṣā tad jñāna anantara udbhavā
yādṛśī sā tad utthā hi dhūpa ādeḥ iva bahni dhīḥ
dīpa vat vā gakāra ādiḥ gavādeḥ pratipādakaḥ
dhuvam pratīyamāna tvāt tat pūrvam pratipādanāt
iti
atrā ucyate varṇāḥ vā dhvanayaḥ vā api sphoṭam na pada vākyayoḥ iti padam vākyam vā svatas tāvat na prasiddham
tatra asati varṇa vyatirikte pade vākye vā pada vākyayoḥ sphoṭam na vyañjayanti iti katham cetasvinām vacana avakāśaḥ syāt
evam ca sati adṛśya pada vākyayoḥ sphoṭam pratiṣedhatā padam vākyam ca abhyupagatam bhavet
atha api para abhiprāyeṇa ucyeta tathā api siddha sādhya tā
na parasya pada vākyayoḥ anyaḥ sphoṭaḥ vidyate yaḥ pratiṣidhyeta
pada vākye eva hi tasya sphoṭaḥ
atha api brūyāt artha avacchedakāḥ viśiṣṭa krama upaniveśinaḥ varṇāḥ padam vākyam ca pratiṣidhyate iti
tat ca na yuktam svatas virodhāt
atha api brūyāt varṇa vyatiriktam padam vākyam vā pratiṣidhyate iti
tathā api vyatiriktam uddiśya tasya vyañjana pratiṣedhāt vyatirikta pada vākya abhyupagamaḥ prasaktaḥ
athā api para kalpita pada vākya pratiṣedhaḥ evam api vyañjaka tvāt iti asiddhaḥ hetuḥ
katham sva ātma vyatiriktasya vā padasya vyañjaka tvam a vyatiriktasya vā vyañjaka tvam arthasya vā vyañjaka tvam varṇānām iti trayī vikalpanā
yadi vyatiriktasya vyañjaka tvam tadā svatas siddhaḥ syāt
atha avyatiriktasya tathā api parasya asiddhaḥ
kim ca vyañjaka tvāt ca vyatiriktasya eva vyañjaka tvam na avyatiriktasya pradīpa ādeḥ iva
anya vyañjana artham hi vyañjakaḥ pradīpa ādiḥ upādīyate na sva ātma vyañjanāya
sva ātma vyakti artham ced upādāsyate januṣā ndhasya api vyajyeta
atha vyatirikta vyañjaka tve siddhe pādasya vyañjakāḥ bhaveyuḥ arthasya vā
tatra aneka sādhyam yathā śibikā udvahana ādi tat anyatamena na śakyam anuṣṭhātum evam anyatamena varṇānām arthasya pratipādanam aneka sādhya tvāt aśakyam iti pratipāditam
na ca kūpa khānaka nyāyena api kiṃcid kiṃcid vyaṅgye ādhāya varṇāḥ nirvartante iti śakyam vaktum
abhidheyasya eka buddhi viṣaya tvāt
yathā ca sugata kṛtānte pradhvaṃsamānam vijñānam utpatsyamānasya vijñānasya saṃskāram ādhātum a paryāptam dharmiṇaḥ kasyacid abhāvāt
evam nyonya saṃbandha abhāvāt ayugapad samaya janmanām varṇānām pūrvasya pūrvasya vinaśyataḥ uttarasya uttarasya ca upajaniṣyamāṇasya bala ādhāna anupapattiḥ iti na arthasya vyañjakāḥ varṇāḥ
pariśeṣāt padasya eva vyatiriktasya abhivyañjitāraḥ iti sthita dharmaḥ
asmākam tu sthite dharmiṇi cetasi pūrva pūrva varṇa pratyupasthita saṃskāra paramparā paripāka viśārade paścima varṇa janma velāyām niravayavam eka buddhi nirgrāhya buddhi nirbhāsa ātmakam jhatiti samunmiṣati iti na saṃskāra ādhāna asāmarthya doṣa prasaṅgaḥ
kim ca yadi api varṇāḥ sva buddhim vyañjayanti
sā buddhiḥ artha pratītim prati karaṇa bhūtā eva abhivyajyate na tu phalam prati varṇāḥ karaṇa tvena vyāpriyante
akaraṇ bhūta buddhi utpādana upakṣaya tvāt
buddhiḥ eva hi phalam prati vyāpāraḥ
yasya hi phalam prati vyāpāraḥ tat pramāṇam sa śabdaḥ
tatas ca artha pratītim prati kāraṇa bhūta buddhi vyavahita tvāt na varṇānām vācaka tvam
parasparayā tu padam pratypāya tvam na varṇānām pratiṣidhyate
tasmāt evam ayam aślokaḥ paṭhitavyaḥ varṇāḥ vā dhvanayaḥ vā api bhinnam eva artham ātmanaḥ
vyañjanti vyañjaka tvena yathā dīpa prabhā ādayaḥ
tathā ghaṭa ādīnām api artha antara pratyupasthāna mātra tvam abhyupagamyate eva
ghaṭa ādayaḥ hi darśana mātreṇa pacana āharaṇa dhāraṇa ādi yogyatā buddhim anyat vā kiṃcid upasthāpayanti eva
tathā varṇānām pāramparyeṇa ātma byatirikta pada pratypasthāpaka tvam sattvāt ghaṭa ādi vat iṣyate eva iti tulyam etat api
sattvāt ghaṭa ādi vat ca iti sādhanāni yathā ruci
laukika vyatirekeṇa kalpite rthe bhavanti hi
laukika vyavahāreṇa all the mss
sarvathā jātiḥ vā buddhiḥ vā bhavatu yatas vā kutaścid uccārita pradhvastu arṇa anasaṃbhavinaḥ varṇa vyatiriktāt artha pratipattiḥ sa sphoṭaḥ
sa ca avaśyam varṇa asaṃbhavi tvāt kāryasya abhyupagamanīyaḥ
tathā ca naṛthasya vācakaḥ sphoṭaḥ varṇebhyaḥ vyatirekataḥ iti bruvataḥ bhyupagama virodhaḥ syāt
api ca varṇebhyaḥ vyatirekataḥ iti anyatara asiddhaḥ
svatas vyatirekasya asiddha tvāt
kim ca nāma ākhya tā upasarga nipāta pada jāti catuṣṭayam abhyupagaddha tā jāti vyañjakam varṇa vyatiriktam anyat abhyupagantavyam
na varṇāḥ pada jātim abhivyañjitum utsahante
varṇāḥ hi varṇa jātim abhivyañjayanti
