na ca avayaveṣu bhinna kāla janma vināśeṣu avayavi jāti vyañjanam upapadyate
vyavasthiteṣu api nāma tāvat avayaveṣu na pāṇi pāda ādayaḥ śarīrāt ṛte śarīra tvam abhivyañjayanti
kim punar avasthiteṣu
kim ca aśvaḥ ayātam ayātam akṣaḥ bhavati tena mama vāyuḥ vāyuḥ ityādiṣu tulya svarūpeṣu nāma tva ākhyāta tve paraspara viruddha jātīye na ekaḥ eva varṇaḥ bhivyanakti
yadi vā aśvaḥ iti nāma jātyāḥ abhivyañjakāḥ akāra śakāra vakāra ākāra visarjanīyāḥ ākhyāta jāti abhivyañjakebhyaḥ bhinnāḥ bhaveyuḥ tadā upapadyate bhinnānām bhinna jāti abhivyañjaka tvam
tat ekatve na upapadyate
yadi api artha prakaraṇa śabda antara sannidhāna ādibhiḥ idam nāma idam ākhyātam iti parikalpyeta tathā api nāma ākhyāta jāti abhivyaktim artha prakaraṇa ādibhiḥ ekaḥ eva parikalpyeta tathā api nāma ākhyāta jāti abhivyaktim artha prakaraṇa ādibhiḥ ekaḥ eva parikalpyeta tathā api nāma ākhyāta jāti abhivyaktim artha prakaraṇa ādibhiḥ varṇaḥ na śaknoti kartum
na hi vrāhmaṇaḥ eva brāhmaṇa tvam kṣatriya tvam ca bhivyanakti
tasmāt bhinnāḥ akārāḥ śakārāḥ vakāra ādayaḥ ca bahavaḥ eṣitavyāḥ
evam go śabda ādayaḥ api bhinnāḥ eva
tathā go śabda tvam aśva śabda tvam ca siddham
evam ma tvam ā tvam am i tvam ca siddham
evam ca sati akāra ādayaḥ varṇāḥ a tva ādīni eva sāmānyāni abhivyañjayanti
na aśva ādīn nāma ākhyāta jāti bhedān iti
tasmāt varṇa vyatiriktam pada tva sāmānya abhivyañjakam padam abhyupagantavyam
evam ca sati eṣa ślokaḥ evam paṭhitavyaḥ pratiṣedhet tu yaḥ sphoṭam varṇa dhī samanantaram
bhavet tasya śaśi candra niṣedha vat
varṇa utthā varṇa dhīḥ eṣā tad jñāna anantara udbhavā
iti
karaṇa buddhi vyavahita tvāt anantara udbhava tvam asiddham
pāramparyeṇa ced siddha sādhya tā
dhūmasya api na vahni dhiyam prati kāraṇa tvam
dhūma dhiyaḥ kāraṇa tvāt
dhūma ādīnām pāramparya vat varṇa ādīnām api pāramparyeṇa upakāraka tvam iṣyate iti uktam
tasmāt ayam api ślokaḥ evam paṭhitavyaḥ varṇa utthā nā artha dhīḥ eṣā tad jñāna anantara udbhavā
yedṛśī sā tad utthā na dhūma ūtar iva vahni dhīḥ
na ca dīpa vat sannipatya gakāra aukārau sāsnādimat artha vyañjakau artha vyakti kāla anavasthānāt anayoḥ dṛṣṭaḥ vyabhicāraḥ visarjanīya viṣaye api samunnīyate niravasthāna ādi
varṇāḥ na artha vyakti samāna kāla avasthāyinaḥ pradīpaḥ tu vyaṅgya kālena tulya kāla avasthānaḥ kāraṇa tvam pratilabhate
tasmāt ayam api evam ślokaḥ paṭhitavyaḥ dīpa vat vā gakāra ādiḥ go ādīnām avācakaḥ
dhruvam pratīyamāna tvāt tat pūrvam pratipādanāt
pramāṇam ca atra bhavati arthasya na vācakāḥ na api artham prati pramāṇam varṇāḥ sākṣāt saṅketa apekṣa tvāt aṅka pratimā ādi vat
yathā śata ādi aṅkāḥ viṣṇu pratimāḥ ca saṅketa apekṣāḥ āgamam eva avadyotayanti
na viṣṇu śata ādi artham prati pramāṇam upayānti
yat tu na apekṣate saṅketam tat pramāṇam yathā vākyam ca
na tathā varṇāḥ iti pratimā vat eṣām a prāmāṇyam āpatitam
tathā varṇāḥ artha pratipādakam ātma vyatiriktam abhivyañjayanti sākṣāt saṅketa apekṣa tvāt aṅka viṣṇu pratimā ādi vat sphoṭaḥ tad saṅketam na sākṣāt apekṣate iti avādiṣma
tasmāt eva aneka yukti parivāra pratyupānīta bala ādhānam kaḥ sphoṭam apākartum śaknoti
tat evam gate bhāṣyam idānīm ucyate tasya padasya saṅketa buddhitaḥ pravibhāgaḥ
śabda artha jñāna vyatibhinna rūpā hi saṅketa buddhiḥ
tasyāḥ sakāśāt padasya pravibhāgaḥ karaṇīyaḥ
saṅketa rūpam darśayati etāvatām varṇānām evaṃjātīyakaḥ nu saṃhāraḥ etasya arthasya vācakaḥ iti
yathā ayam aṅkaḥ śatam sahasram viṣṇuḥ eṣā pratimā iti ca
saṃketaḥ tu pada padārthayoḥ itaretara adhyāsa rūpāḥ smṛtyā ātmā na mramāṇa bhūtaḥ
yathā viṣṇuḥ eṣā pratimā eṣaḥ eva caturbhujaḥ iti tathā pratyayaḥ ubhayam idam ubhayam nu pratyayaḥ iti anyonya adhyasta rūpāḥ viṣṇu pratimā pratyayāḥ
tathā yaḥ yam śabdaḥ saḥ yam arthaḥ yaḥ yam arthaḥ sa śabdaḥ yaḥ ca pratyayaḥ saḥ rthaḥ śabdaḥ ca iti evam itaretara adhyāsa rūpaḥ saṃketaḥ bhavati
evam ete śabda artha pratyayāḥ itaretara adhyāsāt saṃkīrṇāḥ
tat yathā gauḥ iti śabdaḥ gauḥ iti arthāḥ gauḥ iti jñānam iti
yaḥ eṣām śabda artha pratyayānām pravibhāga jñaḥ sa sarvajñaḥ
kasmāt aśakya tvāt pravibhāga jñānasya
na hi a sarvajñāḥ śaknoti pravibhāgena tān avagantum
sarva padeṣu ca asti vākya śaktiḥ
vṛkṣaḥ iti ukte asti iti gamyate
na sattām padārthaḥ vyabhicarati iti
kim artham etat ucyate iha sarva bhūta ruta jñāna upāyaḥ pratipipādayiṣitaḥ
sarva bhūta rutam ca vākya artha viṣayam eva na padārtha viṣayam
padānām kevalānām varṇānām iva anarthaka tvāt saṃvyavahāra abhāvāt ca
yathā eva varṇānām varṇa antara abhisamīkṣayā pada avadyotana prayojanavat tvam evam padānām api pada antara apekṣayā vākya upasthāpana upāya tvam
evam sati vākyasya eva prāmāṇyam kevala pada prayoge artha apratīteḥ
kim ca kevalam padam apramāṇam tāvatā nirṇaya abhāvāt ekaika varṇa vat
nā api padam vācakam saṅketa artha apekṣa tvāt śata ādi aṅka vat
nāma ākhyāte kevale na vācake kevala a prayogāt upasarga vat
yatra api kevalam padam prayuyukṣitam tatra api avaśyam asti tiṣṭhati devadattaḥ ityādi padam buddhau viparivartate iti na kevala a prayoga siddhiḥ
v
devadatta
pralambate paryāgacchati abhyagacchati ityādiṣu upasarga karma pravacanīyānām na kaścid arthaḥ
tathā abhimānāyate sumanāyate durmanāyate ityādiṣu ca upasargāṇām dyotaka tvam siddham
tathā pratiṣṭhate adhīte ityādiṣu api upasargāṇām dyotaka tvam eva na vācaka tvam iti
tathā na hi asādhanā kriyā asti
kevala karma prayoge kim api sādhanam dravyam guṇaḥ vā avagamyate
kim ca prakṛti pratyayānām anavasthitau adhika tvāt vyabhicārāt avācaka tvam
tat yathā daridrātiḥ keṣāñcid dravya mātraḥ eva paṭhyate
daridra śabdaḥ tu nipāta upasarga sthānīyaḥ punar āgacchati drāti nidrāti daridrāti iti
tatra kā prakṛtiḥ iti vaktavyam
kim drākitvam drā iti kim vā daridra iti
keṣāñcid tu daridrā iti etāvat paṭhyate tathā drā śabdaḥ api pṛthak āmnāyate
evam asti sakāra mātram paṭhanti
vi iti ca pratyaye kāram āgamam kurvanti
kecid tu saha kāreṇa paṭhitvā au iti vi iti ca pratyaye lopam kārasya kurvanti
tatra kā prakṛtiḥ iti vaktavyam
na nirjñāyate
prakṛti avadhau pratyaya avadhau vā prakṛti pratyaya artho śakyau vivektum
kvacid upasargaḥ
api asaṃgrāmayata śūraḥ ityādiṣu prakṛti eka deśa tām āpannaḥ
tathā ātateḥ na asya apatyamiḥ iyān adhunā ityādau kaḥ prakṛti artha bhāgam asatyām prakṛtau brūyāt
agni cit sopasut bhidā chidā atho kati amā paca paṭha ityādiṣu pratyaya artham asati pratyaye kaḥ brūyāt
evam ādiṣu lakṣita apacārāṇām prakṛti pratyayanām kaḥ śaknuyāt arthavat tvam kalpayitum
atra bhavatu na anyatra iti na ardhajaratīyam labhyam
uddālaka puṣpa bhañjikā pāram na puṣpa pracāyikāḥ iti atra kaḥ prajñaḥ ityādiṣu pratyanvayaḥ api na asti iti kasya kaḥ rthaḥ iti
ṛṣabhaḥ vṛṣabhaḥ vṛṣaḥ udakam udakubhaḥ kṣīrodaḥ yāvaḥ yāvakaḥ kūpaḥ sūpaḥ yūpaḥ ityādiṣu kasya kaḥ rthaḥ iti vaktavyam
dadhi aśāna madhu atra ityādiṣu kim avadhi kim padam vācakam
tasmāt sarvatra dṛṣṭa apacārāṇām varṇa prakṛti pratyaya padānām anarthakānām adṛṣṭa apacāra niravayava vākya upāya tvam eva
tāni niḥsandhi bandhanāt niravayavāt mithyā bhūta varṇa pada dhvani kṛta citrī bhāvāt vākyāt apoddhṛtya vyākaraṇīyāni
tāni ca vākyasya anavayava bhūtāni upāya tvāt vākya avayava vat avabhāsamānāni yāvat phalam asattvāt śata ādi aṅka vat eva mithyābhūtāni anuccāryamāṇa vākya avadyotana artham karaṇa sannipāte viśeṣeṇa upādāya parihīyamāṇāni svakīya krama niṣpatti vinivṛtti kāla ādi bheda vicitra tayā vākya ātmānam kramavantam iva niṣpadyamānam iva nirvartamānam iva drāghīyāṃsam iva kālavantam iva bhedavantam iva vicitra ākāra tām āpādayanti
evam ca sati yat ucyate śaśa viṣāṇāt apoddhṛtya khara viṣāṇasya kim tat iti etat alīkam yathā eva mṛgatṛṣṇikā toyam alīkam api satyāt ūṣarāt apoddhriyate yathā ca sa thāṇoḥ puruṣaḥ puruṣāt ca sa thāṇuḥ śuktikātaḥ ca rajatam apoddhrtiyate yathā eva ca mṛgatoya ādayaḥ yathābhūta ūṣara ādi vastu pratipatti hetavaḥ tathā varṇa pada prakṛti pratyayāḥ yathā bhūta vākya artha pratipatti kāraṇe tad pratipattau ca apoddhriyante
kvacid artha prāptam apoddhriyate yathā mṛga toya ādikam
kvacid tu prayojana tvena vivakṣitam yathā śata ādi saṅkhyātaḥ śata ādi aṅka apoddhāraḥ kriyate yathā ca lipi akṣarāṇi saṅketa apekṣa tvāt kṛta samaya rūpāṇi akāra ādi varṇāt apoddhriyante
atha ca sarvāṇi etāni yathā bhūta artha pratipādana upāya tvam pratipadyante
na ca tāvatā mithyātvam eṣām na asti
tathā pada ādīni api
ye hi prakṛti pratyaya pada varṇānām saṃketa dvāreṇa anya upāyānām mithyā bhūta lipi akṣara kalpānām svayam api sva saṃketena vākya artha pratipatti upāyam anekadhā nirmāya vyavaharamāṇaḥ satya tvam eṣām manyate nūnam asau abhre candramasam didṛkṣamāṇaḥ candra darśana upāya bhūtam abhram api candra tvena pratipadyate iti
yathā ca vākyam eva satyam tathā vākya arthasya eva satya tvam na padāni padārthāḥ vā kevalāḥ satya tvam upayānti
sarvam eva sāmānya viśeṣa ātmakam vastu
na hi sāmānya vyāvṛttaḥ viśeṣaḥ viśeṣa vyāvṛttam vā sāmānyam asti
gauḥ iti ukte asti iti gamyate
tena kevala pada prayoge api antar nīta pada antara arthaḥ vākya arthaḥ eva pratīyate na kevala padārthaḥ
evam ca sati padārthāḥ gamayanti etam pratyekam saṃśaye sati
sāmastye nirṇaya utpadāt kāka vat
vākya k
iti asiddham asmākam
na hi sthāṇuḥ nāma vākya arthaḥ pṛthak padārtha tvena prasiddhaḥ
yasmāt vṛkṣaḥ san sthāṇuḥ san mūrdhā san kākaḥ san mūrdhani sthāṇoḥ iti antar nīta pratīyamāna pada antara asthān apekṣāyām sthāṇu mūrdha stha kāka buddhiḥ eva na syāt
satsu api teṣu sat buddhi samutpatteḥ sat padārtha antara buddhiḥ avaśyam bhāvinī
tasmāt vākya arthaḥ eva pratyakam api saṃśaya ātmakaḥ iti kutas padārthāḥ pratyekam asantaḥ vākya artham gamayeyuḥ
tasmāt evam ayam ślokaḥ paṭhitavyaḥ vākyam tu gamayati enam pratyekam saṃśaye sati
samastye nirṇaya utpādāt sthāṇu mūrdha stha kāka vat
evam vākyena eva ucyate tasmāt vākya arthaḥ nyaiḥ arūpaṇāt
ante ca asti iti ca vṛkṣeṇa eva ca vṛkṣa tā
yat tu palāśa śabdena vṛkṣatā na ucyate iti satyam evam etat
na hi palāśa vākyena vṛkṣa vākya arthasya abhidhānam
bhinna viṣaya tvāt
anyaḥ hi palāśa vākya arthaḥ palāśaḥ sti tiṣṭhati iti vā
anyaḥ vṛkṣa vākya arthaḥ
yadā ca pāca ṛṇānām niravayavānām pṛthak astitvam abhyupagamyate tadā niravayava varṇa pada upādānam vākyam sa avayavam katham avakalpeta
na hi kriyā ākāśa ādibhiḥ sa avayavam śakyam ārabdhum
atha sāvayava tvam abhyupāyiṣyate tatra api doṣaḥ eva prasajyeta
sadbhāve pada varṇānām bhedaḥ yaḥ paramāṇu vat
sarva abhāvaḥ tatas ca iti sā iyam bāla vibhīṣikā
vākya k
paramāṇunām sattva ādi dharma mātra tva abhyupagamāt vivṛtya suṣṭhu bhāṣāmahe sā iyam vṛddha vibhīṣikā iti
atha kevala pada prayoge padārtha antarasya api saṃgrahāt kim aneka pada prayogeṇa ii ced niyama arthaḥ nuvādaḥ kartṛ karaṇa karmaṇām caitra agni taṇḍulānām sādhanāni vidyante iti artha prāptānām niyamaḥ caitraḥ eva kartā agninā eva karaṇena taṇḍulān eva karma iti
api ca niyama artha mātre ma ntare ṇa anuvādaḥ
dṛṣṭam ca vākya arthe kevalam padam
yathā śrotriyaḥ chandaḥ dhīte iti
sādhana vacanam eva kevana śrotriya padam chandaḥ dhīte iti asmin kriyā sādhana samudāye vartate
tathā jīvati iti kriyā padam ākṣipta kriyā sādhana viśeṣam
cchatram chandaḥ dhīte prāṇān dhārayati iti vākye śritriyaḥ jīvati iti ca padārtha abhivyaktiḥ
sarvathā sarva padeṣu vākya śaktiḥ iti aṅgīkṛta pada antara arthāni eva sarvāṇi padāni iti etat ucyate
tasmāt kvacid kriyāpadena eva sādhanam pakṣiptam
kvacid ca nāma padena eva kriyā abhihitā
tasmāt teṣām vibhāgaḥ duravabodhaḥ iti
tatas vākyāt pravibhajya padam vyākaraṇīyam kriyā vācakam vā jīvati ityādi kāraka vācakam vā śrotriyaḥ kṣatriyaḥ ityādi
anyathā yadi vākyāt pravibhajya na vyākriyeta tadā tatas bhavati aśvaḥ iti evamādiṣu nāma ākhyāta sārūpyāt anirjñātam katham kriyāyām kākake vā bhavati nidhehi iti sarvanāmnaḥ śatṛ antasya vā saptabhyām rūpam
bhavati bījāt aṅkuraḥ iti ākhyātam
aśvaḥ carati iti jāti vācakam
aśvaḥ tvam grāmam iti śvayateḥ luṅ antasya madhyamapuruṣa ekavacana antasya prayogaḥ
ajā payaḥ pīyatām iti nāmapadam
ajā payaḥ tvam rājanam iti japateḥ ṇic antasya laṅ madhyama puruṣīkavacana antasya rūpam
teṣām śabda artha pratyayānām saṅkaram pradarśya vibhāgaḥ pratiādyate prāsādaḥ iti kriyā arthaḥ
śvetaḥ prāsādaḥ iti kārakā arthaḥ
kriyā kāraka tvāt vastunaḥ śvetaḥ iti ca kriyā arthena ca karaka arthena ca abhidhānam
yathā śabdaḥ kriyā kāraka ātmā yaḥ śvetaḥ sa śvetate yaḥ śvetate sa śvetaḥ iti evam kriyā kāraka aṣyatiriktaḥ ekaḥ śabdaḥ tathā arthaḥ tad vācyaḥ kriyā kāraka ātmā
tathā tad viṣayaḥ pratyayaḥ kriyā kāraka ātmā
tathā arthaḥ śabda pratyaya ātmā
pratyayaḥ api śabda artha ātmā
kasmāt saḥ yam iti abhisambandhāt
yaḥ rthaḥ sa śabdaḥ yaḥ śabdaḥ saḥ rthaḥ pratyayaḥ ca yaḥ pratyayaḥ saḥ rthaḥ śabdaḥ ca iti evam abheda ākāra pratyayaḥ smṛti ātmā saṅketaḥ iti
evam saṅkara rūpataḥ pravibhāgaḥ kāryaḥ
katham yaḥ tu śvetaḥ rthaḥ śveta guṇaḥ prāsāda ādiḥ arthaḥ sa śabda pratyayayoḥ ālambanībhūtaḥ vācya tvena viṣaya tvena ca
sa hi svābhiḥ avasthābhiḥ nava purāṇa tva ādibhiḥ vikriyamāṇaḥ na śabda sahagataḥ na api buddhi sahagataḥ
śabda pratyaya abhāve api bhāvāt
evam pratyayaḥ na śabda sahagataḥ na api artha sahagataḥ
itara abhāve api bhāvāt
tathā śabdaḥ api artha pratyaya vyabhivārāt iti evam anyathā arthaḥ anyathā śabdaḥ anyathā pratyayaḥ iti pravibhāgaḥ
evam ca tat pravibhāga saṃyamāt idam varṇaiḥ saṅketitaiḥ vākya ātmakam abhivyajyamānam ayam arthaḥ pratyayaḥ ca ayam iti pravibhāgena saṃyamāt pravibhakta pada padārtha pratyayānām svena rūpeṇa sākṣāt karaṇāt sarva bhūta ruta jñānam sampadyate
saṃskāra sākṣātkaraṇāt pūrva jāti jñānam dvaye khalu amī saṃskārāḥ vāsanā abhidhānāḥ paridṛṣṭāḥ a paridṛṣṭāḥ ca smṛti kleśa hetavaḥ
paridṛṣṭāḥ ubhaye api kleśa karma vipāka anubhava nirvartitāḥ vitta dharmāḥ dharma adharma rūpāḥ dharma adharma nimittāḥ pūrva bhava abhisaṃskṛtāḥ tāḥ atikrānta ananta janma niṣpāditāḥ pariṇāma deṣṭa anirodha śakti jīvana dharmāḥ a paridṛṣṭāḥ
teṣu dvayeṣu saṃskāreṣu saṃyamaḥ kriyamāṇaḥ saṃskāra sākṣātkriyāyai samarthaḥ bhavati
te ca deśa kāla nimitta anubhava viśiṣṭayā nirvartita tvāt sākṣātkaraṇa kāle api deśa ādi viśeṣaṇa viśiṣṭāḥ eva pratyakṣībhavanti
tasmāt na ca te deśa kāla nimitta anubhavaiḥ vinā teṣām asti sākṣātkaraṇam
tat ittham saṃskāra sākṣātkaraṇāt pūrva jāti jñānam utpadyate yoginaḥ
paratra api prāṇiṣu evam eva yeṣām jātim bubhutsate tadīya saṃskāreṣu saṃyamāt saṃskāra sākṣātkaraṇāt tatu pūrva jāti jñānam utpadyate
tatra saṃskāra sākṣātkaraṇa phala vyañjana artham idam ākhyānam upakṣipyate bhagavataḥ jaigīṣavyasya saṃskāra sākṣātkaraṇāt daśasu mahāsargeṣu janma pariṇāmam anupaśyataḥ viveka jam vairāgya nimittam jñānam prādur abhūt
atha bhagavān āvaṭayaḥ tantradharaḥ tam uvāca daśasu mahāsargeṣu bhavya tvāt anabhibhūta buddhisattvena tvayā naraka tiryaggamana duḥkham anupaśyatā devam anuṣyeṣu punar punar utpadyamānena sukha duḥkhayoḥ kim upalabdham adhikam iti
bhagavantam āvaṭyam jaigīṣavyaḥ uvāca daśasu mahāsargeṣu bhavya tvāt anabhibhūta buddhi sattvena mayā naraka tiryaggamanam anupaśyatā devam anuṣyeṣu punar punar utpadyamānena yat kiñcid anubhūtam tat sarvam duḥkham iti duḥkham eva pratyavaimi
bhagavān avaṭyaḥ uvāca yat idam āyuṣmataḥ pradhāna vaśi tvam anuttamam ca san yoṣa sukham kim idam api duḥkha pakṣe nikṣiptam iti
bhagavān jaigīṣavyaḥ uvāca viṣaya sukha apekṣayā eva idam anuttamam santoṣa sukham prdhāna vaśitva sukham ca uktam

buddhisattvasya ayam dharmaḥ triguṇaḥ
triguṇaḥ ca pratyayaḥ heya pakṣe nyastaḥ iti
kim apekṣayā punar etat dvayam sukham bhavati iti āha duḥkha rūpaḥ tṛṣṇā tantuḥ
tṛṣṇā santāna duḥkha upaśama rūpam tu prasannam an ābādham sarva anukūlam sukham idam uktam san yoṣa sukham pradhāna jaya sukham ca

para pratyaye saṃyamāt para pratyayasya sākṣātkaraṇam
tad sākṣātkaraṇe tad saṃbandhinaḥ para cittasya jñānam bhavati
tatra para pratyaya sākṣātkaraṇāt tad duḥkhe duḥkhi tvam tad sukhe skhi tvam ca prāpnoti iti āśaṅkya āha na ca sa ālambanam tasya aviṣayībhūta tvāt
raktam pratyayam jānāti yogī
parasya amuṣmmin ālambane raktaḥ pratyayaḥ iti na jānāti
para pratyayasya yat ālambanam sukha rūpam duḥkha rūpam vā yena sukhī duḥkhī vā bhavet
nanu ca ālambanam a sañjānānaḥ katham amusmin rakte iti sañjānīte iti ucyate raktam amuṣmin iti sāmānyam vijānāti
na punar sukha viśeṣam sukhinaḥ pratyayasya ālambanībhūtam ālambate
para pratyaya mātram tu yogi cittasya ālambanībhūtam
kāya rūpa saṃyamāt tad grāhya śaktiḥ tambhe cakṣuḥ prakāśa a samprayoge antardhānam
yoginaḥ ātmīyasya kāyasya rūpam kāya rūpam
tasmin rūpe saṃyamāt tasya rūpasya yā para cakṣuḥ grāhyā śaktiḥ tām pratibadhnāti niruṇāt hi
tatas pareṣām cakuṣuḥ prakāśaḥ yogi kāya rūpeṇa na samprayujyate
tatas ca āntardhānam
etena śabda ādi antardhānam uktam
yogi śabdasya yā grāhya śaktiḥ tasyām saṃyame sati yā śabdasya grāhya śaktiḥ sā pratiṣṭamyate
tena yogi śandam na paraḥ śṛṇoti
tathā sparśa ādiṣu api draṣṭavyam
nirupakramam ca karma tad saṃyamāt aparāntajñānam ariṣṭebhyaḥ vā
āyuḥ vipākam karma dvividhā
katham tu aritam nimittam ādāya phala padam sa upakramam ucyate
yat tu manda prasaram cireṇa phalam dāsyati tat nirupakramam
yathā ārdram vastram vitānitam vistāritam kṣepīyasā kṣipratareṇa kālena śuṣyet tathā sa upakramam karma kṣipram āyuḥ vipākam kṛtvā kṣīyate
tat eva vastram sampiṇḍitam a vitānitam śuṣyet evam nirupakramam cireṇa āyuḥ karoti
yathā vai agniḥ śuṣke kakṣe yukta vāte anukūla mātariśvani samantataḥ niyuktaḥ kṣepīyasā kālena dahet tathā sa upakramam karma kṣepīyasā kālena āyuḥ dhakṣyati
saḥ eva agniḥ tṛṇa rāśau krameṇa nyastaḥ cireṇa ddaheta tathā nirupakramam karma
tat etat dvividham eka bhavikam āyuṣkaram karma

aparāntasya prāyaṇasya ātmīyasya jñānam
tathā parakīya dvividha karma saṃyamāt para prāyāṇa jñānam api bhavati
prāyaṇa jñāne ca prayojanam puruṣa kartavya tām pratisamīhanam
ariṣṭebhyaḥ vā prāyaṇa jñānam
trividham ariṣṭam ādhyātmikam ādhibhautikam ādhidaivikam ca
tatra ādhyātmikasya udāharaṇam ghoṣam sva dehe pihita karṇaḥ na śṛṇoti
jyotiḥ vā netre vaṣṭbdhe na paśyati
tathā ādhibhautikam yama puruṣān paśyati
pitṝn atītān āgatān aksamāt vetti
ādhidaivikam akasmāt eva siddha ādīn paśyati viparītam vā sarvam paśyati karoti ca
tatra ariṣṭam iti laukikī vācoyuktiḥ
evam hi āha viparīta darśanam mama āsīt ariṣṭam iti
maitrī ādiṣu balāni
maitrī karuṇā muditā iti tisraḥ bhāvanāḥ
tatra bhūteṣu sukhiteṣu maitīm bhāvayitvā maitrī balam labhate
duḥkhiteṣu karuṇām bhāvayitvā karuṇā balam labhate
puṇya śīlesu muditām bhāvayitvā muditā balam labhate
bhāvanātaḥ maitrī ādi bhāvanātaḥ samādhiḥ yaḥ saṃjāyate sa saṃyamaḥ maitrī ādi bhāvanā srthaiḥ yad nimittaḥ
tatas saṃyamāt maitrī ādi gatāt yoginaḥ balāni avandhya vīryāṇi jāyante
pāpa śīleṣu tu asya upekṣā na tu bhāvanā
tatas ca bhāvanāyāḥ abhāvāt tasyām upekṣāyām na asti samādhiḥ iti atas na balam upekṣātaḥ
tatra saṃyama abhāvāt iti
balesu hasti bala ādīni
etaiḥ maitrī ādi nimittaiḥ balaiḥ balavān yogī baleṣu saṃyamam kṛtvā hasti ādi balaḥ bhavati

yā asau jyotiṣmatī pravṛttiḥ uktā tasyām prakāśaḥ ālokaḥ tam prakāśam yogī sūkṣme vā vyavahite vā viprakṛṣṭe vā arthe vinyasya sthāpayitvā tam
bhuvana jñānam sūrye saṃyamāt
sūrye saṃyamam kṛtvā samastam bhuvana prastāram pratyakṣīkurvīta
bhāṣyam tu gata artham sarva purāṇa prasiddha tvāt

sūrye saṃyamanāt bhuvanaprastāram viditvā tad anantaram candre saṃyamam kṛtvā tārāṇām vyūham vijānīyāt
sūrya saṃyamāt bhuvana prastāra mātram prajñātam evam prastīrṇāḥ lokāḥ nadyaḥ samudrāḥ girayaḥ ca iti
na tu tārāḥ ittham vyūhitāḥ anena sambaddhāḥ iti
tu iti
dhruve tat gati jñānam
tatas ca samanantaram dhruve saṃyamam kṛtvā tārāṇām gatim vijānīyāt anena prakāreṇa anena viśiṣṭāḥ iti asmin kāle anena graheṇa ayam grahaḥ virudhyate
ittham udayaḥ tad dvāreṇa prāṇabhṛtām śubham aśubham ca ityādi vijānīyāt
evam anyeṣu ca ūrdhvam vimāneṣu saṃyamam kṛtvā tāni vimānāni ittham prakārāṇi evam gatāni iti evam ādi sarvam vijānīyāt

nābhi cakre saṃyamam kṛtvā kāya vyūham vijānīyāt
vātapita śloṣmāṇaḥ trayaḥ doṣāḥ etāvat pramāṇāḥ etat pratiṣṭhā ityādi jñeyam
tathā dhātavaḥ sapta bāhya abhyantara bhāvena avasthitāḥ
rasaḥ tvac bāhyā sarveṣām
tatas hi antaram lohitam tatas māṃsam tatas sthi tatas medaḥ tatas majjā tatas śuklam sarva abhyantaram iti evam pūrvam pūrvam eṣām bāhyam iti eṣa vinyāsaḥ
tathā nāḍīnām ca vyūham vijānīyāt

jihvāyāḥ adhastāt tantuḥ unnāmikāyām jihvāyām dṛśyate
tantoḥ adhattāt kanṭhaḥ
tatas dhastāt kūpaḥ
tatra saṃyamāt kṣudh pipāse na pratibādhete
karmanḍyām sthairyam kūpasya adhastāt urasi kurmā nāma nāḍī
tasyām kṛta saṃyamaḥ sthira padam labhate citta sthairyam labhate
yathā sarpaḥ godhā vā dhāraṇāt urasā atyantam sthirībhavati

śiraḥ kapāle chidram prabhāsvara tvāt jyotiḥ iti ucyate
tatra saṃyamāt siddhānām dyāvāpṛthivyoḥ antarāla cāriṇām darśanam bhavati
prātibhāt vā sarvam
ātmani saṃyamam kurvataḥ īśvaram vā atyartham praṇīdadhānasya yoginaḥ prātibham tārakam svayam utthitam mānasam jñānam tat vakṣyamāṇa lakṣaṇasya viveka jasya jñānasya pūrvarūpam
yathā udaye prabhā auṣasī kiṃcid unmīlantī lohitāyamānā bhāsakarasya ujjigamiṣataḥ pūrvarūpam
tasmāt vā sarvam vijānanti yoginaḥ prātibhasya jñānasya utpādāt iti

yat idam asmin brahma pure śarīre daharam alpam puṇḍarīkam puṇḍarīka ākāraḥ māṃsa piṇḍaḥ dhomukhaḥ veśma vadane kanāḍī suṣira yogāt veśma
tatra vijñānam cittam tasmin uraḥ saraḥ vilagna āle prāṇaveśmani puṇḍarūke saṃyamāt citte sattve saṃvid bhavati
sattva puruṣayoḥ atyanta asaṃkīrṇayoḥ pratyaya aviśeṣaḥ bhogaḥ para arthāt sva artha saṃyamāt puruṣa jñānam
sattvam cittam puruṣaḥ bhoktā tayoḥ atyanta asaṅkīrnayoḥ atyanta vilakṣaṇayoḥ atīva pṛthak bhūtayoḥ vṛtti sārūpyam pratyaya aviśeṣaḥ sa bhogaḥ puruṣasya
para arthāt sattvāt puruṣa pratyayena saṅkīrṇa ābhāsāt vivicya sva arthe citi mātra svarūpe saṃyamāt puruṣa jñānam
kīdṛśam tat para artham citta sattvam yatas vivicya sva arthe puruṣe saṃyamaḥ kriyate iti
buddhi sattvam prakhyā śīlam samānam sattvam vastu kāryam puruṣa aṛtha kartavya tayā samavashānam upanibandhanam yo yos te samāna sattva upanibandhane rajaḥ tamasī vaśīkṛtya bhāvam āpādya sattva puruṣa anya tā pratyayena yoginaḥ pariṇatam
tasmāt ca sattvāt pariṇāminaḥ triguṇāt anityāt aśuddhāt parārthāt acetanāt atyanta vidharmā viśuddhaḥ apariṇāmī svārthaḥ nityaḥ cit mātra rūpaḥ puruṣaḥ
tayoḥ atyanta asaṅkīrṇayoḥ pratyaya aviśeṣaḥ bhogaḥ puruṣasya darśita viṣaya tvāt
sa bhoga pratyayaḥ
na appariṇāmi tve sati darśita viṣaya tvāt anyaḥ bhogaḥ sambhavati
sattvasya para atha tvāt a viśiṣṭaḥ bhoga pratyayaḥ dṛśyaḥ puruṣeṇa na
yaḥ tu tasmāt gauṇa pratyayāt pratyayinaḥ ca viśiṣṭaḥ cita mātra rūpaḥ pauruṣeyaḥ pratyayaḥ sva arthaḥ puruṣaḥ eva pariṇāma aṇu papatteḥ pratyayaḥ
tatra sayamāt puruṣa viṣayā prajñā jāyate
nanu ca yadi puruṣaḥ pratyayasya viṣayīkriyate tena ced puruṣaḥ gṛhyate para arthaḥ puruṣaḥ prāpnoti
na eṣa doṣaḥ
na ca puruṣa pratyayena puruṣa viṣayeṇa pratyayena buddhi sattva ātmanā buddhi sattva dharmeṇa puruṣaḥ dṛśyate buddheḥ acetana tvāt
puruṣaḥ eva tam pratyayam sva ālambanam puruṣa ābhāsam paśyati puruṣa ābhāsa tvā īm eva pratyayasya puruṣa ālambana tvam
na pratyayasya puruṣa ālambana tvam
yathā mukha sannidhau darpiṇaḥ mukha ākāreṇa pariṇamate tathā cittam puruṣa ākāreṇa pariṇatam puruṣa ābhāsam puruṣeṇa gṛhyate
tathā ca uktam vijñātāram are kena vijānīyāt iti
na kasyacid puruṣaḥ karma tām pratipadyate iti arthaḥ
nanu cakṣuḥ ādarśa tala pratihatam pratinivṛtya yathā mukhasya grāhakam padam puruṣaḥ api citta sattva pratihataḥ pratinivṛtya sva ātmānam gṛhṇīyāt na pariṇāma anupapatteḥ puruṣasya
na hi apariṇāminaḥ cittam prati pravṛttiḥ pratinivṛttiḥ vā sā adhimānam upāśnuvīta
na ca api cakṣuḥ pratinivṛtya mukham grāhayati
mukhasya darpaṇa maṇḍala adhikaraṇa tvena anubhūyamāna tvāt
na hi sva mukham darpaṇa adhikaraṇa stham
kim ca ādarśa anuvidhānāt ca
yathā khaḍge dīrgham mukham dṛśyate
na sva mukham dīrgham
pratihatena ced upalabhyate cakṣuṣā nijā mukham tatra ādarśa anuvidhānam ayuktam
tatas prātibha śrāvāṇa vedana ādarśa āsvāda vārtāḥ jāyante
tatas svārthe samādhānāt pratibhāt ātma saṃyama janitāt mānasāt jñānāt sūkṣma vyavahita viprakṛṣṭa atīta anāgata jñānam sampadyate
śrāvaṇāt divya śabdānām śravaṇam
vedanāt sparśa jña annāt siddha ādīnām sparśam jānāti
ādarśāt cākṣuṣāt jñānāt divyam rūpam avagacchati
āsvādāt rasana indriya jñānāt divya rasa saṃvedanam bhavati
vṛttau bhavam vārtam loka saṃvyavahāra jñānam tasmāt eṣa saṃvyavahāra tattva rūpam yathāvat adhigacchati
te samādhau upasargāḥ vyutthāne siddhayaḥ
te prātibha ādayaḥ puruṣe samāhita cittasya u utpadyamānāḥ upasargāḥ puruṣa darśana pratyanīka tvāt
vyutthita cittasya utpadyamānāḥ siddhayaḥ
yadi api puruṣe saṃyamāt utpadyante tathā api na viraktasya samāhita cittasya jāyate
bandha kāraṇa śaithilyāt pracāra saṃvedanāt ca cittasya para śarīra āveśaḥ
lolībhūtasya ghaṇṭā abhighā tulyasya dedīpyamāna aṅgāra rāśi dyuti cañcalasya manaḥ
śarīra mātra saṃkoca avasthānam
tasya bandhasya karma kāraṇam
kāraṇa śaithilyam karma āśaya śithila tvam samādhi balāt bhavati
pracāra saṃvedanam ca cittasya samādhi janma iva
karma bandha kṣayāt sva citta pracāra saṃvedanāt ca asmin nimitte hṛṣyati muhyati lubhyati ca anena kāraṇena iti evamādi sva citta sañcaraṇa sattava vedanāt ca yogī cittam sva śarīrāt niṣkṛṣya śarīra antareṣu nikṣipati
cittam asya utpatat indriyāṇi anūtpatanti
tasmāt indriya vṛtti lābhāt para śarīreṣu prāṇa ādi vṛttayaḥ utpadyante
yathā madhukara rājam makṣikāḥ utpatantam anūtpatanti niviśamānam anu niviśante tathā indriyāṇī para śarīra āveśe cittam anu vidhīyante
udāna jayāt jala paṅka kaṇṭaka ādiṣu asaṅgaḥ utkrāntiḥ ca
samasta indriya vṛttiḥ jīvanam sarveṣām ekādaśānām indriyāṇām ekena saṃmūrcchtena vyāpareṇa yena śarīram dhriyate tat jīvanam
tasya jīvanasya puruṣa artha kartavya tā niyamāt pañcatayī kriyā prāṇa apāna vyāna udāna samāna bhedena prastīryate
tatra prāṇaḥ mukha nāsikā gatiḥ āhṛdayavṛttiḥ
samam nayanāt samānaḥ āna abhivṛttiḥ āna arbha deśam vartate
mūtra purīṣa ādīnām apanayanāt pānaḥ sa ca nābhi prabhṛti āpādat alam vartate
ūrdhvam śarīrasya nayanāt udānaḥ sa ca pāda talāt ārabhya ā mastaka vṛttiḥ
samasta śarīra vyāpī vyānaḥ iti
eteṣām pradhānaḥ pradhānaḥ prāṇaḥ
tad jayāt ca sarveṣām apāna ādīnām tu jayaḥ bhavati
teṣām tu jaya upāyaḥ vistareṇa hairaṇyagarbhe vyākhyātaḥ
iha tu manaḥ jaya anujita tvāt teṣām jaya upāyaḥ na pṛthak abhihitaḥ prāṇa ayamajayāt tu jīyante eva na pṛthak eṣām jaya upāya pratipādanam ādṛtyam iti phala mātram udāna jiteḥ ucyate udāna jayāt jala paṅka kaṇṭaka ādiṣu ādinā kṛpāṇa dhārā ādiṣu asaṅgaḥ
kim ca utkrāntiḥ ca prāyaṇa kāle bhavati
tām prāyaṇa kāle bhavantīm utkrāntim udāna jayāt vaśīkṛtya svatantra tayā pratipadyate
samānajayāt jvalanam
jita samānaḥ tejasaḥ kṛtvā samāna vāyu āśraya tvāt udāna tejasoḥ tad upadhmāna karma kārakaḥ tāvat yogī jāṭharam jvalayati
śrotra ākāśayoḥ saṃbandha saṃyamāt divyam śrotram
kaḥ punar asau saṃbandhaḥ yatra saṃyamaḥ iti āha sarva śrotrāṇām ākācam pratiṣṭhā
śabdānām ca ākāśa kuṇa tvāt ākāśam eva pratiṣṭhā
grāhyam śabdam prati śratrasya vyavadhāna abhāvaḥ śrotra ākāśayoḥ sambandhaḥ
tathā ca uktam tulya deśa śravaṇānām
śrūyate nena iti śravaṇam
tulya deśāni śravaṇāni yeṣām te tulya deśa aśravaṇāḥ
teṣām eka śruti tvam sarveṣām bhavati
tat ekasmin avakāśa dāyini nirāvaraṇa ātmake vastuni sati yujyate
tat ca etat ākāśasya sattve liṅgam
tathā anāvaraṇa ātmakam ca uktam
kutas tathā mūrtasya anyatra ākāśāt ākāśa vilakṣaṇa asya ghaṭa ādeḥ āvaraṇa darśanāt
atas yasya maṇi vajra ādi madhyeṣu api āvaraṇam na asti tat ākāśam
atas eva vibhu tvam api prakhyātam ākāśasya
śrotrasya liṅgam āha śabda grahaṇa anumitam tu śrotram
yasmāt badhira abadhirayoḥ ekaḥ śabdam gṛhṇāti aparaḥ na gṛhṇāti
yad nimittam a badhirasya śabda grahaṇam itarasya ca a grahaṇam tat śrotram
tasmāt śrotram eva śabda viṣayam
badhireṇa a śravaṇāt
śrotra ākāśayoḥ saṃbandhe kṛta saṃyamasya toginaḥ civyam śrotram pravartate
kāya ākāśayoḥ sambandha saṃyamasya laghu tūla samāpatteḥ ca ākāśagamanam
yatra kāyāḥ tatra ākāśam
tasya avakāśa dānāt kāyasya avinābhāva lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ tena ākāśena
tatra kāya ākāśayoḥ itaretara avinābhāva prāpti lakṣaṇa sambandhe kṛta saṃyamaḥ yogī jitvā tad sambandham tatas laghuṣu tūla ādiṣu ā paramāṇubhyaḥ samāpatteḥ jita sambandhaḥ tūla ādi vat lāghavam pratipadyate
jita kāya ākāśa sambandhaḥ samāpannaḥ jale pādābhyām viharati
tatas ūrdhvam ūrṇā nābhi tantu matre viharati
tatra sañjāta kokila tantu samāna lāghavaḥ punar raśmiṣu viharati
tatas mātariśvani
tatas yathā iṣṭam ākāśe gatiḥ asya bhavati
bahis akalpitā vṛttiḥ mahā videhā tatas prakāśa āvaraṇa kṣayaḥ
śarīrāt bahis deśa antare viṣaya viśeṣe svayam eva samāhi balāt upajāyate yā manasaḥ vṛttiḥ sā mahā videhā nāma dhāraṇā
sā yadi śarīra pratiṣṭhasya eva manasp vṛtti mātreṇa bahis viṣaye bhavati tadānīm kalpitā ucyate
śarīra sthamnaḥ saṅkalpa pūrvaka tvāt
yā tu samādhi bala nimittāt śarīre bandha kāraṇa śaithilyāt
śarīra nirapekṣā bahis bhūtasya eva manasaḥ bahis vṛttiḥ sā khalu akalpitā iti ucyate
yathā eva kalpitāyām śarīra avadhikaḥ eva bahis vṛtti lābhaḥ evam nāka alpa itāyām śarīra adhiṣṭhāna avadhi samīkṣā
sā ca ubhayī api videhāḥ eva bahis upakalpita tvāt
tatra yā iyam akalpitā mahāvidehā iti samākhyāyate
tatra kalpitayā sādhayanti akalpitām mahāvidehām
kalpanā saṃśīlana sāvya tvāt akalpitāyāḥ kalpitayā ca saṃsādhayanti
yayā mahāvidehayā para śarīrāṇi āviśanti yoginaḥ
tatas ca dhāraṇātaḥ mahāvidehātaḥ prakāśa ātmanaḥ buddhi sattvasya yat āvaraṇam kleśa karma vipaka trayam rajaḥ tamaḥ mūlam tasya ca kṣayaḥ bhavati

sthūlam ca svarūpam ca sūkṣmam ca anvayaḥ ca arthavat tvam ca iti evam ekaikam bhūtam pañca ātmakam
tatra pārtivāḥ śabda ādayaḥ śabda sparśa rūpa rasa gandhāḥ viśeṣāḥ pañca lakṣaṇa tanmātra ārabdha tvāt pṛthivyāḥ
saha ākāra ādibhiḥ
pṛthivyāḥ tāvat ākāra ādayaḥ ākāraḥ gauravam raukṣyam ca īraṇam sthairyam eva ca
sthitiḥ bhedaḥ kṣamā kāṣṇryam kāṭhinyam sarva bhogya tā
iti
tathā sneha prabhā saukṣmya mārdava gaurava rakṣā pavitra tva sandhāna ādayaḥ audakāḥ guṇāḥ
tathā taijasāḥ ūrdhva bhāj tva pāvana tā dagdhṛ tva pācaka tva lāghava bhāsvara tva ādayaḥ
tathā vāyavīyāḥ tiryak yāna pavitra tva ākṣepa bala nodana tva ādayaḥ
tathā nābhasāḥ sarva gati a vyūha viṣṭambhāḥ
tat etaiḥ ākāra ādibhiḥ saha śabda ādayaḥ viśeṣāḥ sthūla śabdena saṃvyavahāra artham śāstre paribhāṣitāḥ evam āpyāḥ catvāraḥ rasa ādayaḥ viśeṣāḥ saukṣmya ādibhiḥ saha evam taijasāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ trayaḥ ūrdhva bhāj tva ādibhiḥ saha sthūlāḥ ucyante
tathā vāyavīyāḥ śabda sparśa tiryakpāta āayaḥ sthūlāḥ viśeṣāḥ
evam ākāśasya sarva gata tva ādayaḥ sthūlāḥ viśeṣāḥ
tat etat bhūtānām prathamam sthūlam rūpam uktam
dbitīyam adhunā svarūpam ucyate
tat ca sāmānyam prthiveṣu bhinneṣu abhinnam anugatam mūrtiḥ eva bhūmiḥ iti
tathā rasa ādiṣu āpyeṣu anugatam sāmānyam snehaḥ eva jalam iti
tathā eva agnaye iṣu rūpa ādiṣu anugatam sāmānyam bahniḥ uṣṇa tvam eva
tathā sparśa tiryakpāta ādiṣu anugatam sāmānyam praṇāmi tvam eva vāyuḥ
tathā śabda ādi ṛc anugatam sāmānyam sarvatas gatiḥ eva ākāśaḥ iti etat svarūpa śabdena uktam dvitīyam rūpam
tasya sāmānyasya rūpasya śabda ādayaḥ viśeṣāḥ
tathā ca uktam eka jāti samanvitānām sattva ādi guṇa samanugatānām eṣām bhūtānām pṛthivī ādīn sāmānyānām śabda ādi dharma mātram vyāvartate
sāmānya viśeṣa samudāyaḥ dravyam
kasmāt dviṣṭhaḥ hi samūhaḥ dvābhyām prakārābhyām sthitaḥ dviṣṭhaḥ pratyasta mita bheda avayavaḥ vyāvṛtta pratyaya śūnyaḥ iti arthaḥ
yathā śarīram vṛkṣaḥ yūṭham vanam iti
upātta bheda avayava anugataḥ āgṛhīta bheda avayava anugataḥ samūhaḥ uhaya śabdena upādīyate
ubhaye devam anuṣyāḥ iti
tat yathā samūhasya devāḥ ekaḥ bhāgaḥ manuṣyāḥ ekaḥ bhāgaḥ
tābhyām eva bhāgābhyām āgṛhīta yathāsva bheda anugatābhyām abhidhīyate samūhaḥ ubhaye iti
tayoḥ bheda abhedaḥ vivakṣitaḥ āmnāṇām vanam iti
āmnāṇām iti bhedena vivakṣā
vanam iti abhedena
tābhyām dvābhyām bheda abhedābhyām āmnānām vanam iti ṣaṣṭhī prathamā
tad dvayoḥ vivakṣitaḥ ekaḥ samūhaḥ iti
sa punar dvividhaḥ samūhaḥ yuta siddha avayavaḥ yuta siddha avayavaḥ ca
yuta siddha avayavaḥ pṛthak siddha avayavaḥ samūhaḥ vanam saṅghaḥ iti
ayuta siddha avayavaḥ apṛhak siddha avayavaḥ saṅghātaḥ śarīram vṛkṣaḥ paramāṇuḥ iti
paramāṇūnām api sāvayava tvam sattva ādi kārya tvāt mūrta tvāt ca ghaṭa ādi vat eva
ayuta siddha avayava bheda anugataḥ samūhaḥ dravyam iti patañjaliḥ
etat svarūpam iti uktam sāmānya viśeṣa ātmakam
atha kim eṣām sūkṣmam rūpam iti
tanmātram bhūta kāraṇam
aneka paramāṇu upārabdha tvāt tasya tanmātrasya ekaḥ vayavaḥ paramāṇuḥ
saḥ api sāmānya viśeṣa ātmā ayuta siddha avayava bheda anugataḥ samudāyaḥ iti
evam sarva yanmātrāṇi
tatas ca tanmātrāṇi viśeṣa vinirmuktāni tad avayavāḥ ca paramāṇavaḥ iti etat bhūtānām tṛtīyam sūkṣma ākhyam rūpam saṃyamasya viṣayaḥ iti
tanmātra ārabdha tvāt ca sa avayavam ākāśam anityam ca
na ca śabda vyatirekeṇa ākāśam nāma dravyam upaladhum śakyam
dharma dharmiṇoḥ abhedāt
nanu ca keśa ādīnām kṛṣṇmā api apaiti śuklimā samupajāyate
tathā ca apāya upajana dharmāṇaḥ kṛṣṇima ādayaḥ te guṇāḥ
yat tu na kṛṣṇimānam anu vinaśyati śuklimānam anveti tat dravyam
evam ākāśa ādīnām api guṇa avyatirekeṇa sadbhāvaḥ śabda pratyaya ādi bhedāt iti
na dṛṣṭānta abhāvāt
te eva kṛṣṇāḥ śuklāḥ ca kleśāḥ kṛṣṇa śukla tva ādi dharmaiḥ pariṇamante
sarvam hi sarva ātmakam iti uktam
na khalu kvacid api kūṭasthe vyapanayanena dravya svarūpam
yat api darśana sparśanābhyām yat upalabhyate tat deavyam iti tat api ayuta siddha rūpa sparśa samudāya tvāt ubhābhyām darana sparśanābhyām gṛhyate iti adoṣaḥ
nanu ca na rūpam sparśanena gṛhyate na api darśanena saprśaḥ yat ubhybhyām gṛhyate yat paśyāmi tat eva sparśāmi iti tat dravyam
yat tu cakṣuṣā eva gṛhyate sparśanena eva ca gṛhyate sa guṇa iti
na māṣa tila yava ādi bhinna jāti vimiśra rāśau anaikantika tvāt
gṛhyate ca darśana sparśanābhyām rāśiḥ
kim ca darśana sparśane guṇasya eva grāhake bāhya indriya tvāt śrotra vat
na hi jātiḥ api guṇa vyatiriktā vidyate bhedena a grāhaṇāt
kim ca ghaṭa ādau api paraspara adhyāsena darśana sparśanābhyām rūpa sparśayoḥ eva grahaṇam
yathā idam rūpam durgandhi surabhi randhi ca iti
tasmāt ākāśam api tanmātra ārabdham śabda vyatirekeṇa a śakyam pratipattum iti sa avayavam anityam ca
atha bhūtānām caturtham rūpam
guṇāḥ kārya svarūpa anupātinaḥ kārya dharma anuyāyinaḥ anvaya śabdena uktāḥ
anugamāt
tat etat bhūtānām caturtham rūpam saṃyamasya guṇa anvaya āhkyaḥ viṣayaḥ
atha eṣām pañcamam rūpam arthavat tvam
asya vyākyānam bhoga apavarka artha tā
sā ca guṇeṣu anvayinī
tatra yā guṇeṣu anuvṛttā bhoga apavarga āyatā tat idam bhūtānām pañcamam rūpam saṃyamasya arthavat tva ākhyaḥ viṣayaḥ
guṇāḥ tat mātreṣu bhūteṣu bhūta vikāreṣu ca anvayinaḥ
evam tanmātram sūkṣma rūpam bhūta bhūta vikāreṣu anugatam
bhūta svarūpam ca sthūleṣu bhūta vikāreṣu anugatam iti sarvam arthavat
guṇānām bhoga apavarga artha tvāt teṣām ca sarva anvayi tvāt tad arthavat tvena sarvam bhūta vikāra ādikam arthavat
teṣu idānīm bhūteṣu mañcasu pañca rūpeṣu sthūlāt dip pañca rūpeṣu yathākramam saṃyamāt pūrvam sthūlena saṃyamam kṛtvā sva rūpa saṃyamam kurvīta
punar sūkṣme punar ca anvaye punar ca arthavattve iti evam yathākramam saṃyamāt tasya tasya sthūla ādikasya darśanam jayaḥ ca yathāvat prādurbhavati
tatra bhūta svarūpāṇi jitvā yogī bhūta jayī bhavati
tat jayāt vatsa anusāriṇyaḥ iva gāvaḥ yathā prakṛti bhūtāḥ gāvaḥ asya saṃkalpa anuvidhāyinyaḥ bhūtaprakṛtayaḥ bhavanti
svam saṃyama phalam idānīm āha tatas kāya sampad tat dharma anabhighātaḥ ca
tatra aṇimā kaḥ bhavati iti āha aṇuḥ iti
sūkṣmāt api sūkṣmataraḥ bahu atīt hātaḥ
tena aṇimnā sarvam anupraviśati vajram api
tathā sarvasya adṛśyaḥ bhavati
laghimā laghuḥ laghubhyaḥ tūla ādibhyaḥ api laghutaraḥ bhavati tena nirālambanaḥ sarvatas gantum paryāpnoti
mahimā mahān bhavati
ākāśam api vyāpnoti prāptiḥ ihasthaḥ spṛśati candramasam
prākāmyam pracura kāmaḥ yathā iṣṭa kāmaḥ bhavati id dhānā abhighātaḥ
bhūmau unmajjati ca yathākāma tvāt yathā udake
vaśitvam sarva loka vaśitvam
asya vyākhyānam bhūta bhautika vaśī bhavati avaśyaḥ ca anyeṣām
īśitvam teṣām bhūtānām prabhava vyūha api ayānām utpatti sthiti pralayānām īṣṭe
yatra kāmāvasāyi tvam yasmin kāmaḥ tatra iva tad avasānam tad antam gacchati
satya saṃkalpāt hetoḥ yathā saṃkalpaḥ tathā bhūta prakṛtīnām avasthānam bhavati
śaktaḥ api sa yogī na padārtha viparyāsam karoti
na agnim śītīkaroti
kasmāt anyasya yatrakāmāvasāyinaḥ pūrva siddhasya parama īśvarasya tathā teṣu padārtheṣu viparyāsena saṃkalpāt
na hi padārtha viparyāsam cikīrṣamāṇasya pūrva shiddham prati vinā dveṣeṇa tad viparyāsaḥ bhavati
tat aśuddhi abhāvāt eva na padārtha viparyāsam karoti
kaliāṇatara ācaraṇaḥ hi saḥ iti
etāni aṣṭau aṇima ādi aiśvaryāṇi bhūtajayāt bhavanti
kāya sampad vakṣyamāṇā
tad bhūtānām dharmaiḥ na yoginaḥ abhighātaḥ bhavati
pṛthivī svena dharmeṇa mūrtyā na viruṇaddhi yoginaḥ śarīra ādi kriyām
katham śilām api anupraviśati
na āpaḥ snigdhāḥ yoginam kledayanti varṣa sahasram api udake tiṣṭhantam
na agniḥ uṣṇe dahati
na vāyuḥ praṇāmī vahati
anāvaraṇa ātmake api prakaṭa rūpe api bhavati āvṛtaḥ prakaṭaḥ na bhavati
siddhānām api adṛśyaḥ bhavati
rūpa lāvaṇya bala vajra saṃhanana tvāni kāya sampad
rūpavān darśanīyaḥ
lāvaṇyavān kāntimān atiśaya balaḥ vajra saṃhananaḥ ca bhavati

sarvam etat gata sūtreṇa tuya vyākhyānam
asmitā mātram tu viśeṣaḥ bhūtānām iva tat mātrāṇi
sāmānya viśeṣa ātmā śabda ādiḥ viṣayaḥ
teṣu indriyāṇām yā vṛttiḥ viṣaya viśeṣa avalokana ātmikā tat grahaṇam
na ca tad sāmānya mātre śabda ādi sāmānya ābhāsana mātre manasi grahaṇa ākāraḥ upapadyate
katham anālocitaḥ sva viṣaya viśeṣaḥ
na katham cit anuvyavasīyeta taimirika ataimirikayoḥ anuvyavasāya ananuvyavasāya āhyām
tasmāt nityā na indriyeṇa anālocite viṣaye manasā anuvyavasāyaḥ
tatra asyām viśeṣa ātmikāyām vṛttau prathamam saṃyamaḥ kartavyaḥ
atha svarūpam punar indriyāṇām dvitīyam rūpam
prakāśa ātmanoḥ sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ viṣaya viśeṣa ālocanam indriyāṇām viśeṣaḥ
yathā pradīpasya ghaṭa ādi viśeṣa ākāra ālokaḥ viśeṣaḥ
prakāśa mātram sāmānyam
atas sāmānya viśeṣa ātmakam ayuta siddha avayava bheda anugatam dravyam indriyam pradīpa vat
yathā sāmānya mūrti dharmaḥ sthūra ādiṣu anupravartate tathā indriyam prakāśa ātmakam dravya viśeṣa ātmikāyām grahaṇa vṛttau anupravartate
tat etasmin dvitīye indriyāṇām svarūpe saṃyamaḥ kriyeta
teṣām indriyāṇām tṛtīyam rūpam asmitā lakṣaṇaḥ haṅkāraḥ
tasya ahaṅkārasya sāmānyasya indriyāṇi ayuta siddha avayava bheda anugatāni grahaṇa rūpa anvayīni viśeṣāḥ
tatra asmitāyām saṃyamaḥ karaṇīyaḥ
caturtham rūpam vyavasāya ātmakāḥ prakāśa kriyā sthiti śīlāḥ guṇāḥ
yeṣām incriyāṇi sa ahaṅkārāṇi pariṇāmaḥ
tatra guṇa anugame saṃyamaḥ kartavyaḥ
pañcamam rūpam guṇeṣu yat anugatam puruṣa arthavat tvam
atas sarveṣām arthavat tvam anugamaḥ ca pūrvavat
evam eṣu pañcasu indriya rūpeṣu yathākramam krama anatikrameṇa saṃyamaḥ
tatra pratyekam pañcasu jayam ṛtvā pañcasu arūpa jayam labhate
tasmāt pañca svarūpa jayāt jayaḥ vakṣyamāṇa phalāya prādurbhavati yoginaḥ
yat tu tatas param āvaśya tā indriyāṇām iti tat viṣaya grahaṇa vṛtteḥ vaśitva mātram viṣaya apratipatti rūpam
tatas manojava tvam vikaraṇa bhāvaḥ pradhāna jayaḥ ca tatas kāyasya anuttamaḥ na vidyate smāt uttamaḥ iti anuttamaḥ gati lābhaḥ manojava tvam
videhānām śarīra nirapekṣāṇām indriyāṇām abhipreta deśa apekṣaḥ bhipreta kāla apekṣaḥ bhipreta śabda ādi viṣaya apekṣaḥ ca vṛtti lābhaḥ vikaraṇa bhāvaḥ
sarva prakṛti vikāra vaśitvam aṣṭānām prakṛtīnām tad vikārāṇām ca vaśitvam pradhāna jayaḥ iti etāḥ tisraḥ siddhayaḥ madhupratīkāḥ iti ucyante
tāḥ ca pañca sva rūpa jayāt adhigamyante
sattva puruṣa anyatā khyāti mātrasya sarva bhāva adhiṣṭhātṛ tvam sarvajñātṛ tvam ca sarva prakāreṇa sarva sādhanena nirdhūta rajaḥ tamaḥ malasya sattvasya pare vaiśāradye svaddhe sthiti pravāhe pare vartamānasya parasyām vaśīkāra saṃjñāyām jñāna prasāda mātre niratiśaye vartamānasya sattva puruṣa anyathā khyāti mātra rūpa pratiṣṭhasya sarva bhāva adhiṣṭhātṛ tvam
sarvasya vastu jātasya iṣṭe
sarva ātmanā sakala prakṛti vikāra ātmanā guṇa adhyavasāya ātmakāḥ buddhi ādi kāraṇa bhāva pariṇata adhyavasāya ātmakāḥ svāminam k dṛśi mātram aśeṣa guṇāḥ dṛśya tvena bhogya tvena avasthitāḥ labhyante iti arthaḥ
iti
iti eṣā sarva vaśitva sarvajñātṛ tva lakṣaṇā viśokā nāma siddhiḥ
yām prāpya yogī sarvajñaḥ kṣīṇa kleśa bandhanaḥ viharati vaśī
tad vairāgyāt api doṣa bīja kṣaye kaivalyam
yadā asya evam bhavati sarvajñasya sarva bhāvān adhitiṣṭhataḥ kleśa karma kṣaye vivekī sattvasya pratyayaḥ
puruṣaḥ ca sattva vidharmā apariṇāmī śuddhaḥ sattvāt iti anena prakāreṇa
tatas api sarvajña sarva bhāva adhyakṣa tvāt virajyamānasya yāni kleśa bījāni avidyā vāsanā rūpāṇi dagdha śāli bīja kalpāni prasava a samarthāni tān caritārthena pralīyamānena saha āśrayeṇa manasā pratyastam gaddhanti
teṣu pralīneṣu puruṣaḥ punar idam tāpa trayam ādhyātmika ādi lakṣaṇam na bhuṅkte
tat eṣām guṇānām manasi kleśa karma vipaka sva rūpeṇa abhivyaktānām caritārthānām pratiprasave pralaye puruṣasya ātyantikaḥ guṇa viyogaḥ kaivalyam
tadā svarūpa pratiṣṭhā citi śaktiḥ eva puruṣaḥ
tatra api iti apiśabdāt aprāpta yoga aiśvaryasya api samyak darśanāt kaivalyam iti
sthāni upamantraṇe saṅga smayā akaraṇam punar aniṣṭa prasaṅgāt
sthānam svarga ādikam yeṣān te sthāninaḥ devāḥ indra ādayaḥ
taiḥ upamantraṇam bho bho iha uṣyatām ityādi
tasmin sati ātmanaḥ hīna tvam smarataḥ prāpnutaḥ saṅga smayau arthāt iti tau ca na kartavyau
saṅga smaya karaṇe niṣṭam prasajyeta
catvāraḥ khalu amī yoginaḥ prāthamakalpikaḥ madhubhūmikaḥ prajñājyotiḥ atikrāntabhāvanīyaḥ ca
tān krameṇa vyācaṣṭe tatra abhyāsī abhyāsana śīlaḥ pravṛttajyotiḥ jyotiṣmatī ādīnām anyatamā pravṛttiḥ pravṛttā yasya sa pravṛttajyotiḥ prathamaḥ
ṛtambhara prajñaḥ dvitīyaḥ
bhūtendriyajayī tṛtīyaḥ
sa tu sarveṣu bhāviteṣu bhāvanīyeṣu sākṣāt kṛteṣu jiteṣu ca kṛta rakṣā bandhaḥ upāttasya hi rakṣā vidhānīyā bhāvanīyeṣu sākṣāt karaṇīyeṣu kartavya tā sādhanavān ca
kartavyatāyāḥ sādhanāni kartavyatā sādhanāni abhyāsa vairāgya ādīni yasya saḥ kartavyatā sādhanavān
yaḥ tu atikrāntabhāvanīyaḥ caturthaḥ tasya citta pratisargaḥ eva citta pralayaḥ eva ekaḥ rthaḥ pariśiṣṭaḥ
saptavidhā tasya prānta bhūmim prajñā
tatra madhumatīm bhūmim dvitīyām ṛtaṃbhara prajñā bhūmim sākṣātkurvataḥ brāhmāṇasya sthāninaḥ devāḥ sattva viśuddhim anupaśyantaḥ sthānaiḥ upamantrayante
bhoḥ ityādi prasiddha artham bhāṣyam

kṣaṇam kramam ca svayam eva vistareṇa ācaṣṭe tatra apakarṣa paryantam yatas param apakarṣaḥ na śakyate kartum tat dravyam paramāṇuḥ
evam loka budhi vikalpitāt ahar rātra lakṣaṇāt apakṛṣyamāṇāt kālāt alpīyaḥ parijighṛkṣayā yatas param apakraṣṭum na śakyate saḥ apakarṣa paryantaḥ kālaḥ kṣaṇaḥ vastu bhūtaḥ
yat vā yāvatā samayena vicalitaḥ paramāṇuḥ pūrvam deśam jahyāt uttaram abhisaṃpadyeta sa kālaḥ kṣaṇaḥ
asti kṣaṇaḥ iti arthaḥ
tasya pravāha viccheda bhāvinaḥ tasya kṣaṇasya pravāhaḥ prabandhaḥ a vidhedaḥ nairantaryam tathā bhavitum śīlam yasya kṣaṇasya pravāha aviccheda bhāvinaḥ kṣaṇasya yat ānantaryam saḥ kṣaṇasya kramaḥ
tayoḥ ca kṣaṇa tad kramayoḥ na asti vastu samāhāraḥ kṣaṇa kramasya avastu tvāt kṣaṇasya ca eka tvāt na asti tayoḥ samāhāraḥ samūhaḥ
nanu ca asati kṣaṇa tad krama samāhāre katham māsa saṃvatsara ādāḥ pravarteran iti tad artham āha buddhi samāhārāt buddhi parikalpitāt kṣaṇa tad kramayoḥ iti ādideśa antara saṃbandha avabandha buddhi samudbhāvitāt muhūrta ahar rātra ādayaḥ
tatas ca buddhi sthitaḥ eṣa bhedaḥ
yaḥ hi ekāgra bhūmi pratiṣṭhi citta sattvaḥ tasya sati api kāla anubhave kṣaṇa yuga sahasrayoḥ tulya tā
na evam vyutthita cittasya
tathā svapne api ghaṭikā mātreṇa buddhi parikalpitam yojana sahasram anekam saṃvatsareṇa eva gantavyam
tasmāt buddhi vaicitrya nimrmitaḥ eva kāla samāhāraḥ
yasya tu kriyā vyatiriktaḥ kālaḥ nityaḥ vibhuḥ tasya cira kṣipra tva ādi api kriyā mātre paryavasita tvāt pṛthak kāla astitvena liṅgam ghaṭate
niyata parimāṇā hi kriyā anavagata pariṇāmāyāḥ kriyāyāḥ lakṣaṇam
yathāgodohanam svapiti
odanapākam adhīte iti
saḥ eva ca kālaḥ
na hi nityasya vibhoḥ tasya kūṭasthasya asambandha tvāt vastu antara paricchedaka tvam prastha ādi vat upapadyate
kriyāvān kālaḥ paricchedakaḥ prastha ādi vat iti ced tasya api kriyāvat tvāt kriyāvataḥ ca pariddhedanīya tvāt anyena kriyāvatā paricchedakena kālena bhavitavyam
tasya api anyena iti anavathā prasaṅgaḥ
kriyāvat tvāt ca anitya tvam api
atha sva vyāpāreṇa eva kālaḥ paricchedanīyakam yāyāt iti ced anye api sva vyāpāreṇa eva paricchedyāḥ iti kāla pṛthaktva kalpā nirarthikā
tathā ca kriyā eva astu kālaḥ
atha api sadbhāva mātreṇa kālaḥ paricchedakaḥ iti sarveṣām api sadbhāva aviśeṣāt evam prasaktam
kriyā kāla pakṣe api eṣa vikalpaḥ prāptaḥ iti ced na kriyāyāḥ sarva prasiddha tvāt
paricchedaka tvasya ca ā godohamāḥ te ityādiṣu siddha tvāt kriyā eva pricchedikā labhyate na aparaḥ kālaḥ pariddhedakaḥ iti
ciram kṣipram iti ca prayatna mandima pāṭava kṛtaḥ pratyayaḥ na vyatirikta kāla nibandhanaḥ iti āha sa khalu ayam kālaḥ saṃvatsara ādi rūpaḥ vastu śūnyaḥ buddhi nirmāṇaḥ buddhyā nirmāpiṣyate
śabda dharma anupātī truṭi nimeṣa ahar rātra ādi śabda vikalpa anupravartī
laukikānām vyutthita darśanānām vastu svarūpe iva ābhāsate
kṣaṇaḥ tu vastu rūpaḥ vāstavikaḥ krama avalambī
kramaḥ ca kṣaṇa ānantarya ātmā kṣaṇa pravāha āviddha ida buddhi nimittaḥ
tam kṣaṇam kāla vidaḥ kālaḥ iti ācakṣate yoginaḥ
na ca dvau kṣaṇau saha bhavataḥ yayoḥ samāhāraḥ kalpyeta
ekasmin dharmiṇi saha janmanoḥ kṣaṇayoḥ asaṃbhavāt
jāyamānaḥ hi caitraḥ ekasmin kṣaṇe jāyate
na tatra dvau kaṇau saha bhavataḥ
kramaḥ ca na dvayoḥ
kasmāt dvayoḥ kṣaṇayoḥ saha bhuvoḥ āsambhavāt
pūrvasmāt uttarasya bhāvinaḥ yat ānantaryam kṣaṇasya sa kramaḥ
yathā piṇḍāt uttara bhāvinaḥ ghaṭasya yat ānantaryam sa kramaḥ
na hi cakra antara sthasya mṛd piṇḍasya cakra antara stha mṛd piṇḍa janitaḥ ghaṭaḥ krame vartate
tasmāt vartamānaḥ ekaikaḥ kṣaṇaḥ
na pūrva uttarau atīta anāgatau staḥ pūrva uttarayoḥ dharmi svarūpa mātra tvāt
dharmī ca vartamāna kṣaṇa ārūḍhaḥ eva
tasmāt nityā na asti tad samāhāraḥ kṣaṇa tad krama samāhāraḥ
ye tu bhūta bhāvinaḥ atīta bhaviṣyantaḥ kṣaṇāḥ te dharmiṇaḥ pariṇāma astitayā dharmi pariṇāma apekṣayā vyākhyeyāḥ
tena ekena kṣaṇena kṛtsnaḥ lokaḥ pariṇāmam anubhavati
tad kṣaṇa upārūḍhāḥ vartamāna kṣaṇa upārūḍhāḥ khalu amī sarve dharmāḥ sarva padārthāḥ
yat uktam atīta kṣaṇasya na asti kramaḥ iti tasya tat prayojanam tad krama krama pratiṣedhaḥ
kṣaṇa krama krame hi sati kṣaṇa kramasya vastu tvam prasajyeta
vastunaḥ hi etayoḥ kṣaṇa tad kramayoḥ saṃyamāt tayoḥ sākṣātkaraṇam
tatas ca viveka jam jñānam
kṣaṇa tad krama aṅkitāḥ eva hi sarve padārthāḥ iti tān aśeṣān vivicya vijānāti
tasya viveka jasya jñānasya kīdṛśam jñetam iti tasya viṣaya viśeṣaḥ upakṣipyate jāti lakṣaṇa deśaiḥ anya tāna vat bhedāt tatas pratipattiḥ
tulyayoḥ deśa lakṣaṇa sārūpye jāti bhedaḥ padārthānām anya tāyāḥ hetuḥ
yathā gauḥ iyam baḍabā iyam iti
yatra jāti bhedaḥ na asti ekā eva jātiḥ tatra tulya jāti tve lakṣaṇam liṅgam anya tvāvat heda karam kāla akṣī gauḥ svastimatī gauḥ iti
yatra na jāti bhedaḥ na api lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ tatra deśa bhedaḥ nya tva avaccheda hetuḥ
yathā dvayoḥ āmalakayoḥ jāti lakṣaṇa sārūpye deśa bhedaḥ nyatva karaḥ idam pūrvam āmalakam idam uttaram iti
yadā tu pūrvam āmalakam anya vyagrasya samākulita cittasya uttara deśe upāvartate pūrva deśe ca uttaram tadā tulya deśa tve pūrvam etat uttaram etat iti tulyayoḥ pravibhāga anupapattiḥ
asandigdhena tattva jñānena bhavitavyam jñeyasya vidyamāna tvāt eka rūpasya iti atas idam uktam tatas pratipattiḥ viveka jñānāt iti

tat katham pūrva āmalaka saha kṣaṇaḥ deśaḥ pūrva āmalaka sahacaraḥ deśaḥ uttara āmalaka saha kṣaṇāt uttara āmalaka sahacarāt deśāt bhinnaḥ
te ca āmalake kṣaṇa sahacarite sva deśa la kṣaṇa anubhava bhinne sva deśa cihna bhūte yaḥ kṣaṇaḥ tat anubhava bhinne sva deśa la kṣaṇa anubhā cihnite anya deśa la kṣaṇa anubhavaḥ tayoḥ anya tve hetuḥ iti
anena dṛṣṭāntena paramāṇoḥ atulya jāti lakṣaṇa bheda deśa kṣaṇa sākṣātkaraṇāt pūrva paramāṇu daśena saha bhūtasya kṣaṇasya sākṣātkaraṇāt uttara paramāṇoḥ tat deśa apavṛttau pūrva deśa gatau api uttarasya tat deśa anubhava bhinnaḥ kṣaṇaḥ
kṣaṇa bhedāt tayoḥ īśvarasya yoginaḥ thā tva pratyayaḥ bheda avacchedaḥ bhavati
atra apare varṇayanti ye antyāḥ viśeṣāḥ paramāṇu gatāḥ nityāḥ te eva anyatā pratyayam kurvanti iti kim tad kṣaṇa tad krama saṃyamena
yathā ghaṭa ādi gatāḥ viśeṣāḥ anyatā pratyayam kurvanti tathā paramāṇu gatāḥ ye viśeṣāḥ te eva tad bhāva pratyayam sva sadbhāva pratyayam ca kurvīran
āśraya bheda pratyayam api kurvanti
atrā ucyate deśa lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ mūrti vyavadhi jāti bhedaḥ ca anyatve hetuḥ uktaḥ eva sthūleṣu na tu nanu paramāṇuṣu prati kṣaṇa pariṇāmi tvāt
avasthiteṣu hi viśeṣeṣu antyeṣu syāt anyathā
na ca anavarata pariṇāmeṣu ghaṭate
yadā pūrvaḥ paramāṇuḥ uttara paramāṇu rūpeṇa pariṇamate pūrva paramāṇu rūpeṇa ca uttaraḥ tatra avasthita antya viśeṣa abhāvāt viveka pratipattiḥ anupapannā
tatra avaśyam kṣaṇa tad krama saṃyama janita viveka ñānāt eva saṃpratipattiḥ
anityāḥ ca paramāṇavaḥ iti hi uktam
tasmāt kṣaṇabhedaḥ tu yogi buddhi gamyaḥ eva
tathā ca anitya tvasya paramāṇunām ācārya antara mata pratipādana dvāreṇa prasiddhim darśayati atas uktam mūrti vyavadhi jāti bheda abhāvāt na asti mūla jāti pṛthaktvam iti vārṣagaṇyaḥ
yathā pratikṣetrajñam pradhāna bahu tvam nyāya viruddham mūrti vyavadhi jāti bheda abhāvāt pradhānānām pṛthatvam eka puruṣa artha dṛśya vat anupapannam evam paramāṇunām api mūla tve pṛthaktvam na upakalpate
tatas ca ekam mūlam iti prāptam
na paramāṇu bhedaḥ hi nityaḥ uktaḥ
paramāṇunām ca mūrta tvāt rūpa ādimat tvāt ca anitya tvam ghaṭa ādi vat eva iti
sarva viṣayam sarvathāviṣayam akramam ca iti viveka jam jñānam
kāṣṭhā prāptam jñānam deva ṛṣi gandharva ādīnām
iti ucyate iti
na anyena upadeṣṭam śakyam na api upadeśena yathāvat grahītum śakyate
yasmāt tat sarva vastu viṣayam
na asya kiṃcid aiṣayībhūtam
sarvathā viṣayam ca sarvam atīta anāgata pratyutpannam sarva prayāyaiḥ sarva viśeṣaṇaiḥ sarvathā sarveṇa prakāreṇa jānāti
akramam eka kṣaṇa upārūḍham
ekasmin kṣaṇe sarvam sarvathā gṛhṇāti
na asat ādi vat krameṇa
tat etat viveka jam jñānam paripūrṇam asya eva aṃśaḥ yoga pradīpaḥ
saḥ eva jñāna aṃśaḥ yogaḥ ca pradīpaḥ ca
yogasya vā pradīpaḥ yoga pradīpaḥ
madhumatīm bhūmim upādāya ārabhya yāvat asya viveka jasya jñānasya parisamāptiḥ tāvat
viveka ja jñāna prisamāpti paryantāni jñānāni monojavat tva ādi yuktāni asya eva aṃśaḥ
eva tad vairāgya anantaram kaivalyam iti prāptam atas āha prāpta viveka jñānasya aprāpta viveka jñānasya vā bāhya darśana nivṛttau kaivalyam
katham iti sattva puruṣayoḥ śuddhi sāmye kaivalyam iti
yadā tamaḥ malam puruṣa anyatā pratyaya mātram anyatā mātra pratyaya vaibhava yuktam dagdha kleśa bījam vinivṛtta avidyā pratyaya vāsanā rūpam buddhi sattvam bhavati tadā puruṣasya śuddhi sārūpyam iva āpannam
yadi api triguṇam puruṣa vilakṣaṇam puruṣaḥ ca tad vilakṣaṇaḥ tathā api puruṣa anya tā pratyaya pariṇāmi tvāt śuddhi sārūpyam iva āpannam iti ucyate
etasyām avasyāyām kaivalyam bhavati īśvarasya anīśvarasya vā viveka jñāna bhāginaḥ itarasya vā
yasmāt ubhayoḥ avidyā nivṛttiḥ eva kāraṇam tasmāt
na hi dagdha kleśa bījasya jñāne kācid apekṣā
yatas samyak darśī sarvam triguṇam iti manyate triguṇaḥ ca pratyayaḥ heyaḥ iti madhumatī ādi jñāne tasya na kadācid api apekṣā
yat tu yoga jñānam aiśvaryam ca uktam tat samyak darśana artha anukrānta sattva śuddhi pada mārgeṇa prakrāntam ānuṣaṅgikam
paramārthataḥ tu jñānāt adarśanam vinivartate
tasmin vinivṛtte na santi ukta kleśāḥ asmitā ādayaḥ
teṣām avidyā kṣetra tvāt
kleśa abhāvāt ca karma vipāka abhāavaḥ kleśa mūlaḥ sati mūle tad vipākaḥ iti hi pratipāditam
tasmāt samyak darśana artham eva idam śāstram na jñāna aiśvarya vibhūti prayojanam
carita adhikārāḥ ca etasyām avasthāyām guṇāḥ
na puruṣasya punar dṛśya tvena ātiṣṭhante
tat puruṣasya kaivalyam
tadā puruṣaḥ sva rūpa mātra jyotiḥ iti amalaḥ kevalībhavati iti
iti śabdaḥ samāpti arthaḥ
iti śrī govanda bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī śaṅkarabhagavataḥ kṛtau pātañjala yoga sūtra bhāṣya vivaraṇe
vibhūti pādaḥ tṛtīyaḥ
prathame pāde samādhiḥ prādhānyena nirdiṣṭaḥ
dvitīye tad sādhanāni vyākhyātāni
tṛtīye tu samyak darśana artha yogāṅga anuṣṭhāna anuṣaṅga jñāna aiśvarya anukramaṇam kṛtam
tat ca sarvam duḥkhasya iti jaigīṣa vyakhyānena pratipāditam
duḥkha hānam ca ātyantika guṇa uparamaḥ iti uktam tathā eva tad vairāgyāt api doṣa bīja kṣaye kaivalyam prāpta viveka jñānasya aprāpta viveka jñānasya vā sattva puruṣayoḥ śuddhi sāmye kaivalyam iti anantaram uktam
tat ca kaivalyam pratipakṣa nirvartanena pratipādanīyam iti idam kaivalya pāda anukramaṇam kriyate
tathā aneka janmāntara uparjita vāsanā uddheda prakārāḥ ca kaivalya artham eva pradarśanīyāḥ
tathā kaivalya upayogi samādhi siddhi stuti artham pūrvatra anuktam siddhi antaram prakriyate
talya jātīyānām anyatama nindanena anyatama stutiḥ bhavati
tatra dhyāna jam anāśayam karma śukla akṛṣṇam yoginaḥ trividham itareṣām iti vakṣyamāṇena stuti artha tā āviṣkariṣyate
janma auṣadhi mantra tapaḥ samādhi jāḥ siddhayaḥ
deha antaritā yathā yoga ādinā deha antareṣu svarga ādiṣu janma siddhiḥ
oṣadhibhiḥ asura bhavaneṣu rasāyanena soma āmalaka ādi bhakṣaṇena pūrva deha anapanayena eva
mantraiḥ upajpyamānaiḥ ākāśagamana ādi
tapasā saṃkalpa siddhiḥ kāmarūpī yatra kāma gamane iti evamādiḥ
samādhi jāḥ siddhayaḥ pūrvam eva vyākhyātāḥ
tatra siddhiḥ kāya karaṇānām utkarṣaḥ
janma siddhau tu patita pūrva upārjita kārya karaṇasya śarīra antaram upādāyiṣyate iti na asti tatra saṃśayaḥ
apatita śarīrasya tu jāti antara pariṇāme kim tat eva kārya karaṇam upādānam uta anyat api iti tatra kāya indriyāṇām anya jāti pariṇatānām jāti antara pariṇāmaḥ prakṛti āpūrāt
pūrva pariṇāma apāye samavasthitānām eva pūrva kārya karaṇānām uttara pariṇāma upajanaḥ apūrva avayava anupraveśena bhavati
kasmāt alpa parimāṇasya upādānaya mahā parimāṇa kārya anupapatteḥ
na hi daśa palāt tapanīya piṇḍāt aśīti palā patrī janiṣyate kāya indriya prakṛtayaḥ svam svam vikāram kāyam indriyam vā anugṛhnanti āpūrṇa dharma ādi nimittam ādi grahaṇāt adharmam api nimittam apekṣamāṇāḥ
dharma ādi nimittam apekṣamāṇāḥ svam svam vikāram anugṛhṇānti iti uktam
dharma ādi nimittam prakṛtīnām prayojanam kim vā na iti tat āha nimittam aprayojakam prakṛtīnām varaṇa bhedaḥ tu tatas kṣetrika vat
na hi dharma ādi nimittam prayojakam prakṛtīnām
kasmāt na hi kāryeṇa dharma ādinā nimittena kāraṇam kārya karaṇa pratirūpam pravartyate
katham tarhi varaṇa bhedaḥ tu tatas dharma ādi nimittāt bhavati
kṣetrika vat
yathā kṣetrikaḥ kedārāt apām pūrṇāt kedāra antaram piplāvayiṣuḥ na apaḥ pāṇinā apakarṣati
āvaraṇam tu tāsām bhinatti
tasmin bhinne svayam eva apaḥ kedāra antaram āplāvayanti
tathā dharmaḥ prakṛtīnām āvaraṇam adharmam bhinatti
dharmam adharmaḥ api bhinatti āvaraṇam
tasmin bhinne svayam eva prakṛtayaḥ svam svam vikāram āplāvayanti pūrayanti
yathā vā saḥ eva kṣetrikaḥ tasmin eva kedāre na prabhavati audakān bhaumān vā rasān dhānya mūlāni anupraveśāyitum
kim tu mudga tinduka gavī śruka śyāmāka ādīn tasmāt dhānya mūlāt apakarṣati
apakṛṣṭeṣu teṣu svayam eva rasāḥ dhānya mūlāni anuviśanti
tathā dharmaḥ nivṛtti mātre kāraṇam adharmasya
adharmaḥ api dharmasya
śuddhi aśuddhyoḥ atyanta virodhāt
na tu prakṛti pravṛttau dharmaḥ hetuḥ bhavati iti
yadā tu yogī bahūn kāyān nirmīte tadā kim eka manaskāḥ te bhavanti atha aneka manaskāḥ iti samādhi siddhau kaścid anuktaḥ viśeṣaḥ ucyate nirmāṇa citta anya smitā mātrāt
saḥ haṅkāram citta kāraṇam upādāya nirmāṇa cittāni nirmitāni cittāni aprakṛtāni īśvara cittāni navāni karoti yogī
citta grahaṇam udāharaṇa mātram
indriyāṇi api asmitā mātrāt eva
tatas te sa cittāḥ sa karaṇāḥ ca bhavantiu
citta indriya abhāve ca mṛta deśīyaḥ kāyaḥ nirarthakaḥ syāt
eka citta tve tu guṇa pradhāna bhāvaḥ pravṛtti bhedaḥ ca na upakalpate
tatra vibhu tvāt eka kṣetrajña tve api bahu kāya ārambhi tvam upapadyate
guṇa apradhāna aneka pravṛtti bheda artham tu karaṇa bhedaḥ eṣitavyaḥ
kecid tu kṣetrajñāḥ api anye pratikāya bhedam bhavanti iti manvate
kecid atra codaytanti akṛta abhyāgamam
anye tu tad anurūpa upārjita karmāṇaḥ kṣetrajñāḥ bhavanti iti parihāram āhuḥ
yadi evam bahūnām cittānām eka citta abhiprāya purassarā pravṛttiḥ iti
tatra ucyate pravṛtti bhede prayojakam cittam ekam
pravṛtti bhede sati api sava cittānām prayojakam cittam ekam phala adhikṛta deśīyam śarīra antare nirmimīte
tat ca yogi buddhim anuvartate
anyāni ca nirmāṇa cittāni bhinna aneka pravṛttīni tad nāyaka citta anuvartīni bhavanti
tatas ca teṣām pravṛttiḥ nivṛttiḥ apekṣā iti evamādi pravṛtti bhedaḥ upapadyate
rāha prakṛti pravṛtti bheda vat
evam ekacitta abhiprāya puraḥsarā ca pravṛttiḥ avakalpate
tatra dhyāna jam anāśayam
pañcavidham nirmāṇa cittam janma aiṣadhi mantra tapaḥ samādhi sāmarthya nirmitam
tatra teṣu yat eva dhyāna jam cittam tat eva anāśayam kleśa karma āśaya apavarjitam
tasya eva na asti āśayaḥ rāga ādi pravṛttiḥ atas na puṇya pāpa abhisaṃbandhaḥ kṣīṇa kleśa tvāt yoginaḥ
kleśa mūlaḥ hi karamāśayaḥ iti uktam
tad abhāvāt ca karma āśaya anupapattiḥ
apareṣām tu janma ādi siddhānām karama āśayaḥ akṣīṇa kleśa tvāt vidyate eva
kutas etat yoginaḥ eva na karama āśayaḥ itareṣām tu asti iti
yatas karma a śukla a kṛṣṇam yoginaḥ trividham itareṣām
siddha asiddha sāmānya viṣayam idam sūtram
nanu ca pūrva sūtram api sāmānya viṣayam eva
na
samādhi siddhi stuti artha tvāt
sāmānya viṣaya tve tu samādhi siddhi stutiḥ anupapannā syāt
siddhi parisaṃkhyānena tu viśeṣa viṣaya tve tulya jātīya janma ādi siddhi catuṣṭaya sāvadya tva saṃkīrtanāt samādhi siddheḥ stutiḥ upapadyate
kim ca janma ādi siddhi sādhanānām kaivalya arthatā pratiṣedhaḥ ca arthāt iti viśiṣṭa viṣayam eva pūrva sūtram
idam tu sāmānya viṣayam eva pūrva sūtra hetu tvena upādānāt
catuṣpadī khalu ayam karma jātiḥ
kṛṣṇā durātmanām śāstra mārga ativarti duṣṭa cetasām aśuddhatarā
yā tu bahis sādhana sādhyā jāyā putra paśu yājaka ādi niṣpādyā sā śukla kṛṣṇā
kā sau yatra anugraha dvāreṇa karma āśaya pracayaḥ sā kleśa bāhulaka niṣpāda nyatvāt kṛṣṇā ca śuklā ca
nanu jyotiṣṭoma ādi karma śāstra samadhigata tvāt na kṛṣṇam śuklam eva tu tat
atra ucyate na kāmyaiḥ anaikāntika tvāt
tāni eva ca artha anartha ubhaya kāraṇāni
atha tat phalasya svarga ādeḥ abhimata tvāt artha tvam eva iti ced na para dāra abhimarśanasya api vāñchita tvāt artha tva prasaṅgāt
atha para dāra abhisaraṇa ādau abhyugra doṣa sampātāt pratiṣiddha tvāt ca rāga āgi niyoga pravṛtteḥ ca asamānam iti ced na tatra api samāna tvāt
kāma ātma tā niṣedhāt aniṣṭa yogaḥ ca
janma maraṇayoḥ abhyugra doṣa bhūtayoḥ avaśyam bhāvi tvāt iṣṭa aniṣṭa dvaya hetu tvam eva
sa ca aniṣṭa yogaḥ para pīḍā ādeḥ iti avasīyate
tat pratiṣedha upapatteḥ
avaśyam hi janma maraṇa dvayena vinā svarga ādi phalam upabhoktum na śakyam
tat ced asti tasya duḥkha rūpa tvāt āyātam tarhi jyotiṣṭoma ādīnām ubhaya ātmaka tvam
atha karma antaram eva pratiṣiddham janma maraṇa ārambha kāraṇam iti ced na tad bhāva bhāvi tvāt
tasmin hi sati janma maraṇa bhāvāt
atha tu bhavat pakṣe nityam eva kurvīta na janma maraṇe pravarteyātām
kurvataḥ eva te bhavataḥ na a kurvataḥ
tasmāt nityā nimitta tvam avagamyate
kim ca yena janma maraṇam ārapsyate svarga ādau tat karma yadi janma antara gatam tatra anirmokṣa prasaṅgaḥ
kāmya pratiṣiddha akriyāyām api pūrva janma kṛta phalasya avaśya prāpaṇīya tvāt
atha prāktana janma karma kṣaya arthāni nityāni iti ced tat na niyama anupapatteḥ
aniṣṭa phalāni eva ārabdha kāryāṇi pūrva karmāṇi na tu iṣṭa phalāni iti na nityantum śakyate
adṛṣṭa phaleṣu hi satsu nityāni eva kurvataḥ api mokṣa anupapattiḥ janma ārambhi tvam ca
tatas iṣṭānām api ubhaya hetu tvam siddham
bāhya sādhanānām karmaṇām pīḍā anugraha rūpa tvāt
na vai khalu api nityena pūrva kṛta karmaṇām iṣṭānām jyotiṣṭoma ādīnām nivṛttiḥ upakalpate
virodha abhāvāt
avirodhaḥ ca ubhaeṣām śuddhi rūpa tvāt
tantra siddheḥ ca
atha api brūyāt de dane ka janma ārabdhāni karmāṇi na anārabdha kāryam avaśiṣyate iti
tathā api pūrva jnma karmaṇā edānīntana janma phala dānena kṣayaṅgata tvāt adhunātana janma niṣpāditānām abhinavānām eva kāmyānām svarga phala janma maraṇa duḥkha ārambhi tvam iti śukla kṛṣṇa rūpa āpattiḥ
tatas ca janma maraṇa duḥkhasya svarga abhidhānāyāḥ prīteḥ ca darśanāt tad kāraṇasya dvi rūpa tvam anumāsyāmahe
tathā ca siddhe pratiṣiddha bhūta hiṃsā caraṇam kratu artham api agnīṣomīya ādau pravartmānam ṛṣṇa rūpam iti anumāsyāmahe kratu arthā api satī hiṃsā aniṣṭa bhūtā eva tārthatām pratipadyate
yat uktam a biśeṣeṇa yat śāstram śirovat iti ca uttaram iti tatra śirovat iti evam jātīyaka dṛṣṭānta asiddha tvam
aviśeṣeṇa yat śāstram iti tu homa svarūpasya virodhāt bādhya bādhaka tvam upapadyate
hiṃsāyāḥ tu virodha abhāvāt ubhayoḥ hetu tvam bhojanasya iva sukha śarīra sthiti dvaya hetu tvam
yathā ca tīrtha snānasya hlādā dṛṣṭa artha tvam tathā hiṃsā api aniṣṭa phala tvam a parityajantī mahā phalam kratum na eva na abhinirvartayati
atha bāhya sādhana sādhyam api nityam kevalam kāma saṃyoga abhāvāt śuklam eva iti ced evam ucyate na doṣavat tvena nitya kāmyānām aviśeṣāt
yathā kāminaḥ kāmyāni iti kāma saṃyogena kāmyānām doṣavat tvam evam kāma ādi hetu bhūta avidyā doṣavat tvam aviśiṣṭam iti nityānām api ubhaya ātmaka tvam eva
avidyāvat tvam ca nityeṣu pravṛttasya prāyaścitta nimitta utpatteḥ avaśyam bhāvi tvāt
api ca a viduṣaḥ eva sarvam karma
viduṣaḥ karma anutpatteḥ
vidvān hi puruṣaḥ svarūpa avasthāna vyatirekeṇa phalam na abhimanyate
sva rūpa mātra avasthānam ca samasta vyāpāra virāmeṇa pravartate
na ca evam viduṣaḥ kriyā uṣṭhānam ghaṭate
na hi jala mārga abhiprasthāna sādhanam nāvā ādikam anutiṣṭhati
nanu na ca nitya kāmyayoḥ evam satya viśeṣaḥ syāt
atrā ucyate karma mātra nivṛtti prayojana tvāt nityānām adoṣaḥ
yaḥ hi kāmyāt vinivṛttaḥ tasya bahulam karmaṇām kāma rahitena śuddhena kartrā kṛta tvāt ati śuddha phala tvam śukla tva bahu tvāt ca saṃskāra artha tvam
api ca kāma nivṛttiḥ eva mahat phalam
kim ca nityam kurvataḥ kim artham karomi kim vā asya phalam ke vā asya anuṣṭhāne doṣāḥ iti samyak darśana rūpaḥ parāmarśaḥ jāyate iti nityasya asti viśeṣaḥ
śukla jṛṣṇa ātmaka tvam tu aviśiṣṭam ubhayeṣām api karmaṇām
bāhya sādhana sādhanīya tvena para pīḍā upapatteḥ
iti tasmāt ucyate
śuklā karmajātiḥ tapas svādhyāyānavatām
sā hi kevale manasi āyatta tvāt abahis sādhanā bāhya sādhāna anapekṣā na parān pīḍayitvā bhavati
aśukla akṛṣṇā saṃnyāsinām kṣīṇa kleśānām caram adehānām
eṣām ārabdha eka śarīrāṇām a śuklā saṃnyāsāt a kṛṣṇā ca an upāānāt a karaṇāt
na api śukla kṛṣṇa vimiśrāḥ bāhya saṃnyāsa anupādānābhyām hetubhyām
tathā ca uktam aniṣṭam iṣṭam miśram ca trividham karmaṇaḥ phalam
bhavati yoginām pretya na tu saṃnyāsinām kvacid
iti
itareṣām tu bhūtānām janma auṣadhi mantra tapaḥ siddhānām anyeṣām ca trividham śuklam kṛṣṇam miśram ca pūrvam iva yathā dvitīye pāde kleśa mūlaḥ ityādau
kaivalyasya prastuta tvāt tasya ca prativandha hetavaḥ kleśāḥ karmāṇi ca vyākhyātavyāḥ kleśānām tu vyāpāraḥ pratipakṣaḥ nivṛttiḥ ca teṣām vistareṇa vyākhyātāḥ
evam karmaṇām api vāsanānām tulya vyāpāra avasthāna pratipakṣa nivṛttayaḥ nirvarṇanīyāḥ iti atas uttarāṇi sūtrāṇi ārabhyante yatas tad nivṛtau kaivalyam upapadyate na anyathā
tatas tad vipāka anuguṇānām evā abhivyaktiḥ vāsanānām
tatas tasmāt trividhāt ukta lakṣaṇāt kṛṣṇa śukla vimiśra rūpāt karmaṇaḥ pravipacyamānāt hetu bhūtāt tad vipaka anuguṇānām tasya eva karmaṇaḥ vipākaḥ phalam tad anuguṇānām tad anurūpāṇām tādṛśīnām eva vāsanānām abhivyaktiḥ
etat uktam bhavati deva tiryak manuṣya vipāka hetuṣu karmasu madhye yad jātīyasya karmaṇ yādṛśaḥ vipākaḥ tasya vipākasya anuguṇāḥ vāsanāḥ tat karma vipākam anuśarete anūtpadyante tāsām eva abhivyaktiḥ
tad sadṛśena karma vipākena saṃskṛta tvāt
yathā sadṛśīm pravilokya vatsaḥ nu dhāvati na anyāsām a tad anuguṇānām abhivyaktiḥ
na hi daivam karma vipacyamānam phala abhimukhībhāvam āpadyamānam nāraka tiryak manuṣa vāsanāḥ abhivyakti nimittam sam bhavati
nimitta naimittakayoḥ pratiniyata anuguṇa tvāt
kim tu daiva anuguṇāḥ eva asya abhivyajyante
nāraka tiryak mānuṣeṣu evam samānaḥ carcaḥ samādhiḥ
nārake karmaṇi vipacyamāne tad karma anuguṇāḥ vāsanāḥ prādurbhavanti
tathā tairyagyona karmaṇi vipacyamāne tad vipāka anurūpāḥ vāsanāḥ vyajyante
tathā mānuṣe api samānaḥ nyāyaḥ
na hi sva vipāka sadṛśīḥ an upādāya vāsanāḥ tasya tasya karmaṇaḥ vipākaḥ saṃbhavati
nā api vāsanānām ātma niṣpādaka vipāka ārambhi karma tulya rūpāṇi karmāntarāṇi vipāka abhimukhāni antareṇa abhivyaktiḥ
evam karmaṇām vāsanānām ca paraspara hetu hetamat bhāvaḥ
tatra vāsanānām aneka jāti kāla deśa vyavadhānena davīyasīnām ānantaryam vipacyamānena karmaṇā saha nā asti
yathā davīyasām mitra sva jana ādinām
yathā eva ca nedīyasī vāsanā paṭīyasī na tathā daviyasī paṭīyamānam āsīdati
tasmāt nityā na asti davīyasīnām ānantaryam vāsanānām
tad abhāve ca ayam doṣaḥ prāpnoti yathā kalpa śāta antaritaḥ vṛṣadaṃśa vipākaḥ bhaviṣyataḥ daiva vipākaḥ
tatra nedīyasī daiva vāsanā viruddha tvāt vṛṣadaṃśa vipāka abhivyakti hetutām na pratipadyate
kalpa śata vyavahitānām api vṛṣadaṃśa vāasnānām viprakarṣāt an upādāne vṛṣadaṃśa vipāka hetoḥ karmaṇaḥ vipākaḥ na avakalpeta
tatas ca karmaṇām vāsanānām ca ānarthakyam prasajyeta iti
atrā ucyate jāti deśa kāla vyavahitānām api ānantaryam smṛti saṃskārayoḥ eka rūpa tvāt
vṛṣadaṃśa vipāka ādayaḥ sva karma vyañjaka añjanāḥ vyañjakena svena karmaṇā vyajyamānāḥ yadi jāti śatena vā duradeśatayā vā kalpa samasreṇa vā vyavahitāḥ
nanu ca jāti vyavadhānena eva kāla viprakarṣaḥ uktaḥ kim kāla grahaṇena ucyate bhūyaṃsi janmāni divase ekasmin api kṣudra jantu prabhṛtīnām keṣāṃcid bhavanti
na tatra atīta kāla viprakarṣaḥ iti kāla grahaṇam
teṣu vṛṣadaṃśa vipāka ādayaḥ pūrvam api sva vyañjaka nirvartitāḥ santaḥ punar ca sva vyañjaka añjana udayāḥ drāk iti eva kṣipram eva vṛṣadaṃśa vipāka abhisaṃskṛtāḥ vāsanāḥ upādāya abhibyajyante
kasmāt evam yatas vyavahitānām api āsām sadṛśam karma abhivyañjakam nimittībhūtam iti
na hi balīvarda vipāka abhivyakti kāraṇam karma vṛṣadaṃśa vāsanā abhivyakti nimittam bhavati
visadṛśa tvāt
anurūpam hi nimittam abhivyañjakam
āmla ādi kṣaṇa darśane jihvā sravati
tasmāt ānantaryam eva vāsanānām
yatas tāsām vyañjakam tulyam
tathā ca sati na ca āsanānām nedīyaḥ tāḥ davīyaḥ tāḥ vā samāna citta āśraya tvāt
kutas ca ayam api aparaḥ hetuḥ ānantaryasya smṛti saṃskārayoḥ eka rūpa tvāt iti
pūrvam tulya jātīyam karma abhivyañjakam vāsanā ānantarya hetuḥ uktaḥ
idānīm ayam anyaḥ ucyate yathā anubhavāḥ tathā saṃskārāḥ
yādṛśāḥ pratyayāḥ tathā vāsanāḥ
te ca saṃskārāḥ vāsanā rūpāḥ
yathā vasanāḥ smṛtayaḥ iti
tathā ca uktam grāhya uparaktaḥ pratyayaḥ grāhya grahaṇa ubhaya ākāra nirbhāsaḥ ityādi
jāti deśa kāla vyavahitebhyaḥ saṃskārebhyaḥ smṛtayaḥ
smṛtibhyaḥ ca punar saṃskāraḥ iti evam ete smṛti saṃskārāḥ karma āśaya vṛttilābha vaśa ābeśāt abhivyajyante
karma āśayasya api vṛttilābhaḥ deśa ādi nimitta apekṣayā iti pratipāditam
atas ca vyavahitānām api nimitta naimittika bhāva anucchedāt ānantaryam eva
yādṛśaḥ saṃskāraḥ tādṛśī smṛtiḥ
pratiniyata vyañjaka tvāt ca tayoḥ na viprakarṣaḥ kāraṇam
yatas kalpa śata vyavahitāt api saṃskārāt eva tulya jātīyā smṛtiḥ iti ānantaryam eva siddham
ā udānīm vāsanānām anādi tvena vipāka nirvartaka tvam abhidarśayati saṃskārasya ca anādi tvam ekaikasya ca asaṅkhya yoni gamanam vairāgya pratipatti artham pratipādayati tāsām anādi tvam ca āśiṣaḥ nitya tvāt
tāsām vāsanānām āśiṣaḥ nitya tvāt anādi tvam
yā iyam ātma āśīḥ maraṇam mā nu bhūt iti evam āśīḥ vā bhūyasam iti sarvasya dṛśyate
svābhāvikī sva rasa pravṛttā api nirūḍhā api
kasmāt jāta mātrasya an annubhūta janana maraṇa dharmasya dveṣa anusmṛti nimittaḥ duḥkha anusmṛti hetukaḥ vā maraṇa trāsaḥ katham bhavvet na hi kathañcana duḥkha smaraṇa ādi nimitta upādānam svābhāvikasya upapadyate
na ca svābhāvikam vastu nimittam upādatte
na hi jvalanasya uṣṇa tvam svābhāvikam sat ātmīya kārye nimittam īkṣeta
na ca ananubhūte viṣaye smṛtiḥ iṣṭe niṣṭe vā kasyacid upaploṣyate
anubhūta priya an anusmaraṇe na ca tad viṣya vāñdhā
tathā anubhūta apriya ananusmaraṇe na tad viṣayaḥ dveṣaḥ trāsaḥ ca loke paridṛśyate
tathā ca yaḥ yaḥ jātaḥ tasya tasya iha janmani ananubhūta janma maraṇasya janma anantaram eva ātma āśīḥ abhidṛśyate
tasmāt tad āśīḥ itya tvāt pūrva janma maraṇa anubhavaḥ numīyate
tatas pūrvaḥ tatas api pūrvaḥ iti smṛti saṃskārāṇām tad kāraṇānām ca janma maraṇa anubhavānām anādi tvam anumimīmahe
tathā eva ekaikasya prāṇabhṛtaḥ neka yoni gamana siddhiḥ
evam etāḥ vāsanāḥ duravahānāḥ a vihānīyāḥ
kutas evam yasmāt anādi vāsanā anuviddham cittam idam nimitta vaśāt karma nimitta vaśāt kāścid eva ca āsanāḥ pravipacyamāna karma tulya jātīya kriyāḥ vipāka abhi na niṣpāditāḥ pratilabhya puruṣasya bhogāya upāvartate yāvat avasita adhikāram iti
tat etat cittam ghaṭa prāsāda pradīpa kalpam saṃkoca vikāsi hasti maśaka ādi śarīra parimāṇa ākaram yathā dīpaḥ ghaṭa prāsāda ādiṣu
tat evam apare pratipannaḥ
tatra ca yuktam āha tathā ca iti
tathā ca saṃkoca vikāsi tve ca antra abhāvaḥ maraṇāt uttara kālam janmanaḥ ca prāk etasmin antarāle bhavati iti antara abhāvaḥ saṃsaraṇam sañcaraṇ yena sañcarati tat api śarīram ātivāhikam cittasya avibhu tve yuktam iti bruvanti
vṛttiḥ eva asya vibhunaḥ cittasya saṅkoca vikāsinī iti ācāryāḥ
ācārya grahaṇam upapattimat tvāt pūjā artham
cittasya sthitiḥ gatiḥ ca pariṇāmi tvāt vibhu tve pi indriyāṇām ca upapadyate yoginām ca vikarana bhāvaḥ sarvajña tvam vibhu tve ghaṭate
na ca upabhoga śūnyasya ātivāhika śarīrasya kalpanāyām asti pramāṇam
caśa viṣāṇa vat an upalabhyamāna tāt
na ha vai sa śarīrasya sataḥ priya apriyayoḥ apahatiḥ asti iti śruteḥ
tathā atha yaḥ ha etān anantān upāste iti śrutiḥ karaṇa vyāpi tvam khyāpayati
tat ca saṃkoca vikāsi tvam vṛtteḥ dharma ādi nimitta apekṣam
nimittam ca dvidhā bāhyam ādhyātmikam ca śarīra ādi sādhana apekṣam bāhyam stuti abhivādana ādi karma
kim punar ādhyātmikam āha kevala citta mātra adhīnam śraddhā ādi
tathā ca uktam ye vā ete maitrī ādayaḥ dhyāyinām vihārāḥ vitta vyāpārāḥ veṣṭāni te bāhya sādhana niranugrahāḥ bāhya sādhana nirapekṣāḥ kevala citta mātra nirvṛttāḥ prakṛṣṭam dharmam abhinirvartayanti
tayoḥ bāhya ādhyātmikayoḥ nimittayoḥ mānasam ādhyātmikam maitrī ādi citta abhiniṣpannam nimittam balīyaḥ
katham iti jñāna vairāgye kena atiśyyete na kena api iti arthaḥ

daṇḍaka araṇyam citta bala vyatirekeṇa kaḥ kartum śaknoti
kaḥ ca pibet samudram agastya vat iti
atas mānasa balam eva balam
na śārīram
tasmāt mānasam paramam vadanti iti śruteḥ tathā ca bhagavān ābhāṣe śreyān dravya mayāt yajñāt jñāna yajñaḥ parantapa
sarvam karma akhilam pārtha jñāne parisamāpyate
R ṅ
iti
katham punar tāsām vāsanānām nivṛttiḥ
an ādi rūḍha tvāt na nivṛttiḥ āsām
na ca tad nivṛttim antareṇa kaivalya upapattiḥ iti atas ucyate hetu phalaka āśraya ālambanaiḥ saṃgṛhīta tvāt eṣām abhāve tad abhāvaḥ
hetuḥ ca phalam ca āśrayaḥ ca ālambanam ca hetu phala āśraya ālambanāni
taiḥ saṃgṛhīta tvāt upagrathita tvāt eṣām hetu ādīnām abhāve tad abhāve vāsanānām abhāvaḥ
tasmāt upapadyate vāsanānām nivṛttiḥ
kaḥ sau hetuḥ iti āha dharmaḥ tāvat avidhā vinamita cetasām
tatas dharmāt sukham
sukha anuśayī rāgaḥ
evam avidyātaḥ eva adharmaḥ
tatas duḥkham
duḥkha anuśayī dveṣaḥ
tatas sukha upārjane duḥkha parihāre ca pūrvavat eva prayatnaḥ
tena prayatnena vācā kāyena parispandamānaḥ param anugṛhṇāti upahanti ca
punar ca tatas para anugraha para pīḍanābhyām dharma adharmau
tābhyām sukha duḥkhe
tābhyām ca rāga dveṣau pūrvavat eva
tatas prayatnaḥ
iti evam anavarata prārabdha paribhramaṇam pravṛttim idam ṣaṣ aram saṃsāra cakram
asya ca pratikṣaṇam āvartamānasya avidyā netrī ratha cakasya turaṅga yuvatiḥ iva
sā mūlam sarva kleśānām iti yat etat a vidhā netṛkam ṣaṣ aram cakram eṣa hetuḥ vāsanānām
etat cakra āvṛtti kṛtāḥ hi tāḥ
avidyāyāḥ tu abhāve viśīrṇa nābhi bandhanam iva cakram dharma ādi hetu cakram api viśīryate
tat viśareṇa ca cakra āvṛtti kṛta janmanām vāsanānām akārya kṣama tvam
phalam tu yam artham āśritya yasya pratytpanna tā tat tasya phalam
tat api vāsanānām saṃgrāhakam
tad abhāve vāsanā abhivyakti abhāvāt
sukha ādi phalasya vāsanā ādhāyi tvāt
na hi apūrva upajanaḥ
na atyantam asat utpadyate
manaḥ sādhikāram kartavyatāvat na puruṣa artha śūnyam
kṛta puruṣa artha svarūpa jñānam vinivṛtta avidyākam iti sa adhikāram āśrayaḥ vāsanānām
tat āśritya hi hetu cakra paribhramaṇam
na hi avasita adhikāre karaṇīya puruṣa artha śūnye manasi nirāśrāyāḥ vāsanāḥ sthātum utsahante
yat abhimukhībhūtam vastu yām vāsanām vyankti tasyāḥ tat ālambanam
evam hetu phala āśraya ālambaniḥ etaiḥ saṃgṛhītāḥ sarvāḥ vāsāaḥ
teṣām hetu ādīnām abhāve tad saṃśrāyāṇām api vāsanānām abhāvaḥ chatra abhāve chāyā nivṛtti vat
eṣām ca abhāva upāyaḥ dvitīya pāde vyākhyātaḥ
tasmāt na ca āsanā samyak darśane sati kaivalya prativandhinī
bhavati eva avidyā anvṛttau kaivalyam iti
nanu ca eṣām abhāve tad abhāvaḥ iti uktam
tathā ca asiddhāntahānniḥ
katham evam hi siddhāntaḥ na asti asataḥ sambhavaḥ utpattiḥ
na ca asti sataḥ vināśaḥ iti
atha punar santi vāsanāḥ tadā dravya tvena vastu satyaḥ sambhavantyaḥ katham nivartiṣyante
na eva nirvartiṣyante iti arthaḥ
tatra katham uktam eṣām abhāve tad abhāve iti
katham vā kaivalyam anuvṛttāsu vāsanāsu iti atas uttaram paṭhati atīta anāgatam svarūpataḥ sti adhva bhrdāt dharmāṇām
evam vā etat
atha vā siddhānta pakṣeṇa eva na iyam bhāṣyam
katham eṣām abhāve tad abhāvaḥ iti hetu ādīnām vāsanānām ca na atyanta abhāvaḥ ucyate
kasmāt nā asti asataḥ sambhavaḥ na ca asti sataḥ vinācā iti dravya tvena vastu tayā sambhavantyaḥ katham nirvartiṣyante vāsanāḥ
śabda vikalpita tve vāsanāḥ na atyantam nivariṣyante
santi eva atīta svarūpeṇa iti arthaḥ
bhaviṣyat vyaktikam bhaviṣyati vyaktiḥ yasya tat bhaviṣyat vyaktikam
yathā piṇḍa avasthāyām ghaṭa rūpam
pravṛtta itikartavya tā sādhanam tat anāgatam
bhūta vyaktikam atītam bhūtā atikrāntā vyaktiḥ upalabdhi viṣaya tva āpattiḥ yasya
yathā prabhagnaḥ ghaṭaḥ tat atītam iti ucyate
avyaṅgyam abhaviṣyat yasya vyañjane sādhanam upādeyam
anatīta vyaktikam abhūtam
kim tarhi vyāpāri pārūḍham tat vartamānam
yathā ghaṭaḥ sva kriyāyāḥ
trayam ca etat atīta anāgata vartamāna lakṣaṇakam vartamāne dharmiṇi vartamānam dharma rūpam vastu samasta loka viniścita rūpasya avyabhicāriṇaḥ jñānasya pramāṇa bhūtasya jñeyam iti saṅgirāmahe
kasmāt niścita jñāna utpatti viṣaya tvāt
yadi ca etat vastu svarūpataḥ na abhaviṣyat na idam nirviṣayam jñānam udapatsyata
yathā śaśaviṣāṇa ādi niścita jñāna utpatti kāraṇam na bhavati
na ca tathā iha niścita vastu jñāna utpatti viṣaya tvāt
atha vā na avastu viṣayam atīte bhaviṣyati ca ghaṭa ādau jñānam
śabda vikalpita tve sati niścita rūpeṇa utpadyamāna tvāt vartamāna ghaṭa ādi viṣaya jñāna vat
avyabhicārāt ca
liṅga anumeya tvāt ca dhūmena agni ādi jñāna vat
liṅga darśana anantara utpatteḥ vā
yat vā atītam anāgatam ca vastu sat sva rūpeṇa liṅga darśana anantara buddhi viṣaya tvāt prasiddha anumeya vat
tasmāt atīta anāgatam svarūpataḥ sti
kim ca bhoga bhāgīyasya bhoga hitasya yāga ādeḥ apavarga bhāgīyasya vā apavarga hitasya samādhi ādeḥ karmaṇaḥ phalam utpatsu yasya na asti tasya vādinaḥ tat nirupākhyam prāpnoti śaśa viṣāṇa vat
na hi śaśaviṣāṇam bhaviṣyati iti upākhyāyate
na tathā iha
kim tarhi yāhena svargaḥ bhaviṣyati samādhi ādinā mokṣaḥ bhaviṣyati iti ca kuśalaiḥ atikṭhoḥ matibhiḥ upākhyāyate
tasmāt nirupākhya tvāt tad uddeśena phala uddeśena
nirupākhya tvāt tena phalena nimittena kuśala anujñānam idam kuru bhaviṣyati ca anena adaḥ iti svayam a pratipadyamānāḥ kuśalāḥ katham īyuḥ upadiśeyuḥ vā
kim ca dṛṣṭa mātra pratipattau ca prāpnoti
kuśalānām vā mithyā pratipattiḥ akuśalāḥ samīcīna darśanāḥ iti
kim ca abhāva jñānāt kuśalāḥ api phalāya na abhisamīheran
abhāva aviśeṣāt ca kāraṇa niyamaḥ na akalpiṣyata
na sarvatas vā sarvam udapatsyata
na api kāraṇam upādāsyata
upādāne vā taila arthī saikatam api upādāsyata kim kilaiḥ aneka āyāsa niṣpādyaiḥ
atyanta asat apūrvam ca idam ajaniṣyata
na ca etat dṛṣṭam
tasmāt tat bhoka bhāgīyam apavarga bhāgīyam vā karma nimittam kāraṇam vidyamānasya eva tasya phalasya vartamānīkaraṇe samartham na apūrva upajane
siddham hi svena ātmanā nimittam sthālī kṣīra dharma ātañjana ādi dadhi ādikasya naimittakasya karkaśatara bhāva ādi abhivyakti dvāreṇa viśeṣa anugraham kurute na apūrvam eva dadhi utpādayati tathā iha bhogabhāgīya ādi karma
kim ca dharmī ca aneka dharma svabhāvaḥ neka dharma ātmā
yathā kanaka piṇḍaḥ śānta udita avyapadeśya rucaka kuṇḍala ādi dharma ātmakaḥ
tasya dharmiṇaḥ adhva bhedena atīta ādi lakṣaṇa bhedena dharmāḥ pratyavasthitāḥ
yathā vartamānam vastu vyakti viśeṣa āpannam kuṇḍala ādi vyakti prāptam dravyataḥ kārya rūpataḥ asti vyāpāra adhirūḍha tayā na evam atītam anāgatam ca
kim tarhi svena eva vyaṅyena sva rūpeṇabhaviṣyatā an āatam asti
svena ca anubhūta vyaktikena atikrānta upalabdhikena atītam asti
vartamānasya eva tu adhvanaḥ svarūpataḥ vyaktiḥ iti na sā vyaktiḥ bhavati atīta anāgatayoḥ adhvanoḥ
ekasya ca adhvanaḥ samaye kāle dvau adhvānau dharmi samanvāgātau virodhāt na bhavataḥ eva iti
tathā ca uktaḥ dhva saṃkara parihāraḥ
yasya punar atītam anāgatam ca lakṣaṇam sva rūpeṇa na asti tasya dharmāṇām adhva bhedaḥ na prāpnoti
katham na hi tasya ghaṭaḥ bhaviṣyan atītaḥ vā vidyate
na hi kapālāni piṇḍaḥ vā a ghaṭaḥ
atas ca vartamānaḥ eva ghaṭaḥ tītaḥ na āgataḥ iti ca ucyeta piṇḍa kapālayoḥ aghaṭa tvāt mṛdi ca ghaṭasya abhāvāt bhaviṣyati ghaṭaḥ tītaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti ca piṇḍa kapāle nirucyeyātām
tathā ca vivakṣataḥ gauḥ api syāt aśvaḥ api gauḥ iti
atha ucyeta ghaṭasya pragabhāva pradhvaṃsa abhāvau atīta anāgata tvena abhidhīyete iti
tatas api eṣa vastu vācinā śabdena na agataḥ iti ca abhāvasya abhidhānam yujyate
na api niyamaḥ upapadyate
ghaṭena eva vyapadiśyate ghaṭaḥ u tītaḥ ghaṭaḥ bhaviṣyati iti ca
na punar kulāla ādibhiḥ apadiśyate kulāla ādayaḥ tītāḥ bhaviṣyanti vā iti
atha ghaṭasya eva tatra anpalabhyamāna tvāt iti ced na hasti śārtula ādīnām api tatra anupalambhe vyapadeśa prasaṅgāt
atha upalabdha pūrvasya eva vyapadeśaḥ iti ced na ghaṭa kriyā ādiṣu api prasaṅgāt
atha ghaṭasya tena kriyā ādi abhāvaḥ iti ced nā abhāvasya sambandha viśeṣa anupapatteḥ
na hi samavāya lakṣaṇaḥ prāpti lakṣaṇaḥ vā sambandhaḥ bhāva abhāvayoḥ avakalpate
yena asau ghaṭasya abhāvaḥ na punar kriyā ādīnām
anyatara sambandhe ca abhāvasya vastu tva prasaṅgaḥ
atha vastu eva iti ced siddhaḥ tarhi bhaviṣyan atītaḥ ca padārthaḥ
atha upacārāt siddha kapāla avasthāḥ avayavāḥ bhaviṣyati ghaṭaḥ bhūtaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti ca āpadiśyeran sambandhāt tat yathā annam prāṇāḥ iti atra api yathā kulāla cakra daṇḍa sūtra ādiṣu ghaṭi na asti tathā piṇḍa kapāleṣu api iti tad abhāva aviśeṣe ca kapāleṣu ghaṭaḥ tītaḥ iti vyapadeśaḥ na kulāla ādiṣu iti niyama anupapattiḥ
na ca api vidyamānānām sādhanānām ghaṭa ādi niṣpādinām api a vidyamānaiḥ utpādyaiḥ ghaṭa ādibhiḥ sambandhaḥ upapadyate
na ca asati sambandhe ghaṭa utpādana abhiprāyeṇa kāraka pravṛttiḥ
atha ayuta siddhaḥ samavāya lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ janyānām kāraṇānām ca na pratiṣidhyate iti ced na yuta siddha ayuta siddha tvasya samāna kāla bhāvinām vastūnām darśanāt
na abhāva abhāvayoḥ kvacid api yuta siddha tvam ayuta siddha tvam vā dṛśyate
tasmāt janya janakānām api sambandha abhyupagamāt vidyamāna tvam eva iti utpatteḥ prāk ūrdhvam ca vidyate kāryam vastu antara sambandhāt
upalapsyamāna tvāt upalabdha tvāt ca apavaraka stha ghaṭa ādi vat
uddiśya kartrā prāpya tvāt deśa antara vat
tathā kartṛ vyāpāra prāpya tvāt ca iti
kim ca na oaukikāḥ atīta anāgata śabdābhyām gagana kamalinī vat a vidyamānam artham pratiyanti pratipādayanti ca nirmokṣaḥ
tasmāt adītam anāgatam ca svarūpataḥ vidyate eva
na a bhūtvā bhāvaḥ trayāṇām adhvanām
kim tarhi vidyamānānām eva abhivyaktiḥ
tasmāt vyakti rūpeṇa vāsanānām atyanta vinivṛttiḥ
guṇa rūpeṇa tu satīnām api kārya asamartha tvāt na kaivalya abhāva doṣaḥ
nā api siddhānta virodhaḥ
atīta anāgata vartamāna dharmāḥ kena punar rūpeṇa santi iti tad pratipādana artham āha te vyakta sūkṣmāḥ guṇa ātmānaḥ
te khalu amī tri adhvānaḥ atīta anāgata vartamāna adhva traya upārūḍhāḥ dharmāḥ vartamānāḥ vartamāna lakṣaṇa upārūḍhāḥ vyakta ātmānaḥ lika pratyaya viṣayībhūta svabhāvāḥ
atīta anāgatāḥ sūkṣma ātmānaḥ loka pratyaya viṣaya bhāvam aprāptāḥ ṣaṣ aviśeṣa svarūpāḥ asmitā ādi svabhāvāḥ
tatas ca vyakta ātmānaḥ ṣoḍaśa vikārāḥ kārya kāraṇa lakṣaṇāḥ
sarvam idam ādhyātmikam kārya kāraṇa rūpam vyakta ātmakam yat ca sūkṣmam a viśeṣa lakṣaṇam asmitā ādi yat ca nirmokṣaḥ liṅga mātram sūkṣma tva aviśeṣāt sarvam idam jagat guṇānām sattva rajaḥ tamasām prakhyā pravṛtti sthiti śīlānām sanniveśa viśeṣa mātram iti paramārthataḥ guṇa ātmānaḥ guṇa svabhāvāḥ
tathā ca śāstra anuśāsanam guṇānām paramam rūpam svam parama artha rūpam an pāya upajana ātmakam ekaikasya
tat ca na dṛṣṭi patham ṛcchati
na dṛṣṭi gocarībhavati
yat tu dṛṣṭa patham prāptam guṇa a parimardena viṣam abhāva kṛta sanniveśa lakṣaṇam tat māyā iva na tu māyā eva asāra tvāt tu māyā vat iti
su tucchakam ati alpam eka deśa mātra pariṇāma tvāt sāmya avasthānām guṇānām
yadā sarve guṇāḥ pṛthivī ādayaḥ tadā katham ekaḥ śabdaḥ śaṅkha ādi janitaḥ
ekam indriyam śrotra ādikam iti eka buddhi ālambana tvam bhavet
na khalu bhavitavyam
triguṇa tvena hi kāraṇena trayaḥ iti syāt
evam indriyṇām ca pratyekam tri tvam
tathā ca niyamaḥ na prāpnoti
na hi grāhya tvam ekasya eva śabdasya grāhaka tvam ca ekasya śrotrasya iti niyam upakalpate
tathā sparśa ādiṣu tvac indriya ādiṣu ca yojyam
niyamaḥ ca dṛśyate
kāraṇam tatra vacanīyam iti āha pariṇāma eka tvāt vastu tattvam
prakhyā pravṛtti sthiti śīlānām guṇānām grahaṇa ātmakānām sattva prādhānyāt boddhā ātmanām asmitā saṃsthānānām karaṇa bhāvena ekaḥ pariṇāmaḥ śrotra indriyam
