yathā viruddhānām taila varti tejasām pradīpaḥ
tathā tvac ādi indriyeṣu prayuktānām ekaikam indriyam pariṇāmaḥ iti yojyam
bhūta antareṣu api yojyam
śabda sparśa rūpa rasānām sneha smāna jātīyānām ekaḥ pariṇāmaḥ rasa tanmātra avayavaḥ jala paramāṇuḥ
teṣām paramāṇunām ekaḥ pariṇāmaḥ jalam
śabda sparśa rūpāṇām uṣṇa tva samāna jātīyānām ekaḥ pariṇāmaḥ tejaḥ paramāṇuḥ
teṣām paramāṇunām ekaḥ pariṇāmaḥ bahniḥ salila indhanaḥ dāru śakala dīpanaḥ ca
tathā śabda sparśayoḥ praṇāmi tva samāna jātīyayoḥ sparśa tanmātra avayavaḥ vāyu paramāṇuḥ ekaḥ pariṇāmaḥ
teṣām paramāṇunām ekaḥ pariṇamāḥ vāyuḥ sapta marut gaṇāḥ ca
tathā śabda tanmātra avayavānām anāvṛtta tva samāna jātīyānām ekaḥ pariṇāmaḥ ākāśaḥ
iti evam uktena mārgeṇa sneha auṣṇya praṇāmi tva ādi upādāya sāmānyam eka vikāra ārambhaḥ samāḍheyaḥ yojyaḥ
tasmāt bahūnām api eka pariṇāmi tvāt eka viṣaya tvam grāhya grahaṇa niyamaḥ ca sarvam upapadyate
nanu ca nā asti eva asau eka pratyaya viṣayaḥ śabda ādiḥ
etat tu sarvam vijñāna parijṛmbhitam eva vijñāna bhāva bhāvi tvāt
katham tad bhāva bhāvi tvam iti āha na asti arthaḥ vijñāna visahacaraḥ pṛthak vijñānāt upalabdhaḥ pṛthak bhāvī vā
vijñānam artha visahacaram pṛthaktvena upalabdham pṛthak bhāvi vā asti
tasmāt arthaḥ vijñāna vyatirekeṇa na asti iti pratijānīmahe
pramāṇam api atra bhavati vijñāna vyatirekeṇa na asti grāhyam vastu vijñāna vyatirekeṇa an upalabhyamāna tvāt vijñāna sva rūpa vat
bāhya artha śūnyāni jāgrat vijñānāni vijñāna tvāt svapna samaya vijñāna vat
vijñāna parikalpitāḥ vā jāgrat viṣayāḥ viṣaya tvāt svapna viṣaya vat
vijñānam vā viṣayāḥ vyatireki vijñāna tvāt svapna vijñāna vat iti
yadi evam syāt kim naḥ chinnam syāt puruṣasya dṛśya viyogāt kaivalyam prastutam na siddham syāt
yathā upalabhyamānasya stambha ādeḥ abhāvaḥ evam upalabhyamāna tvāt vijñānasya api abhāvaḥ
tat abhāve ca liṅga abhāvāt upalabdhuḥ api abhāvaḥ prāpnuyāt iti kasya kaivalyam kena dṛśyena viyogaḥ syāt kena samprayoge vā bandhaḥ pratijñāyeta bandha abhāve ca abhyudaya niḥśreyasa artha pravṛtti phala tā na prasajyeta
kim ca anyat vijñāna vyatirekeṇa arthaḥ na asti iti bruvatā vijñānam arthaḥ iti ca ekaḥ padārthaḥ abhyupagataḥ bhavati yathā agniḥ analaḥ iti
evam ca sati vijñānam grāhyam grāhakam arthaḥ grāhyaḥ grāhakaḥ ca iti nāma mātre vipratipattiḥ na punar ekasya grāhya grāhaka bhāvaḥ pratyākhyāyate
tathā ca sati puruṣasya api grāhya grāhaka bhāvaḥ prāptaḥ
tathā api vipramokṣa anavak
iti evamādayaḥ bhūyāṃsaḥ doṣāḥ prāpnuvanti
tasmāt amuyā diśā anena nyāya ābhāsa balena ye vastu svarūpam apahṇuvate jñāna parikalpanā mātram vastu svapna viṣaya upamam na tu paramārthataḥ asti iti te svayam tathā iti abhyupagamya sva māhātmyena pratupasthitam vastu katham apramāṇa ātmakena vikalpa jñāna balena vastu svayam upagṛhya abhyupagamya tat eva abhyupagatam apalapantaḥ idam iti abhyupetya idam na asti iti apahnuvānāḥ śeaddheya vacanāḥ syuḥ
na hi sva anubhava pratyākhyāyinaḥ śraddhānīya vacana vistārāḥ bhavitum arhanti
tatra vijñāna vyatirekeṇa arthaḥ na asti iti pratyakṣa virodhinī pratijñā
saṃvedanī kārakam vijñānam pratīyāmaḥ
pṛthu budhna ādi ākāram artham pratipadyemahi
grāhakam ca vijñānam avabhāsakam avabhāsanīyaḥ ca arthaḥ
sva lakṣaṇa bhedena artha jñānayoḥ upalabhyamāna tvāt na avyatireka gandhaḥ api
tatas ca vyatirekeṇa anupalabhyamāna tvāt iti asiddhaḥ hetuḥ tava
na ca jñānasya eva pṛthu budhna ādi ākāra tā
jñānasya ekasya avabhāsya avabhāsaka tva anupapatteḥ pradīpasya iva kevalasya
bhinnayoḥ pradīpayoḥ prakāśya prakāśaka tva anupalmbhāt ekasya ca svātmani prāpti asambhavāt evam jñānasya
svapna jñānam api upalabdha artha viṣaya tvāt na nirālaṃbanam
pratijñāyāḥ pratyakṣa virodhaḥ loka virodhaḥ ca
sarvam jñānam sa ālambanam jñāna tvāt prativādi duṣṭa vākya jñānavat sva vākya guṇa jñānavat ca
tatas ca jñāna tva ādīnām evamādibhiḥ anaikāntika tā
kutas ca etat anyāyyam vastu na asti iti vastu sāmye citta bhedāt tayoḥ viviktaḥ panthāḥ
bahu citta ālambanībhūtam aneka citta viṣayībhūtam ekam vastu putra ādikam sādhāraṇam samānam
tat khalu na eka citta tantram bhavati
eka citta tantra tva abhāvāt aneka citta parikalpitam api na bhavati
kin tu sva rūpa pratiṣṭham citta nirapekṣam svatantra tayā vyavasthitam
katham vastu sāmye vastunaḥ putra ādeḥ eka tve citta bhedāt ekasmin putra ādi viṣaye viṣayiṇām jñānānām aneka tvāt
katham citta bhedaḥ iti āha dharma apekṣam cittasya vastu sāmye api yathā putrataḥ eva mātā pitroḥ sukha jñānam bhavati
tatas eva putra ādeḥ adharma apekṣam ahitānām duḥkha jñānam upajaniṣyate
yadi kasyacid cittena parikalpitam abhaviṣyat na anya citta parikalpitena anyeṣām cittam upāraṃkṣyata
na etat yuktam atyanta asaṃbaddhānām adarśanāt
yadi ca anya parikalpitena api anya citta uparāgaḥ bhaviṣyat tadā sarve api sarvam samjñāsyanta
na ca idam dṛṣṭam
tasmāt na citta parikalpitam vastu iti vastu jñānayoḥ grāhya grahaṇa bhedāt bhinnayoḥ viviktaḥ panthāḥ
na anayoḥ saṅkara gandhaḥ api asti
sukha jñāna ālambanībhūtam pur tā ādi vastu na tad jñāna parikalpitam tad viruddha aneka citta uparañjaka tvāt vādi prativādi pratijñā guṇa doṣa tad ābhāsa vat
ca ādi prativādi prabhṛtīnām api vijñāna mātra tve sādhya sādhana ādi vyavahāra vilopaḥ syāt
atha sva vijñāna vyatirekeṇa teṣām jñāna rūpāṇām eva pṛthaktvam iti ced astu
tat eva vastu jñāna antara viṣaya tvāt artha amtaram siddham
saṃjñā mātre vipratipattiḥ
viṣayi viṣaya bhedaḥ tu na sādhyaḥ
tasmāt nityā na anayoḥ saṃkara gandhaḥ u pi iti
atha vastuni svarūpa pratiṣṭhe api sukha ādi bhinna pratyaya ālambana tā na samīcīna rūpā iti ced atrā ucyate vastu punar triguṇam calam guṇa vṛttam iti dharma ādi nimittam ca apekṣya vittaiḥ sukha duḥkha ādi bheda rūpeṇa abhisaṃbadhyate pariṇāmi tvāt aneka śakti tvāt ca
dharma ādi nimitta anurūpasya ca utpadyamānasya pratyayasya tena tena nimittena ātmanā hetuḥ bhavati
sattva ātmanā dharma ādi nimitta apekṣam putra ādi vastu sukha hetuḥ bhavati
rajaḥ ātmanā tu adharma nimitta apekṣam duḥkha hetuḥ bhavati
tamaḥ ātmanā tu avidyā apekṣam tat eva vastu moha hetuḥ bhavati
sattā mātra ātmanā samyak darśana apekṣam tat eva mādhyasthya jñāna hetuḥ bhavati
kecid āhuḥ eṣām eva bauddhānām anyatame bāhyam artham abhyupagacchantaḥ āhuḥ eva arthaḥ yathā vijñānam pratikṣaṇam dharmi śūnyam utpadyate vinaśyati ca tathā shā eva jñānena arthaḥ vijñāyate vinaśyati ca bhogya tvāt sukha ādi vat
tat yathā sukha duḥkha ādi rūpam bhogyam vijñāna saha utpatti vināśam asādhāraṇam evam ghaṭa ādiḥ arthaḥ api vijñāna samāna samaya janma vināśaḥ eva bhogya tvāt iti
te api tathā eva vijñānavādi vat sādhāraṇa tvam aneka sukha ādi citta ālambana tvam bādhamānāḥ pūrva uttara kṣaṇeṣu svakīya vijñāna utpatteḥ paurastyeṣu kṣaṇeṣu pāścātyeṣu ca vastu na asti iti vastu svarūpam eva apahnuvate
tasmāt na hi vastunaḥ svarūpam vijñāna sahabhāvi tat eva idam iti pratyabhijñānāt
na acara janma pralayam tat eva idam iti pratyabhijñāyate yathā vijñānam
na hi tat eva adaḥ me vijñānam iti bhavati
vastu punar tat eva idam iti pratyabhijñāyate
artha jñānayoḥ eva eka samaya bhavi tve api pariśeṣaḥ viśeṣaḥ syāt
na api sādṛśyāt pratyabhijñānam
grāhya grāhakayoḥ yugapad utpatti vināśavat tvāt
vyavasthite hi vastu antara dṛśye anya tad sadṛśa vastu darśanena sādṛśya pratyayaḥ
evam tad sadṛśam vā drakṣyāmi iti uttara abhilāṣaḥ
na hi tat ahar niścita maraṇasya aparedyus artha darśana ākāṃkṣā jāyate
na api mad sacṛśaḥ īkṣiṣyate iti abhilaṣati
na ca evam dṛṣṭam
sarmaḥ hi sva artham īhate
bhinna santatiṣu adarśanāt
tasmāt idānīṃtanaḥ rthaḥ na idānīntana jñāna sahabhūḥ eva iti grāhya tvāt atīta artha vat
atītaḥ vā na atīta jñāna saha nāśa janmā grāhya tvāt idānīntana artha vat
bhūta bhaviṣyat jñāna grāhyāḥ arthāḥ adhunā api santi grāhya tvāt adhunātana pratyaya grāhya vat
idānīntanam api vastu pūrva uttara kṣaṇeṣu tathā eva
atha sukha duḥkha jñāna ādibhiḥ anekāntikam iti ced na atīta anāgatam svarūpataḥ sti iti sādhi tvāt
evam ca sati sukha ādīnām ca svarūpeṇa sadbhāvāt sukha ādi vat iti sādhyasamānaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ
atha vartamāna rūpa viśeṣeṇa atīta anāgata lakṣaṇayoḥ arthasya sukha ādi vat abhāvaḥ iti ced siddha sādhya tā
na hi kumāra bhāve eva vṛddha tvam vidyate
itas ca citta tantra tā vastunaḥ na avakalpate
eka citta tantram vā vastu bhavet aneka citta tantram vā eka citta tantra tve brūmaḥ na ca eka citta tantram vastu tat apramāṇakam tadā kim syāt na tāvat eka citta tantram eka citta tantram ced vastu syāt yadi ca idam ucyate tat citte yat citta tantram vastu tasmin citte vyagre parāsakte niruddhe vā vinaṣṭe vā tena pramāṇa cittena aparāmṛṣṭam ca anyasya ca aviṣayībhūtam eka citta tantra tayā eva tadā tat vastu apramāṇakam agṛhīta svabhāvam pramāṇa citta nirodhāt
na hi kim cit api syāt
citta pramāṇakam tat tad abhāve na tena bhavitavyam
nanu ca yathā tat pramāṇa cittam nirudhyate tathā eva tat api kṣaṇika tvāt niruddham eva
kim tatra abhidhānīyam syāt
ucyate na vyavahāra vilopāt niyama anupapatteḥ ca
agniḥ ayam mā asprākṣīḥ imam gṛhāṇa adaḥ pradehi iti vyavahāraḥ vilupyeta
eka citta saha kṣaya tvāt vastunaḥ
tad santati jam atyanta sadṛśam vyavahāra pratipattaye bhavet iti ced atra api tad santānāt eva tad samānena anyena anubhavanīyam para pramāṇasya ca tat viṣaya bhūtam iti kaḥ niyacchet
na hi niyama hetuḥ asti
api ca eka citta tantra tvāt vyavahāra velāyām yujyate
na hi khalu api bahu cita tantram vastu
tatas ca kṛhāṇa idam prayuccha adaḥ iti katham vyavaharemahi
na api evam darśana śālinaḥ śiṣya ācārya upadeśa pradāna ādibhiḥ anyonyam vyavahareran
tasmāt nityāḥ na ca eka citta tantram vastu
pramāṇa citta vināśe tad vyagra bhāve vā anavadhṛta svabhāva tvāt vastunaḥ
saṃbandhyamānam vā vastu punar cittena kutas utpadyeta
na kutas cit utpattiḥ upapadyate tad santānāt iti hi pratyavocāma
kim ca asya vastunaḥ anupasthitāḥ ekasya pratyayasya aviṣayībhūtāḥ ye bhāgāḥ te ca asya na syuḥ
ekaḥ hi vastu bhāgaḥ viṣayībhūtaḥ cittatantraḥ na anyaḥ iti
na asti pṛṣṭham iti udaram api abhimukhībhūtam na syāt eva
atha api kākatālīya nyāyena bhūyāṃsi cittāni yugapad utpadyeran tad viṣayam ca vastu tad samāna kālam unmajjati iti tat etena eva pṛṣṭha udara abhāvan darśanena pratyākhyāyi
nā api kākatālīya vṛttāntena anādi samaya adhīnaḥ vyavahāra sāgaraḥ uttīryate
sarve ca vijñāna darśana ślādhiṣu doṣāḥ iha api samānāḥ eva
tasmāt āha svatantraḥ rthaḥ sarva puruṣa sādhāraṇaḥ yasmin avasthite samasta loka vyavahāraḥ upakalpiṣyate
svatantrāṇi ca cittāni prati puruṣam pravartante
tayoḥ ca artha cittayoḥ smbandhāt upalabdhiḥ puruṣasya bhogaḥ
tasmāt bhoktā puruṣaḥ cittam karaṇam arthaḥ viṣayaḥ karma bhūtaḥ iti eteṣām bhoktṛ karaṇa karmaṇām viviktaḥ panthāḥ
katham citta tad viṣayayoḥ sambandhāt puruṣasya bhogaḥ iti āha yat vā yasya citta vyatirekeṇa vastu na asti citta tantram eva vā vastu tasya jñāta ajñāta viṣaya tvam anupapannam iti āha tad uparāgaḥ cittasya vastu jñāta ajñātam
tena viṣayeṇa cittasya uparāgaḥ tam prati apekṣā yasya tat cittam tad uparāga apekṣam tasya bhāvaḥ tad uparāga apekṣa tvam tasmāt tad uparāga apekṣa tvāt cittasya vastu jñāta ajñātam
yena vastunā cittam uparajyate tat jñātam yena ca na uparajyate tat ajñātam
sa ca uparāgaḥ citta pariṇāma apekṣaḥ
indriya mārgeṇa cittam bāhya ākāreṇa pariṇāmamānam hi sambadhyate
kim punar citta pariṇāma nimittam iti āha ayaskānta maṇi kalpāḥ ayaskānta samānaḥ viṣayāḥ ayaḥ sadharmakam ekam cittam ca viṣaya sannidhāne vikriyate iti
viṣayāṇām api ayaskkānta maṇi kalpa tvam sannidhi mātreṇa citta vikriyā āpādana sāmarthyāt
atas viṣayāḥ ātma ākāreṇa pariṇitam cittam abhisaṃbadhya uparañjayanti
yena ca viṣayeṇa uparaktam cittam sa viṣayaḥ jñātaḥ
tatas nyaḥ ṇye punar viṣayaḥ yā ajñātaḥ tāḥ
tasmāt vastunaḥ jñāta ajñāta svarūpa viṣaya tvāt pariṇāmi cittam
atha punar cittatantraḥ eva viṣayaḥ cittam eva vā viṣayaḥ tasya vādinaḥ sarva viṣaya jña tvam a viṣaya jña tvam vā bhavet
ajñātasya cittasya abhāvāt
na ca idam dṛśyate
kim tarhi jñāta ajñāta viṣaya tvam eva cittasya pratipadyāmahe
tat ca etat sthira avasthānānām viṣayāṇām prāpti abhāvāt anyathā ca saṃbandha anavakalpanāt citta pariṇāma apekṣam eva iti pariṇāmi tvam
yasya tu svāminaḥ bhoktuḥ tat eva jñāta ajñāta viṣayam cittam vṛtti rūpeṇa viṣayaḥ na hi niruddha vṛttinaḥ cetasaḥ viṣaya tvam iti tasya puruṣasya sadā jñātāḥ cita vṛttayaḥ tat prabhoḥ puruṣasya apariṇāmi tvāt
tāsām pratyakṣa tvāt sadā jñāta viṣaya tvam aprasādhyam
yat vā pratyakṣa gamyaḥ citta vṛttayaḥ upalabdha tvena śabda liṅgān apekṣam smaryamāṇa tvāt pratyakṣa upalabdha ghaṭa vat
niścita rūpa tvāt ca tathā eva
saṃśaya aviṣaya tvāt ca
yadi hi sadā eva apratyakṣāḥ citta vṛttayaḥ tāḥ bāhya viṣaya vat saṃśayitāḥ api kadācid kāścana bhaveyuḥ
na hi kāścana kadācana saṃśaya mārga saṃpātinyaḥ dṛṣṭāḥ
api ca bhavati hi kadācid jñātaḥ san arthaḥ jñātaḥ iti
citta vṛtti pratyakṣa agrāhya tve tat na upapadyate
na ca phala dvāreṇa anumātum tatra śakyate
phalasya an avadhāraṇāt
tasmāt saṃśayasya ca aviṣaya tvāt pṛthak ca viṣayāt citta vṛttīnām sva rūpa mātreṇa eva svaryamāṇa tvāt sarvadā sarvāḥ pratyakṣāḥ citta vṛttayaḥ
tathā pratipattuḥ avabhāsaka tvāt karaṇa tvāt abhivyañjaka tvāt ca pradīpa ādi vat
na tu cakṣuḥ ādibhiḥ anaikāntika tvam
tatra api pratyakṣa grāhya tvāt
yathā pradīpa ādi āloka viśiṣṭāḥ ghaṭa ādayaḥ gṛhyante tathā śrotra ādi sva āloka viśiṣṭāḥ eva śabda ādayaḥ gṛhyante
na ca vivicya agrahaṇāt apratyakṣa tvam iti śakyam vaktum
yathā pradīpayoḥ paraspara vyatibhinnāḥ raśmayaḥ na ca asya ayam raśmiḥ asya ca ayam iti
vivicyate na ca tāvatā teṣām apratyakṣa tvam evam iha api cakṣuḥ ādīnām tulya jātīya bāhya āloka ādi vyatiṣaṅgāt vivicya agrahaṇam
na ca tāvat mātreṇa teṣām apratyakṣa tvam
yaḥ hi pratyakṣa avasīyamāna citta vṛtti apalāpam karoti nūnam asau ātmānam api apalopet iti sarva upalabdheḥ citta vṛtti adhīna tvāt rūpa upalabdheḥ iva āloka pratyāyakam tattvam pratyaya adhīna tvam
tasmāt āha sadā jñātāḥ citta vṛttayaḥ puruṣasya iti
yat ca etat sadā jñāta viṣaya tvam tat prabhoḥ puruṣasya apariṇami tvāt
nitya upalabdhṛ sva rūpa prayuktam hi tat iti
yadi citta vat prabhuḥ api puruṣaḥ pariṇameta tatas tad viṣayāḥ citta vṛttayaḥ cittasya iva śabda ādi viṣayāḥ jñātāḥ ajñātāḥ api syuḥ
yat tu jñāta ajñātam śabda ādi viṣaya jātam tat pariṇāminaḥ cittasya pariṇāma apekṣam draṣṭavyam
tathā evā indriyāṇām api pariṇāma apekṣam eva jñāta ajñāta viṣaya tvam dṛśyate
na ca tathā citta vṛttīnām anyatamāsām api jñāta tvam ajñāta tvam ca
nityatas tad jñātāḥ eva citta vṛttayaḥ
tasmāt yat vṛtti rūpena sadā jñāta tvam manasaḥ tat prabhoḥ puruṣasya apariṇāmi tvam anumāpayati
apariṇāmī puruṣaḥ iti pratijñā
sadā jñāta viṣaya tvāt iti hetuḥ
vaidharmyeṇa cittam indriyāṇi ca dṛṣṭāntaḥ
upalabdhuḥ ca viṣayiṇaḥ prakṛta tvāt sadā jñāta viṣaya tva pratiṣedhāya mukta ātma vat iti dṛṣṭāntaḥ na upapadyate
muktasya aviṣayi tvāt
syāt āśaṅkā cittam eva su ābhāsam viṣaya ābhāsam ca bhaviṣyati iti
grāhyam grāhakam ca iti
sva saṃvidita ākārāḥ eva hi vṛttayaḥ
yathā pradīpaḥ prakāśayati ghaṭa ādīn ātmānam ca
kim puruṣeṇa citta vṛtti upalambhinā citta vyatiriktena kalpitena iti
atra ucyate na tat su ābhāsam dṛśya tvāt
yathā itarāṇi indriyāṇi śrotraḥ ādīni viṣayāḥ ca śabdaḥ ādayaḥ
na su ābhāsāni indriyāṇi
na api su ābhāsāḥ śabda ādayaḥ
dṛśya tvāt
tathā manaḥ api pratyetavyam
na su ābhāsam cittam dṛśya tvāt iti pratipattavyam
nanu ca agni vat eva sva ābhāsa tvam viṣaya ābhāsa tvam ca yathā eva ghaṭa ādayaḥ prakāśyāḥ sva rūpa upalambhana artham apekṣante na tathā pradīpaḥ
yathā pradīpaḥ su ābhāsaḥ viṣaya ābhāsaḥ ca
tathā manaḥ api avabhāsaka tvāt evam bhavatu kim ātmanā na hi pradīpa pratipattaye pradīpa antaram ādadate laukikāḥ
yadi ca upādīyeran anavasthā eva syāt
evam vijñānasya api vyatiriktena grāhya tve tasya ca anyena grahaṇam tasya ca anyena iti evam prasajyeta
kim ca vijñānasya avabhāsa ātmaka tvāt grāhakasya api avabhāsa rūpa rvāt na paraspara upakārya upakāraka bhāvaḥ
tat yathā pradīpayoḥ dvayoḥ
tasmāt kalpitaḥ api vijñānasya grahītā anarthakaḥ iti bhavatu jñānam su ābhāsam para ābhāsam ca iti
atrā ucyate tat etat dṛṣṭānta apaśada avaṣṭambhena sakala loka prasiddha mārga upārohiṇā ātmanaḥ nirākaraṇam aśakyam
kasmāt na ca agnisya dṛṣṭāntaḥ
na hi agniḥ ātma svarūpam aprakāśam prakāśayati yadi ca agniḥ aprakāśaḥ san ātmanā eva ghaṭa ādi vat prakāśayiṣyata tatas upāpatsyata dṛṣṭāntaḥ
na tu evam
na hi kadācid agniḥ aprakāśaḥ
prakāśaḥ ca ayam
sa ca prakāśya prakāśaka saṃyohe dṛṣṭaḥ
na ca svarūpa mātre sti saṃyogaḥ
dvayoḥ hi saṃyogaḥ
na asati saṃyoge sva rūpa avabhāsaka tvam
yat api ucyate ghaṭa ādi vat prakāśa antaram na agniḥ apekṣate iti
tat prakāśya rūpa abhāvāt
na tu tasya ghaṭa ādi vat prakāśyam rūpam asti
na tāvatā vyatirikta agrāhya tvam
cakṣuṣā tulya vyatiriktena gṛhyate eva
prakāśyasya haṭa ādeḥ prakāśaḥ
na tu a prakāśya rūpa tvāt
agneḥ āloka antara an ākāṅkṣaṇam tu bhavatā eva abhihitam dvayoḥ pradīpayoḥ na asti paraspara upakāraḥ iti
yatra nāma bhede api dvayoḥ pradīpayoḥ na asti a prakāśya rūpa tvāt anyonya upakāraḥ kim uta asati bhede prakāśa antaram eva na apekṣate iti
na tu vyatirikta grāhyatvam vyabhicarati pradīpayoḥ dṛśya tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat
etena vyatirikta grāhya tvam jñānasya dṛśya tvāt pradīpa ādi vat siddham bhavati
pradīpa ādi vat ca jñānasya prakāśa svarūpa tvāt karaṇa antara anapekṣā api siddhā
tathā ca anavasthā doṣa gandhaḥ na vidyate
yat api ucyate jñānasya avabhāsa ātmaka tvāt tat grāhakasya api avabhāsa rūpa tvāt na paraspara upakārya upakāraka bhāvaḥ pradīpayoḥ iva dvayoḥ iti
na asau doṣaḥ
cakṣuḥ pradīpa vat ātma jñānayoḥ jāti antara tvāt
nanu ca ahaṃpratyayena cittam pratyayi gṛhyate iti viṣaya viṣayi tvam ekasya eva
na eṣa doṣaḥ
triguṇa tvāt cittasya
yat tatra tamaḥ pradhānam cittam tat anyayā sattva ātmikayā vṛttyā samālambyate hastena iva śarīram kaṇḍūyamānam
tatra api upalabdhā viṣayī bhinnaḥ eva puruṣaḥ
etena jāti antara grāhya grāhaka tvena niravayava tvena puruṣaḥ ca svayam eva grāhyaḥ grāhakaḥ ca iti etat pratyavocāma
kim ca su ābhāsam cittam iti ucyamāne ca agrāhyam eva cittam syāt iti
evam śabda arthaḥ
su ābhāsam iti hi ukte anyena na avabāsyate na gṛhyate iti arthaḥ
na tu svayam ātmānam gṛhṇāti iti ucyate
evamādi śabda prayogeṣu śabdasya viparīta artha tvam
tat yathā sva ātma pratiṣṭham ākāśam apratiṣṭham iti śabda arthaḥ
tathā svasthaḥ devadattaḥ iti iti arthaḥ na tu sva ātma nisthitaḥ iti
tatra dṛśya tvāt iti hetoḥ asiddhim ācakṣāṇasya pratyakṣa virodhaḥ loka virodhaḥ vyavahāra vilopaḥ ca iti āha sva buddhi pracāra pratisaṃvedanāt sattvānām prāṇinām pravṛttiḥ dṛśyate
kruddhaḥ ham bhogī ham amutra me rāgaḥ mutra me krodhaḥ iti svām svām buddhim evam carantīm pratisaṃvedya dṛṣṭvā krodha lobha ādi parihārāya vivekavatām pravṛttuḥ upalabhyate
tathā prasannam me cittam kalupitam mūḍham iti ca
tat etat sva buddheḥ agrahaṇe na yuktam iti
na hi niśamya parispandinīm buddhiḥ adṛyā iti yuktam vaktum
abhyupagamya vādaḥ yam yadi api sva ābhāsam viṣaya ābhāsam ca manaḥ bhavatu
tatra dūṣaṇam ca ubhaya anavadhāraṇam
viṣaya paricchedaka tve nānā kṣana tvāt ātma paricchedaḥ na yujyate
atha punar ātmānam avadhārayati na tadā viṣaya abhimukham sva ātma pariddha idaka tve nānā kṣaṇa tvāt
atha ubhaya paricchittiḥ ekā eva iti ced na niravayava tvāt paricchitteḥ
na hi vinava yavāyāḥ citta vṛtteḥ pradīpa vat aneka abvabhāsaka tvam yuktam
avayava bhedāt tu pradīpasya aneka prakāśaka tvam saṃbhavati
na tu jñānasya sāvayava tvam paraiḥ abhyupeyate
kim ca jñānam ekam ekasmin kṣaṇe ubhayam avadhārayati iti ca abhyupagame kriyā kāraka bheda prasaṅgaḥ
yat ubhaya avadhāraṇam sā kriyā
yat avadhārayati tat kārakam
na ca ekasmin kṣaṇe sva para ubhaya avadhāraṇam kṣaṇavādinaḥ yuktam
kasmāt uktam hi kṣaṇka tva siddhye yat utpattiḥ sā eva kriyā tat eva ca kārakam iti abhupagamaḥ
kriyā kāraka bhede ca syāt
kārakeṇa hi kriyā kṣaṇam avasthānīyam
syāt matiḥ kasya api svara sanniruddham cittam citta antareṇa gṛhyate iti bhāvena vinaṣṭam bhaṅgurataram cittam citta antareṇa samanantareṇa saṃjāyamānena gṛhyate iti atha api nitya avasthita puruṣa parikalpinā nirarthikāḥ eva
atrā ucyate citta antara dṛśye buddhi buddheḥ atiprasaṅgaḥ smṛti saṅkaraḥ ca
yadi cittam citta antareṇa sva rasa niruddham paurastyam pāścātyena jāyamānena samanantareṇa gṛhyeta buddhi buddhiḥ ghaṭa viṣayā buddhiḥ buddhiḥ ucyate tad viṣayā tu buddhi buddhiḥ sā kena gṛhyate vyavasthita grāhaka abhāvāt
sā api anyayā grahītavyā sā api anyā iti atiprasaṅgaḥ
na ca agṛhītāsu buddhi buddhiṣu saṃvyavahāraḥ ghaṭate smṛti saṃskāra anupapatteḥ
tatra eka jātīyānām eva ghaṭa buddhi buddhīnām dāśatayī mālā syāt anavasthitā na ghaṭa buddhiḥ
parisamāptau ca ghaṭa buddhi buddhīnām asatyām katham ghaṭa ādi buddhiḥ upatiṣṭheta
ayam ca aparaḥ doṣaḥ smṛti saṃkaraḥ ca iti
buddhi buddhīnām tad saṃskārāṇām ca eka rūpa tvāt smṛti saṃkaraḥ prāpnoti
yāvantaḥ buddhi buddhīnām anubhavāḥ tāvatyaḥ smṛtayaḥ saṃkīrṇāḥ prāpnuvanti
tad saṅkarāt smṛti saṅkarāt smṛti anavadhāraṇam iyam asyāḥ buddheḥ smṛtiḥ iti an avadhārayantaḥ katham vyavaharemahi
tathā ca sarūpa tvāt smṛti saṃkaraḥ prāpnoti
yāvantaḥ buddhi buddhīnām vidānāḥ sva buddhi smṛti pūrva vyavahāra asambhavāt sarve sammohena saṅgacchemahi
yadi ca anavasthā parijihāsayā kvacid buddhi antare samavatiṣṭhemahi tam eva buddhi pratisaṃvedinam buddhi pratisaṃvedana liṅgena spaṣṭataram api puruṣam apalapacbhiḥ vaināśikaiḥ ākulīkṛtam jagat iti
nanu ca ālayavijñāna kalpanayā navasthā doṣam pariharemahi
tathā ca ātma kalpanām apalapemahi iti evam te bhoktṛ svarūpam yatra kvacana kalpayantaḥ na nyāyena
tasya api alayavijñānasya grāhya tvāt anavasthita tvāt ca abhihita sakala doṣa anuṣaṅgaḥ
kecid vaināśika viśeṣāḥ sattva mātram api śabda antareṇa sattva mātram bhoktṛ svarūpam parikalpya asti sa sattvaḥ yaḥ etān pañca skandhān rūpa vedanā saṃjñā saṃskāra vijñāna lakṣaṇān nikṣipya parityajya anyān ca skandhān pratisandhāti gṛhṇāti iti uktvā tatas eva bhūta anāgata skandha pratisandhātṛ eka sattva prikalpanātaḥ trasyanti
tathā anyā viruddha kalpanā skandhānām mahā nirvedāya virāgāya anutpādāya praśāntaye guroḥ antike brahmacaryam carāmi iti uktvā punar tam eva abhyāgatam sattvasya sattva sādhya sādhana sambandha apahnuvate
vijñānamātram kṣaṇikam śūnyam ca iti ātmānam apalapanti
nam abhisandadhīmahi
tat evam sāṅkhya yoga ādayaḥ tu pravādāḥ
sva śabdena puruṣam eva svāminam vittasya bhoktāram abhyupayanti iti
katham bhoktāram sva śabdena eva abhyupayanti yatas citeḥ apratisaṃkramāyāḥ tad ākāra āpattau satyām sva buddhi saṃvedanam bhavati
citiḥ caitanyam puruṣaḥ iti arthaḥ
sā ca apariṇāmi tvāt apratisaṃkramā
tasyāḥ apratisaṃkramāyāḥ api satyāḥ citeḥ tad ākāra āpattiḥ
tat iti prakṛtam cittam pratyāmnāyate tasya ākāra āpattiḥ tad ākāra āpattiḥ
tasyāḥ citeḥ tad ākāra āpattau satyām sva buddhi saṃbedanam bhavati
svasya bauddhasya pratyayasya upalabdhiḥ bhavati
tat artham eva hi sā buddhiḥ śabda ādi pratyaya rūpeṇa apariṇamate
tat etat pratipādayati pratītya apariṇāminī hi bhoktṛ śaktiḥ dṛś śaktiḥ yathā traya ākhyātā
apratisaṃkramā ca satī pariṇāminī arthe pratisaṃkrāntā iva pratyayi viṣaya tvāt tad vṛttim anupatantī iva anupatantī draṣṭṛ tvāt upalabhamānā
bauddhaḥ pratyayaḥ jāyamānaḥ eva tasyāḥ karmatām āpadyate
tam bauddham pratyayam vṛttim anupatanti upalabhamānā bhoktṛ śaktiḥ
tasyāḥ ca prāpta caitanya upagraha rūpāyāḥ prāptam caitanya upagraha rūpam puruṣa upagraha rūpam yayā buddhi vṛttyā samāsādita pāvaka upagraha rūpa tapta loha piṇḍa vat dṛśi karma tvāt eva anukāra mātra tayā buddhi vṛtti sārūpya mātra tayā
buddhi vṛtti a viśiṣṭā jña vṛttiḥ iti
jñaḥ eva upalabdhiḥ eva vṛttiḥ iti ākhyāyate
vṛtti sārūpyam itaratra iti
tathā pratyaya aviśeṣaḥ bhogaḥ iti prakhyāpitam
bhoktṛ bhogya bhede ca sati citta ākāra āpattiḥ upapadyate
na ca asati vyatirikte bhoktari cittasya eva draṣṭṛ dṛśya ubhaya ābhāsa tvam akasmāt upakalpate
tasmāt suṣṭhu ucyate sāṅkhya yoga ādayaḥ eva puruṣam sva śabdena abhyupayanti iti
anye tu śabda antareṇa upayantaḥ api tatas eva bibhyati
tathā u ca uktam buddhi vṛtti anukāra mātra tayā buddhau eva jña vṛttiḥ upalabhyate na anyatra iti
na pātālam no vivaram girīṇām na eva andhakāraḥ kukṣayaḥ naḥ udadhīnām evam ādīni na guhā
yasyām guhāyām nihitam brahma śāśvatam sā guhā na pātā āchādīni
kasyām punar guhāyām nihitam iti āha buddhau eva guhāyām vṛttim ātma ākhyām brahma ākhyām aviśiṣṭam apṛthak bhūtām buddhi vṛtti aviśiṣṭām vedayante vivekinaḥ
kasmāt punar kāraṇāt puruṣasya citta ākāra āpattiḥ
tasyām vā satyām sva buddhi saṃvedanam
kutas vaināśikānām cittam eva grāhyam grāhakam ca iti bhrāntiḥ iti āha draṣṭṛ dṛśya uparaktam cittam sarva artham drasṭā puruṣaḥ dṛśyam śabda ādi tābhyām uparaktam cittam sarva artham puruṣasya bhoga apavarga artham bhavati
manaḥ bhimantavyena arthena ayaskānta maṇi deśīyena viṣayeṇa uparaktam svayam ca viṣaya tvāt puruṣasya viṣayiṇā puruṣeṇa asannihitena ātmīyayā vṛttyā mānasena pratyayena viṣaya tayā abhisambaddham
tat etat cittam ātma vṛtti dvāreṇa puruṣeṇa sambandhāt draṣṭuḥ sva rūpa upraktam śabda ādinā vā mantavyena uparaktam iti draṣṭṛ dṛśya uparaktam cittam eva na puruṣaḥ
draṣṭṛ drśya uparaktam iti asya vyākhyānam karoti viṣaya viṣayi nirbhāsam cetana acetana svarūpa āpannam
katham punar svayam acetanam sat cetana svarūpa āpannam iti na eṣa doṣaḥ puruṣeṇa nitya sannidhānāt cetanam iva
tat eva avivekibhiḥ cetanam iti ucyate
na tathā viṣayāḥ
nityam acetana ātmakāḥ hi te
svatas tu vittam acetanam eva iti cetana acetana svarūpa āpannam iti ucyate
viṣaya ātmakam iva śabda ādi svarūpa mātram iva ca iti arthaḥ
acetanam cetanam iva puruṣa svarūpa āpannam iva ca iti arthaḥ
sphaṭika maṇi kalpam yathā sphaṭika maṇiḥ alaktaka ādi sannidhau tad ākāra tām biharti
tathā eva tat sarva artham cittam ucyate
tasmāt anena citta sārūpyeṇa bhrāntāḥ kecid
etat tu citta sārūpyam vaiśeṣikāṇām pramoha kāraṇam
vaiśeṣika ādayaḥ tu citta sārūpya māhendrajāla vyāmohita cetasaḥ tat eva cittam cetanam iti āhuḥ
katham yasmāt manaḥ pruṣa saṃyoga jam caitanyam guṇaḥ uddhedanīyaḥ iti manyate
vaināśikebhyaḥ tu ayam viśeṣaḥ sthiram ekam dharmiṇam icchanti iti
apare bauddhāḥ cit mātram evā id dam sarvam na asti gavādiḥ ghaṭa ādiḥ ca sva ākāreṇa viśiṣṭaḥ sarveṣām pratyayasya sādhāraṇaḥ lokaḥ iti sva anubhavam api apalapanti
te evam bhrāntāḥ sukumāratara buddhayaḥ vainācikāḥ anukapmanīyāḥ
kasmāt asti hi teṣām bhrānti bījam sarva rupa ākāra nirbhāsam cittam iti
sa nimittā hi teṣām bhrāntiḥ na loka upāyatikānām śūnyatva ādinām iva nirbījā
kevala jagat vañcana artha pravṛtta tvāt tu na eteṣu anukampā kartavyā
tasmāt yuktam uktam teṣām varākāṇām sa bīja bhrānta cetasām anukampanīyam iti
ke punar a bhrāntāḥ iti āha iti
samādhi prajñā grahaṇam abhrānta citta grahaṇa artham
vikṣipta cetasaḥ hi bhrāntāḥ
samādhi prajñāyām viśuddhāyām vivekavatyām prasanna gambhīratarāyām prajñeyaḥ rthaḥ pratibimbībhūtaḥ nirmala darpaṇa maṇḍalaḥ iva tasyām samādhi prajñāyām karaṇa bhūtāyām ālambanībhūta tvāt anyaḥ prajñātaḥ sakāśāt jāti sva rūpa kriyā ādibhiḥ anyaḥ
sa ced anyaḥ cittamātram syāt katham prajñayā eva prajñā rūpam avadhāryeta
sva ātmani kriyā virodhāt na hi kathañcid avadhāryeta
tasmāt prajñāyāḥ anyaḥ saḥ arthaḥ saḥ yasyām prajñāyām pratibimbībhūtaḥ rthaḥ yena avadhāryate saḥ tasyāḥ prajñāyāḥ ālambanībhūtāt ca arthāt anyaḥ kartṛ kāraka bhūtaḥ
sa puruṣaḥ
iti evam grahītṛ grahaṇa grāhya svarūpa bhedāt kartṛ karaṇa karma bheda upapatteḥ na hi niravayavam ekam eva ekasmin vastu kartṛ ca karma ca bhavati
tatas ye trayam api etat jātitaḥ pravibhajante te samyak darśanaḥ taiḥ adhigataḥ pouruṣaḥ prāptaḥ iti arthaḥ
sāmarthyāt tu jñātaḥ iti gamyate
kutas ca asti puruṣaḥ citta vyatiriktaḥ pūrvam cittasya dṛśya tvena vyatirikta puruṣa siddhiḥ āpāditā
tasya eva tu vittasya saṃhati kāri tvena adhunā svāmi siddhu artham āha tat asaṅkhyeya vāsanā citram api para artham saṃhatya kāri tvāt
yadi api tat eva cittam asaṃkhyeyābhiḥ vāsanābhiḥ anādi samayābhiḥ citrīkṛtam bhrānti kāraṇam uktam tathā api parāḥ artham parasya bhoga artham eva iti pratijñāyate
saṃhatyakāri tvāt kārya karaṇa viṣaya ādi vyāpāra apekṣam artha sādhaka tvāt saṃhatyakāri tvam atas saṃhatyakāri tvāt gṛha ādi vat iti pārārthyam cittasya
na hiḥ kiṃcana loke saṃhatya kāri dṛṣṭam svātham
tasmāt saṃhatya kāriṇā cittena na sva arthena bhavitavyam
na hi sukha cittam sukha artham sukha citta artham vā
na api jñāna cittam jñāna artham vā jñāna citta artham vā
kim tarhi sukha cittam jñāna cittam api etat ubhayam para artham
yaḥ ca bhogena sukha cittena jñāna cittena ca apavarheṇa arthena arthavān puruṣaḥ saḥ eva paraḥ
na para sāmānya mātram śarīram indriyāṇi viṣayāḥ vā
na hi vaināśīkaḥ sukha cittam śarīra indriya viṣaya atham icchati
tathā ca icchan abhyupagatam virundhīta
vijñānasya eva hi sukha apavargābhyām arthi tvam abhimanyate
tasmāt yaḥ eva śarīra indriya vijñānasya eva hi sukha apavargābhyām arthi tvam abhimanyate
a tasmāt yaḥ eva śarīra indriya viṣaya vyatiriktaḥ puruṣaḥ bhoga apavargābhyām arthavān anyaḥ vijñānāt abhyupagamanīyaḥ
yadi yat kiṃcid para sāmānya mātram udāharet vaināśikaḥ yadi tu vaināśikaḥ saṃhatya kāriṇām gṛha ādīnām devadatta ādi saṃhata para artha tvam iti vyāmohāt abhimanyamānāḥ kaṃcana viśiṣṭam na param icchet evam ced manvīta saḥ idam vaktavyam yaḥ paraḥ śarīra indriya viṣaya pratyayānām sāmānyam uta sarve eva iti kim eṣām anyatamaḥ kim vā kaścid eva etebhyaḥ bhinna jātīyaḥ iti
na tāvat sāmānyam
na hi bhoga apavarga arthena arthi sāmānya vastu vaināśikaḥ bhyupaiti sva samaya virodhāt
na api śarīra ādīni samastāni bhoga apavargābhyām arthīni iti
vijñāna santateḥ eva bhoga apavarga arthi tva abhimanāt
na ca api jñāna santatiḥ iti ekam vastu santateḥ kṣaṇika tvam
na ca api santānasya avastu tayā śaśaviṣāṇa kalpasya bhoga apavargābhyām arthi tvam
na api śarīra indriya ādīnām anyatama tvam icchati
vijñāna vyatiriktānām ātmīya samaye bhoga apavarga arthi tva an abhyupagamāt
nā api śarīra indriyāṇām saṅghātaḥ nāma vastutas bhavataḥ vidyate yena cittam saṃhata para artham prārthayethāḥ
avastunaḥ hi katham arthi tvam
na api śarīra indriya ādibhyaḥ saṃhata bhinna jātīyam pratijānīṣe
yadi bhinna jātīyam bhoga apavargābhyām arthavantam adṛṣṭam parikalpayethāḥ saḥ eva asmābhiḥ uktaḥ paraḥ iti
tasya ca saṃhata tve paratvam dṛṣṭa anātmavat na upakalpate
pariśeṣāt tu asaṃhataḥ bhoga apavargābhyām arthī paraḥ iti
kim ca anyat saṃhata para artham cittam iti sādhayataḥ rthinaḥ saṃhatasya anyasya anupapatteḥ sva artham eva cittam iti uktam bhavati
tathā ca sati bhavataḥ dṛṣṭānta abhāvaḥ bhyupagama virodhaḥ ca
tathā manvānasya anyat vāci hṛdaye ca anyat aniśamyakāri tvam ca āpatati
yena cakṣuḥ ādi para artha tva sādhanena viruddha tā doṣaḥ pratyākhyāyi
teṣām vijñāna parārtha tvam iti ced vijñānasya api parārtha tvam prasādhitam
atha vijñānasya api kṣaṇika tvāt asaṃhata tvam iti ced na tasya vyatirikta dṛśya tvāt dharma mātra anabhyupagamāt ca kṣaṇika tva anabhyupagamāt ca iti etat api pratyavocāma
tasmāt ucyate yat kiṃcid para sāmānya mātram sva rūpeṇa udāharet vaināśikaḥ sa sarvaḥ saṃhatya kāri tvāt para arthaḥ eva syāt
na devadatta ādi saṃhata artha tvam
ubhābhyām āvābhyām anabhyupagamāt
tvam api vijñāna vyatirekeṇa na anyam abhyupaiṣi
vayam api puruṣa vyatirekeṇa na anya artha tvam abhibāñchāmaḥ
cit jñāna mātra tvam ca na upapadyate iti uktam
atas yaḥ tu asau paraḥ viśeṣaḥ sa na saṃhatya kārī puruṣaḥ svārthe iti siddhaḥ
tasmāt asti bhoktā tasya sva arthasya svena dṛśyena para arthena yad nimittaḥ saṃyogaḥ
tad viyogāt kaivalyam upakalpate
guṇapuruṣa yogasya avidyā nimittm uktam
sā ca viśeṣa darśinaḥ ātmānam vijijñāsamānasya vinivartate
tad nivṛttau ca liṅgam āha viśeṣa darśinaḥ ātma bhāva bhāvanā nivṛttiḥ
vyakta avyakta sāmānyāt viśiṣṭaḥ puruṣaḥ asādhāraṇaḥ viśeṣaḥ
tam viśeṣam vyakta avyakta sāmānyāt pravivicya draṣṭum śīlam yasya sa viśeṣa darśī
tasya ātma bhāva bhāvanā nivartate
sā ca samyak darśana abhimukhā kaivalya prāpi karma nimittā
katham punar ātma bhāva bhāvanā asya asti iti vijñāyate iti āha yathā prāvṛṣi tṛṇasya aṅkura udbhedena liṅgena tad bīja sadbhāvaḥ te tathā mokṣa mārga śravaṇena yasya roma harṣa aśru pātaḥ dṛśyate tatra api asti viśeṣa darśana bīja sama pavarga bhāgīyam karma abhinirvartitam iti roma harṣa aśru pāta ādi liṅgena anumīyate
tasya viśeṣa darśinaḥ ātma bhāva bhāvanā kaivalya bhāgīya karma nimittā svābhāvikī janma antara karma nimittā vā
sā hi ācārya upadeśa anapekṣā svābhāvikī pravartate
tasya karmaṇaḥ tādṛśasya abhāvāt idam uktam svabhāva doṣāt aśuddha karmayogāt eṣām samyak darśana tad upāya viparyaye ruciḥ bhavati aruciḥ ca nirṇaye samyak darśane
tatra ātma bhāva bhāvanā kā punar iti āha kaḥ ham āsam katham aham āsam kim svid idam katham svid idam ke bhaviṣyāmaḥ katham bhaviṣyāmaḥ iti
sā tu viśeṣa darśinaḥ nivartate
yad viṣayā hi jijñāsā tasmin adhigate tad viṣayā jijñāsā vinivartate
kutas etat evam yatas cittasya eva eṣaḥ ke bhaviṣyāmaḥ iti ādiḥ citraḥ pariṇāmaḥ na puruṣasya
puruṣa tva satyām avidyāyām śuddhaḥ citta dharmaiḥ aprāmṛṣṭaḥ iti
yasmāt evam atas evam viśeṣa darśinaḥ tasya ātmabhāva bhāvanā kuśalasya nirvartate
yadā ca viśeṣa darśanam udapādi tadā viveka nimnam kaivalya prāgbhāram cittam
yat asya cittam viṣaya nimnam viṣaya pravaṇam ajñāna prāgbhāram ajñāna niṣṭham saṃsāra abhimukham āsīt tat asya viśeṣa darśinaḥ tadānīm anyathā bhavati kaivalya mrāgbhāram viveka nimnam iti prati snotas vṛttiḥ jñāyate
tat chidreṣu pratyaya antarāṇi saṃskārebhyaḥ
viveka nimnasya uttara uttara viveka pravaṇa cetasaḥ puruṣasya jñāninaḥ anyatā khyāti pravāha adhirohiṇaḥ sattva puruṣa anyatā srotaḥ plāvinaḥ cittasya tad chidreṣu viveka pratyaya pravāha antareṣu pratyaya antarāṇi viparyaya lakṣaṇāni asmi iti vā mama iti vā
kkutas tāni bhavanti iti āha kṣīyamāṇa kleśa ādi bījasya cittasya pūrva upacita viparīta saṃskārebhyaḥ pratyaya antarāṇi jāyante
hānam eṣām kleśa vat uktam
yathā kleśāḥ dagdha bīja bhāvāḥ na paroha samarthāḥ bhavanti iti te pratiprasaba heyāḥ sūkṣmāḥ iti atra uktam evam jñāna agni dagdha bīja bhāvāḥ asmi mama ityādi pratyaya saṃskārāḥ na paroha samarthāḥ bhavanti
dagdha śāli bīja vat pūrva saṃskāraḥ na pratyaya prasūḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ
jñāna saṃskārāḥ tu katham a pratipakṣāḥ santaḥ cittam adhikāre na yojayiṣyanti iti te tu samyak darśana saṃskārāḥ citta adhikāra parisamāptim anuśerate
jsahā eva āśrayeṇa avasita prayojanena cittena pralīyante
na punar cittam adhikāra pravaṇam kkurvanti
adhikāra hetoḥ avidyāyāḥ pratipakṣa tvāt jñānasya
tyatra niṣphala tvāt na vintyante
na hi svayam patataḥ patana hetuḥ anbeṣaṇīyaḥ
viveka khyāti pravaṇa antaḥkaraṇasya brāhmāṇasya prasṃkhyāne api a kusīd asya sarvathā viveka khyāteḥ dharma medhaḥ samādhiḥ
sa yadā ayam brāhmaṇaḥ prasṃkhyāne viveka darśana śīlite api a kusīdaṅ a vṛddhikaḥ bhavati tatas api prasaṃkhyāna prāsāda viśeṣāt adhikam na kiṃcid prārthayate
apiśabdāt prasṃkhyāne api na prārthanā
tatra pi prasṃkhyāne viraktaḥ
sarvathā sarveṇa prakāreṇa viveka khyātiḥ yasya sa sarvathā viveka khyātiḥ eva bhavati
kleśa saṃskāra bīja kṣayāt na asya śarīra ādau śūnye iva īśmani iva asmi mama iti vā jñāna prasāda mātra eka āyatanasya pratyaya antarāṇi utpadyante
tadā sya brāhmāṇasya sarvathā viveka khyāteḥ dharmameghaḥ nāma samādhiḥ bhavati
kaivalya ākhyam param dharmam varṣati iti dharmameghaḥ iti saṃjñā
tatas kleśa karma nivṛttiḥ
tasya dharmamedha nāmnaḥ samādheḥ samyagdarśana pāka abhirūpasya lābhāt bhāvāt abidyā ādayaḥ kleśāḥ samūlakāṣam kaṣitāḥ vāsanābhiḥ saha samastāḥ pralīnāḥ bhavanti
kuśala a kuśśalāḥ ca karma āśayāḥ sa mūlaghātam hatāḥ bhavanti
mūlaiḥ kleśaiḥ saha ucchinnāḥ bhavanti
kleśa karma nivṛttau jīvan eva vidvān muktaḥ bhavati
kasmāt evam yatas viparyayaḥ mithyājñānam bhavasya janmanaḥ kāraṇam
na hi kṣīṇa viparyayaḥ kaścid kvacid jātaḥ dṛśyate
tadā sarva āvaraṇa mala apetasya jñānasya ānantyāt jñeyam alpam
tadā dharma medha samādhi samaye sarvaiḥ kleśa karma āvaraṇaiḥ rajaḥ tamaḥ janmabhiḥ vimuktasya jñānasya sattva puruṣa anya tā khyāti mātrasya bhavati ānantyam
tat katham iti tamasā na abhibhūtam anantam jñāna sattvam tasya tiraskṛta rajaḥ malasya anantasya nistaraṅga mahodadhi deśīyasya nirahitasya avikriyasya katham tat grahāṇa sāmarthyam iti āha kvacid rajasā pravartitam citta sattvam uddhāṭitam vāyunā iva mahā payoda maṇḍalam āhatam cūcitam grahaṇa samartham
svatas sattvasya apravartanāt rajasaḥ hiḥ pravṛtti sāmarthyam iti
tadā asya cittasya bhavati ānantyam aśeṣa jñeya viṣaya tvam ambara tala madhya vartinaḥ jaladhara nirodha nirgatasya sveḥ iva
tasya jñānasya ānantyā aśeṣa viṣaya tvāt jñeyam alpam saṃpadyate
yathā ākāśe khadyotaḥ iti
yathā ākāśa apekṣayā khadyotaḥ na kiṃcid evam etat jñāna abhisamīkṣayā jñeyam na kiṃcid iti
paramārtha jñāna avasthāyām aśeṣa biparyaya tirodhāne sarva puruṣa artha śūnyatā ca iti etad pradarśana artham udāharaṇam āha yatra idam uktam andhaḥ maṇim avindat tam anaṅguliḥ āvayat
agrīvaḥ tam pratyamuñcat tam ajihvaḥ bhyapūjayat
iti
yathā andhaḥ ādīnām maṇī vedha ādikam asambhavat api viparyayeṇa andhaḥ maṇim avidhyat iti vyavahriyate tathā jñāna jñeya saṃvyavahāraḥ api viparyaya avasthāyām eva
viparyaya abhāve tu sarva puruṣa artha śūnyāḥ eva guṇāḥ sampadyante iti
tatas kṛtārthānām pariṇāma krama parisamāptiḥ guṇānām
tatas dharma medha samādhi samudayāt kṛtārthāḥ citta guṇāḥ sampadyante
citta adhīna tvāt ca kārya karaṇa ārambhiṇaḥ api sattva ādayaḥ kṛtārthāḥ bhavanti
samastasya puruṣa arthasya kṛta tvāt eṣām kṛtārthānām guṇānām janma maraṇa pra bhāva vāha rūpaḥ pariṇāma kramaḥ parisamāpyate
na hi kṛta bhoga apavarga arthāḥ kṣaṇam api prayojana abhāvāt avasthātum utsahante
pariṇāma krama parisamāptiḥ iti uktam
atha kaḥ yam guṇa kramaḥ nāma yasya parisamāptiḥ upavarṇitā
tasya ayam adhigama upāyaḥ ucyate kṣaṇa pratiyogī kramaḥ
kṣaṇam prati yujyate iti kṣaṇa pratiyogī
kṣaṇāntarya ātmā kṣaṇasya anantara tā kṣaṇa ānantaryam tad ātmā tad svabhāvaḥ
kṣaṇa ānantaryam eva kṣaṇa tad kramayoḥ iti
kim punar asya grahaṇe liṅgam iti āha pariṇāmasya apara antena vināśa avasthā rūpeṇa avasānena liṅgena nigṛhyate saḥ kramaḥ
katham apara antena nirgrahaṇam iti ucyate na hi ananubhūta kramā kramam an avalambamānā kṣaṇe purāṇa tā vastrasya ante vināśa kāle bhavati iti
na hi kadācid bhūta mātrasya eva vastrasya purāṇa tā dṛśyate
tasmāt purānata abhivyakti liṅgena abhyūhyate yena iyam purāṇa tā vastrasya abhivyaktim upasaṃprāpitā sa kramaḥ
tatra yadi alabdha avasāna tvam ca kramasya syāt tatas yuktam kṛtārthānām pariṇāma krama parisamāptiḥ guṇānām iti vaktum
tat ca labdha alabdha avasāna tvam kramasya nitya anitya tve ghaṭate
tatra anityeṣu vastra ādiṣu kramaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na tu nityeṣu
tatas ca guṇānām nityānām pariṇāma krama prisamāptiḥ ayuktā syāt iti āśaṅkamānaḥ āha nityeṣu ca kramaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ kim sarvatra na iti āha dvividhā iyam nitya tā pariṇāma nitya tā guṇānām kūṭastha nitya tā puruṣasya iti
nanu pariṇāminām guṇānām katham nitya tā syāt iti vravīti yasmin pariṇammāne tattvam na vihanyate
yasya yat rūpam pramāṇena upalabdham tasya tat tattvam
yadi asmin na vihanyate na vyabhicarati tat api nityam
guṇānām api sukha duḥkha moha ātma tā prakāśa kriyā sthiti śīla tā ca tattvam na vihanyate
tasmāt ete api pariṇāma nityāḥ
ubhayatra ca guṇa apuruṣeṣu tattvasya avighātāt nitya tvam
tatas guṇeṣu api nityeṣu pariṇāmaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti labdha alabdha prayavasāna tvam sthitam
tatra guṇa dharmeṣu mahat ādisu kramaḥ labdha paryavasānaḥ śarīra ādiṣu api
nityeṣu tu guṇeṣu dharmiṣu alabdha paryavasānaḥ nitya tvāt eṣām
kūṭastha nityeṣu sva rūpa mātra pratiṣṭheṣu mukta puruṣeṣu sva rūpa astitā krameṇa eva anubhūyate
tena mukta puruṣeṣu asān api anubhavadāreṇa śabda pṛṣṭhena astikriyām upādāya vikalpitaḥ iti alabdha paryavasānaḥ eva
paramārthataḥ puruṣeṣu apariṇāmi tvāt na asti kramaḥ iti arthaḥ
atha asya saṃsārasya sthityā pradhāna rūpeṇa gagtyā vikāra ātmanā dvayam ca guṇa ātmakam iti guṇeṣu ca vartamānasya asti krama parisamāptiḥ na vā iti avacanīyam etat
asti eva iti avadhāraṇam na śakyam kartum
na api na asti eva iti
kim tu vibhajya kasyacid asti kasya api na asti iti vacanīyam eva
katham asti praśnaḥ ekānta vacanīyaḥ a pravibhajya api
yathā sarvaḥ jātaḥ mariṣyati ajñānī iti
nanu jñānavān api mariṣyati eva
ucyate ajñasya hi maraṇm iti abhimānaḥ na jñāninaḥ
tathā ca uktam mithyā etat āhuḥ mriyati iti mūḍhāḥ iti
atha sarvaḥ mṛtvā janiṣyate iti vibhajya vacanīyam etat ekānta anupapatteḥ
katham pratyudita khyātiḥ kṣīṇa tṛṣṇaḥ kuśalaḥ na janiṣyate itaraḥ ajñaḥ aniṣyate
tathā manuṣya jātiḥ śreyasī eva naḥ eva vā iti avacanīyaḥ praśnaḥ
pravibhajya tu vacanīyaḥ eva
katham paśūn uddiśya śreyasī bhavati
devān ṛṣīn ca adhikṛtya na śreyasī bhavati
ayam tu avacanīyaḥ eva a pravibhajya sāmānyena praśnaḥ yathā saṃsāraḥ yam antavān eva iti anantaḥ eva iti vā
bandha mokṣa anupapatteḥ
pravibhajya tu vacanīyaḥ eva
yathā kuśalasya asti saṃsāra cakra parisamāptiḥ na itarasya iti
anyatara avadhāraṇe doṣaḥ
saṃsāraḥ ntavān eva anantaḥ eva iti vā anyatara avadhāraṇe doṣaḥ
tasmāt a vyākaraṇīyaḥ eva ayam sāma anena a pravibhajya praśnaḥ yathā sarvaḥ mṛtvā janiṣyate iti evam manuṣya jātiḥ śreyasī eva iti ca
tasmāt suṣṭhu uktam kṛtārthānām pariṇāma krama parisamāptiḥ guṇānām iti viśeṣaṇam
guṇa adhikāra parisamāptau kaivalyam uktam
tad svarūpam avadhāryate
kaivalyam prati vipratipatteḥ
keṣāṃcid vijñāna santānasya atyanta upaśamaḥ kaivalyam
keṣām cit tu navānām ātma guṇānām buddhi icchā dveṣa prayatna sukha duḥkha dharma adharma saṃskārāṇām ucchedena acetanasya dravya mātrasya puruṣasya avasthānam
keṣāṃcid īśvara sāyujyam
keṣāṃcid sarvajña tvāt īśvara tulya dharma tva prāptiḥ kaivalyam iti bhinnā matiḥ
iha api vipratipatti praṇodāya kaivalya svarūpam avadhāryate puruṣa artha śūnyānām guṇānām yaḥ pratiprasavaḥ pratisaṃsargaḥ sva kāraṇe prati astamayaḥ iti arthaḥ pārya karaṇa ātmaka tayā apariṇatānām tat kaivalyam puruṣasya kevala tvam guṇaiḥ abhiśrībhāvaḥ iti arthaḥ
sva rūpa pratiṣṭhā vā citiḥ śktiḥ iti
buddhi sattva anabhisaṃbandhinī yā puruṣasya citi śaktiḥ amiśrā kevalā tasyāḥ sadā tathā eva avasthānam kevalāyāḥ bhāvaḥ kaivalyam
nanu kaivalyasya ekatve katham vikalpaḥ kriyāyām hi vikalpaḥ na vastuni
vastu svarūpasya bheda anupapatteḥ kaivalyam api vastu katham tat vikalpyate iti na eṣa doṣaḥ
nimitta naimittakayoḥ prabheda upapatteḥ nimitta naimittka bheda upacaritaḥ api vikalpaḥ rūpatā sā kārya karaṇa ātmakānām puruṣa artha śūnyānām guṇānām prati a sṃsargāt nimittāt apagacchati iti nimittam eva pratiprasava ākhyam kaivalya śabdena upacaritam pūrvam
dvitīyam tu guṇa pratiprasava nimitta bhāvi yat svarūpa avasthānam puruṣasya guṇaiḥ amiśrita tayā tat kaivalyam iti viśeṣaḥ
guṇa puruṣa antara svarūpa tattva nirdhāraṇena tantra antarīya tatva svarūpa nirākaraṇena ca kaivalya antarāṇi niveditavyāni
tatra oṅkāraḥ maṅgala arthaḥ prayuktaḥ parameśvara nāma aṅkita mastaka tayā tantra pracaya artham śānti artham vā veda āraṇyaka vat iti om iti
oṅkāraḥ yasya vaktā samacarat phalaiḥ karma yasmāt aśeṣam niṣkarma kleśa pākaḥ ghaṭayati sakalam yaḥ phalena kriyāṇām
īśānām īśvaraḥ yaḥ sthiti bhava nidhana prakriyāṇām vidhātā dhyāya naḥ śuklimānam vyapanudatu tarām kṛṣṇimānam sa kṛṣṇaḥ
yātrā kṛtaḥ trijagatām yat acintya śakti leśām daśa āhuḥ iha mīnamukha avatārān
kleśa udbhava trividha tāpa paramparā ārtāḥ tam nāga nātha śayanam śaraṇam vrajāmaḥ
phaṇa ratna ogha vidyoti pṛthivī dyu nabhaḥ diśe
yogi indrāya phaṇi indrāya tad patañjalaye namaḥ
yogena cittasya padena vācām malam śarīrasya tu vaidyakena
yaḥ u pākarot tam pravaram munīnām patañjalim prāñjaliḥ ānataḥ smi
sa jayati patañjali muniḥ yena śreyaḥ rtha sārtha sasyānām
vihitaḥ harṣaḥ tāpa tritaya hṛtā dharma meghena
yaḥ tatāna bhava mārga laṅghinām kleśa karma maya dharma nuttaye
dharma medha mukha yoga toyadam tam patañjalim ṛṣim praṇataḥ smi
vadana āhita pūrṇa candrakam gurum īśānam abhūtibhūṣaṇam
praṇamāmi a bhujaṅga saṅgraham bhagavat pādam apūrva śaṅkaram
iti śrī govanda bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣyasya paramahaṃsa parivrājaka ācāryasya śrī śaṅkarabhagavataḥ kṛtau pātañjala yoga sūtra śāstra bhāṣya vivaraṇe caturthaḥ kaivalya pādaḥ
samāptam ca idam vivaraṇam
